# Late (Lat)

## Chapter 1

**1:1**
Zolai: Mi nuamsa i cihte pen migilote’ thu a zui lo mi, mimawhte’ gamtat bangin a gamta lo mi, mi a thusim lote tawh a kipawl lo mi ahi hi.
English: Blessed is the man that walketh not in the counsel of the ungodly, nor standeth in the way of sinners, Nor sitteth in the seat of the scornful.

**1:2**
Zolai: Ama nopsakna pen Topa thu sung bek mah hi a, sun le zanin ama thu a ngaihsunsun mi ahi hi.
English: But his delight is in the law of the LORD ; And in his law doth he meditate day and night.

**1:3**
Zolai: Amah pen lui tuiluang gei-a a kisuan ama gah hunin gah a, a teh a vul ngei lo singkung tawh kibang hi. Ama hihna khempeuhah a maa pai mahmah hi.
English: And he shall be like a tree planted by the rivers of water, That bringeth forth his fruit in his season; His leaf also shall not wither; And whatsoever he doeth shall prosper.

**1:4**
Zolai: Migilote ahihleh tua bang hi lo uh a, huih in a letkhiat anvai tawh kibang lel uh hi.
English: The ungodly are not so: But are like the chaff which the wind driveth away.

**1:5**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin migilote in thukhenna thuak zo lo ding uh a, mimawhte pen midikte’ pawl sungah kihel thei lo ding uh hi;
English: Therefore the ungodly shall not stand in the judgment, Nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.

**1:6**
Zolai: bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in midikte lam lakin hu tawntung a, migilote ahihleh sia maimang ding uh hi.
English: For the LORD knoweth the way of the righteous: But the way of the ungodly shall perish.

## Chapter 2

**2:1**
Zolai: Bang thu hangin minam dangte siatna dingah kithukhat sim uh a, mite in a mawkna dingpi-in sawmsim uh ahi hiam?
English: Why do the heathen rage, And the people imagine a vain thing?

**2:2**
Zolai: Leitung kumpite le gam ukte in Topa le ama sathau nilh pa langpangin vaihawm uh a,
English: The kings of the earth set themselves, and the rulers take counsel together, Against the LORD , and against his anointed, saying ,

**2:3**
Zolai: “Amau’ hong henna khaute sutat khia-in, amau’ khaute ei kiang panin paaikhia ni,” ci uh hi.
English: Let us break their bands asunder, And cast away their cords from us.

**2:4**
Zolai: Vantunga a tupa in amaute na nuihsan a, tua Topa in amaute a zahko hi.
English: He that sitteth in the heavens shall laugh: The Lord shall have them in derision.

**2:5**
Zolai: Tua ciangin hehna tawh amau kiangah thu gen ding a, hehluat mahmahna tawh amaute linglawng sakin,
English: Then shall he speak unto them in his wrath, And vex them in his sore displeasure.

**2:6**
Zolai: “Ka mual siangtho Zion tungah ka kumpi ka tusak khin hi,” ci hi.
English: Yet have I set my king upon my holy hill of Zion.

**2:7**
Zolai: Topa’ thukhenna tu-in ka hong gen ding hi: Amah in keima tungah, “Nang pen ka tapa na hi a, tuni-in na Pa ka suak hi.
English: I will declare the decree: the LORD hath said unto me, Thou art my Son; this day have I begotten thee.

**2:8**
Zolai: Keima tungah hong ngen in; nangma luah dingin minamte ka bawl ding a, leimong dongin na neihsa ka hisak ding hi.
English: Ask of me, and I shall give thee the heathen for thine inheritance, And the uttermost parts of the earth for thy possession.

**2:9**
Zolai: Sik tawn khat tawh amaute na satkham ding a, beelseek pa in beel a denkhap bangin leilakah amaute na dengzan ding hi,” hong ci hi.
English: Thou shalt break them with a rod of iron; Thou shalt dash them in pieces like a potter's vessel.

**2:10**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin kumpite aw, tu-in pil ta un; leitung gam a ukte aw, tu-in thu phawk ta un.
English: Be wise now therefore, O ye kings: Be instructed, ye judges of the earth.

**2:11**
Zolai: Launa tawh Topa’ na sem unla, linna tawh a khe nam un; tua hikeileh amah sinso-in lamkalah na siamang ding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh amah heh pakpak hi. Amah a bel khempeuh mi nuamsate ahi hi.
English: Serve the LORD with fear, And rejoice with trembling.

## Chapter 3

**3:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka galte tam mahmah a, mi tampi tak in kei hong langpan’ nainai uh hi.
English: LORD , how are they increased that trouble me! Many are they that rise up against me.

**3:2**
Zolai: Pasian in amah huh lo ding, mi tampi in hong ci uh hi.
English: Many there be which say of my soul, There is no help for him in God. Selah.

**3:3**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa aw, nang pen ka kidalna lum, ka minthanna le ka lu hong phong pa na hi hi.
English: But thou, O LORD , art a shield for me; My glory, and the lifter up of mine head.

**3:4**
Zolai: Nakpi takin Topa ka galsap a, amah in a mual siangtho panin kei a hong dawng hi.
English: I cried unto the LORD with my voice, And he heard me out of his holy hill. Selah.

**3:5**
Zolai: Lumin ka ihmu a, Topa in hong kem ahih manin ka thokik hi.
English: I laid me down and slept; I awaked; for the LORD sustained me.

**3:6**
Zolai: Keimah a hong galbawl keimah a hong umcih mi tul sawm tampite ka kihta kei hi.
English: I will not be afraid of ten thousands of people, That have set themselves against me round about.

**3:7**
Zolai: Tho in, Topa ! Kei hong hon in, ka Pasian! Bang hang hiam cih leh ka galte khempeuh’ paang nangmah in na beenggawp a, migilote’ ha na sutan hi.
English: Arise, O LORD ; save me, O my God: For thou hast smitten all mine enemies upon the cheek bone; Thou hast broken the teeth of the ungodly.

**3:8**
Zolai: Gualzawhna pen Topa nangma hang ahi hi. Na mite tungah na thupha hong tung ta hen!
English: Salvation belongeth unto the LORD : Thy blessing is upon thy people. Selah.

## Chapter 4

**4:1**
Zolai: A thuman ka Pasian aw, ka hong sap ciangin hong dawng in. Gimna ka thuak ciangin nopsakna nong pia hi. Kei hong hehpih inla, ka thungetna hong za in.
English: Hear me when I call, O God of my righteousness: Thou hast enlarged me when I was in distress; Have mercy upon me, and hear my prayer.

**4:2**
Zolai: Mite aw, ka minphatna in bang tanvei daina thuak ding ahi hiam? Bang tanvei thumawkna deihin zuauthu zong ding na hi uh hiam?
English: O ye sons of men, how long will ye turn my glory into shame? How long will ye love vanity, and seek after leasing? Selah.

**4:3**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa in ama a dingin miphate a tuamkoihlam thei ta un. Ke’n ka sap ciangin Topa in hong za hi.
English: But know that the LORD hath set apart him that is godly for himself: The LORD will hear when I call unto him.

**4:4**
Zolai: Lau-in ling unla, mawhna peel un. Na lupna tung uhah lungngai phapha unla, om khikhe un.
English: Stand in awe, and sin not: Commune with your own heart upon your bed, and be still. Selah.

**4:5**
Zolai: A man biakpiaknate lui unla, Topa muang un.
English: Offer the sacrifices of righteousness, And put your trust in the LORD .

**4:6**
Zolai: Mi tampi in, “Thupha tampi hong pia in. Ko tungah na maitang vang hong taangsak in, Topa !” ci uh hi.
English: There be many that say, Who will shew us any good? LORD , lift thou up The light of thy countenance upon us.

**4:7**
Zolai: Amaute, an le leengtui a hauh cianga a nuam uh sangin nuamna lianzaw ka lung sungah nong guan hi.
English: Thou hast put gladness in my heart, More than in the time that their corn and their wine increased.

**4:8**
Zolai: Nuamtakin lumin ka ihmu ta ding hi; bang hang hiam cih leh Topa aw, nangmah bek in lungmuanna munah na hong omsak hi.
English: I will both lay me down in peace, and sleep: For thou, LORD , only makest me dwell in safety.

## Chapter 5

**5:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, kong paunate hong ngai inla, ka hong thumnate hong thudon in.
English: Give ear to my words, O LORD , Consider my meditation.

**5:2**
Zolai: Ka kumpi le ka Pasian aw, nangma tungah hong thum ka hih manin ka kikona aw hong ngai in.
English: Hearken unto the voice of my cry, my King, and my God: For unto thee will I pray.

**5:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, zingsang simin ka aw nong za a, zingsang simin nangma a dingin biakna bawlin kong ngak hi.
English: My voice shalt thou hear in the morning, O LORD ; In the morning will I direct my prayer unto thee, and will look up.

**5:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh gitlohna lamsang a deih Pasian na hi kei a, siatna pen tawlkhat zong nang tawh a omkhawm thei ahi kei hi.
English: For thou art not a God that hath pleasure in wickedness: Neither shall evil dwell with thee.

**5:5**
Zolai: A kisathei mite nangma mit tawh kituak lo a, siatna a bawlte khempeuh nangmah in na mudah hi.
English: The foolish shall not stand in thy sight: Thou hatest all workers of iniquity.

**5:6**
Zolai: Zuauthu a gen mite nangmah in na susia hi. Topa in mi thahnopna lungsim le mi khemnopna lungsim a neite a mudah hi.
English: Thou shalt destroy them that speak leasing: The LORD will abhor the bloody and deceitful man.

**5:7**
Zolai: Kei ahihleh a kicing itna kip suangin na inn sungah ka tum ding a, nangmah zahtakna tawh kunin a siangtho na biakinn lam nga-in kong bia ding hi.
English: But as for me, I will come into thy house in the multitude of thy mercy: And in thy fear will I worship toward thy holy temple.

**5:8**
Zolai: Topa aw, gal tampi nei ka hih manin na thumanna tawh kei hong makaih inla, keima mai-ah na lampi taangsak in.
English: Lead me, O LORD , in thy righteousness because of mine enemies; Make thy way straight before my face.

**5:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amau sungah thuman om lo hi. Amau lungsimah siatna bek ngaihsun uh a, amau’ gawlgui pen a kihongsa hankhuk tawh kibang hi. A kam uh tawh mawk phat uh hi.
English: For there is no faithfulness in their mouth; Their inward part is very wickedness; Their throat is an open sepulchre; They flatter with their tongue.

**5:10**
Zolai: Pasian aw, a mawhna uh amau mah thuaksak inla, amau’ thu mah tawh amaute puksak in. Amaute in nangmah hong lehdo uh ahih manin amau’ mawhna tampite hangin amaute paaikhia in.
English: Destroy thou them, O God; let them fall by their own counsels; Cast them out in the multitude of their transgressions; for they have rebelled against thee.

**5:11**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nang hong belte khempeuh lungdamsak inla, nuamna la sasak tawntung in. Nangma min a deihte nangma hangin gualzo-in a lungdam theih nadingun amaute na hu hi.
English: But let all those that put their trust in thee rejoice: Let them ever shout for joy, because thou defendest them: let them also that love thy name be joyful in thee.

**5:12**
Zolai: Topa aw, thuman mi thupha na pia a, lum tawh dal bangin deihsakna tawh na dal hi.
English: For thou, LORD , wilt bless the righteous; With favour wilt thou compass him as with a shield.

## Chapter 6

**6:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, na heh laitak hong taii kei inla, lungso sa-in hong thuhilh kei in.
English: O LORD , rebuke me not in thine anger, Neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.

**6:2**
Zolai: Topa aw, thaneem ka hih manin kei tungah dikna hong zang in. Topa aw, ka guh ka taang na mahmah ahih manin hong damsak in.
English: Have mercy upon me, O LORD ; for I am weak: O LORD , heal me; for my bones are vexed.

**6:3**
Zolai: Ka hingim mahmah hi. Topa aw, bang tanvei nang hong zekai lai ding na hi hiam?
English: My soul is also sore vexed: But thou, O LORD , how long?

**6:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, hong kihei inla, kei hong hon in. Itna kip a nei pa na hih manin keimah hong hon in.
English: Return, O LORD , deliver my soul: Oh save me for thy mercies' sake.

**6:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh misite omna gam sungah nangmah phawk theih nading bangmah om lo ahih manin, Leinuai panin kua in nang hong phat thei ding ahi hiam?
English: For in death there is no remembrance of thee: In the grave who shall give thee thanks?

**6:6**
Zolai: Ka tautauna-in ka gim hi. Zan sialin ka khitui in ka lupna tum a, ka kahkahna-in ka lupna kawt dikdek hi.
English: I am weary with my groaning; all the night make I my bed to swim; I water my couch with my tears.

**6:7**
Zolai: Dahna hangin ka mit mial a, ka galte’ hong bawlna hangin ka mitzung zaw semsem hi.
English: Mine eye is consumed because of grief; It waxeth old because of all mine enemies.

**6:8**
Zolai: Siatna a bawlte khempeuh aw, ka kiang panin kihemkhia un; bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in ka kahna aw a za hi.
English: Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; For the LORD hath heard the voice of my weeping.

**6:9**
Zolai: Topa in keima thumna hong za khinzo a, Topa in ka thungetna hong sang ta hi.
English: The LORD hath heard my supplication; The LORD will receive my prayer.

**6:10**
Zolai: Ka galte khempeuh zahhuai mahmahin genthei ding uh hi. Amaute nungkikin maizumna thuak pah ding uh hi.
English: Let all mine enemies be ashamed and sore vexed: Let them return and be ashamed suddenly.

## Chapter 7

**7:1**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, nangmah ka hong bel hi. Kei hong delhte’ kiang panin hong dal inla hong hon in.
English: O LORD my God, in thee do I put my trust: Save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me:

**7:2**
Zolai: Kei hong hon kei lecin a hong hon ding dang kuamah om lo ahih manin amaute in humpinelkai bangin hong kaikhia-in hong balgawp ding uh hi.
English: Lest he tear my soul like a lion, rending it in pieces, While there is none to deliver.

**7:3**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, ka gamtat a siat a, ka khut a khialh leh,
English: O LORD my God, if I have done this; If there be iniquity in my hands;

**7:4**
Zolai: bangmah thu om lopi-in ka lawmte khemin, ka galte ka huh taak leh,
English: If I have rewarded evil unto him that was at peace with me; (Yea, I have delivered him that without cause is mine enemy:)

**7:5**
Zolai: galte in kei hong delhin hong pha uh hen la, leilakah kei hong tuancilsak inla, leilakah kei hong sialpai ta uh hen.
English: Let the enemy persecute my soul, and take it ; Yea, let him tread down my life upon the earth, and lay mine honour in the dust. Selah.

**7:6**
Zolai: Tho in, Topa, a hehsa-in thasaan inla, ka galte’ hehna panin kei hong dal in. Khanglo in, ka Pasian aw, thukhenna ding hun khat na seh khinzo hi.
English: Arise, O LORD , in thine anger, lift up thyself because of the rage of mine enemies: And awake for me to the judgment that thou hast commanded.

**7:7**
Zolai: Nangma omna kiimah mite kikhawmsak inla, amaute’ omna tung a sangna munah tu in.
English: So shall the congregation of the people compass thee about: For their sakes therefore return thou on high.

**7:8**
Zolai: Topa in mite thu a khen hi. Topa aw, ka thumanna le keima sunga om ka dikna tawh kizui-in thu hong khen in.
English: The LORD shall judge the people: Judge me, O LORD , According to my righteousness, and according to mine integrity that is in me.

**7:9**
Zolai: Lungsim le ngaihsutna a en a thuman Pasian aw, migilote’ siatna beisak inla, mi thumante kipsak in.
English: Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end; but establish the just: For the righteous God Trieth the hearts and reins.

**7:10**
Zolai: Pasian, kei hong hupa hi a, lungsim man mite a hon hi.
English: My defence is of God, Which saveth the upright in heart.

**7:11**
Zolai: Pasian, thu a tangin a khen pa hi a, migilote tungah a heh den pa ahi hi.
English: God judgeth the righteous, And God is angry with the wicked every day.

**7:12**
Zolai: Mite a kibawlphat kik kei leh, Pasian in a thalkhau sui zo a, a namsau taat ding hi.
English: If he turn not, he will whet his sword; He hath bent his bow, and made it ready.

**7:13**
Zolai: Amah in mei thaltang bawl a, sih theihna ama galhiamte a baihsa-in a koihzo hi.
English: He hath also prepared for him the instruments of death; He ordaineth his arrows against the persecutors.

**7:14**
Zolai: Migilo in thusia paii a, suak nuamin na a, zuauthu a hingkhia hi.
English: Behold, he travaileth with iniquity, And hath conceived mischief, and brought forth falsehood.

**7:15**
Zolai: Amah in gum to a, ama tawhsa gum sung mahah amah a kia hi.
English: He made a pit, and digged it, And is fallen into the ditch which he made.

**7:16**
Zolai: Ama lunggulh hoih lo pen ama lu tungah tukik a, ama gamtatsia pen ama luzang mahah tukik hi.
English: His mischief shall return upon his own head, And his violent dealing shall come down upon his own pate.

**7:17**
Zolai: Ke’n ahihleh, ama dikna om bangin Topa’ tungah lungdamna ka lak ding a, a Sangpen Topa’ min phatna la ka sak ding hi.
English: I will praise the LORD according to his righteousness: And will sing praise to the name of the LORD most high.

## Chapter 8

**8:1**
Zolai: Topa kote’ Topa aw, leitung khempeuhah na min lian mahmah hi. Nangmah a hong kiphatna awgingte in vantung ban a,
English: O LORD our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the earth! Who hast set thy glory above the heavens.

**8:2**
Zolai: naungekte le naupangte’ kam tawh nangmah phatna la kisa hi. Gal na neih manin galte le langpangte na daihsakna dingin panmunkip na bawl khin hi.
English: Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings hast thou ordained strength because of thine enemies, That thou mightest still the enemy and the avenger.

**8:3**
Zolai: Na nasepna, na bawlsa, kha le aksite, le na vantungte ka et ciangin,
English: When I consider thy heavens, the work of thy fingers, The moon and the stars, which thou hast ordained;

**8:4**
Zolai: na ngaihsut tham dingin mihing bang hi lel a, na phawk tham dingin mihing’ ta bang hi lel ahi hiam?
English: What is man, that thou art mindful of him? And the son of man, that thou visitest him?

**8:5**
Zolai: Ahi zongin, vantungmi sangin a neuzaw deuh bekin na bawl a, minthanna le pahtawina nangmah in na guan hi.
English: For thou hast made him a little lower than the angels, And hast crowned him with glory and honour.

**8:6**
Zolai: Na khut tawh na bawlsate khempeuh tungah ukna thu ama tungah na pia a, na khempeuh na uksak hi.
English: Thou madest him to have dominion over the works of thy hands; Thou hast put all things under his feet:

**8:7**
Zolai: Tuu le bawng khempeuh, gamsa khempeuh zong,
English: All sheep and oxen, Yea, and the beasts of the field;

**8:8**
Zolai: huih lak a leng vasate, tui sunga om ngasate, tui, lampi-a a tawn khempeuhte, na khempeuh ama khenuai-ah na koih hi.
English: The fowl of the air, and the fish of the sea, And whatsoever passeth through the paths of the seas.

**8:9**
Zolai: Topa, kote’ Topa aw, leitung khempeuhah na min lian mahmah hi.
English: O LORD our Lord, How excellent is thy name in all the earth!

## Chapter 9

**9:1**
Zolai: Ka lungsim khempeuh tawh Topa tungah lungdamna kong ko ding a, na bawl a lamdangte khempeuh ka gen ding hi.
English: I will praise thee , O LORD , with my whole heart; I will shew forth all thy marvellous works.

**9:2**
Zolai: Nangma hangin nuamin ka diang ding a, na min phatna ka sa ding hi, Sangpenpa aw.
English: I will be glad and rejoice in thee: I will sing praise to thy name, O thou Most High.

**9:3**
Zolai: Ka galte a nungkik ciangin, nangma mai-ah amaute pukin kisia uh hi.
English: When mine enemies are turned back, They shall fall and perish at thy presence.

**9:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh keima thutanna na hong kipsak a, tokhom tungah tu-in thu a manin na khen hi.
English: For thou hast maintained my right and my cause; Thou satest in the throne judging right.

**9:5**
Zolai: Minamte na taii a, migilote na susia hi. A maimang dingin amau’ min na phiat hi.
English: Thou hast rebuked the heathen, thou hast destroyed the wicked, Thou hast put out their name for ever and ever.

**9:6**
Zolai: Siat denna sungah galte beimang hi. A khuate uh na zunglot a, amaute kiphawkkha nawn lo hi.
English: O thou enemy, destructions are come to a perpetual end: And thou hast destroyed cities; Their memorial is perished with them.

**9:7**
Zolai: Topa ahihleh kumpi za-ah tu ngitnget a, thukhen nadingin a tokhom a bawl hi.
English: But the LORD shall endure for ever: He hath prepared his throne for judgment.

**9:8**
Zolai: Leitung mite’ thu a mantakin khen a, a kilawm bangin mite’ thu a khen hi.
English: And he shall judge the world in righteousness, He shall minister judgment to the people in uprightness.

**9:9**
Zolai: Topa pen, netniamna a thuakte a’ dingin munkip hi a, haksat hun ciangin munmuanhuai ahi hi.
English: The LORD also will be a refuge for the oppressed, A refuge in times of trouble.

**9:10**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang a hong zongte nusia lo na hih manin, na min a theite in nang hong muang uh hi.
English: And they that know thy name will put their trust in thee: For thou, LORD , hast not forsaken them that seek thee.

**9:11**
Zolai: Zion-ah a om Topa phatna la sa un! Ama nasepnate mite’ lakah gen un!
English: Sing praises to the LORD , which dwelleth in Zion: Declare among the people his doings.

**9:12**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh mi thahna a hua pa in amaute phawk a, a thuak mite’ awging amah in mangngilh lo hi.
English: When he maketh inquisition for blood, he remembereth them: He forgetteth not the cry of the humble.

**9:13**
Zolai: Ka tungah hong dik in, Topa ! Sihna pan hong honkhia pa aw, kei hong mudahte’ hangin keima gim thuaknate hong en inla,
English: Have mercy upon me, O LORD ; Consider my trouble which I suffer of them that hate me, Thou that liftest me up from the gates of death:

**9:14**
Zolai: nangmah a hong kiphatnate phawk kikkik inla, na hong hotkhiatna hangin Jerusalem khua sungah ka nuamna ka gengen ding hi.
English: That I may shew forth all thy praise in the gates of the daughter of Zion: I will rejoice in thy salvation.

**9:15**
Zolai: Amau’ bawlsa gum sung mahah minamte kiasuk uh a, a ngenthang siahna uhah amau’ khe mah a awk hi.
English: The heathen are sunk down in the pit that they made: In the net which they hid is their own foot taken.

**9:16**
Zolai: Topa in thu hong khenin migilote amau’ nasepna mahah awksakna tawh amah hong kilang hi.
English: The LORD is known by the judgment which he executeth: The wicked is snared in the work of his own hands. Higgaion. Selah.

**9:17**
Zolai: Pasian a mangngilh minam khempeuh sung panin migilote, Leinuai-ah pai ding uh hi.
English: The wicked shall be turned into hell, And all the nations that forget God.

**9:18**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh mi cimawhte kimangngilh den lo ding a, mizawngte’ lametna bei paisuak lo ding hi.
English: For the needy shall not alway be forgotten: The expectation of the poor shall not perish for ever.

**9:19**
Zolai: Tho in, Topa ! Mi kizosak ke’n; na mai-ah minamte sam inla, amaute’ tungah thu khen in!
English: Arise, O LORD ; let not man prevail: Let the heathen be judged in thy sight.

**9:20**
Zolai: Amaute lausak in, Topa ! Mi ahih lelna uh minamte theisak in!
English: Put them in fear, O LORD : That the nations may know themselves to be but men. Selah.

## Chapter 10

**10:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, bang hangin gamla din na hi hiam? Haksat hunin bang hangin nang bucip khong na hi hiam?
English: Why standest thou afar off, O LORD ? Why hidest thou thyself in times of trouble?

**10:2**
Zolai: Migilote in kiphatsakna tawh mizawngte uuk delh uh hi. Amau ngaihsut vaihawmna mahah amaute awksak in.
English: The wicked in his pride doth persecute the poor: Let them be taken in the devices that they have imagined.

**10:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh migilo in a lungsim deihna kisaktheihpih a, ngahna dingah a huaiham pa in Topa phuisamin a taisan hi.
English: For the wicked boasteth of his heart's desire, And blesseth the covetous, whom the LORD abhorreth.

**10:4**
Zolai: Migilo in kiphatsakna lungsim nei a, Topa zong lo hi. Ama ngaihsutna khempeuhah, “Pasian om kei,” a ci hi.
English: The wicked, through the pride of his countenance, will not seek after God: God is not in all his thoughts.

**10:5**
Zolai: A hihna khempeuhah a maa pai ngitnget hi. Na thukhennate khempeuh ama muhna in a batzawh lohin sang mahmah a, a galte khempeuh ahihleh amah in nehpiksan lel hi.
English: His ways are always grievous; Thy judgments are far above out of his sight: As for all his enemies, he puffeth at them.

**10:6**
Zolai: A lungsim sungah, “Kiling ngei kei ning; khang tawntungin kamsiatna tuak kei ning,” ci-in a ngaihsun hi.
English: He hath said in his heart, I shall not be moved: For I shall never be in adversity.

**10:7**
Zolai: Ama kampaute pen hamsia, khemna, le netniamna tawh kidim a, siatna le man lohna bekbek thugenin a nei tawntung hi.
English: His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and fraud: Under his tongue is mischief and vanity.

**10:8**
Zolai: Khuaneute sungah mi a buksimin tu a, munbu kawmah mawhnei lote a that hi. Ama mit in mi tuahsiate ensim a,
English: He sitteth in the lurking places of the villages: In the secret places doth he murder the innocent: His eyes are privily set against the poor.

**10:9**
Zolai: humpinelkai in a kuahawm sung pan a buk bangin amah in buksimin, mizawngte a man dingin buk a, a ngenthang sungah mizawngte kai-in a man hi.
English: He lieth in wait secretly as a lion in his den: He lieth in wait to catch the poor: He doth catch the poor, when he draweth him into his net.

**10:10**
Zolai: A thatanghat thu tawh mi tuahsia mi sucipin a puksuk sak hi.
English: He croucheth, and humbleth himself, That the poor may fall by his strong ones.

**10:11**
Zolai: Ama lungsim sungah, “Hih thute pen Pasian in mangngilh hi; a mai seel hi, en lo ding hi,” ci-in a ngaihsun hi.
English: He hath said in his heart, God hath forgotten: He hideth his face; he will never see it .

**10:12**
Zolai: Tho in, Topa ! Pasian aw, na tha hong san inla, a thuakte mangngilh kei in.
English: Arise, O LORD ; O God, lift up thine hand: Forget not the humble.

**10:13**
Zolai: Bang hangin migilo in Pasian simmawh a, a lungsim sungah, “Hong thei kei na’n teh,” ci ahi hiam?
English: Wherefore doth the wicked contemn God? He hath said in his heart, Thou wilt not require it .

**10:14**
Zolai: Nangmah in na mu hi. Na huh theih nadingin haksatna le gimna a thuakte na ciamteh hi. A tuahsia mi in nangma tungah ama pumpi hong ap a, pa nei lote a huhpa na hi hi.
English: Thou hast seen it ; for thou beholdest mischief and spite, to requite it with thy hand: The poor committeth himself unto thee; Thou art the helper of the fatherless.

**10:15**
Zolai: Giloin siatna a bawlte’ khut kuaitan gawp inla, siatna a bawlzo nawn lo dingin gim pia in.
English: Break thou the arm of the wicked And the evil man: seek out his wickedness till thou find none.

**10:16**
Zolai: Topa, a tawntungin kumpi hi a, ama leitang panin minam dangte beimang ding hi.
English: The LORD is King for ever and ever: The heathen are perished out of his land.

**10:17**
Zolai: Topa aw, lungnemte’ deihna na ngai ding hi. A lungsim uh na hatsak ding a, na bil na ngat ding hi.
English: LORD , thou hast heard the desire of the humble: Thou wilt prepare their heart, thou wilt cause thine ear to hear:

**10:18**
Zolai: Pa nei lote le netniamna a thuakte tungah nang na thutang a, leitung mite in launa tuakkha nawn lo ding uh hi.
English: To judge the fatherless and the oppressed, That the man of the earth may no more oppress.

## Chapter 11

**11:1**
Zolai: Ke’n Topa ka bel hi. Bang hangin ka tungah, “Vasa leeng bangin mualtungah tai in;
English: In the LORD put I my trust: How say ye to my soul, flee as a bird to your mountain?

**11:2**
Zolai: bang hang hiam cih leh, en in, migilote in khuamial sung panin lungsim thutangte a kap dingin a thalkhau uhah thaltang bulhin a thal uh a keek uh hi.
English: For, lo, the wicked bend their bow, they make ready their arrow upon the string, That they may privily shoot at the upright in heart.

**11:3**
Zolai: Bulpite kisusia khin leh midikte in bangcih thei nawn ding hiam?” nong ci thei diam?
English: If the foundations be destroyed, What can the righteous do?

**11:4**
Zolai: Topa a biakinn siangtho sungah om a, Topa’ tokhom vantungah om hi. Amah in mihingte hong en a, mihingte’ gamtatna khempeuh a theitel hi.
English: The LORD is in his holy temple, The LORD 's throne is in heaven: His eyes behold, his eyelids try, the children of men.

**11:5**
Zolai: Topa in midikte le migilote entel a, a ngongtat nuam mite a lungsim in mudah hi.
English: The LORD trieth the righteous: But the wicked and him that loveth violence his soul hateth.

**11:6**
Zolai: Amah in migilote tungah mei-am le kaat zusak ding a, amau’ ngah ding gimna huihsa mahmah hi ding hi.
English: Upon the wicked he shall rain snares, fire and brimstone, and an horrible tempest: This shall be the portion of their cup.

**11:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa dik mahmah a, dik gamtatna a deih hi. Thutang mi in ama mai a mu ding hi.
English: For the righteous LORD loveth righteousness; His countenance doth behold the upright.

## Chapter 12

**12:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, hong huh in; bang hang hiam cih leh mihingte lak panin mi thumante maimang ta a, mipha khat zong om nawn lo hi.
English: Help, LORD ; for the godly man ceaseth; For the faithful fail from among the children of men.

**12:2**
Zolai: Mi kim in a vengte kiangah zuauthu gen ciat a, phat khemna kam zol le lungsim nam nih tawh thu a gen uh hi.
English: They speak vanity every one with his neighbour: With flattering lips and with a double heart do they speak.

**12:3**
Zolai: “I Leii tawh gualzo ding, i mukte eima neihsa; i to kua hiam?” a ci vial, kiphatsakna a piangsak leii, phat khemna muk khempeuh, Topa in atkhia tahen.
English: The LORD shall cut off all flattering lips, And the tongue that speaketh proud things:

**12:5**
Zolai: Topa in, “Mizawngte a neihsa kihawkkhia a, mi cimawhte thumin tau uh ahih ciangin tu-in dingin, amau’ lunggulh, lungmuanna munah amaute ka koih ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: For the oppression of the poor, For the sighing of the needy, Now will I arise, saith the LORD ; I will set him in safety from him that puffeth at him.

**12:6**
Zolai: Topa’ thuciamnate, a siangtho thuciamna hi a, meikhuk sungah sagihvei a kisiangsak ngun tawh kibang hi.
English: The words of the LORD are pure words: As silver tried in a furnace of earth, purified seven times.

**12:7**
Zolai: Topa aw, kote hong dal inla, tukhang mite kiang panin kote hong kem in.
English: Thou shalt keep them, O LORD , Thou shalt preserve them from this generation for ever.

**12:8**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh mihingte lakah siatna kipahtawi a, mun khempeuhah migilote kidimin vak kawikawi uh hi.
English: The wicked walk on every side, When the vilest men are exalted.

## Chapter 13

**13:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, bang tanvei hi lai ding ahi hiam? Kei hong mangngilh paisuak ding na hi hiam? Bang tanvei kei kiang pan na maitang seel ding na hi hiam?
English: How long wilt thou forget me, O LORD ? for ever? How long wilt thou hide thy face from me?

**13:2**
Zolai: Bang tanvei gimna thuakin, sunthapai-in ka lungsim dah ding ahi hiam? Bang tanvei kei tungah ka galte gualzo ding ahi hiam?
English: How long shall I take counsel in my soul, Having sorrow in my heart daily? How long shall mine enemy be exalted over me?

**13:3**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, ngaihsun inla hong dawng in. Ihmulum kha ding ka hih manin ka mitte hong vaksak in.
English: Consider and hear me, O LORD my God: Lighten mine eyes, lest I sleep the sleep of death;

**13:4**
Zolai: Ka galte in, “Ama tungah gualzo khin ung,” ci kha ding hi. Kei ka lin’ manin ka galte nuam kha ding hi.
English: Lest mine enemy say, I have prevailed against him; And those that trouble me rejoice when I am moved.

**13:5**
Zolai: Ahih hangin na itna kip ka muang a, nong hotkhiatna hangin ka lungdam ding hi.
English: But I have trusted in thy mercy; My heart shall rejoice in thy salvation.

**13:6**
Zolai: Nong hehpihna kicing ahih manin, Topa, la kong sak ding hi.
English: I will sing unto the LORD , because he hath dealt bountifully with me.

## Chapter 14

**14:1**
Zolai: Mihaite in a lungsim sung uhah, “Pasian om lo hi,” ci-in ngaihsun uh hi. Amaute sia uh a, kihhuai gamtat uh a, a hoihin a gamta kuamah om lo hi.
English: The fool hath said in his heart, there is no God. They are corrupt, they have done abominable works, There is none that doeth good.

**14:2**
Zolai: A pil gamtat, Pasian a zong a om uh hiam, cih a theih nadingin Topa in vantung panin mihingte hong ensuk hi.
English: The LORD looked down from heaven upon the children of men, To see if there were any that did understand, And seek God.

**14:3**
Zolai: Amaute khempeuh a vekpi-un pukkhin uh hi. A kibangin sia kim uh a, a hoihin a gamta khat zong om lo hi.
English: They are all gone aside, they are all together become filthy: There is none that doeth good, no, not one.

**14:4**
Zolai: Topa’ tungah thu a ngen lo, annek bangin ka mite a netum, siatna a bawlte in thutheihna nei lo ahi hiam?
English: Have all the workers of iniquity no knowledge? Who eat up my people as they eat bread, and call not upon the LORD .

**14:5**
Zolai: Launa lianpi sungah amaute om ding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh Pasian in midikte ompih hi.
English: There were they in great fear: For God is in the generation of the righteous.

**14:6**
Zolai: Mizawngte’ geelna susia nuam uh a, ahih hangin Topa pen mizawngte’ belh ahi hi.
English: Ye have shamed the counsel of the poor, Because the LORD is his refuge.

**14:7**
Zolai: Israel-te a’ ding hotkhiatna Zion panin hong tunna ding thu ka ngenngen hi. Topa in ama mite tungah nopsakna a piakkik ciangin, ama mi Israel-te kipak mahmah ding uh hi.
English: Oh that the salvation of Israel were come out of Zion! When the LORD bringeth back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, and Israel shall be glad.

## Chapter 15

**15:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, na biakinn sungah kua om ding ahi hiam? Na mual siangtho tungah kua teng ding ahi hiam?
English: LORD , who shall abide in thy tabernacle? Who shall dwell in thy holy hill?

**15:2**
Zolai: Paubaang loin gamta-in, a manin na sem a, lungsim tak a gen mi,
English: He that walketh uprightly, and worketh righteousness, and speaketh the truth in his heart.

**15:3**
Zolai: mi gensia loin, a lawmte tungah siatna bawl lo a, a vengte a mawhsak lo mi,
English: He that backbiteth not with his tongue, nor doeth evil to his neighbour, Nor taketh up a reproach against his neighbour.

**15:4**
Zolai: migilote thusim lo a, ahi zongin Topa a zahtakte a pahtawi mi, ama natna ding nangawnah a ciampel lo mi,
English: In whose eyes a vile person is contemned; But he honoureth them that fear the LORD . He that sweareth to his own hurt, and changeth not.

**15:5**
Zolai: ama sum a meetin a kha lo, thutang mite a langpan lo, golhguk a la lo mite teng ding uh hi. Hih bangin a gamtate pen ling ngei lo ding hi.
English: He that putteth not out his money to usury, Nor taketh reward against the innocent. He that doeth these things shall never be moved.

## Chapter 16

**16:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, nang hong bel ka hih manin keimah hong kem in.
English: Preserve me, O God: For in thee do I put my trust.

**16:2**
Zolai: Topa tungah, “Nang, ka Topa na hi hi; nang tawh loin hoihna ka nei kei hi,” ka ci hi.
English: O my soul , thou hast said unto the LORD , Thou art my Lord: My goodness extendeth not to thee;

**16:3**
Zolai: Leitungah a om mi siangthote ahih le, amaute nampi hi a, amaute sungah ka lungkimna teng om hi.
English: But to the saints that are in the earth, And to the excellent, in whom is all my delight.

**16:4**
Zolai: Pasian dang a teelte in amau’ dahna khangsak hi. Amau’ si theh biaknate ke’n bawlpih loin, amau’ pasian-te ka biakpih kei ding hi.
English: Their sorrows shall be multiplied that hasten after another god: Their drink offerings of blood will I not offer, Nor take up their names into my lips.

**16:5**
Zolai: Topa pen keima luah dinga ka teelsa, keima muanpi na hi a, keima ngah ding khempeuh na khut sungah om hi.
English: The LORD is the portion of mine inheritance and of my cup: Thou maintainest my lot.

**16:6**
Zolai: Kei-a’ pen mun nuam mahmah sung hong tu ahih manin gamhluah hoih nei ka hi hi.
English: The lines are fallen unto me in pleasant places ; Yea, I have a goodly heritage.

**16:7**
Zolai: Ngaihsutna a hong lak Topa ka phat a, zanin zong ka lungsimah hong suak hi.
English: I will bless the LORD , who hath given me counsel: My reins also instruct me in the night seasons.

**16:8**
Zolai: Topa ka maingat tawntung a, ka taklamah amah om ahih manin ka kiling kei ding hi.
English: I have set the LORD always before me: Because he is at my right hand, I shall not be moved.

**16:9**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin lungdamin ka kipak a, lungmuangin ka om hi.
English: Therefore my heart is glad, and my glory rejoiceth: My flesh also shall rest in hope.

**16:10**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Leinuai nong zuansak kei a, na mihoih pa Leihawmpi na musak kei hi.
English: For thou wilt not leave my soul in hell; Neither wilt thou suffer thine Holy One to see corruption.

**16:11**
Zolai: Nangmah in nuntakna lampi keimah nong lak hi. Nangma omna munah lungdamna lianpi om a, nangma taklamah nop tawntungnate a om hi.
English: Thou wilt shew me the path of life: In thy presence is fulness of joy; At thy right hand there are pleasures for evermore.

## Chapter 17

**17:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, thuman ka hong ngetna hong za inla, ka otna hong ngai in! Lungsim takpi tawh ka hong thungetna hong ngai in!
English: Hear the right, O LORD , attend unto my cry, Give ear unto my prayer, that goeth not out of feigned lips.

**17:2**
Zolai: Thuman mu na hih manin ka dikna hong kilangsak in.
English: Let my sentence come forth from thy presence; Let thine eyes behold the things that are equal.

**17:3**
Zolai: Keima lungsim hong sin inla, zan hun sungin ka kiangah hong hawh inla, keimah hong ze-et lecin, ka sungah gitlohna na mu kei ding hi. Ka kampau-in zong bangmah ka khial kei hi.
English: Thou hast proved mine heart; thou hast visited me in the night; Thou hast tried me, and shalt find nothing; I am purposed that my mouth shall not transgress.

**17:4**
Zolai: Gamtatna thu-ah ci leng, nangma thupiaknate ka zui a, mi ngongtatte’ gamtat ziate ka pelh hi.
English: Concerning the works of men, by the word of thy lips I have kept me from the paths of the destroyer.

**17:5**
Zolai: Nangma lampi zui-in ka pai a, na lam ka pial ngei kei hi.
English: Hold up my goings in thy paths, that my footsteps slip not.

**17:6**
Zolai: Pasian aw, hong dawng ding na hih manin nang kong sam hi. Na bil hong ngat inla, ka thu hong za in.
English: I have called upon thee, for thou wilt hear me, O God: Incline thine ear unto me, and hear my speech.

**17:7**
Zolai: Amau’ galte’ kiang panin nang hong belte a honpa aw, na itna kip lamdang takin hong lak in.
English: Shew thy marvellous lovingkindness, O thou that savest by thy right hand them which put their trust in thee From those that rise up against them .

**17:8**
Zolai: Kei a hong sugawp migilo, kei a hong umcih a kihtakhuai mahmah ka galte kiang panin mitnauta bangin hong kem inla, na kha liimah hong seel in.
English: Keep me as the apple of the eye, Hide me under the shadow of thy wings,

**17:10**
Zolai: Amaute in hehpihna lungsim bangmah nei lo uh a, a kam uh tawh amaute kiphatsak pau uh hi.
English: They are inclosed in their own fat: With their mouth they speak proudly.

**17:11**
Zolai: Amaute in kei hong sulzuih uh a, tu-in kei hong umcihin, keimah leilak den nadingin a hong en uh hi.
English: They have now compassed us in our steps: They have set their eyes bowing down to the earth;

**17:12**
Zolai: Amaute pen a balnen nuam humpinelkai tawh kibang uh a, humpinelkai khanglai sabuk tawh kibang uh hi.
English: Like as a lion that is greedy of his prey, And as it were a young lion lurking in secret places.

**17:13**
Zolai: Topa aw, tho in! Amaute maiphut inla, thalpaih in! Topa aw, a deih khempeuh uh hih leitungah a nei migilote kiang panin na khut le na namsau tawh kei hong honkhia in. Amau a dingin na koihcing gimnate thuaksak inla, a tate un zong a cingvalin thuak uh hen la, a naungekte uh a’ ding nangawn nusiat lai ta uh hen.
English: Arise, O LORD , disappoint him, cast him down: Deliver my soul from the wicked, which is thy sword:

**17:15**
Zolai: Kei ka hih leh, thumanna tawh na maitang ka en ding a, ka khanlawh ciangin nangma mel muhna tawh ka lungkim ding hi.
English: As for me, I will behold thy face in righteousness: I shall be satisfied, when I awake, with thy likeness.

## Chapter 18

**18:1**
Zolai: Ka thahatna ahi Topa aw, nangmah ka hong it hi.
English: I will love thee, O LORD , my strength.

**18:2**
Zolai: Topa pen keima suangpi, ka munkip muanhuai, kei a hong honkhia pa, ka Pasian, ka suangpi, ka belh pa, ka lum, ka kihotkhiatna ki, ka munkip ahi hi.
English: The LORD is my rock, and my fortress, and my deliverer; My God, my strength, in whom I will trust; My buckler, and the horn of my salvation, and my high tower.

**18:3**
Zolai: A phattaak Topa ka sam a, ka galte kiang panin kei hong honkhia hi.
English: I will call upon the LORD , who is worthy to be praised: So shall I be saved from mine enemies.

**18:4**
Zolai: Sihna khaute in hong gakcip a, sihna tuihualte in kei hong nawk hi.
English: The sorrows of death compassed me, And the floods of ungodly men made me afraid.

**18:5**
Zolai: Leinuai sihna khaute in kei hong kancip a, sihna thangte in kei hong dawntuah hi.
English: The sorrows of hell compassed me about: The snares of death prevented me.

**18:6**
Zolai: Ka gimna-ah Topa ka sam a, ka Pasian’ tungah huhna ngenin ka kiko hi. Amah in a biakinnpi panin ka aw hong za a, amah ka kohna aw in ama bilte va banto hi.
English: In my distress I called upon the LORD , And cried unto my God: He heard my voice out of his temple, And my cry came before him, even into his ears.

**18:7**
Zolai: Ama hehna hangin leitung kipumpei-in kivei a, mual bulpite zong kisingin ling damdam hi.
English: Then the earth shook and trembled; The foundations also of the hills moved and were shaken, because he was wroth.

**18:8**
Zolai: Ama nakvangte panin meikhu pusuak hi. Ama kam panin mei husia pusuak a, ama tung panin mei-am san kuangkhia hi.
English: There went up a smoke out of his nostrils, And fire out of his mouth devoured: Coals were kindled by it.

**18:9**
Zolai: Amah in vanpi niamsakin hong kumsuk a, ama khenuai-ah meiivom sahpi a om hi.
English: He bowed the heavens also, and came down: And darkness was under his feet.

**18:10**
Zolai: Kherub khat tungah amah tuangin hong leeng a, huih khate tungah manlang takin hong leeng hi.
English: And he rode upon a cherub, and did fly: Yea, he did fly upon the wings of the wind.

**18:11**
Zolai: A kimkotah a ki-um nadingin khuamial bawl a, a tung kikhuh nadingin meii sahpi le tui tawh a zingsak hi.
English: He made darkness his secret place; his pavilion round about him Were dark waters and thick clouds of the skies.

**18:12**
Zolai: Ama mai-a khuaphia sung panin gialpi le mei-amte in ama meii sahpite a phulet hi.
English: At the brightness that was before him his thick clouds passed, Hail stones and coals of fire.

**18:13**
Zolai: Topa zong vantungah awng a, Sangpenpa in gialpi le mei-am ahi ama aw hong gingsak hi.
English: The LORD also thundered in the heavens, and the Highest gave his voice; Hail stones and coals of fire.

**18:14**
Zolai: Amah in a thaltangte lawn a, a galte kithehthangsak hi. Khuaphialep phiasak a, a galte a susia hi.
English: Yea, he sent out his arrows, and scattered them; And he shot out lightnings, and discomfited them.

**18:15**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma mawhsakna na awging hangin tuipi taw kidawk a, lei bulpite a guakin om hi.
English: Then the channels of waters were seen, and the foundations of the world were discovered at thy rebuke, O LORD , At the blast of the breath of thy nostrils.

**18:16**
Zolai: Amah in a sangna panin a khut tawh zamin kei hong la a, tui thukpi panin keimah hong kaikhia hi.
English: He sent from above, he took me, He drew me out of many waters.

**18:17**
Zolai: Ka gal hat pa kiang pan le hong mudahte kiang panin kei hong honkhia hi; bang hang hiam cih leh kei a dingin amaute hatlua uh hi.
English: He delivered me from my strong enemy, and from them which hated me: For they were too strong for me.

**18:18**
Zolai: Amaute in ka kamsiat hunin kei hong nehthawh uh hangin Topa in kei hong huh hi.
English: They prevented me in the day of my calamity: But the LORD was my stay.

**18:19**
Zolai: Amah in mun tanzau khatah kei hong paikhiatpih a, ka tungah lungkim ahih manin a hong honkhia hi.
English: He brought me forth also into a large place; He delivered me, because he delighted in me.

**18:20**
Zolai: Topa in ka thumanna tawh kizui-in noptuamna hong pia a, ka sianthona tawh kizui-in hong dinkik hi.
English: The LORD rewarded me according to my righteousness; According to the cleanness of my hands hath he recompensed me.

**18:21**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa’ lampite ka tawn khin a, ka Pasian’ kiang panin gitlohna tawh ka paikhia kei hi.
English: For I have kept the ways of the LORD , And have not wickedly departed from my God.

**18:22**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ama biakna ngeina thukip omte khempeuh limtakin ka zui a, ama thukhamte ka paaikhia kei hi.
English: For all his judgments were before me, And I did not put away his statutes from me.

**18:23**
Zolai: Ama mai-ah kawkbaang hetloin ka om a, kisuanna dingte panin kei ka kikem hi.
English: I was also upright before him, And I kept myself from mine iniquity.

**18:24**
Zolai: Tua ahih manin Topa in ka thumanna le ama muhna-ah ka sianthona tawh kizui-in kei hong dinkik khin hi.
English: Therefore hath the LORD recompensed me according to my righteousness, According to the cleanness of my hands in his eyesight.

**18:25**
Zolai: Thuman mi tungah nang na thuman a, kawkbaang lo mi tungah nang na diktat hi.
English: With the merciful thou wilt shew thyself merciful; With an upright man thou wilt shew thyself upright;

**18:26**
Zolai: A siangtho mi tungah na siangtho gamtat a, thukawi mite na galbawl hi.
English: With the pure thou wilt shew thyself pure; And with the froward thou wilt shew thyself froward.

**18:27**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh mi niamte na honkhia a, ahih hangin mi kiphasakte na niamsak hi.
English: For thou wilt save the afflicted people; But wilt bring down high looks.

**18:28**
Zolai: Nangmah in keima mei nong vaksak a, Topa ka Pasian in ka khuamial na vaksak hi.
English: For thou wilt light my candle: The LORD my God will enlighten my darkness.

**18:29**
Zolai: Nangma hangin galkap honkhat ka sugawpzo a, ka Pasian hangin khuakulh khat ka kanzo hi.
English: For by thee I have run through a troop; And by my God have I leaped over a wall.

**18:30**
Zolai: Hih Pasian - a thu kicing a, Topa’ kamciamna a manna kilang hi. Amah a belte khempeuh a dingin kidalna lum ahi hi.
English: As for God, his way is perfect: The word of the LORD is tried: He is a buckler to all those that trust in him.

**18:31**
Zolai: Topa longal, Pasian kua hiam? Pasian longal, suangpi kua hiam?
English: For who is God save the LORD ? Or who is a rock save our God?

**18:32**
Zolai: Keima tungah thahatna a hong guan Pasian, ka lampi lungmuan nadingin a bawl pa ahi hi.
English: It is God that girdeth me with strength, And maketh my way perfect.

**18:33**
Zolai: Amah in sangaipi khe bangin keima khe hong bawlsak a, mual sang dawnah ka khe hong kipsak hi.
English: He maketh my feet like hinds' feet , And setteth me upon my high places.

**18:34**
Zolai: Galsim siam nadingin ka khutte hong hilh a, keima khut in sumngo thal nangawn a keekzo hi.
English: He teacheth my hands to war, So that a bow of steel is broken by mine arms.

**18:35**
Zolai: Na hotkhiatna lum kei hong pia khinin, na taklam khut in kei hong phong a, nangma hong huhna in keimah hong liansak hi.
English: Thou hast also given me the shield of thy salvation: And thy right hand hath holden me up, and thy gentleness hath made me great.

**18:36**
Zolai: Ka kalsuanna ding mun tanzau nong pia a, ka khe taal lo hi.
English: Thou hast enlarged my steps under me, That my feet did not slip.

**18:37**
Zolai: Ka galte delhin ka pha a, a vekpi-un a kisiat khit matengun ka ciahkik kei hi.
English: I have pursued mine enemies, and overtaken them: Neither did I turn again till they were consumed.

**18:38**
Zolai: Amaute khempeuh a thawhkik zawh loh nadingun ka sunletgawp a, ka khenuai-ah a puk uh hi.
English: I have wounded them that they were not able to rise: They are fallen under my feet.

**18:39**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh galdo nadingin keimah tha nong guan a, keimah a hong dote ka nuai-ah na nengniam hi.
English: For thou hast girded me with strength unto the battle: Thou hast subdued under me those that rose up against me.

**18:40**
Zolai: Ka galte na nungkiksak a, kei hong mudahte ka susia hi.
English: Thou hast also given me the necks of mine enemies; That I might destroy them that hate me.

**18:41**
Zolai: Huhna ding ngenin amaute kikoko uh a, ahih hangin a hon ding kuamah om lo hi. Amaute in Topa’ tungah ko uh a, ahih hangin amah in dawng lo hi.
English: They cried, but there was none to save them: Even unto the LORD , but he answered them not.

**18:42**
Zolai: Huihpi mai-ah leivui bangin amaute ka satvui a, kongzing buante bangin amaute ka lawnkhia hi.
English: Then did I beat them small as the dust before the wind: I did cast them out as the dirt in the streets.

**18:43**
Zolai: A lehdo mite kiang panin nangmah in kei na hong honkhia a, minamte’ lutangin kei na hong bawl a, ka theih ngei loh mite in keima na hong sem uh hi.
English: Thou hast delivered me from the strivings of the people; And thou hast made me the head of the heathen: A people whom I have not known shall serve me.

**18:44**
Zolai: Ka thu a zak phetun amaute in hong mang pah uh a, gamdang mite in kei hong mai-et uh hi.
English: As soon as they hear of me, they shall obey me: The strangers shall submit themselves unto me.

**18:45**
Zolai: Gamdang mite lungkia uh a, a phualkip panun a lingsa-in hong paikhia uh hi.
English: The strangers shall fade away, And be afraid out of their close places.

**18:46**
Zolai: Topa hing hi. Keima suangpi in thupha ngah hen la, ka kihotkhiatna Pasian,
English: The LORD liveth; and blessed be my rock; And let the God of my salvation be exalted.

**18:47**
Zolai: hong thuhkik sakin keima nuai-ah mite a hong zawhsak Pasian,
English: It is God that avengeth me, And subdueth the people under me.

**18:48**
Zolai: ka galte kiang panin keimah a hong honkhia pa minthangin vanglian tahen. Ka langte tungah keimah nong liansak a, mi ngongtatte kiang panin na hong honkhia hi.
English: He delivereth me from mine enemies: Yea, thou liftest me up above those that rise up against me: Thou hast delivered me from the violent man.

**18:49**
Zolai: Topa aw, hih thu hangin minam dangte lakah nang ka hong phat ding a, nangma min phatna la ka sa ding hi.
English: Therefore will I give thanks unto thee, O LORD , among the heathen, And sing praises unto thy name.

**18:50**
Zolai: Zawhna lianpi ama kumpipa tungah pia a, a sathau nilh pa David le a suan a khakte tungah a tawntungin itna kip a lak hi.
English: Great deliverance giveth he to his king; And sheweth mercy to his anointed, to David, and to his seed for evermore.

## Chapter 19

**19:1**
Zolai: Vantung in Pasian’ minthanna gen a, vanpi in ama nasepna taangko hi.
English: The heavens declare the glory of God; And the firmament sheweth his handywork.

**19:2**
Zolai: Nisimin thu gengen a, zan simin theihtelna pulaklak hi.
English: Day unto day uttereth speech, And night unto night sheweth knowledge.

**19:3**
Zolai: Pauna le kammal om lo a, amau’ aw kiza lo hi.
English: There is no speech nor language, Where their voice is not heard.

**19:4**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a aw uh leitung khempeuhah kizel a, a kammal uh leimong dongah a tung hi. Amau’ sungah ni a’ ding omna khat bawl khin a,
English: Their line is gone out through all the earth, And their words to the end of the world. In them hath he set a tabernacle for the sun,

**19:5**
Zolai: a innsung pan a hong pusuak zi pi tangval tawh ahi zongin, lungtaii takin tai ding a kipan mi thahat khat tawh ahi zongin a kibang hi.
English: Which is as a bridegroom coming out of his chamber, and rejoiceth as a strong man to run a race.

**19:6**
Zolai: Ama suahna van mong pan hi a, mong khat dongin pai a, ama satna panin a kiliah thei bangmah om lo hi.
English: His going forth is from the end of the heaven, and his circuit unto the ends of it: And there is nothing hid from the heat thereof.

**19:7**
Zolai: Topa’ thu kicing a, nuntakna a thaksuaksak hi. Topa’ teci panna hi takpi a, mi pillote pilsak hi.
English: The law of the LORD is perfect, converting the soul: The testimony of the LORD is sure, making wise the simple.

**19:8**
Zolai: Topa’ thuhilhte man a, lungsim nuamsak hi. Topa’ thupiakna siang a, mitte vaksak hi.
English: The statutes of the LORD are right, rejoicing the heart: The commandment of the LORD is pure, enlightening the eyes.

**19:9**
Zolai: Topa a kizahtakna siang a, kip tawntung hi. Topa’ ngeina kipte thuman a, a vekin kituakin man kim hi.
English: The fear of the LORD is clean, enduring for ever: The judgments of the LORD are true and righteous altogether.

**19:10**
Zolai: Kham sangin ahi zongin kham hoihpen sang ahi zongin tuate deihhuaizaw a, khuaizu le khuailuzu taakte sangin zong khumzaw lai hi.
English: More to be desired are they than gold, yea, than much fine gold: Sweeter also than honey and the honeycomb.

**19:11**
Zolai: Tua tham loin tuate’ hangin a nasem pa in thuphawkna ngah a, tuate zuihna-ah noptuamna lian a om hi.
English: Moreover by them is thy servant warned: And in keeping of them there is great reward.

**19:12**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kua in ama khialhnate mukhia theitawm ahi hiam? Theih loh manin khialhna panin kei hong siangsak hi.
English: Who can understand his errors? Cleanse thou me from secret faults .

**19:13**
Zolai: Mawh kaltangnate panin zong na nasempa hong kem inla, tuate keima tungah hong uksak kei in! Tua ciangin kei ka kawkbaang kei ding a, mawhna liante panin ka siang ding hi.
English: Keep back thy servant also from presumptuous sins ; Let them not have dominion over me: Then shall I be upright, and I shall be innocent from the great transgression.

**19:14**
Zolai: Topa, ka belh suangpi le keimah hong tankhia pa aw, ka kammal le ka lungsim ngaihsutnate nangma muhna-ah a sanhuai suaksak ta in!
English: Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart, be acceptable in thy sight, O LORD , my strength, and my redeemer.

## Chapter 20

**20:1**
Zolai: Gimna na thuak ciangin Topa in nang hong en hen la, Jakob’ Pasian in nangmah hong dal ta hen!
English: The LORD hear thee in the day of trouble; The name of the God of Jacob defend thee;

**20:2**
Zolai: Siangtho mun panin huhna nang hong puak hen la, Zion panin nang hong panpih ta hen!
English: Send thee help from the sanctuary, And strengthen thee out of Zion;

**20:3**
Zolai: Na biakpiaknate khempeuh amah in hong phawk hen la, na meihal biakpiakna hong sang ta hen!
English: Remember all thy offerings, And accept thy burnt sacrifice; Selah.

**20:4**
Zolai: Na lungsim’ deihna amah in hong pia hen la, na geelna khempeuh hong tangtungsak ta hen!
English: Grant thee according to thine own heart, And fulfil all thy counsel.

**20:5**
Zolai: Na gualzawhna-ah eite lungdamin awngin, i Pasian’ min tawh i lante khai ni!
English: We will rejoice in thy salvation, and in the name of our God we will set up our banners: The LORD fulfil all thy petitions.

**20:6**
Zolai: Topa in a sathau nilh pa a huh ding tu-in ka thei ta a, ama vantung siangtho panin amah dawng ding a, a vangliatna tawh amah gualzosak ding hi.
English: Now know I that the LORD saveth his anointed; He will hear him from his holy heaven With the saving strength of his right hand.

**20:7**
Zolai: Mi pawlkhat in leengte kihihsakpih a, mi pawlkhat in sakolte kihihsakpih hi. Ahih hangin eite in Topa i Pasian’ min bek i kihihsakpih hi.
English: Some trust in chariots, and some in horses: But we will remember the name of the LORD our God.

**20:8**
Zolai: Amaute kinawmsawmin pukgawp ding uh a, ahih hangin eite tho-in i dingtang ding hi.
English: They are brought down and fallen: But we are risen, and stand upright.

**20:9**
Zolai: Topa aw, kumpipa tungah gualzawhna pia inla, kong sap ciangun hong dawng in.
English: Save, LORD : Let the king hear us when we call.

## Chapter 21

**21:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, na hatna hangin kumpipa lungdam a, na huhna hangin amah nak nuam mahmah hi.
English: The king shall joy in thy strength, O LORD ; And in thy salvation how greatly shall he rejoice!

**21:2**
Zolai: Ama lungsim deihna teng nangmah in na pia khin a, ama hong ngette na khaktan kei hi.
English: Thou hast given him his heart's desire, And hast not withholden the request of his lips. Selah.

**21:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh thupha hoihte tawh amah na dawntuah a, ama lu tungah kham siang lukhu na khusak hi.
English: For thou preventest him with the blessings of goodness: Thou settest a crown of pure gold on his head.

**21:4**
Zolai: Nangma tung panin amah in nuntakna hong ngen a, ama tungah nuntak sau na pia hi.
English: He asked life of thee, and thou gavest it him, Even length of days for ever and ever.

**21:5**
Zolai: Nangma huhna hangin ama minthanna lian a, hoihna le minliatna ama tungah na pia hi.
English: His glory is great in thy salvation: Honour and majesty hast thou laid upon him.

**21:6**
Zolai: Nangmah in a tawntungin thupha ngah pen dingin amah na bawl a, nangma ompihna hangin lungdamna tawh amah na kipaaksak hi.
English: For thou hast made him most blessed for ever: Thou hast made him exceeding glad with thy countenance.

**21:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh kumpipa in Topa muang a, Sangpenpa’ itna kip hangin amah a kiling kei ding hi.
English: For the king trusteth in the LORD , And through the mercy of the Most High he shall not be moved.

**21:8**
Zolai: Na khut in na galte khempeuh sugawp ding a, na khut taklam in nang hong mudahte sugawp ding hi.
English: Thine hand shall find out all thine enemies: Thy right hand shall find out those that hate thee.

**21:9**
Zolai: Na kilat ciangin meiphual kuang bangin amaute na hih ding hi. Topa in hehna tawh amaute nawmvalh ding a, meikuang in amaute kangtum ding hi.
English: Thou shalt make them as a fiery oven in the time of thine anger: The LORD shall swallow them up in his wrath, and the fire shall devour them.

**21:10**
Zolai: Leitung panin a suan a khakte, mi’ tate’ lak panin amau’ tate na susia ding hi.
English: Their fruit shalt thou destroy from the earth, And their seed from among the children of men.

**21:11**
Zolai: Nangma langah siatna ding vaihawmin, gitlohna a bawl uh hangin tangtung lo ding uh hi.
English: For they intended evil against thee: They imagined a mischievous device, which they are not able to perform .

**21:12**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute na taisak ding a, na thal tawh a maitang uh na ngim ding hi.
English: Therefore shalt thou make them turn their back, When thou shalt make ready thine arrows upon thy strings against the face of them.

**21:13**
Zolai: Topa aw, na hatna hangin nang hong kipahtawi ta hen! Nangma vangliatna la sa-in ka hong phat ding uh hi.
English: Be thou exalted, LORD , in thine own strength: So will we sing and praise thy power.

## Chapter 22

**22:1**
Zolai: Ka Pasian, ka Pasian aw, bang hangin kei hong nusia na hi hiam? Nong huhna ding ka hong thumna panin bang hangin gamla om na hi hiam?
English: My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me? Why art thou so far from helping me, and from the words of my roaring?

**22:2**
Zolai: Ka Pasian aw, sunin kong kiko a, ahi zongin nong dawng kei hi. Zanin zong ka kiko a, ahi zongin lungsim nopna ka mu thei tuan kei hi.
English: O my God, I cry in the daytime, but thou hearest not; And in the night season, and am not silent.

**22:3**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nang na siangtho a, Israel-te’ pahtawi-in na tu hi.
English: But thou art holy, O thou that inhabitest the praises of Israel.

**22:4**
Zolai: Ka pate un nangmah hong muang uh hi. Amaute in hong muang uh a, nangmah in amaute na honkhia hi.
English: Our fathers trusted in thee: They trusted, and thou didst deliver them.

**22:5**
Zolai: Nangma tungah amaute in hong ko uh a, amaute kihon hi. Nangmah hong muang uh a, guaksuak lo uh hi.
English: They cried unto thee, and were delivered: They trusted in thee, and were not confounded.

**22:6**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei pen lungno khat bang lel ka hi a, mi ka bang kei hi. Mite’ ko gawpgawp, mite’ simmawh ka hi hi.
English: But I am a worm, and no man; A reproach of men, and despised of the people.

**22:7**
Zolai: Hong mu mi khempeuh in kei hong zahko-in, hong mukpiksan uh a, a lu uh hong peisan hi.
English: All they that see me laugh me to scorn: They shoot out the lip, they shake the head, saying ,

**22:8**
Zolai: “ Topa’ tungah amah in ama thu ap hi. Amah kihonkhia sak un; amah deih ahih manin honkhia ta hen!” hong cihsan uh hi.
English: He trusted on the LORD that he would deliver him: Let him deliver him, seeing he delighted in him.

**22:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nang pen gil sung panin kei a hong suaksakpa na hi a, ka nu’ ang sungah a muanhuai-in keimah na hong kem hi.
English: But thou art he that took me out of the womb: Thou didst make me hope when I was upon my mother's breasts.

**22:10**
Zolai: Ka suah tung a kipan nangma tungah kong tung a, ka nu in hong paii lai a kipan keima Pasian na hi hi.
English: I was cast upon thee from the womb: Thou art my God from my mother's belly.

**22:11**
Zolai: Haksatna nai ahih manin kei tawh kigamla om kei in; kei a hong huh ding kuamah dang om lo hi.
English: Be not far from me; for trouble is near; For there is none to help.

**22:12**
Zolai: Bawngtal tampi tak in kei hong umcih uh a, Bashan gam bawngtal hatte in kei hong umcih uh hi.
English: Many bulls have compassed me: Strong bulls of Bashan have beset me round.

**22:13**
Zolai: Humpinelkai hawk, a sabawh nuam bangin amaute in kei hong kamkat beba uh hi.
English: They gaped upon me with their mouths, As a ravening and a roaring lion.

**22:14**
Zolai: Tui buakkhiat bangin kei hong kibuakhia a, ka guh ka taang khempeuh kilawi mangkhin hi. Ka lungtang khuainun bang a, ka awm sungah tuisuak hi.
English: I am poured out like water, and all my bones are out of joint: My heart is like wax; It is melted in the midst of my bowels.

**22:15**
Zolai: Ka thahatna, leibeel phel bangin keu a, ka leii zong toncip ta hi. Nangmah in leivui sungah kei na hong koih hi.
English: My strength is dried up like a potsherd; And my tongue cleaveth to my jaws; And thou hast brought me into the dust of death.

**22:16**
Zolai: Ka kiimah uite om a, siatna bawl mi honkhat in kei hong umcih uh hi. Ka khut ka khete hong sunletzo uh hi.
English: For dogs have compassed me: The assembly of the wicked have inclosed me: They pierced my hands and my feet.

**22:17**
Zolai: Ka guh khempeuh kimu thei hi. Amaute in hong sal gega uh hi.
English: I may tell all my bones: They look and stare upon me.

**22:18**
Zolai: Amaute in ka puante hawm uh a, ka puan a hawm nadingun lai ai a san uh hi.
English: They part my garments among them, And cast lots upon my vesture.

**22:19**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa aw, gamla om kei in. Keimah a hong huhpa aw, a huh dingin hong manlang in.
English: But be not thou far from me, O LORD : O my strength, haste thee to help me.

**22:20**
Zolai: Namsau panin keimah hong hon inla, uite’ kiang panin ka nuntakna hong hon in.
English: Deliver my soul from the sword; My darling from the power of the dog.

**22:21**
Zolai: Humpinelkai kam panin keimah hong hon inla, gamsialte’ ki panin a cimawh keimah hong hon in.
English: Save me from the lion's mouth: For thou hast heard me from the horns of the unicorns.

**22:22**
Zolai: Ka u ka naute tungah nangma min ka gen ding a, mihon kikhopna laizangah nangmah kong phat ding hi.
English: I will declare thy name unto my brethren: In the midst of the congregation will I praise thee.

**22:23**
Zolai: Topa a zahtak mi khempeuh aw, amah phat un. Jakob’ suan mi khempeuh aw, amah minthangsak un. Israel mi khempeuh aw, amah lamdang sa un.
English: Ye that fear the LORD , praise him; All ye the seed of Jacob, glorify him; And fear him, all ye the seed of Israel.

**22:24**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in a thuak mi’ gimna simmawh bawl lo a, zong kihbawl lo hi. Ama kiang pan a mai seello a, ama tungah a koh ciangin, amah in a za hi.
English: For he hath not despised nor abhorred the affliction of the afflicted; Neither hath he hid his face from him; But when he cried unto him, he heard.

**22:25**
Zolai: Mihonpite lakah nang ka hong phatna ding na piangsak a, nang a hong zahtakte’ mai-ah ka thuciamna kong pia ding hi.
English: My praise shall be of thee in the great congregation: I will pay my vows before them that fear him.

**22:26**
Zolai: Gimna a thuakte in kham takin ne ding uh a, amah a zongte in Topa phat ding uh hi. A lungsim uh nuam tawntung ta hen!
English: The meek shall eat and be satisfied: They shall praise the LORD that seek him: Your heart shall live for ever.

**22:27**
Zolai: Leitung mi khempeuh in phawkin Topa’ lamah kihei ding uh a, minam khempeuh in ama mai-ah bia ding uh hi.
English: All the ends of the world shall remember and turn unto the LORD : And all the kindreds of the nations shall worship before thee.

**22:28**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ukna pen Topa a’ hi a, minamte tungah amah in a uk hi.
English: For the kingdom is the LORD 's: And he is the governor among the nations.

**22:29**
Zolai: Hi hi, a kiphasak mi khempeuh ama mai-ah kunsuk ding uh a, a sithei mihing khempeuh ama mai-ah kun ding uh hi.
English: All they that be fat upon earth shall eat and worship: All they that go down to the dust shall bow before him: And none can keep alive his own soul.

**22:30**
Zolai: A hong khangkik mite in ama na sem ding uh hi. Mite in a hong piang lai ding mite tungah Topa’ thu gen ding uh a,
English: A seed shall serve him; It shall be accounted to the LORD for a generation.

**22:31**
Zolai: a suak nai lo mite tungah ama sepsa, hotkhiatna thu gen ding uh hi.
English: They shall come, and shall declare his righteousness Unto a people that shall be born, that he hath done this .

## Chapter 23

**23:1**
Zolai: Topa pen tuucin bangin hong cing hi a, kisapna teng kicing ta hi.
English: The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.

**23:2**
Zolai: Lo nona-ah hong lumsak a, tuidam kiangah hong paipih hi.
English: He maketh me to lie down in green pastures: He leadeth me beside the still waters.

**23:3**
Zolai: Thahatna thak kei hong guan hi. A hong ciamsa mah bangin-ah lampi manah kei hong kha hi.
English: He restoreth my soul: He leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.

**23:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, kei hong ompih na hih manin khuamial thukpi ka nawk hangin ka lau kei hi. Na molhtum le na ciangkhut in kei hong hu hi.
English: Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil: for thou art with me; Thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.

**23:5**
Zolai: Keima galte’ muhna munah an nong lui hi. Thupi takin nong pahtawi a, keima hai zong dimlet ta hi.
English: Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies: Thou anointest my head with oil; my cup runneth over.

**23:6**
Zolai: Na hoihna le nong itna in ka khantawnin a hong zuih ding tel takin-ah ka thei ta a, a tawntungin na inn sungah ka om ding hi.
English: Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life: And I will dwell in the house of the LORD for ever.

## Chapter 24

**24:1**
Zolai: Leitung le a tunga omte, leitung le a tunga tengte Topa -a’ ahi hi.
English: The earth is the LORD 's, and the fulness thereof; The world, and they that dwell therein.

**24:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in tuipite sungah a bul phut a, tui tungah a kipsak hi.
English: For he hath founded it upon the seas, And established it upon the floods.

**24:3**
Zolai: Topa’ mual tungah kuate kahto ding ahi hiam? Ama mun siangtho-ah kuate ding ding ahi hiam?
English: Who shall ascend into the hill of the LORD ? Or who shall stand in his holy place?

**24:4**
Zolai: Gamtat siangtho le lungsim siangtho a nei, a man lo thu-ah a nuntakna pia loin, khemna tawh a kiciam lo mite ahi hi.
English: He that hath clean hands, and a pure heart; Who hath not lifted up his soul unto vanity, nor sworn deceitfully.

**24:5**
Zolai: Tua bang mite in Topa’ tung panin thupha ngah ding uh a, amaute a honkhia Pasian’ kiang panin diksakna ngah ding uh hi.
English: He shall receive the blessing from the LORD , And righteousness from the God of his salvation.

**24:6**
Zolai: Tua bang mite pen, amah a zong, Jakob’ Pasian’ mai a zong minam ahi hi.
English: This is the generation of them that seek him, That seek thy face, O Jacob. Selah.

**24:7**
Zolai: Minthang Kumpipa hong tumtheih nadingin, kulh kongpite lian hon unla, tanglai kongkhakte gol hon un.
English: Lift up your heads, O ye gates; And be ye lift up, ye everlasting doors; And the King of glory shall come in.

**24:8**
Zolai: Minthang Kumpipa kua ahi hiam? Hatin a vanglian Topa, galhat Topa ahi hi.
English: Who is this King of glory? The LORD strong and mighty, the LORD mighty in battle.

**24:9**
Zolai: Minthang Kumpipa hong tumtheih nadingin, kulh kongpite lian hon unla, tanglai kongkhakte gol hon un.
English: Lift up your heads, O ye gates; even lift them up, ye everlasting doors; And the King of glory shall come in.

**24:10**
Zolai: Hih a minthang Kumpipa kua ahi hiam? Vanglian Topa, minthang Kumpipa ahi hi.
English: Who is this King of glory? The LORD of hosts, he is the King of glory. Selah.

## Chapter 25

**25:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma tungah thu ka hong ngen hi.
English: Unto thee, O LORD , do I lift up my soul.

**25:2**
Zolai: Ka Pasian aw, nangmah ka hong muang hi. Hong zahhuaisak kei in. Keima tungah ka galte gualzo-in lungdamsak kei in.
English: O my God, I trust in thee: Let me not be ashamed, let not mine enemies triumph over me.

**25:3**
Zolai: Nangmah a hong ngakte kuamah zahhuaisak kei in. Thukhual loin a zuau theite zahhuaisak in.
English: Yea, let none that wait on thee be ashamed: Let them be ashamed which transgress without cause.

**25:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, na zia na tong a thei-in hong bawl inla, na lampite hong hilh in.
English: Shew me thy ways, O LORD ; Teach me thy paths.

**25:5**
Zolai: Na thuman sungah kei hong paipih inla, lam hong hilh in. Bang hang hiam cih leh kei a hong hon Pasian na hi a, nang kong muang tawntung hi.
English: Lead me in thy truth, and teach me: For thou art the God of my salvation; on thee do I wait all the day.

**25:6**
Zolai: Topa aw, tanglai pek a kipan a omsa ahih manin, na hehpihna le na itna kip hong phawkkik in.
English: Remember, O LORD , thy tender mercies and thy lovingkindnesses; For they have been ever of old.

**25:7**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka khangno lai-a ka mawhna le ka khialhnate ciamteh kei inla, na hoihna na ngaihsutna le na itna kip tawh kizui-in kei hong phawk in!
English: Remember not the sins of my youth, nor my transgressions: According to thy mercy remember thou me for thy goodness' sake, O LORD .

**25:8**
Zolai: Topa hoihin thutang hi. Tua ahih manin mimawhte lam a hilh hi.
English: Good and upright is the LORD : Therefore will he teach sinners in the way.

**25:9**
Zolai: Amah in lungsim kiniamkhiatte a manah paipihin a zia a tong a hilh hi.
English: The meek will he guide in judgment: And the meek will he teach his way.

**25:10**
Zolai: Ama thuciamna le a thupiak a zuite a dingin Topa’ lampi pen itna kip le cihtakna ahi hi.
English: All the paths of the LORD are mercy and truth Unto such as keep his covenant and his testimonies.

**25:11**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka mawhna lian ahih manin, nangma min phat nadingin keima mawhna hong maisak in.
English: For thy name's sake, O LORD , Pardon mine iniquity; for it is great.

**25:12**
Zolai: Topa a zahtak mi kua ahi hiam? Ama lampi zuih ding Pasian’ hilhna a ngah mi ahi hi.
English: What man is he that feareth the LORD ? Him shall he teach in the way that he shall choose.

**25:13**
Zolai: Amah nuamsa tawntung ding a, a tate in leitang nei ding uh hi.
English: His soul shall dwell at ease; And his seed shall inherit the earth.

**25:14**
Zolai: Topa tawh kilawmtatna pen amah a zahtakte a’ ding hi a, a thuciamna amau tungah kitheithangsak hi.
English: The secret of the LORD is with them that fear him; And he will shew them his covenant.

**25:15**
Zolai: Topa’ lam ka en tawntung hi; bang hang hiam cih leh amah in ngenthang panin ka khete hong sutkhia ding hi.
English: Mine eyes are ever toward the LORD ; For he shall pluck my feet out of the net.

**25:16**
Zolai: Kei lamah nang hong kihei-in, kei hong hehpih in; bang hang hiam cih leh kei guakbek hi-in gimna ka thuak hi.
English: Turn thee unto me, and have mercy upon me; For I am desolate and afflicted.

**25:17**
Zolai: Ka lungsim natnate khempeuh hong damsak inla, ka gimnate khempeuh panin hong paikhiatpih in.
English: The troubles of my heart are enlarged: O bring thou me out of my distresses.

**25:18**
Zolai: Ka gimna le ka thuaknate hong ngaihsun inla, ka mawhna khempeuh hong maisak in.
English: Look upon mine affliction and my pain; And forgive all my sins.

**25:19**
Zolai: Ka galte bangzah takin a tamna le kei hong muhdah luatnate hong ngaihsun in.
English: Consider mine enemies; for they are many; And they hate me with cruel hatred.

**25:20**
Zolai: Kei hong cing inla, hong honkhia in. Nangmah hong bel ka hih manin kei hong maizumsak kei in.
English: O keep my soul, and deliver me: Let me not be ashamed; for I put my trust in thee.

**25:21**
Zolai: Nang hong muang ka hih manin, kicinna le thutanna in kei hong kem tahen.
English: Let integrity and uprightness preserve me; For I wait on thee.

**25:22**
Zolai: Pasian aw, amau’ haksatna khempeuh panin na mi Israel-te honkhia ta in.
English: Redeem Israel, O God, out of all his troubles.

## Chapter 26

**26:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, a hoihin gamta-in Topa hong muang ka hih manin, ka thutanna hong lak in.
English: Judge me, O LORD ; for I have walked in mine integrity: I have trusted also in the LORD ; therefore I shall not slide.

**26:2**
Zolai: Topa aw, hong ze-et inla hong sin in. Ka lungsim le ka ngaihsutna hong entel in.
English: Examine me, O LORD , and prove me; Try my reins and my heart.

**26:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh na itna kip in lam hong lak a, nangma tungah citakin ka gamta hi.
English: For thy lovingkindness is before mine eyes: And I have walked in thy truth.

**26:4**
Zolai: Mikhialte tawh tukhawm loin, thusim neite tawh ka kipawl kei hi.
English: I have not sat with vain persons, Neither will I go in with dissemblers.

**26:5**
Zolai: Siatna a bawl mite ka mudah a, migilote tawh ka tukhawm kei hi.
English: I have hated the congregation of evil doers; And will not sit with the wicked.

**26:6**
Zolai: Topa aw, mawh baan lohna ka lahna-in ka khutte ka sil a, biakna pia-in na biakna tau kiim ah ka pai hi.
English: I will wash mine hands in innocency: So will I compass thine altar, O LORD :

**26:7**
Zolai: Lungdam kohna la a gingin sa-in, nangma nasep a lamdangte ka gen kawm hi.
English: That I may publish with the voice of thanksgiving, And tell of all thy wondrous works.

**26:8**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma inn-a ten ding le na minthang a omna munah om ding ka ut hi.
English: LORD , I have loved the habitation of thy house, And the place where thine honour dwelleth.

**26:9**
Zolai: Mimawhte, mi that nuamte, siatna a bawl mite, le golhguk a la nuamte tawh kei hong susia khawm kei in.
English: Gather not my soul with sinners, Nor my life with bloody men:

**26:11**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei ahihleh, ka hoih gamtat hi. Hong hehpih inla, kei hong honkhia in.
English: But as for me, I will walk in mine integrity: Redeem me, and be merciful unto me.

**26:12**
Zolai: Leizang munah ka ding hi. Mihon tampi lakah Topa ka phat ding hi.
English: My foot standeth in an even place: In the congregations will I bless the LORD .

## Chapter 27

**27:1**
Zolai: Topa, ka khuavak le hong honpa ahi hi. Kua kihta ding ka hi hiam? Topa, kei a dingin munmuanhuai ahi hi. Bang laupih ding ka hi hiam?
English: The LORD is my light and my salvation; whom shall I fear? The LORD is the strength of my life; of whom shall I be afraid?

**27:2**
Zolai: Hong langpangte le ka galte ahi, siatna bawlte in hong do a, kei nektum hong sawm ciangun, amaute kisukha-in puk ding uh hi.
English: When the wicked, even mine enemies and my foes, came upon me to eat up my flesh, They stumbled and fell.

**27:3**
Zolai: Mi honkhat in keimah hong langpangin phual a sat uh hangin, ka lungsim lau lo ding hi. Keimah hong langpangin gal hong kuan hangin tua nangawnah ka lungmuang ding hi.
English: Though an host should encamp against me, my heart shall not fear: Though war should rise against me, in this will I be confident.

**27:4**
Zolai: Topa’ tung panin na khat ka ngen khin a, tua ngenin ka zon ding pen: Topa’ inn sungah ka khan tawntungin om ding, Topa’ hoihna et ding le ama biakinn sungah thu dot dingte ahi hi.
English: One thing have I desired of the LORD , that will I seek after; That I may dwell in the house of the LORD all the days of my life, To behold the beauty of the LORD , and to enquire in his temple.

**27:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh haksat hun ciangin amah in a buk sungah kei hong seel ding hi. A puanbuk khuhna nuai-ah kei hong seel ding a, a sangna suang tungah kei hong koih ding hi.
English: For in the time of trouble he shall hide me in his pavilion: In the secret of his tabernacle shall he hide me; he shall set me up upon a rock.

**27:6**
Zolai: Tu-in ka kimkotah a om ka galte tungah ka gualzo ding hi. Lungdamin kikona tawh ama buk sungah biakna ka pia ding a, la ka sa ding hi. Topa tungah la ngaih ka sa ding hi.
English: And now shall mine head be lifted up, Above mine enemies round about me: Therefore will I offer in his tabernacle sacrifices of joy; I will sing, yea, I will sing praises unto the LORD .

**27:7**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka otna aw hong za inla, kei hong hehpihin hong dawng in!
English: Hear, O LORD , when I cry with my voice: Have mercy also upon me, and answer me.

**27:8**
Zolai: “Ka mai hong zong in,” na hong ci khinzo hi. Keimah in nangma tungah, “ Topa aw, nangma mai kong zong hi,” ka hong ci hi.
English: When thou saidst , Seek ye my face; my heart said unto thee, Thy face, LORD , will I seek.

**27:9**
Zolai: Kei kiang panin na maitang seel kei in. Hehpihna tawh na nasempa hong hawlkhia kei in; kei hong nei pa na hi hi. Hong paaikhia kei inla, hong nusia kei in, kei hong honkhia Pasian aw.
English: Hide not thy face far from me; Put not thy servant away in anger: Thou hast been my help; Leave me not, neither forsake me, O God of my salvation.

**27:10**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka nu le ka pa in hong nusiat hangin Topa in kei hong kem ding hi.
English: When my father and my mother forsake me, Then the LORD will take me up.

**27:11**
Zolai: Topa aw, na lampi hong hilh inla, ka galte’ hangin lam phei-ah kei hong kha in.
English: Teach me thy way, O LORD , And lead me in a plain path, because of mine enemies.

**27:12**
Zolai: Ka langte’ deihna bangin kei hong nusia kei in; bang hang hiam cih leh teci man lote ka langah pang khin a, amaute in zuau genin kei hong tawng niloh uh hi.
English: Deliver me not over unto the will of mine enemies: For false witnesses are risen up against me, and such as breathe out cruelty.

**27:13**
Zolai: A hingte’ gam sungah Topa’ hoihna a mu dingin kei ka ki-um hi.
English: I had fainted , Unless I had believed to see the goodness of the LORD in the land of the living.

**27:14**
Zolai: Topa muang in. Thakhauh inla, na lungsim hangsakin, Topa muang in.
English: Wait on the LORD : Be of good courage, and he shall strengthen thine heart: wait, I say, on the LORD .

## Chapter 28

**28:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, awngin nang kong sam hi. Ka belh suangpi aw, keima thu-ah hong bilngong kei in. Tua bangin kei tungah hong dai dide lecin, Leihawm sunga a paisukte tawh a kibang ka suak ding hi.
