English: Unto thee will I cry, O LORD my rock; be not silent to me: Lest, if thou be silent to me, I become like them that go down into the pit.

**28:2**
Zolai: Siangtho pen mun lamah ka khutte hong laamto a, nangma kiangah huhna kong nget mah bangin kong thumna aw hong za in.
English: Hear the voice of my supplications, when I cry unto thee, When I lift up my hands toward thy holy oracle.

**28:3**
Zolai: Amau’ lungsim sungah siatna a om hinapi a vengte tawh kilemna thu a gen khem, siatna bawlte, migilote tawh kei hong lakhiakhawm kei in.
English: Draw me not away with the wicked, and with the workers of iniquity, Which speak peace to their neighbours, but mischief is in their hearts.

**28:4**
Zolai: Amau’ sepna le a gamtat siatnate uh bangin amaute thukkik in. Amau’ sepna tawh a kizui-in amaute tungah thuk inla, amau’ ngah ding a kilawm thaman pia in.
English: Give them according to their deeds, And according to the wickedness of their endeavours: Give them after the work of their hands; Render to them their desert.

**28:5**
Zolai: Amaute in Topa’ nasepnate thupi ngaihsut lo ahih manun, amah in amaute susia-in a donkik nawnkei ding hi.
English: Because they regard not the works of the LORD , nor the operation of his hands, He shall destroy them, and not build them up.

**28:6**
Zolai: Ka thumna aw hong za ahih manin Topa in thupha ngah tahen.
English: Blessed be the LORD , Because he hath heard the voice of my supplications.

**28:7**
Zolai: Topa, ka hatna le ka lum hi a, amah ka muang hi. Tua ahih manin kei hong kihuh a, lungdamin ka diang a, ka lasakna tawh ama tungah lungdamna ka ko hi.
English: The LORD is my strength and my shield; my heart trusted in him, and I am helped: Therefore my heart greatly rejoiceth; and with my song will I praise him.

**28:8**
Zolai: Topa, ama mite’ hatna hi a, amah pen a sathau nilh pa’ bukna le a honkhia pa ahi hi.
English: The LORD is their strength, And he is the saving strength of his anointed.

**28:9**
Zolai: Na mite hon inla, na luahte thupha pia in. Amau a cing pa hi inla, a tawntungin amaute huh in.
English: Save thy people, and bless thine inheritance: Feed them also, and lift them up for ever.

## Chapter 29

**29:1**
Zolai: Topa -a’ ci un, van mite aw; minthanna le hatna Topa -a’ ci un.
English: Give unto the LORD , O ye mighty, give unto the LORD glory and strength.

**29:2**
Zolai: Ama minthanna Topa’ tungah pia unla, a siangtho kizepna tawh Topa bia un.
English: Give unto the LORD the glory due unto his name; Worship the LORD in the beauty of holiness.

**29:3**
Zolai: Topa’ awging tuipite tungah kiza hi. A minthang Pasian’ aw ging damdam a, tui tampite tungah Topa’ aw kiza hi.
English: The voice of the LORD is upon the waters: The God of glory thundereth: The LORD is upon many waters.

**29:4**
Zolai: Topa’ awging vanglian a, Topa’ awging, liatna tawh kidim hi.
English: The voice of the LORD is powerful; The voice of the LORD is full of majesty.

**29:5**
Zolai: Topa’ awging in taamtak singte kitansak a, Topa’ awging in Lebanon mual taamtak singte a kuaitan hi.
English: The voice of the LORD breaketh the cedars; Yea, the LORD breaketh the cedars of Lebanon.

**29:6**
Zolai: Lebanon mual le Sirion mualte bawngno le gamsialno bangin amah in a diangsak hi.
English: He maketh them also to skip like a calf; Lebanon and Sirion like a young unicorn.

**29:7**
Zolai: Topa’ awging in meikuang taangkhia sak hi.
English: The voice of the LORD divideth the flames of fire.

**29:8**
Zolai: Topa’ awging in gamlak lok a, Topa in Kadesh gamlak lok hi.
English: The voice of the LORD shaketh the wilderness; the LORD shaketh the wilderness of Kadesh.

**29:9**
Zolai: Topa’ awging in singkungte heekgawp a, gammang tulak hawkkhia-in a kolhsak hi. Ama biakinn sungah a vekpi-un awngin, “Pasian’ min thang ta hen,” a ci uh hi.
English: The voice of the LORD maketh the hinds to calve, and discovereth the forests: And in his temple doth every one speak of his glory.

**29:10**
Zolai: Topa in tui thukpite uk a, a tawntung kumpi hihna tawh Topa a tu hi.
English: The LORD sitteth upon the flood; Yea, the LORD sitteth King for ever.

**29:11**
Zolai: Topa in ama mite tungah thahatna pia tahen. Topa in ama mite tungah nopsakna thupha pia tahen.
English: The LORD will give strength unto his people; The LORD will bless his people with peace.

## Chapter 30

**30:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangmah hong phatin ka diang ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh kei nong laamto khin a, ka tungah ka galte na lungdamsak kei hi.
English: I will extol thee, O LORD ; for thou hast lifted me up, And hast not made my foes to rejoice over me.

**30:2**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, huhna a hong ngenin nang tungah kong awng a, kei na hong damsak khin hi.
English: O LORD my God, I cried unto thee, and thou hast healed me.

**30:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, Leinuai panin kei nong paikhiatpihto khin a, Leihawm sungah a pai khinsate lak panin kei nong nungta kiksak hi.
English: O LORD , thou hast brought up my soul from the grave: Thou hast kept me alive, that I should not go down to the pit.

**30:4**
Zolai: Ama mi siangthote aw, Topa tungah phatna la sa-in ama tungah lungdamna ko un.
English: Sing unto the LORD , O ye saints of his, And give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.

**30:5**
Zolai: Ama hehna tomno sung bek hi a, ama hong deihsakna pen khang tawntung ading ahi hi. Zan hun sungteng kahna omkha mah ding a, ahih hangin zing khuavak tawh nuamna hong tung hi.
English: For his anger endureth but a moment; in his favour is life: Weeping may endure for a night, but joy cometh in the morning.

**30:6**
Zolai: Keimah in ahihleh, ka daupai laitakin, “Ka kiling ngei kei ding hi,” ka ci kha hi.
English: And in my prosperity I said, I shall never be moved.

**30:7**
Zolai: Topa aw, nong deihsakna tawh mual kip bangin kei nong phut khin hi. Ahi zongin tu-in na maitang na seel a, kei ka khasia hi.
English: LORD , by thy favour thou hast made my mountain to stand strong: Thou didst hide thy face, and I was troubled.

**30:8**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma tungah kong kiko a, Topa tungah kong thum hi:
English: I cried to thee, O LORD ; And unto the LORD I made supplication.

**30:9**
Zolai: “Leihawm sungah paisukin ka sihna-ah bang meetna om ahi hiam? Leivui in nang hong phat ding ahi hiam? Na thumanna gen ding ahi hiam?
English: What profit is there in my blood, When I go down to the pit? Shall the dust praise thee? Shall it declare thy truth?

**30:10**
Zolai: Topa aw, hong za inla, kei hong hehpih in. Topa aw, keimah huhpa hong hi in,” ka ci hi.
English: Hear, O LORD , and have mercy upon me: LORD , be thou my helper.

**30:11**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, nangma tungah lungdamna ka hong koh tawntung theih nading, ka lungsim in nang hong phat theih nading, a dai om mawk loh nadingin ka thumna le ka taunate lamna tawh nong heisak a, dahna lim ahi ka puanhampi hong suahkhiat sakin nuamna na hong guan hi.
English: Thou hast turned for me my mourning into dancing: Thou hast put off my sackcloth, and girded me with gladness;

## Chapter 31

**31:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang kong bel hi. Hong maizumsak ngei kei inla, na thumanna tawh kei hong honkhia in!
English: In thee, O LORD , do I put my trust; Let me never be ashamed: deliver me in thy righteousness.

**31:2**
Zolai: Na bil hong ngat inla, hong hon pak in! Ka belh ding suangpi hong hi inla, kei hong dal ding munkip muanhuai hong hi in!
English: Bow down thine ear to me; deliver me speedily: Be thou my strong rock, for an house of defence to save me.

**31:3**
Zolai: Nang pen ka suangpi le ka munkip muanhuai na hi hi. Nangma min ngaihsutna tawh kei hong kha-in lam hong lak inla,
English: For thou art my rock and my fortress; Therefore for thy name's sake lead me, and guide me.

**31:4**
Zolai: keima belh pa na hih manin hong kisiahna ngenthang panin kei hong lakhia in.
English: Pull me out of the net that they have laid privily for me: For thou art my strength.

**31:5**
Zolai: Nangma khut sungah keimah kong ki-ap hi. Topa, a thuman Pasian aw, keimah na hong hon ding hi.
English: Into thine hand I commit my spirit: Thou hast redeemed me, O LORD God of truth.

**31:6**
Zolai: Mawkna milim a thupi ngaihsutte na mudah hi; ahih hangin keimah in Topa ka hong muang hi.
English: I have hated them that regard lying vanities: But I trust in the LORD .

**31:7**
Zolai: Na itna kip hangin lungdamin ka kipak ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh ka thuakna mu khinin, ka kamsiatna-ah na hong don khin hi.
English: I will be glad and rejoice in thy mercy: For thou hast considered my trouble; thou hast known my soul in adversities;

**31:8**
Zolai: Galte’ khut sungah kei na hong pia kei a, mun tanzau-ah ka khe na dingsak hi.
English: And hast not shut me up into the hand of the enemy: Thou hast set my feet in a large room.

**31:9**
Zolai: Topa aw, genthei ka hih manin kei hong hehpih in. Dahna hangin ka mit thuk a, ka lungsim le ka pumpi zong gim mahmah ta hi.
English: Have mercy upon me, O LORD , for I am in trouble: Mine eye is consumed with grief, yea , my soul and my belly.

**31:10**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka nuntakna dahna vive hi a, ka hunte khuisatna vive ahi hi. Ka gentheihna hangin ka tha kiamgawp ta a, ka guhte zong ngaam ta hi.
English: For my life is spent with grief, And my years with sighing: My strength faileth because of mine iniquity, And my bones are consumed.

**31:11**
Zolai: Ka vengte khempeuh’ nuihsat ka suak a, ka vengte tungah a cikzethuai ka hi a, ka meltheih khempeuhte’ gimneih mi ka suak hi. Konglakah hong mute in kei hong peelin hong taisan uh hi.
English: I was a reproach among all mine enemies, but especially among my neighbours, And a fear to mine acquaintance: they that did see me without fled from me.

**31:12**
Zolai: Misi bangin kei hong kiphawk nawn lo a, beel kitam khat tawh ka kibang lel ta hi.
English: I am forgotten as a dead man out of mind: I am like a broken vessel.

**31:13**
Zolai: Ka galte’ kihuauna ka za a, ka kiim ka pamah launa om hi. Kei hong langpangin amaute in vai hawmkhawm a, thah dingin kei hong sawm uh hi.
English: For I have heard the slander of many: Fear was on every side: while they took counsel together against me, They devised to take away my life.

**31:14**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nang kong muang hi, Topa aw. Keima Pasian na hi hi.
English: But I trusted in thee, O LORD : I said, Thou art my God.

**31:15**
Zolai: Keima nuntakna nangma khut sungah om hi. Keima galte le kei a hong bawlsiate’ khutsung panin kei hong honkhia in!
English: My times are in thy hand: Deliver me from the hand of mine enemies, and from them that persecute me.

**31:16**
Zolai: Na nasempa tungah na mai hong taangsak inla, na itna kip tawh kei hong hon in!
English: Make thy face to shine upon thy servant: Save me for thy mercies' sake.

**31:17**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma tung panin huhna hong ngen ka hih manin kei hong maizumsak kei in. Migilote maizumsak inla, amaute a pau ding thei loin Leinuai-ah paisak in.
English: Let me not be ashamed, O LORD ; for I have called upon thee: Let the wicked be ashamed, and let them be silent in the grave.

**31:18**
Zolai: Thumante’ langah pang a, kihihsak pau-in, kiphatsakna le simmawhna tawh pau-in zuauthu a gen mite a pau thei loin omsak in.
English: Let the lying lips be put to silence; Which speak grievous things proudly and contemptuously against the righteous.

**31:19**
Zolai: Nang hong zahtakte a dingin na koihsa na hoihte, nang hong beelte a dingin mite’ muhna-ah na bawl, nangma hoihna kicing a, mi khempeuh in thei uh hi.
English: Oh how great is thy goodness, which thou hast laid up for them that fear thee; Which thou hast wrought for them that trust in thee before the sons of men!

**31:20**
Zolai: Mite’ sawmsimna panin na omna huam sungah amaute na seel a, kitotna mun panin na buk sungah a muanhuai-in amaute na kem hi.
English: Thou shalt hide them in the secret of thy presence from the pride of man: Thou shalt keep them secretly in a pavilion from the strife of tongues.

**31:21**
Zolai: Gal in khuapi a umcih bangin kei hong ki-umcih hun lai-in a itna kip a lamdangin kei tungah hong lak ahih manin Topa in thupha ngah tahen.
English: Blessed be the LORD : For he hath shewed me his marvellous kindness in a strong city.

**31:22**
Zolai: Lauthawngna tawh, “Nangma muhna panin a gamlapi-ah kei hong notkhia hi,” ka ci khin hi. Ahih hangin nang tungah huhna ka hong nget ciangin keima hong thumnate nangmah in na hong za hi.
English: For I said in my haste, I am cut off from before thine eyes: Nevertheless thou heardest the voice of My supplications when I cried unto thee.

**31:23**
Zolai: Ama mi siangtho khempeuh aw, Topa phat un! Pasian in thuman mite kem a, ahih hangin a kiphatsak gamtatte nakpitakin a thuk hi.
English: O love the LORD , all ye his saints: For the LORD preserveth the faithful, and plentifully rewardeth the proud doer.

**31:24**
Zolai: Topa a ngak mi khempeuh aw, na tha uh khauhsak unla, na lungsim uh hangsak ta un!
English: Be of good courage, and he shall strengthen your heart, All ye that hope in the LORD .

## Chapter 32

**32:1**
Zolai: Ama khialhna kimaisak a, ama mawhna a kiselcipsak mi, thupha ngah ahi hi.
English: Blessed is he whose transgression is forgiven, Whose sin is covered.

**32:2**
Zolai: Topa in mawhna a khuksak loh mi, a lungsim sungah khemna a om lo mi, thupha ngah ahi hi.
English: Blessed is the man unto whom the LORD imputeth not iniquity, And in whose spirit there is no guile.

**32:3**
Zolai: Ka mawhna ka pulak loh ciangin, sunthapai ka tautauna hangin ka pumpi a thaneem hi.
English: When I kept silence, my bones waxed old Through my roaring all the day long.

**32:4**
Zolai: Sun le zan tawntung gim nong piakna ka thuak a, khuakhal nisa’ kat bangin ka thahatna a keucip hi.
English: For day and night thy hand was heavy upon me: My moisture is turned into the drought of summer. Selah.

**32:5**
Zolai: Keima khialhnate nangma tungah kong pulak a, ka mawhna ka im kei hi. “Ka khialhnate khempeuh Topa’ tungah ka pulak ding hi,” ka ci hi. Tua ciangin ka mawhna nin nong maisak hi.
English: I acknowledged my sin unto thee, And mine iniquity have I not hid. I said, I will confess my transgressions unto the LORD ; And thou forgavest the iniquity of my sin. Selah.

**32:6**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin nang hong kimuh theih lai-in mihoih khempeuh, nang tungah thu kingensak in. Tua hileh tuikhang in amaute ban lo ding hi.
English: For this shall every one that is godly pray unto thee in a time when thou mayest be found: Surely in the floods of great waters they shall not come nigh unto him.

**32:7**
Zolai: Nang pen kei a dingin ka bukna mun na hi a, haksatna pan kei hong kemin hotkhiatna kicing nong pia hi.
English: Thou art my hiding place; thou shalt preserve me from trouble; Thou shalt compass me about with songs of deliverance. Selah.

**32:8**
Zolai: Na pai nading lampi lakin ka hong hilh ding a, ka mit tawh hong enin thu kong hilh ding hi.
English: I will instruct thee and teach thee in the way which thou shalt go: I will guide thee with mine eye.

**32:9**
Zolai: A kamkaih tawh uk lohin a phamawh, thutheihna a nei lo, sakol le la bang kei in.
English: Be ye not as the horse, or as the mule, which have no understanding: Whose mouth must be held in with bit and bridle, lest they come near unto thee.

**32:10**
Zolai: Migilote in gimna tampi thuak uh a, Topa a muangte ahihleh itna kip in a hu hi.
English: Many sorrows shall be to the wicked: But he that trusteth in the LORD , mercy shall compass him about.

**32:11**
Zolai: Thumante aw, Topa tungah lungdamin kipak un. Lungsim man mi khempeuh aw, lungdamin awng un!
English: Be glad in the LORD , and rejoice, ye righteous: And shout for joy, all ye that are upright in heart.

## Chapter 33

**33:1**
Zolai: No thuman mite aw, Topa tungah lungdam un! Pahtawina pen thutangte tawh kilawm kituak hi.
English: Rejoice in the LORD , O ye righteous: For praise is comely for the upright.

**33:2**
Zolai: Laia khausai lasakna tawh Topa phat unla, harp zang sawm khausai lasakna tawh ama tungah la ngaih sa un.
English: Praise the LORD with harp: Sing unto him with the psaltery and an instrument of ten strings.

**33:3**
Zolai: Ama tungah la thak sa unla, a gingpha mahmahin hoihtakin khausai tum un.
English: Sing unto him a new song; Play skilfully with a loud noise.

**33:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa thutang a, ama hihna khempeuh thuman tawh a sem hi.
English: For the word of the LORD is right; And all his works are done in truth.

**33:5**
Zolai: Amah in thuman le thutang deih a, leitungah Topa’ itna kip a kidim hi.
English: He loveth righteousness and judgment: The earth is full of the goodness of the LORD .

**33:6**
Zolai: Topa’ kampauna tawh vantung piang a, a kam pana husanna tawh vantung nate a piang hi.
English: By the word of the LORD were the heavens made; And all the host of them by the breath of his mouth.

**33:7**
Zolai: Amah in tuipi tuite thawl khat sunga thun bangin mun khatah gawm a, tuithukpite tuibeem-ah a koih hi.
English: He gathereth the waters of the sea together as an heap: He layeth up the depth in storehouses.

**33:8**
Zolai: Leitung khempeuh in Topa zahtak uh hen la, leitung a tengte khempeuh, amah lamdangsakna tawh ding ta uh hen!
English: Let all the earth fear the LORD : Let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.

**33:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah pau a, leitung hong piang hi; amah in thu pia a, na khempeuh hong om hi.
English: For he spake, and it was done ; He commanded, and it stood fast.

**33:10**
Zolai: Topa in minamte’ thungaihsutna a mawkna suahin, mite’ geelna a khaktan hi.
English: The LORD bringeth the counsel of the heathen to nought: He maketh the devices of the people of none effect.

**33:11**
Zolai: Topa’ thungaihsutna kip ngitnget a, ama lungsim ngaihsutna khang tawntungin a kip hi.
English: The counsel of the LORD standeth for ever, The thoughts of his heart to all generations.

**33:12**
Zolai: Topa, Pasian-a a nei minam, ama luah dingin teelna a ngah minamte thupha ngah ahi hi.
English: Blessed is the nation whose God is the LORD ; And the people whom he hath chosen for his own inheritance.

**33:13**
Zolai: Topa in vantung panin hong ensuk a, mihing khempeuh a mu hi.
English: The LORD looketh from heaven; he beholdeth all the sons of men.

**33:14**
Zolai: A tutna mun panin amah hong dakkhia-in, leitung mite a en hi.
English: From the place of his habitation he looketh upon all the inhabitants of the earth.

**33:15**
Zolai: Amau’ lungsim a bawlpa in amaute’ gamtatnate en gige hi.
English: He fashioneth their hearts alike; He considereth all their works.

**33:16**
Zolai: Kumpi khat a galkap tampite in suaktasak zo lo a, galkap hang pa ama hatna tawh kihonkhia zo lo hi.
English: There is no king saved by the multitude of an host: A mighty man is not delivered by much strength.

**33:17**
Zolai: Sakol galkapte pen gualzawh nadingin a mawkna lametna hi a, amau’ hatna tawh hon zo lo hi.
English: An horse is a vain thing for safety: Neither shall he deliver any by his great strength.

**33:18**
Zolai: Amah a zahtakte, a itna kip lametna a neite, sihna panin honkhia-in, kialpi hun sungin amaute a hinkep theih nadingin Topa in amaute en tawntung hi.
English: Behold, the eye of the LORD is upon them that fear him, Upon them that hope in his mercy;

**33:20**
Zolai: Topa i ngak hi; amah pen eite hong huhpa le i lum ahi hi.
English: Our soul waiteth for the LORD : He is our help and our shield.

**33:21**
Zolai: Ama min siangtho eite in muang ihih manin ama sungah i lungdam hi.
English: For our heart shall rejoice in him, Because we have trusted in his holy name.

**33:22**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang kong lamet uh mah bangin kote’ tungah na itna kip hong omsak in.
English: Let thy mercy, O LORD , be upon us, According as we hope in thee.

## Chapter 34

**34:1**
Zolai: Topa ka phat tawntung ding a, amah phatna ka gengen ding hi.
English: I will bless the LORD at all times: His praise shall continually be in my mouth.

**34:2**
Zolai: Topa ka phat ding hi. Gimna thuakte zasak unla, lungdam uh hen.
English: My soul shall make her boast in the LORD : The humble shall hear thereof , and be glad.

**34:3**
Zolai: Kei tawh Topa nak phat un, ama min pahtawi khawm ni!
English: O magnify the LORD with me, And let us exalt his name together.

**34:4**
Zolai: Keimah in Topa ka zong a, amah in kei hong dawngin, ka launa khempeuh panin kei hong honkhia hi.
English: I sought the LORD , and he heard me, And delivered me from all my fears.

**34:5**
Zolai: Amah en unla, maitai un; tua hileh na mai uh zum ngei lo ding hi.
English: They looked unto him, and were lightened: And their faces were not ashamed.

**34:6**
Zolai: Hih mi hehpihhuai pa kiko-in, Topa in amah za a, ama haksatna khempeuh panin amah a honkhia hi.
English: This poor man cried, and the LORD heard him , And saved him out of all his troubles.

**34:7**
Zolai: Amah a zahtakte’ kiimah Topa’ vantungmi in giahphual sat a, amaute a honkhia hi.
English: The angel of the LORD encampeth round about them that fear him, And delivereth them.

**34:8**
Zolai: Topa tawh kikhawl phot unla, ama hoihna thei un! Amah a beel mite mi lungdam ahi uh hi.
English: O taste and see that the LORD is good: Blessed is the man that trusteth in him.

**34:9**
Zolai: Ama mi siangthote aw, Topa zahtak un; bang hang hiam cih leh amah a zahtak mite in kitangsapna nei lo hi.
English: O fear the LORD , ye his saints: For there is no want to them that fear him.

**34:10**
Zolai: Humpinelkai khanglaite in kisapna le gilkialna thuak a, ahih hangin Topa a zongte in na hoih a kisap uh om lo hi.
English: The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger: But they that seek the LORD shall not want any good thing .

**34:11**
Zolai: Tate aw, hong pai unla hong ngai un; Topa zahtakna thu ka hong hilh ding hi.
English: Come, ye children, hearken unto me: I will teach you the fear of the LORD .

**34:12**
Zolai: Nopna a neih theih nadingin nuntakna le khansau a deih kua ahi hiam?
English: What man is he that desireth life, And loveth many days, that he may see good?

**34:13**
Zolai: Siatna ding panin na leii kem inla, zuau genna panin na muk kem in.
English: Keep thy tongue from evil, And thy lips from speaking guile.

**34:14**
Zolai: Siatna panin kihemkhia inla, a hoih bawl in. Kilemna ding hanciam inla, na phak mateng delh in.
English: Depart from evil, and do good; Seek peace, and pursue it.

**34:15**
Zolai: Topa’ mit in thuman mite’ lam en a, amau’ kikona lamah a bil a ngat hi.
English: The eyes of the LORD are upon the righteous, And his ears are open unto their cry.

**34:16**
Zolai: Siatna a bawl mite hih leitung panin a kiphawkna a kisuktat nadingin Topa in amaute a langpang hi.
English: The face of the LORD is against them that do evil, To cut off the remembrance of them from the earth.

**34:17**
Zolai: Huhna a ngen dingin thumante a kiko ciangin Topa in za a, a haksatna khempeuh panun amaute a honkhia hi.
English: The righteous cry, and the LORD heareth, And delivereth them out of all their troubles.

**34:18**
Zolai: Lungsim kitamzante kiangah Topa hong om a, lungsim zangawpte a hon hi.
English: The LORD is nigh unto them that are of a broken heart; And saveth such as be of a contrite spirit.

**34:19**
Zolai: Thuman mi’ thuakna a tam mahmah hangin tuate khempeuh panin Topa in amah a hon hi.
English: Many are the afflictions of the righteous: But the LORD delivereth him out of them all.

**34:20**
Zolai: Amah in thuman mipa kem a, a guh khat zong kitan lo hi.
English: He keepeth all his bones: Not one of them is broken.

**34:21**
Zolai: Siatna in migilote that ding a, thuman a mudah mite gim kipia ding hi.
English: Evil shall slay the wicked: And they that hate the righteous shall be desolate.

**34:22**
Zolai: Topa in ama nasemte honkhia a, amah a bel mi khat beek gim kipia lo ding hi.
English: The LORD redeemeth the soul of his servants: And none of them that trust in him shall be desolate.

## Chapter 35

**35:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, kei hong langpangte langpang inla, kei hong dote do in.
English: Plead my cause , O LORD , with them that strive with me: Fight against them that fight against me.

**35:2**
Zolai: Lum lian le lum neu la inla, keimah hong huh in!
English: Take hold of shield and buckler, And stand up for mine help.

**35:3**
Zolai: Teipi le teitangzang dok inla, kei hong delhte’ lam ngat in! Keima tungah, “Nang a hong honpa ka hi,” hong ci in.
English: Draw out also the spear, and stop the way against them that persecute me: Say unto my soul, I am thy salvation.

**35:4**
Zolai: Kei hong sawmte mai zumin mindaisak ta in! Keima siatna ding a bawlte nungkik sakin sisak in!
English: Let them be confounded and put to shame that seek after my soul: Let them be turned back and brought to confusion that devise my hurt.

**35:5**
Zolai: Topa’ vantungmi’ hawlna tawh huih letkhiat ansite tawh amaute kibangsak in.
English: Let them be as chaff before the wind: And let the angel of the LORD chase them .

**35:6**
Zolai: Topa’ vantungmi’ delhna-ah a taina lampi uh mialin nalsak in.
English: Let their way be dark and slippery: And let the angel of the LORD persecute them.

**35:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in thu om lopi-in a ngenthang uh tawh kei hong siah uh a, thu om lopi-in gum to-in kei hong siah uh hi.
English: For without cause have they hid for me their net in a pit, Which without cause they have digged for my soul.

**35:8**
Zolai: A phawk loh kalun amaute’ tungah siatna tungsak in! Amau’ ngenthang mahah amaute mah awksak inla, a kisiamang khin dingin amaute puksak in.
English: Let destruction come upon him at unawares; and let his net that he hath hid catch himself: Into that very destruction let him fall.

**35:9**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa tungah ka lungdam mahmah ding a, ama hotkhiatna-ah nuamin ka diang ding hi.
English: And my soul shall be joyful in the LORD : It shall rejoice in his salvation.

**35:10**
Zolai: Ka lungsim khempeuh tawh, “ Topa aw, ama a dingin a hatluate kiang panin a thahat lo mi a honkhia, a bawlsiate’ kiang panin mizawngte a honkhia, nang tawh a kibang kua om ahi hiam?” ka ci ding hi.
English: All my bones shall say, LORD , who is like unto thee, which deliverest the poor from him that is too strong for him, Yea, the poor and the needy from him that spoileth him?

**35:11**
Zolai: Mi a el tecite hong kipan uh a, ka theih loh thute kei hong dong uh hi.
English: False witnesses did rise up; They laid to my charge things that I knew not.

**35:12**
Zolai: Amaute in ka hoihnate siatna tawh hong thuk uh a, ka khawngai mahmah hi.
English: They rewarded me evil for good To the spoiling of my soul.

**35:13**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei ahihleh, amaute a cinat uh ciangin, puanhampi silhin an tangin kei ka kigimtawm sak hi.
English: But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing was sackcloth: I humbled my soul with fasting; And my prayer returned into mine own bosom.

**35:14**
Zolai: Ka lawm, ka sanggampa hangin a dah bangin ka dah hi. A nu’ hanga a kap mi bangin kapin ka vak kawikawi a, kunin ka kidikdik hi.
English: I behaved myself as though he had been my friend or brother: I bowed down heavily, as one that mourneth for his mother.

**35:15**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei ka tukna-ah amaute nuamin kikhawm uh a, kei simmawh dingin kikaikhawm uh hi. Ka theih ngei hetloh khebaite nangawn in tawlnga hetloin kei hong gensia niloh uh hi.
English: But in mine adversity they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together: Yea , the abjects gathered themselves together against me, and I knew it not; they did tear me , and ceased not:

**35:16**
Zolai: Zahtakna mel nei hetloin kei hong zahko niloh uh a, a ha uh hong gawisan uh hi.
English: With hypocritical mockers in feasts, They gnashed upon me with their teeth.

**35:17**
Zolai: Topa aw, bang tanvei hong enkhong ding na hi hiam? Amau’ hong sukgawpna panin keimah hong honkhia inla, humpinelkaite kiang panin kei hong hon in.
English: Lord, how long wilt thou look on? Rescue my soul from their destructions, my darling from the lions.

**35:18**
Zolai: Tua ciangin mihon kikhopna lian sungah nangma tungah lungdamna ka hong ko ding a, mihonpite lak panin nang ka hong phat ding hi.
English: I will give thee thanks in the great congregation: I will praise thee among much people.

**35:19**
Zolai: A man lopi a ka gal a hite kei tungah lungdamsak kei inla, thu om lopi a kei hong mudahte, mitheek kipiasak kei in.
English: Let not them that are mine enemies wrongfully rejoice over me: Neither let them wink with the eye that hate me without a cause.

**35:20**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in kilemna thu gen lo uh a, daitakin a om mite langpangin, khemna thu ngaihsun uh hi.
English: For they speak not peace: But they devise deceitful matters against them that are quiet in the land.

**35:21**
Zolai: Amaute in kei hong kamkat beba uh a, amaute in, “Ha, Ha! Mu khin hang ei!” ci uh hi.
English: Yea, they opened their mouth wide against me, And said, Aha, aha, our eye hath seen it .

**35:22**
Zolai: Topa aw, na mu khin hi; dai ommawk ke’n! Topa aw, kei kiang panin gamla om ke’n!
English: This thou hast seen, O LORD : keep not silence: O Lord, be not far from me.

**35:23**
Zolai: Ka Topa, ka Pasian aw, ka thu hong thei inla, kei a dingin nangmah hong kisosuah tawm in!
English: Stir up thyself, and awake to my judgment, Even unto my cause, my God and my Lord.

**35:24**
Zolai: Ka Topa, ka Pasian aw, na thumanna tawh a kituakin keima thutanna hong langsak inla, keima gimna-ah amaute lungdamsak ke’n!
English: Judge me, O LORD my God, according to thy righteousness; And let them not rejoice over me.

**35:25**
Zolai: Amau le amau tungah, “Ha, i tuptup tung ei!” kicisak kei in. “Amah nawmvalhtum khin hang,” amaute cisak kei in.
English: Let them not say in their hearts, Ah, so would we have it: Let them not say, We have swallowed him up.

**35:26**
Zolai: Kei’ kamsiatna-ah a lungdamte maizumsak inla, zahhuaigawp sak in! Kei tungah a hong kiliansakte maizumna le mindaina thuaksak in!
English: Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion together that rejoice at mine hurt: Let them be clothed with shame and dishonour that magnify themselves against me.

**35:27**
Zolai: Kei thutang ka hihna lahkhiat ding a deihte lungdamin awngin, kipaaksak inla, “A nasempa’ hoihna-ah a lungkim Topa lian hi,” cici sak in.
English: Let them shout for joy, and be glad, that favour my righteous cause: Yea, let them say continually, Let the LORD be magnified, which hath pleasure in the prosperity of his servant.

**35:28**
Zolai: Tua ciangin na thumanna le nangmah phatna sunthapai-in ka gengen ding hi.
English: And my tongue shall speak of thy righteousness And of thy praise all the day long.

## Chapter 36

**36:1**
Zolai: Mawhna in migilo pa’ lungsim tawngah thu gen a, amah in Pasian zahtakna nei het lo hi.
English: The transgression of the wicked saith within my heart, That there is no fear of God before his eyes.

**36:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ama mawhna kidawkkhia lo a, muhdahna thuak lo ahih manin amah kimawkphat tawm hi.
English: For he flattereth himself in his own eyes, until his iniquity be found to be hateful.

**36:3**
Zolai: Ama kammalte pen siatna le khemna vive hi a, pil gamtatna le hoih gamtatna bei khinta hi.
English: The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit: He hath left off to be wise, and to do good.

**36:4**
Zolai: A lupna tungah lumin siat gamtat ding a ngaihsun hi. Hoih lohna lamah amah kibulhtawm a, amah in siatna nolh lo hi.
English: He deviseth mischief upon his bed; He setteth himself in a way that is not good; He abhorreth not evil.

**36:5**
Zolai: Topa aw, na itna kip in vantung ban a, na cihtakna in vanpi dong banto hi.
English: Thy mercy, O LORD , is in the heavens; And thy faithfulness reacheth unto the clouds.

**36:6**
Zolai: Na thumanna pen Pasian’ mualte tawh kibang a, na thukhennate pen tuipi thuk tawh kibang hi. Mihing le ganhing na hon hi, Topa aw.
English: Thy righteousness is like the great mountains; Thy judgments are a great deep: O LORD , thou preservest man and beast.

**36:7**
Zolai: Pasian aw, na itna kip manpha mahmah hi. Mihing tate na kha liimah bu uh hi.
English: How excellent is thy lovingkindness, O God! Therefore the children of men put their trust under the shadow of thy wings.

**36:8**
Zolai: Na inn sunga na tampite tawh amaute nuamsa uh a, na hoihna gun panin amaute na dawnsak hi.
English: They shall be abundantly satisfied with the fatness of thy house; And thou shalt make them drink of the river of thy pleasures.

**36:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nuntakna tuinak nangmah tawh om a, na khuavak sungah kote in khuavak ka mu uh hi.
English: For with thee is the fountain of life: In thy light shall we see light.

**36:10**
Zolai: Nang hong theite tungah na itna kip hong zom inla, lungsim thutangte tungah na hotkhiatna hong zom in!
English: O continue thy lovingkindness unto them that know thee; And thy righteousness to the upright in heart.

**36:11**
Zolai: A kihisak mite kei hong sukhasak kei inla, migilote, hong hawlkhiasak kei in.
English: Let not the foot of pride come against me, And let not the hand of the wicked remove me.

**36:12**
Zolai: Hua lai-ah siatna bawlte a cimawhin kun uh a, amaute kisuncip sukin, thozo nawn lo uh hi.
English: There are the workers of iniquity fallen: They are cast down, and shall not be able to rise.

## Chapter 37

**37:1**
Zolai: Migilote’ hangin kilungsosak kei inla, a man loin a gamta mite en’ dingin ngaihsun kei in.
English: Fret not thyself because of evildoers, Neither be thou envious against the workers of iniquity.

**37:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh lopa bangin amaute vulpak ding uh a, lokung hingte bangin keutum ding uh hi.
English: For they shall soon be cut down like the grass, And wither as the green herb.

**37:3**
Zolai: Topa muang inla, gamtat hoih in. Gam nuamah teng inla, thumanin om in.
English: Trust in the LORD , and do good; So shalt thou dwell in the land, and verily thou shalt be fed.

**37:4**
Zolai: Topa sungah lungkim in; amah in na deihna hong pia ding hi.
English: Delight thyself also in the LORD ; And he shall give thee the desires of thine heart.

**37:5**
Zolai: Topa tungah na vai teng ap in. Amah muang in; amah in hong sem ding hi.
English: Commit thy way unto the LORD ; Trust also in him; And he shall bring it to pass.

**37:6**
Zolai: Amah in nangma dikna khuavak bangin, nangma thumanna nitaang bangin hong langsak ding hi.
English: And he shall bring forth thy righteousness as the light, And thy judgment as the noonday.

**37:7**
Zolai: Topa’ mai-ah khawl dide inla, lungduai takin ngak in. A hihna a daupai pa tung le siatna a bawlpa tungah kilungso tawmsak ke’n!
English: Rest in the LORD , and wait patiently for him: Fret not thyself because of him who prospereth in his way, because of the man who bringeth wicked devices to pass.

**37:8**
Zolai: Hehna panin kikham inla, sinsona nusia in. Nangmah kilungso tawmsak ke’n; tua in siatna bekah a hong paipih hi.
English: Cease from anger, and forsake wrath: Fret not thyself in any wise to do evil.

**37:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh migilote kipuaseh ding a, ahih hangin Topa a ngakte in leitung luah ding uh hi.
English: For evildoers shall be cut off: But those that wait upon the LORD , they shall inherit the earth.

**37:10**
Zolai: Ahih hangin tawlkhat sungin migilo pa om nawn lo ding a, ama omna mun na lim zon mahmah hangin tua lai-ah amah na om lo ding hi.
English: For yet a little while, and the wicked shall not be: Yea, thou shalt diligently consider his place, and it shall not be .

**37:11**
Zolai: Ahih hangin lungnemte in leitung luahin, genzawh lohin amaute nuamsa ding uh hi.
English: But the meek shall inherit the earth; And shall delight themselves in the abundance of peace.

**37:12**
Zolai: Migilo in thuman pa sawm a, a ha a gawisan hi.
English: The wicked plotteth against the just, And gnasheth upon him with his teeth.

**37:13**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa in migilo pa’ hun a tungta ahihlam mu ahih manin amah a nuihsan lel hi.
English: The Lord shall laugh at him: For he seeth that his day is coming.

**37:14**
Zolai: Mizawngte le mi cimawhte a suniam ding, a thutangte a that dingin migilote in namsau dokin, a thal uh a keek hi.
English: The wicked have drawn out the sword, and have bent their bow, To cast down the poor and needy, and to slay such as be of upright conversation.

**37:15**
Zolai: A namsau uh amau’ lungtang mahah tumin, a thalte uh kitan ding hi.
English: Their sword shall enter into their own heart, And their bows shall be broken.

**37:16**
Zolai: Migilote’ hauhna sangin thuman mite in tawmno khat bek a neihna hoihzaw lai hi.
English: A little that a righteous man hath is better Than the riches of many wicked.

**37:17**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh migilote’ thahatna kipaih khiatsak ding a, ahih hangin Topa in mihoihte a huh hi.
English: For the arms of the wicked shall be broken: But the LORD upholdeth the righteous.

**37:18**
Zolai: Topa in a paubaang lote kem a, amau’ gamh kipden ding hi.
English: The LORD knoweth the days of the upright: And their inheritance shall be for ever.

**37:19**
Zolai: Siatna hun ciangin amaute kimaizumsak lo a, kial hun ciangin tampi nei uh hi.
English: They shall not be ashamed in the evil time: And in the days of famine they shall be satisfied.

**37:20**
Zolai: Ahih hangin migilote kisia hi. Topa’ galte pen lono etlawm tawh kibang a, amaute mangthang pak uh hi. Meikhu bangin mangthang uh hi.
English: But the wicked shall perish, And the enemies of the LORD shall be as the fat of lambs: They shall consume; into smoke shall they consume away.

**37:21**
Zolai: Migilo in leitawi la a, lohkikzo nawn lo hi. Thuman mi ahihleh cingh-in mi a pia hi.
English: The wicked borroweth, and payeth not again: But the righteous sheweth mercy, and giveth.

**37:22**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa’ thupha piakte in leitung luah ding uh a, ahih hangin a samsiatte kipuaseh ding hi.
English: For such as be blessed of him shall inherit the earth; And they that be cursed of him shall be cut off.

**37:23**
Zolai: Topa in mi a lam pai nading lak a, ama lungkim bangin a gamta pa amah in a kipsak hi.
English: The steps of a good man are ordered by the LORD : And he delighteth in his way.

**37:24**
Zolai: Amah a puk hangin lutuk lo ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in ama khut len hi.
English: Though he fall, he shall not be utterly cast down: For the LORD upholdeth him with his hand.

**37:25**
Zolai: Thuman mi a kinusiacip, a suanlekhakte ngen tawmin a kivak, ka neu lai a kipanin tu-a ka teek hun ciang dong ka mu ngei nai kei hi.
English: I have been young, and now am old; Yet have I not seen the righteous forsaken, nor his seed begging bread.

**37:26**
Zolai: Amah in mi citpiak ngitngetin, mi tungah leitawi piakhia a, a suanlekhakte zong thupha ngah mi a suak hi.
English: He is ever merciful, and lendeth; And his seed is blessed.

**37:27**
Zolai: Siatna panin kikem inla, gamtat hoih in; tua hileh na khantawnin, na kip paisuak ding hi.
English: Depart from evil, and do good; And dwell for evermore.

**37:28**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in thutang deih a, ama mi siangthote nusia lo ding hi. Thuman mite kikemcing den ding a, ahi zongin migilo’ suanlekhakte kipuaseh ding hi.
English: For the LORD loveth judgment, And forsaketh not his saints; they are preserved for ever: But the seed of the wicked shall be cut off.

**37:29**
Zolai: Thuman mi in leitung luah ding a, tua leitang tungah teng paisuak ding hi.
English: The righteous shall inherit the land, And dwell therein for ever.

**37:30**
Zolai: Thuman mi’ kam in pilna gen a, a leii in thutang gen hi.
English: The mouth of the righteous speaketh wisdom, And his tongue talketh of judgment.

**37:31**
Zolai: A lungsim sungah ama Pasian’ thukham om a, a gamtatna khempeuhah lampial het lo hi.
English: The law of his God is in his heart; None of his steps shall slide.

**37:32**
Zolai: Migilo in thuman mi encik a, thah dingin a zong hi.
English: The wicked watcheth the righteous, And seeketh to slay him.

**37:33**
Zolai: Topa in migilo pa’ khut sungah amah nusia lo ding a, thusit dingin a kipaipih ciangin mawhna thuaksak lo ding hi.
English: The LORD will not leave him in his hand, Nor condemn him when he is judged.

**37:34**
Zolai: Topa ngak inla, ama lampi zui in. Leitang a luah dingin nang hong liansak ding a, migilote’ siatna nangmah in na en ding hi.
English: Wait on the LORD , and keep his way, and he shall exalt thee to inherit the land: When the wicked are cut off, thou shalt see it .

**37:35**
Zolai: Lebanon taamtak sing bangin a sang pha mahmah migilo kiphasak khat keimah in ka mu hi.
English: I have seen the wicked in great power, And spreading himself like a green bay tree.

**37:36**
Zolai: Ama kiangah ka paikik a, amah na om nawn lo hi. Amah ka zonzon hangin kimuzo nawn lo hi.
English: Yet he passed away, and, lo, he was not: Yea, I sought him, but he could not be found.

**37:37**
Zolai: Paubaang lo mi ciamteh inla, thutang mi en in; bang hang hiam cih leh gal a phuang lo mi a dingin nopna a om hi.
English: Mark the perfect man , and behold the upright: For the end of that man is peace.

**37:38**
Zolai: Ahih hangin thupalsatte kisusiamang khin ding a, migilote’ suanlekhakte kipuaseh ding hi.
English: But the transgressors shall be destroyed together: The end of the wicked shall be cut off.

**37:39**
Zolai: Topa in thuman mite honkhia a, amah pen haksat hun ciangin amaute’ bukna ahi hi.
English: But the salvation of the righteous is of the LORD : He is their strength in the time of trouble.

**37:40**
Zolai: Amaute in Topa beel ahih manin amah in amaute huhin honkhia a, migilote’ kiang panin amaute honin suaktasak hi.
English: And the LORD shall help them, and deliver them: He shall deliver them from the wicked, and save them, because they trust in him.

## Chapter 38

**38:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, a hehsa-in kei hong taii kei inla, lungsosa in kei hong thuhilh kei in.
English: O LORD , rebuke me not in thy wrath: Neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.

**38:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma thaltangte ka sungah hong tum khin a, ka tungah na khuttum hong tu khinta hi.
English: For thine arrows stick fast in me, And thy hand presseth me sore.

**38:3**
Zolai: Nangma hehna hangin kei ka ci na a, ka mawhna hangin ka pumtangin ka na hi.
English: There is no soundness in my flesh because of thine anger; Neither is there any rest in my bones because of my sin.

**38:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka mawhnate in ka lu dong hong tuumzo a, keima puak dingin a giklua vangik tawh kibang hi.
English: For mine iniquities are gone over mine head: As an heavy burden they are too heavy for me.

**38:5**
Zolai: Ka haina hangin ka liamnate nai-in uih a,
English: My wounds stink and are corrupt Because of my foolishness.

**38:6**
Zolai: keimah hong kikunsak a, hong kibokcipsak hi. Sunthapai-in kapin ka vak kawikawi hi.
English: I am troubled; I am bowed down greatly; I go mourning all the day long.

**38:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka ci sa mahmah a, nakpitakin ka ci na hi.
English: For my loins are filled with a loathsome disease: And there is no soundness in my flesh.

**38:8**
Zolai: Kei hong kinengcip gawpin ka thahatna beimang khin a, ka lungsim gimna hangin thumin ka tautau hi.
English: I am feeble and sore broken: I have roared by reason of the disquietness of my heart.

**38:9**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka deihna khempeuh na thei a, ka khuisatnate na za hi.
English: Lord, all my desire is before thee; And my groaning is not hid from thee.

**38:10**
Zolai: Ka lungtang kisat a, ka tha in lel hi. Ka mit in zong khua mu thei nawn lo hi.
English: My heart panteth, my strength faileth me: As for the light of mine eyes, it also is gone from me.

**38:11**
Zolai: Ka gim thuakna-ah ka lawmte le ka kithuahpihte kidang koih uh a, keima behte nangawn kei kiang pan gamla om uh hi.
English: My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my sore; And my kinsmen stand afar off.

**38:12**
Zolai: Kei a hong that nuamte in a thang uh zak a, kei’ natna ding a zongte in siatna ding thu bek gen uh a, sunthapai-in khemna bekbek ngaihsutin nei uh hi.
English: They also that seek after my life lay snares for me: And they that seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and imagine deceits all the day long.

**38:13**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei pen bilngong ka bang a, khua ka za kei hi. A kam a ka thei lo, a pau thei lo mi ka bang hi.
English: But I, as a deaf man , heard not; And I was as a dumb man that openeth not his mouth.

**38:14**
Zolai: Bil khua za lo, tawnna kam a za thei lo mi khat tawh kei ka kibang takpi hi.
English: Thus I was as a man that heareth not, And in whose mouth are no reproofs.

**38:15**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa aw, nangmah ka hong muang hi. Topa ka Pasian aw, a hong dawng ding pa nangmah na hi hi.
English: For in thee, O LORD , do I hope: Thou wilt hear, O Lord my God.

**38:16**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh, “Ka khe a taal ciangin kei tunga hong kihisakte, keima gim thuakna-ah lungdam sak kei in,” cih bek ka hong thum hi.
English: For I said, Hear me , lest otherwise they should rejoice over me: When my foot slippeth, they magnify themselves against me.

**38:17**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh puk dingin ka kithawi a, ka gimna kam tuan lo hi.
English: For I am ready to halt, And my sorrow is continually before me.

**38:18**
Zolai: Ka thuman lohna ka pulak a, ka mawhna hangin ka dah hi.
English: For I will declare mine iniquity; I will be sorry for my sin.

**38:19**
Zolai: A thuman lopi-in ka gal a hite thahat a, kei a hong mudah khialte tam mahmah uh hi.
English: But mine enemies are lively, and they are strong: And they that hate me wrongfully are multiplied.

**38:20**
Zolai: A hoih gamta ka hih manin ka hoihna pen siatna tawh a hong thukte ka langpangte ahi hi.
English: They also that render evil for good Are mine adversaries; because I follow the thing that good is .

**38:21**
Zolai: Topa aw, kei hong nusia kei in. Ka Pasian aw, ka kiang pan gamla om ke’n!
English: Forsake me not, O LORD : O my God, be not far from me.

**38:22**
Zolai: Topa, kei hong honpa aw, keimah a hong huh dingin hong manlang in.
English: Make haste to help me, O Lord my salvation.

## Chapter 39

**39:1**
Zolai: “Ka leii tawh ka khialhloh nadingin ka gamtatna ka kikem ding a, ka omna-ah migilote a omlaiteng ka kam ka kham ding hi,” ka ci hi.
English: I said, I will take heed to my ways, That I sin not with my tongue: I will keep my mouth with a bridle, While the wicked is before me.

**39:2**
Zolai: Pau loin ka dai om a, ka dai omna a mawkna suak a, ka thuakna khang semsem hi.
English: I was dumb with silence, I held my peace, even from good; And my sorrow was stirred.

**39:3**
Zolai: Ka sungah ka lung so a, ka lungngaih ciangin ka lung so semsem hi. Tua ciangin ka paukhia a,
English: My heart was hot within me, while I was musing the fire burned: Then spake I with my tongue.

**39:4**
Zolai: “ Topa aw, ka mong le ka hun a kisehzah hong theisak inla, ka nuntakna a beipak hun ding hong theisak in!” ka ci hi.
English: LORD , make me to know mine end, and the measure of my days, what it is ; That I may know how frail I am .

**39:5**
Zolai: Ka nuntakna hun khutme tan bang bekin na bawl a, ka nuntakna hun nangma muhna-ah bangmah gentham lo hi. Mihing khempeuh, husan’ bang bek hi takpi hi.
English: Behold, thou hast made my days as an handbreadth; And mine age is as nothing before thee: Verily every man at his best state is altogether vanity. Selah.

**39:6**
Zolai: Niliim bangin mihing pai kawikawi takpi hi. A mawkna-in amau lungkham takpi uh a, kua’ ngah ding cih thei lopi-in mite in na a khol uh hi.
English: Surely every man walketh in a vain shew: Surely they are disquieted in vain: He heapeth up riches , and knoweth not who shall gather them.

**39:7**
Zolai: Tu-in Topa aw, ke’n, bang ngaklai ding ka hi hiam? Keima lametna nangma sung bekah om hi.
English: And now, Lord, what wait I for? My hope is in thee.

**39:8**
Zolai: Ka thupalsatna khempeuh panin kei hong honkhia inla, mite’ nuihsatin kei hong bawl kei in.
English: Deliver me from all my transgressions: Make me not the reproach of the foolish.

**39:9**
Zolai: Hih bangin a hong bawl nangmah na hih manin pau loin ka om a, ka kam ka ka kei hi.
English: I was dumb, I opened not my mouth; Because thou didst it .

**39:10**
Zolai: Nong vuakna ma ka tung panin lakhia in. Na hong vuakna hangin ka tha beita hi.
English: Remove thy stroke away from me: I am consumed by the blow of thine hand.

**39:11**
Zolai: Mi khat a mawhna hangin tai-in na sat ciangin, nget in a nektum bangin ama na manpha na beisak hi. Mihing khempeuh husan’ khat bang bek hi takpi hi.
English: When thou with rebukes dost correct man for iniquity, Thou makest his beauty to consume away like a moth: Surely every man is vanity. Selah.

**39:12**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka thungetna hong ngai inla, ka kikona hong za in. Ka khitui luanna hong thudon in. Bang hang hiam cih leh ka pu ka pate khempeuh bangin kei zong na zin, na peemta ka hi hi.
English: Hear my prayer, O LORD , and give ear unto my cry; Hold not thy peace at my tears: For I am a stranger with thee, And a sojourner, as all my fathers were .

**39:13**
Zolai: Ka manthan hun matengin ka lungnop theih nadingin kei hong en in!
English: O spare me, that I may recover strength, Before I go hence, and be no more.

## Chapter 40

**40:1**
Zolai: Topa lamenin ka ngak ngiungeu a, amah kei lam hong nga-in ka kikona aw hong za hi.
English: I waited patiently for the LORD ; And he inclined unto me, and heard my cry.

**40:2**
Zolai: Dahna dum sung, buannawng panin kei hong kaikhia-in suangpi tungah ka khete nga a, ka khesikna mun a muanhuaisak hi.
English: He brought me up also out of an horrible pit, out of the miry clay, And set my feet upon a rock, and established my goings.

**40:3**
Zolai: Eima Pasian phatna la thak keimah hong hilh hi. Mi tampite in hih thu mu-in amah zahtak ding uh a, amaute khempeuh in Topa muang ding uh hi.
English: And he hath put a new song in my mouth, even praise unto our God: Many shall see it , and fear, And shall trust in the LORD .

**40:4**
Zolai: Topa a muang a, mi kiphasakte lamah a kihei lo, pasian man lote lamah a pialkhia lo mi thupha ngah ahi hi.
English: Blessed is that man that maketh the LORD his trust, And respecteth not the proud, nor such as turn aside to lies.

**40:5**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, na sep a lamdangte le ko a dingin na ngaihsutnate tampi tak na phasak a, kuamah dang tawh tehtheih na hi kei hi. Tuate pulakin gen ding hi leng, genkhit zawh ding hi lo hi.
English: Many, O LORD my God, Are thy wonderful works which thou hast done, And thy thoughts which are to us-ward: They cannot be reckoned up in order unto thee: If I would declare and speak of them , They are more than can be numbered.

**40:6**
Zolai: Gan gawh biakna le khawhsa tawh biakna na deih kei a, khua ka zak theih nading bil na hong guan hi. Meihal biakna le mawhmaina ding biakna zong na kulsak kei hi.
English: Sacrifice and offering thou didst not desire; Mine ears hast thou opened: Burnt offering and sin offering hast thou not required.

**40:7**
Zolai: Tua ciangin keimah in, “En in, laibu sungah keima thu a kigelh khinsa bangin ka hong pai hi.
English: Then said I, Lo, I come: In the volume of the book it is written of me,

**40:8**
Zolai: Nangma deih bang hihna-ah nuam ka sa hi, ka Pasian aw. Nangma thukham ka lung sungah om hi,” ka ci hi.
English: I delight to do thy will, O my God: Yea, thy law is within my heart.

**40:9**
Zolai: Hotkhiatna hangin lungdam thu mihonpi lakah ka gen ding hi. Topa aw, lungdam thugen ka khawl ngei kei ding hi.
English: I have preached righteousness in the great congregation: Lo, I have not refrained my lips, O LORD , thou knowest.

**40:10**
Zolai: Nangma hotkhiatna thu ka im kei a, na thumanna le na hotkhiatna ka gen khin hi. Na itna kip le na thumanna mihonpi tungah ka im kei hi.
English: I have not hid thy righteousness within my heart; I have declared thy faithfulness and thy salvation: I have not concealed thy lovingkindness, And thy truth from the great congregation.

**40:11**
Zolai: Topa aw, na hehpihna kei kiang panin humcip kei inla, na itna kip le na thumanna kei a hong kem tawntung ding hisak ta in.
English: Withhold not thou thy tender mercies from me, O LORD : Let thy lovingkindness and thy truth continually preserve me.

**40:12**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh a malin simzawh loh ding siatna tampite in kei hong umcih a, khua a hong musak thei lo zah dong dingin ka mawhna thaman ka thuak khinta hi. Amaute ka sam mal sangin tamzaw uh a, ka lung in a lel ta hi.
English: For innumerable evils have compassed me about: Mine iniquities have taken hold upon me, so that I am not able to look up; They are more than the hairs of mine head: Therefore my heart faileth me.

**40:13**
Zolai: Topa aw, keimah hong honkhia nuam in. Topa aw, hong huh meng in.
English: Be pleased, O LORD , to deliver me: O LORD , make haste to help me.

**40:14**
Zolai: Kei a hong that nuamte zahhuaisak inla, maisiasak in. Keima siatna ding a deihte nungkiksak inla minsiasak in.
English: Let them be ashamed and confounded together That seek after my soul to destroy it; Let them be driven backward and put to shame that wish me evil.

**40:15**
Zolai: Keima tungah, “Ha ha!” hong ci vialte zahhuaina tawh maikhingsak in.
English: Let them be desolate for a reward of their shame That say unto me, Aha, aha.

**40:16**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nang a hong zongte khempeuh nangma hangin nuamin kipak hen la, na hotkhiat ding a deihte in, “ Topa lian hi!” ci ngitnget ta uh hen.
English: Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: Let such as love thy salvation say continually, the LORD be magnified.

**40:17**
Zolai: Kei ahihleh zawngin ka cimawh a, ahih hangin Topa in kei hong mangngilh lo hi. Nang pen kei hong huhpa le hong honkhia pa na hi hi. Zekai kei in, ka Pasian aw.
English: But I am poor and needy; Yet the Lord thinketh upon me: Thou art my help and my deliverer; Make no tarrying, O my God.

## Chapter 41

**41:1**
Zolai: Mi genthei a khualte thupha ngah ahi hi. Topa in haksatna hunah amaute honkhia ding hi.
English: Blessed is he that considereth the poor: The LORD will deliver him in time of trouble.

**41:2**
Zolai: Topa in amaute hu-in hingsak ding a, leitungah amaute thupha ngah mi kici ding hi. Amau’ galte’ khut sungah amaute pia lo ding hi.
English: The LORD will preserve him, and keep him alive; and he shall be blessed upon the earth: And thou wilt not deliver him unto the will of his enemies.

**41:3**
Zolai: A ci uh a nat ciangin Topa in amaute kem ding a, a cinatna khempeuh uh damsakkik ding hi.
English: The LORD will strengthen him upon the bed of languishing: Thou wilt make all his bed in his sickness.

**41:4**
Zolai: Ke’n ahihleh, “ Topa aw, kei hong hehpih inla, kei hong damsak in; bang hang hiam cih leh nang tungah kong khialzo hi,” ka ci hi.
English: I said, LORD , be merciful unto me: Heal my soul; for I have sinned against thee.

**41:5**
Zolai: Ka galte in elna tawh keima thu gen uh a, “Cik ciangin amah a si tam, cik ciangin a min a mang tam,” ci uh hi.
English: Mine enemies speak evil of me, When shall he die, and his name perish?

**41:6**
Zolai: Keimah a en dingin mi hong pai ciangin, kam mawkna a pau uh hi. A lungsim uhah siatna kaikhawm uh a, a paikhiat uh ciangin a genthang uh hi.
English: And if he come to see me , he speaketh vanity: His heart gathereth iniquity to itself; When he goeth abroad, he telleth it .

**41:7**
Zolai: Kei hong mudah khempeuh in keima thu kihuauhuau uh a, kei a dingin a sia thei pen ding a geelgeel uh hi.
English: All that hate me whisper together against me: Against me do they devise my hurt.

**41:8**
Zolai: Amaute in, “Amah nak gim mahmah hi. A lupna panin thokikzo nawn lo ding hi,” ci uh hi.
English: An evil disease, say they , cleaveth fast unto him: And now that he lieth he shall rise up no more.

**41:9**
Zolai: Ka muan, ka lawm it pa, keima an a ne pa nangawn in a khetul tawh kei hong peek vial hi.
English: Yea, mine own familiar friend, in whom I trusted, Which did eat of my bread, hath lifted up his heel against me.

**41:10**
Zolai: Ahih hangin, Topa aw, amaute na thukkik theih nadingin kei hong hehpih inla, hong damsak in.
English: But thou, O LORD , be merciful unto me, And raise me up, that I may requite them.

**41:11**
Zolai: Ka galte in keimah hong zo lo ding a, keima tungah nong lungkimna ka thei ding hi.
English: By this I know that thou favourest me, Because mine enemy doth not triumph over me.

**41:12**
Zolai: Keima hoihna hangin na hong huh ding a, nangma omna-ah nong omsak tawntung ding hi.
English: And as for me, thou upholdest me in mine integrity, And settest me before thy face for ever.

**41:13**
Zolai: Israel Pasian, Topa in khang tawntungin thupha ngah tahen. Amen, Amen!
English: Blessed be the LORD God of Israel From everlasting, and to everlasting. Amen, and Amen.

## Chapter 42

**42:1**
Zolai: Sakhi in tuiluang sialsial a lunggulh bangin nang ka hong lunggulh hi, ka Pasian aw.
English: As the hart panteth after the water brooks, So panteth my soul after thee, O God.

**42:2**
Zolai: A nungta Pasian kong deih hi. Cik ciangin kei hong pai-in Pasian’ maitang hong mu thei ding ka hi hiam?
English: My soul thirsteth for God, for the living God: When shall I come and appear before God?

**42:3**
Zolai: Mite in keima tungah, “Na Pasian koi-ah om ahi hiam?” hong cihcih sungteng, sun le zanin ka khitui an-in ka ne hi.
English: My tears have been my meat day and night, While they continually say unto me, Where is thy God?

**42:4**
Zolai: Ka lungsim sung ka suahkhia a, pawi bawl mihon khat kipakin otna le nuamna la tawh Pasian’ inn-ah ka makaihna, mihonpi tawh ka paina ka phawkkik hi.
English: When I remember these things , I pour out my soul in me: For I had gone with the multitude, I went with them to the house of God, With the voice of joy and praise, With a multitude that kept holyday.

**42:5**
Zolai: Bang hangin khakunkun a, lunghimawh niloh ka hi hiam? Pasian’ sungah lametna nei ning; bang hang hiam cih leh kei a hong huh ka Pasian ka phatkik ngawn ding hi.
English: Why art thou cast down, O my soul? And why art thou disquieted in me? Hope thou in God: For I shall yet praise him For the help of his countenance.

**42:6**
Zolai: Ka lungsim tamkham ahih manin Jordan le Hermon gam, Mizar mualtung panin nang ka hong phawk hi.
English: O my God, my soul is cast down within me: Therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan, and of the Hermonites, from the hill Mizar.

**42:7**
Zolai: Nangma tuizeu gingte khatlekhat kidawng uh a, dahna tuihualte in kei a hong tuum hi.
English: Deep calleth unto deep at the noise of thy waterspouts: All thy waves and thy billows are gone over me.

**42:8**
Zolai: Topa in sun tawntungin a itna kip hong lak a, zan hun ciangin nuntakna a hong pia Pasian’ tungah thungetna la ka sa hi.
English: Yet the LORD will command his lovingkindness in the daytime, And in the night his song shall be with me, and my prayer unto the God of my life.

**42:9**
Zolai: “Bang hangin kei hong mangngilh na hi hiam? Galte in hong sukcip manin bang hangin kapin kidikdik ka hi hiam?” ci-in ka Pasian, kei a hong huhpa’ tungah ka gen hi.
English: I will say unto God my rock, why hast thou forgotten me? Why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?

**42:10**
Zolai: Ka langte in kei tungah, “Na Pasian koi-ah om ahi hiam?” hong cihcih sungteng, ka sungah meima nai tawm bangin hong tum ngangngang hi.
English: As with a sword in my bones, Mine enemies reproach me; While they say daily unto me, Where is thy God?

**42:11**
Zolai: Bang hangin khakunkun a, lunghimawh niloh ka hi hiam? Pasian’ sungah lametna nei ning; bang hang hiam cih leh kei a hong huh ka Pasian ka phatkik ngawn ding hi.
English: Why art thou cast down, O my soul? And why art thou disquieted within me? Hope thou in God; For I shall yet praise him, who is the health of my countenance, and my God.

## Chapter 43

**43:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, ka dikna hong langsak inla, migilote tawh ka thu-ah kei hong panpih in. Mi khemte le thutang lote kiang panin kei hong honkhia in.
English: Judge me, O God, and plead my cause against an ungodly nation: O deliver me from the deceitful and unjust man.

**43:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka hong belh Pasian na hi hi. Bang hangin kei hong nilkhia na hi hiam? Galte’ sukcip manin bang hangin kapin kidikdik ka hi hiam?
English: For thou art the God of my strength: why dost thou cast me off? Why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?

**43:3**
Zolai: Na khuavak le na thuman hong sawlkhia inla, na mual siangtho, na omna-ah kei hong paipih sakin, hong khasak in.
English: O send out thy light and thy truth: Let them lead me; Let them bring me unto thy holy hill, and to thy tabernacles.

**43:4**
Zolai: Tua ciangin na biakna tau-ah ahi a, ka lung a hong damsak Pasian kiangah ahi zongin ka pai ding a, laiza khausai lasakna tawh nang ka hong phat ding hi, aw Pasian, ka Pasian aw.
English: Then will I go unto the altar of God, unto God my exceeding joy: Yea, upon the harp will I praise thee, O God my God.

**43:5**
Zolai: Bang hangin khakunkun a, lunghimawh niloh ka hi hiam? Pasian sungah lametna nei ning; bang hang hiam cih leh kei a hong huh ka Pasian ka phatkik ngawn ding hi.
English: Why art thou cast down, O my soul? And why art thou disquieted within me? Hope in God: For I shall yet praise him, Who is the health of my countenance, and my God.

## Chapter 44

**44:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, ka pu ka pate uh a khan lai-a na hihnasate, amaute in kote tungah hong gen uh a, kote in ka bil uh tawh ka za khin uh hi.
English: We have heard with our ears, O God, our fathers have told us, What work thou didst in their days, in the times of old.

**44:2**
Zolai: Nangmah in minam dangte na hawlkhia mang a, ahih hangin amau’ munah ka pu ka pate uh na tengsak hi. Midangte na sugawp a, ahih hangin amaute na suaktasak hi.
English: How thou didst drive out the heathen with thy hand, and plantedst them; How thou didst afflict the people, and cast them out.

**44:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in namsau tawh leitang ngah lo uh a, amau’ khut in amaute’ tungah gualzawhna pia lo hi. Na khut taklam le na baan, na hehpihna maipha hizaw hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute tungah nang na lungkim hi.
English: For they got not the land in possession by their own sword, Neither did their own arm save them: But thy right hand, and thine arm, and the light of thy countenance, Because thou hadst a favour unto them.

**44:4**
Zolai: Nang pen Jakob a dingin gualzawhna a sehkhol, keima Kumpipa le keima Pasian na hi hi.
English: Thou art my King, O God: Command deliverances for Jacob.

**44:5**
Zolai: Nangma huhna tawh ka galte uh ka sawnpai uh a, ko a hong do mite na min suangin ka tuancil uh hi.
English: Through thee will we push down our enemies: Through thy name will we tread them under that rise up against us.

**44:6**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih ka thalpi suanin ka nei kei a, ka namsau in zong kei hong hon zo lo hi.
English: For I will not trust in my bow, Neither shall my sword save me.

**44:7**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nangmah in ka galte’ kiang panun kote na hong hon a, ko a hong mudahte na zahhuai gawpsak khin hi.
English: But thou hast saved us from our enemies, And hast put them to shame that hated us.

**44:8**
Zolai: Pasian’ hangin kote ka angtang ngitnget uh a, nangma tungah ka lungdam tawntung ding uh hi.
English: In God we boast all the day long, And praise thy name for ever. Selah.

**44:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nangmah in kote hong nusia-in, nong minsiasak khin a, ka galkap hon uh tawh na hong kuankhawm kei hi.
English: But thou hast cast off, and put us to shame; And goest not forth with our armies.

**44:10**
Zolai: Galte kiang panin kote nong nungkiksak a, ka galte un ka neihsa teng uh buluah khin uh hi.
English: Thou makest us to turn back from the enemy: And they which hate us spoil for themselves.

**44:11**
Zolai: Tuu gawh ding bangin kote na hong bawl a, minam dangte lakah nong thehthang khin hi.
English: Thou hast given us like sheep appointed for meat; And hast scattered us among the heathen.

**44:12**
Zolai: Na mite a man tawmno khatin na hong zuak a, a man ding na sang nget kei hi.
English: Thou sellest thy people for nought, And dost not increase thy wealth by their price.

**44:13**
Zolai: Ka vengte uh’ zahko, ka kiim uha omte’ nuihsat leh thusim lohin kote na hong bawl khin hi.
English: Thou makest us a reproach to our neighbours, A scorn and a derision to them that are round about us.

**44:14**
Zolai: Minam dangte lakah a sia lama gentehna, mite lakah ciamnuih-a neihin kote na hong bawl khin hi.
English: Thou makest us a byword among the heathen, A shaking of the head among the people.

**44:15**
Zolai: Keimah a hong ko mi le keimah a hong minsiasak mite’ kampauna ahi a, galte le langte in hong bawlna hang ahi zongin, sunthapai-in ka zahhuai den a, maizumna tawh ka kidim hi.
English: My confusion is continually before me, And the shame of my face hath covered me,

**44:17**
Zolai: Na thuciamna-ah khial lo napi, nang hong mangngilh lo napi, hih thute khempeuh ko tungah hong tung khin hi.
English: All this is come upon us; yet have we not forgotten thee, Neither have we dealt falsely in thy covenant.

**44:18**
Zolai: Ngiate’ omna-ah kote hong balnen gawpin, khuamialpi sungah nong paihdak ding zahin, ka lungsim uh kihei nai lo a, ka kalsuan uh lampial nai lo hi.
English: Our heart is not turned back, Neither have our steps declined from thy way;

**44:20**
Zolai: Ka Pasian uh mangngilh khinin pasian dang tungah ka khutte uh a khakkhin hi le ung,
English: If we have forgotten the name of our God, or stretched out our hands to a strange god;

**44:21**
Zolai: Pasian in hih thu mukhia lo ding ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in lungsim thusim a thei hi.
English: Shall not God search this out? For he knoweth the secrets of the heart.

**44:22**
Zolai: Nangma hangin sunthapai-in kote hong kithat a, gan gote’ tuu gawh ding bangin kote hong kikoih hi.
English: Yea, for thy sake are we killed all the day long; We are counted as sheep for the slaughter.

**44:23**
Zolai: Topa aw, bang hangin ihmu na hi hiam? Nangmah hong tho tawm in!
English: Awake, why sleepest thou, O Lord? Arise, cast us not off for ever.

**44:24**
Zolai: Bang hangin na maitang seel na hi hiam? Bang hangin ka thuakna uh le hong kisukcipnate mangngilh na hi hiam?
English: Wherefore hidest thou thy face, And forgettest our affliction and our oppression?

**44:25**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh leilakah ka puk uh a, leivui lakah guallelin ka lum uh hi.
English: For our soul is bowed down to the dust: Our belly cleaveth unto the earth.

**44:26**
Zolai: Tho to in, kote a hong huh dingin hong pai in! Na itna kip hangin kote hong honkhia in!
English: Arise for our help, And redeem us for thy mercies' sake.

## Chapter 45

**45:1**
Zolai: Thubul hoih khat tawh ka lungsim hong dimletin, kumpipa la ka phuah a, ka leii pen laithei pa’ laikung tawh hong kibang hi.
English: My heart is inditing a good matter: I speak of the things which I have made touching the king: My tongue is The pen of a ready writer.

**45:2**
Zolai: Mihingte lakah nangmah na hoihpen a, thugen na siam a, na kam khum zungzung hi. Tua ahih manin Pasian in nang thupha hong pia tawntung hi.
English: Thou art fairer than the children of men: Grace is poured into thy lips: Therefore God hath blessed thee for ever.

**45:3**
Zolai: Vanglian kumpipa aw, na minthanna le na liatna tawh na namsau kuah in.
English: Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O most mighty, With thy glory and thy majesty.

**45:4**
Zolai: Thumanna a omna ding le thuman a hu dingin na minliatna tawh gualzo-in hong pusuak inla, dipkuathuai hihnate na taklam khut nangmah kihilhsak in.
English: And in thy majesty ride prosperously Because of truth and meekness and righteousness; And thy right hand shall teach thee terrible things.

**45:5**
Zolai: Kumpipa’ galte’ lungtangah na thaltang hiamte lut a, mite na nuai-ah puk uh hi.
English: Thine arrows are sharp in the heart of the king's enemies; Whereby the people fall under thee.

**45:6**
Zolai: Na kumpi tokhom siangtho kip tawntung hi. Na kumpi ciangkhut thumanna ciangkhut hi a,
English: Thy throne, O God, is for ever and ever: The sceptre of thy kingdom is a right sceptre.

**45:7**
Zolai: thuman deihin gitlohna na mudah hi. Tua ahih ciangin Pasian ahi, nangma Pasian in na khangualte tungah a kikhai to-in lungdamna sathau nang hong nilhzo a,
English: Thou lovest righteousness, and hatest wickedness: Therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of gladness above thy fellows.

**45:8**
Zolai: na puantualpite myrrh paknamtui, aloes paknamtui, le thalsing namtuite a nam hi. Saiha tawh kibawl innpite panin khausai lasaknate in nang hong lungdamsak a,
English: All thy garments smell of myrrh, and aloes, and cassia, Out of the ivory palaces, whereby they have made thee glad.

**45:9**
Zolai: kumpite’ tanute, numei uliante lakah om a, na taklamah Ofir gam khamte tawh kizemin kumpinu a ding hi.
English: Kings' daughters were among thy honourable women: Upon thy right hand did stand the queen in gold of Ophir.

**45:10**
Zolai: Tanu aw, ngai dih in; ngaihsun inla, na bil hong ngat in. Na mite le na behte mangngilh in.
English: Hearken, O daughter, and consider, and incline thine ear; Forget also thine own people, and thy father's house;

**45:11**
Zolai: Na melhoihna hangin kumpipa in hong deih ding hi. Na topa ahih ciangin ama mai-ah kun in.
English: So shall the king greatly desire thy beauty: For he is thy Lord; and worship thou him.

**45:12**
Zolai: Mi haupen ahi Taia mite in na manpha namkim letsong tawh nang hong maivil ding uh hi.
English: And the daughter of Tyre shall be there with a gift; Even the rich among the people shall intreat thy favour.

**45:13**
Zolai: Kumpi tanu a inndei sungah kham puantualpi tawh kizem a, mel tuamtuam a nei puantualpite silh a, mihon kigual deudaute lakah a kithuahpih nungakte le amah a khate tawh kumpipa kiangah kipaipih hi.
English: The king's daughter is all glorious within: Her clothing is of wrought gold.

**45:15**
Zolai: Kumpipa’ inn-ah a tun ciangun lungdamna le nuamna tawh amaute kitumpih hi.
English: With gladness and rejoicing shall they be brought: They shall enter into the king's palace.

**45:16**
Zolai: Na pate’ tang ding na tapate hong hi ding a, nangmah in leitung khempeuhah amaute, ulian na suaksak ding hi.
English: Instead of thy fathers shall be thy children, Whom thou mayest make princes in all the earth.

**45:17**
Zolai: Keimah in khang tawntungin na min ka kiphawksak ding hi. Tua ahih ciangin mite in nang hong phat den ding uh hi.
English: I will make thy name to be remembered in all generations: Therefore shall the people praise thee for ever and ever.

## Chapter 46

**46:1**
Zolai: Pasian, i belh leh i thahatna hi a, haksat hunin a hong huh pahpah pa ahi hi.
English: God is our refuge and strength, A very present help in trouble.

**46:2**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin, leitung kikhinin, mualte tuipi sung a kidenna zongin, a tuite ging zuazua-in phuan zuazua a, hih ginna hangin mual liante a ling zongin, i lau kei ding hi.
English: Therefore will not we fear, though the earth be removed, And though the mountains be carried into the midst of the sea;

**46:4**
Zolai: Sangpenpa’ tenna khua siangtho, Pasian’ khuapi, a lungdamsak gun khat a om hi.
English: There is a river, the streams whereof shall make glad the city of God, The holy place of the tabernacles of the most High.

**46:5**
Zolai: Ama laizangah Pasian om a, amah a kiling kei ding hi. Pasian in phalvak tungin amah huh ding hi.
English: God is in the midst of her; she shall not be moved: God shall help her, and that right early.

**46:6**
Zolai: Minamte lungkham uh a, kumpi gamte kiling hi. Ama aw gingkhiasak a, leitung kicimgawp hi.
English: The heathen raged, the kingdoms were moved: He uttered his voice, the earth melted.

**46:7**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa eite tawh hong omkhawm a, Jakob Pasian eima belh ahi hi.
English: The LORD of hosts is with us; The God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah.

**46:8**
Zolai: Hong pai unla, Topa’ sepna hong mu un. Leitung khempeuh gamkhing a suahsak khitna hong en un.
English: Come, behold the works of the LORD , What desolations he hath made in the earth.

**46:9**
Zolai: Amah in leimong dongah gal beisak hi. Amah in thalpi kuaitanin teipi susia a, leengte mei tawh a haltum hi.
English: He maketh wars to cease unto the end of the earth; He breaketh the bow, and cutteth the spear in sunder; He burneth the chariot in the fire.

**46:10**
Zolai: “Om hithiat unla, Pasian ka hihna thei un. Minamte lakah keimah hong kisangsak a, leitung khempeuhah ka min hong kithangsak hi,” a ci hi.
English: Be still, and know that I am God: I will be exalted among the heathen, I will be exalted in the earth.

**46:11**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa, eite tawh hong omkhawm a, Jakob’ Pasian, eima belh ahi hi.
English: The LORD of hosts is with us; The God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah.

## Chapter 47

**47:1**
Zolai: Mi khempeuh aw, na khut uh beeng un! Lungdamna la nakpi-in sa-in Pasian phat un.
English: O clap your hands, all ye people; Shout unto God with the voice of triumph.

**47:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa, a Sangpenpa, dipkuathuai a, leitung khempeuh a uk kumpi lian khat ahi hi.
English: For the LORD most high is terrible; He is a great King over all the earth.

**47:3**
Zolai: Mi khempeuh eima nuai-ah, minamte i khenuai-ah amah in hong zawhsak hi.
English: He shall subdue the people under us, And the nations under our feet.

**47:4**
Zolai: Ama it Israel-te’ angtanpih eima luah ding leitang amah in hong teelsak hi.
English: He shall choose our inheritance for us, The excellency of Jacob whom he loved. Selah.

**47:5**
Zolai: Awging tawh Pasian paito a, peengkul aw tawh Topa paito hi.
English: God is gone up with a shout, The LORD with the sound of a trumpet.

**47:6**
Zolai: Pasian tungah phatna la sa un, phatna la sa un! I Kumpipa tungah phatna la sa un, phatna la sa un!
English: Sing praises to God, sing praises: Sing praises unto our King, sing praises.

**47:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Pasian pen leitung khempeuhte’ kumpi ahi hi. La sakna tawh amah phat un!
English: For God is the King of all the earth: Sing ye praises with understanding.

**47:8**
Zolai: Pasian in minamte uk a, a tokhom siangtho tungah Pasian tu hi.
English: God reigneth over the heathen: God sitteth upon the throne of his holiness.

**47:9**
Zolai: Uliante le Abraham’ Pasian’ mite kipawl khawm uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh leitung mite’ lumte khempeuh Pasian-a’ suak khinta a, amah a sangpi-in kithangsak hi.
English: The princes of the people are gathered together, even the people of the God of Abraham: For the shields of the earth belong unto God: He is greatly exalted.

## Chapter 48

**48:1**
Zolai: Topa lian a, i Pasian’ khuapi sungah nakpitakin phat ding ahi hi.
English: Great is the LORD , and greatly to be praised In the city of our God, in the mountain of his holiness.

**48:2**
Zolai: Kumpi lianpa’ khuapi, leilu lama a om ama mual siangtho hoihin a sang mahmah Zion mual pen leitung khempeuh’ lungdamna ahi hi.
English: Beautiful for situation, the joy of the whole earth, Is mount Zion, on the sides of the north, The city of the great King.

**48:3**
Zolai: A muanhuai tua mualah amah a hu taktakpa ahihna Pasian in a lakkhin hi.
English: God is known in her palaces for a refuge.

**48:4**
Zolai: Ahi zongin, kumpite kikaikhawmin, a sim dingin hong kuankhawm uh hi.
English: For, lo, the kings were assembled, They passed by together.

**48:5**
Zolai: Amaute in Zion a muh phetun lamdangsa mahmah uh a, dipkua vatin tai uh hi.
English: They saw it, and so they marvelled; They were troubled, and hasted away.

**48:6**
Zolai: Numei nausuak na a sa bangin amaute linggawp uh hi.
English: Fear took hold upon them there, And pain, as of a woman in travail.

**48:7**
Zolai: Nisuahna huihpi tawh Tarshish kici teembaw liante nang na susia hi.
English: Thou breakest the ships of Tarshish With an east wind.

**48:8**
Zolai: Ka zaksa bangun Vanglian Topa’ khuapi, i Pasian’ khuapi, Pasian in a phuhkip ngitngetna ka mu khin uh hi.
English: As we have heard, so have we seen in the city of the LORD of hosts, in the city of our God: God will establish it for ever. Selah.

**48:9**
Zolai: Pasian aw, na biakinn sungah nangma itna kip ka ngaihsun uh hi.
English: We have thought of thy lovingkindness, O God, In the midst of thy temple.

**48:10**
Zolai: Pasian aw, na min in leimong dong a zelh bangin, nangmah hong kiphatna in zong a zel hi. Na taklam khut gualzawhna tawh a kidim hi.
English: According to thy name, O God, so is thy praise unto the ends of the earth: Thy right hand is full of righteousness.

**48:11**
Zolai: Zion Mual lungdamsak in. Na thukhenna hangin Judah mite lungdamsak in.
English: Let mount Zion rejoice, Let the daughters of Judah be glad, because of thy judgments.

**48:12**
Zolai: Hih pen eima Pasian hi a, a tawntungin eima Pasian hi, ci-in khangkikte tungah na gen theih nadingun Zion kiimvelin pai-in, a tausang phazah sim unla, a kulh phungmai a hoih mahmahte ngaihsunin, a phualpi muanhuaite va nawk kim un. Amah pen a tawntungin lam hong lak ding pa ahi hi.
English: Walk about Zion, and go round about her: Tell the towers thereof.

## Chapter 49

**49:1**
Zolai: Hih thu za un, mi khempeuh aw! Ngai un, leitung a a teng khempeuh,
English: Hear this, all ye people; Give ear, all ye inhabitants of the world:

**49:2**
Zolai: milian mineu, mihau mizawngte aw!
English: Both low and high, Rich and poor, together.

**49:3**
Zolai: Ka kam in pilna thu gen ding a, ka lungsim ngaihsutna kitelsiang ding hi.
English: My mouth shall speak of wisdom; And the meditation of my heart shall be of understanding.

**49:4**
Zolai: Paunak thu theihhak khat ka ngaihsun ding a, laiza lasakna tawh a khiatna ka gentel ding hi.
English: I will incline mine ear to a parable: I will open my dark saying upon the harp.

**49:5**
Zolai: Haksat hun, hong bawlsiate’ gitlohna in hong nencip ciangin bang hangin lau ding ka hi hiam?
English: Wherefore should I fear in the days of evil, When the iniquity of my heels shall compass me about?

**49:6**
Zolai: Mite in a hauhna uh muangin, tampi a neihna uh a kisaktheihpih hangun,
English: They that trust in their wealth, And boast themselves in the multitude of their riches;

**49:7**
Zolai: amah le amah a kitankhia tawmzo taktak, a nuntakna man ding Pasian’ tungah a piazo mi kuamah om lo hi.
English: None of them can by any means redeem his brother, Nor give to God a ransom for him:

**49:8**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh a nuntakna tatna ding a man tam mahmah a, Leihawmpi mu ngei lo zah ding a hing tawntung dingin kitankhiazo ngei lo hi.
English: (For the redemption of their soul is precious, And it ceaseth for ever:)

**49:10**
Zolai: Amah in a pilte nangawn a si mu ding a, a haite le a tei lote a kibangin sia-in, amau’ neihsa khempeuh midangte’ tungah nusiat uh hi.
English: For he seeth that wise men die, Likewise the fool and the brutish person perish, and leave their wealth to others.

**49:11**
Zolai: Amaute in leitangte amau’ min a puaksak uh hangin hankhuk pen khang tawntung amau’ omna hi ngitnget ding hi.
English: Their inward thought is, that their houses shall continue for ever, And their dwelling places to all generations; They call their lands after their own names.

**49:12**
Zolai: Ama hauhna-ah mi kipsuak thei lo a, a sithei ganhingte tawh a kibang lel ahi hi.
English: Nevertheless man being in honour abideth not: He is like the beasts that perish.

**49:13**
