**72:10**
Zolai: Tarshish kumpite le tuikulh neu-a kumpite in ama tungah siah pia uh hen la, Sheba le Seba kumpite in letsong puak ta uh hen.
English: The kings of Tarshish and of the isles shall bring presents: The kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.

**72:11**
Zolai: Kumpi khempeuh ama mai-ah bok uh hen la, minam khempeuh in ama na sem ta uh hen.
English: Yea, all kings shall fall down before him: All nations shall serve him.

**72:12**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh mi cimawhte in a koh ciangin amah in honkhia a, mizawng, a huh ding a om lote amah in a honkhia hi.
English: For he shall deliver the needy when he crieth; The poor also, and him that hath no helper.

**72:13**
Zolai: A thakiam, a cimawh mite amah in hehpih a, mi cimawhte’ nuntakna amah in a honkhia hi.
English: He shall spare the poor and needy, And shall save the souls of the needy.

**72:14**
Zolai: Amah in amaute pammaihsa ahih manin netniamna le ngong hihna panin amaute a honkhia hi.
English: He shall redeem their soul from deceit and violence: And precious shall their blood be in his sight.

**72:15**
Zolai: Amah a khansau hen la, Sheba gam a khamte ama tungah kipia tahen. Ama a dingin thu kingetsak tawntung hen la, sunthapai-in ama a dingin thupha kingetsak tahen.
English: And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Sheba: Prayer also shall be made for him continually; and daily shall he be praised.

**72:16**
Zolai: Gam sung khempeuhah an tampi tak piang hen la, mual liante dawnah dim mema-in Lebanon gam hoih sung bang ta hen la, gamlak a lopate bangin khuapite sunga om mite pung ta uh hen.
English: There shall be an handful of corn in the earth upon the top of the mountains; The fruit thereof shall shake like Lebanon: And they of the city shall flourish like grass of the earth.

**72:17**
Zolai: Ama min kip tawntung hen la, a minthanna kip paisuak hen. Ama hangin mite in thupha ngah hen la, minam khempeuh in amah pen thupha ngah pa, ci ta uh hen.
English: His name shall endure for ever: His name shall be continued as long as the sun: And men shall be blessed in him: All nations shall call him blessed.

**72:18**
Zolai: Na lamdangte a bawl amah bek ahi Israel Pasian, Topa in thupha ngah tahen.
English: Blessed be the LORD God, the God of Israel, Who only doeth wondrous things.

**72:19**
Zolai: A minthang ama min in thupha ngah tawntung hen la, ama minthanna tawh leitung khempeuh kidim tahen. Amen! Amen!
English: And blessed be his glorious name for ever: And let the whole earth be filled with his glory; Amen, and Amen.

**72:20**
Zolai: Jessi’ tapa David’ thungetnate a beita ahi hi.
English: The prayers of David the son of Jesse are ended.

## Chapter 73

**73:1**
Zolai: Israel mite bangin a lungsim a siangtho a thutang mite tungah Pasian hoih takpi hi.
English: Truly God is good to Israel, Even to such as are of a clean heart.

**73:2**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei ka hih leh ka khe kisuipuk dektak a, ka khe taal dektak hi.
English: But as for me, my feet were almost gone; My steps had well nigh slipped.

**73:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh migilote’ daupaina ka muh ciangin mi kihisakte ka eng hi.
English: For I was envious at the foolish, When I saw the prosperity of the wicked.

**73:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in nat velvalna bangmah thuak lo uh a, a pumpi uh cidamin zol hilhial hi.
English: For there are no bands in their death: But their strength is firm.

**73:5**
Zolai: Amaute in midangte bangin haksatna thuak lo uh a, amaute in midangte bangin gimna ngah lo uh hi.
English: They are not in trouble as other men; Neither are they plagued like other men.

**73:6**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in khainiang bangin kiphatsakna ok uh a, puan bangin ngongtatna silh uh hi.
English: Therefore pride compasseth them about as a chain; Violence covereth them as a garment.

**73:7**
Zolai: A lungsim panun gitlohna pusuaksak uh a, a ngaihsutna uh gitlohna tawh a dimlet hi.
English: Their eyes stand out with fatness: They have more than heart could wish.

**73:8**
Zolai: Amaute in mi thusim loin el pau uh a, kiliatsakna tawh a sucip dingin mi a tawng uh hi.
English: They are corrupt, and speak wickedly concerning oppression: They speak loftily.

**73:9**
Zolai: Amaute’ gensiatna in vantung dong banto a, kiliatsakna tawh leitungah thu gen kawikawi uh hi.
English: They set their mouth against the heavens, And their tongue walketh through the earth.

**73:10**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin mite in amaute phat uh a, amau’ mawhna zong lo uh hi.
English: Therefore his people return hither: And waters of a full cup are wrung out to them.

**73:11**
Zolai: Amaute in, “Pasian in bangci theih ding ahi hiam? Sangpenpa in phawk ding ahi hiam?” ci uh hi.
English: And they say, How doth God know? And is there knowledge in the most High?

**73:12**
Zolai: Amaute migilo ahi uh hi. A tawntungin nuamtakin om hithiat uh a, amaute a hauhna uh khang semsem zaw lai hi.
English: Behold, these are the ungodly, who prosper in the world; they increase in riches.

**73:13**
Zolai: Ka lungsim siangsak a, mawhna ka bawl loh hangin a phattuamna om tuan lo hi.
English: Verily I have cleansed my heart in vain, and washed my hands in innocency.

**73:14**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh sunthapai-in gimna ka thuak a, zingsang simin hong kithuhilh hi.
English: For all the day long have I been plagued, And chastened every morning.

**73:15**
Zolai: Tu-a bangin thu a gen hi leng, nangma mite tungah a thutak lo ka suak ding hi.
English: If I say, I will speak thus; Behold, I should offend against the generation of thy children.

**73:16**
Zolai: Ahih hangin hih thu a bangci hiam, ci-in ka ngaihsut ciangin kei a dingin a lunggimhuai mahmah nasep khat hong suak a,
English: When I thought to know this, It was too painful for me;

**73:17**
Zolai: Pasian’ biakinn sungah ka pai ciangin a thutawpna dongte ka tel hi.
English: Until I went into the sanctuary of God; Then understood I their end.

**73:18**
Zolai: Nangmah in amaute mun nalna-ah na koih takpi ding a, a sia dingin amaute na tuksak ding hi.
English: Surely thou didst set them in slippery places: Thou castedst them down into destruction.

**73:19**
Zolai: Tomno sungin amaute kisusia-in, lau mahmahna in amaute nilkhiamang ding hi.
English: How are they brought into desolation, as in a moment! They are utterly consumed with terrors.

**73:20**
Zolai: Amaute pen zan a mangmat tawh kibang lel a, na khanlawh ciangin amaute a bangci pian hiam, ci-in na phawk nawn kei hi.
English: As a dream when one awaketh; So , O Lord, when thou awakest, thou shalt despise their image.

**73:21**
Zolai: Ka lung khamin ka lungsim hong nat ciangin,
English: Thus my heart was grieved, And I was pricked in my reins.

**73:22**
Zolai: keimah hai-in bangmah ka thei kei a, nangma mai-ah ganhing tawh ka kibang hi.
English: So foolish was I, and ignorant: I was as a beast before thee.

**73:23**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nangmah tawh ka omkhawm ngitnget a, ka khut taklamin kei na hong len hi.
English: Nevertheless I am continually with thee: Thou hast holden me by my right hand.

**73:24**
Zolai: Thulahna tawh keimah nong makaih a, a nung ciangin minthanna munah na hong tunpih ding hi.
English: Thou shalt guide me with thy counsel, And afterward receive me to glory.

**73:25**
Zolai: Nang simloh vantungah kua nei ka hi hiam? Nang simloh ka deih ding leitungah kuamah om lo hi.
English: Whom have I in heaven but thee? And there is none upon earth that I desire beside thee.

**73:26**
Zolai: Ka lungsim le ka pumpi zawngkhal kha ding a, ahih hangin Pasian pen ka lungsim hatna le keima a’ hi tawntung ding hi.
English: My flesh and my heart faileth: But God is the strength of my heart, and my portion for ever.

**73:27**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nang tawh a kigamlate kisia ding uh a, nangma tungah a hong khialte na beisak ding hi.
English: For, lo, they that are far from thee shall perish: Thou hast destroyed all them that go a whoring from thee.

**73:28**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei a dingin Pasian’ kiangah om ding a hoih ahi hi. Na sepnate khempeuh ka gentheih nadingin Topa Pasian ka hong bel hi.
English: But it is good for me to draw near to God: I have put my trust in the Lord GOD , That I may declare all thy works.

## Chapter 74

**74:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, bang hangin kote hong paaikhia paisuak na hi hiam? Bang hangin na gam sunga om nangma tuute tungah heh na hi hiam?
English: O God, why hast thou cast us off for ever? Why doth thine anger smoke against the sheep of thy pasture?

**74:2**
Zolai: Tanglai-in na ngahsa na mihonte, nangma luah minam dingin na tatkhiatsate phawk in! Na tennasa Zion Mual hong phawk in.
English: Remember thy congregation, which thou hast purchased of old; The rod of thine inheritance, which thou hast redeemed; This mount Zion, wherein thou hast dwelt.

**74:3**
Zolai: A sia densa munah hong pai in. Na biakinn sunga om khempeuh galte in susia khinta hi.
English: Lift up thy feet unto the perpetual desolations; Even all that the enemy hath done wickedly in the sanctuary.

**74:4**
Zolai: Nangma galte mun siangtho laizangah awng uh a, amau’ dialte gualzawhna lim dingin a khai uh hi.
English: Thine enemies roar in the midst of thy congregations; They set up their ensigns for signs.

**74:5**
Zolai: Amaute pen tulak sing phatna-ah pai-in heipi tawh sing a phuk bang uh hi.
English: A man was famous according as he had lifted up axes upon the thick trees.

**74:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin biakinn na a kizemte khempeuh sek-hei le sekpi tawh a satkham uh hi.
English: But now they break down the carved work Thereof at once with axes and hammers.

**74:7**
Zolai: Amaute in mei tawh na biakinn hal uh a, nangmah hong kibiakna mun a susia uh hi.
English: They have cast fire into thy sanctuary, They have defiled by casting down the dwelling place of thy name to the ground.

**74:8**
Zolai: Amaute in, “A vekpi-in zo mang khin ni,” kici uh a, gam sung tenga om Pasian biakna inn khempeuh mei tawh a hal uh hi.
English: They said in their hearts, Let us destroy them together: They have burned up all the synagogues of God in the land.

**74:9**
Zolai: Kote in ka mailam thu ding uh ka thei kei uh hi. Kamsang khat zong om nawn lo a, bang tanvei hi ding, ci-in a thei kuamah ka om kei uh hi.
English: We see not our signs: There is no more any prophet: Neither is there among us any that knoweth how long.

**74:10**
Zolai: Pasian aw, ka galte in bang tanvei hong thusim loin om ding ahi hiam? Langpangte in nangma min hong simmawh den ding ahi uh hiam?
English: O God, how long shall the adversary reproach? Shall the enemy blaspheme thy name for ever?

**74:11**
Zolai: Bang hangin na khut dokkik a, na khut taklam na ang-ah koihcip na hi hiam?
English: Why withdrawest thou thy hand, even thy right hand? Pluck it out of thy bosom.

**74:12**
Zolai: Ahi zongin Pasian pen tanglai pek a kipanin kumpi hi tawntung a, hih leitungah a hong honkhia zelzel ngei ka Kumpi ahi hi.
English: For God is my King of old, Working salvation in the midst of the earth.

**74:13**
Zolai: Na vangliatna tawh tuipi na khenkham a, tuite tunga gulpite’ lutangte na sukham hi.
English: Thou didst divide the sea by thy strength: Thou brakest the heads of the dragons in the waters.

**74:14**
Zolai: Nangmah in Awle’ lutangte na sukham a, amah pen, gamlak ganhingte’ nek dingin na pia hi.
English: Thou brakest the heads of leviathan in pieces, And gavest him to be meat to the people inhabiting the wilderness.

**74:15**
Zolai: Ciktuite le luite na phulsak a, guntui luangte na kangsak hi.
English: Thou didst cleave the fountain and the flood: Thou driedst up mighty rivers.

**74:16**
Zolai: Sun pen nangma a’ hi a, zan zong nangma a’ mah ahi hi. Nangmah in ni le kha na bawl hi.
English: The day is thine, the night also is thine: Thou hast prepared the light and the sun.

**74:17**
Zolai: Leitung gamgi khempeuhte le phalbi hun le khuakhal hunte na bawl khin hi.
English: Thou hast set all the borders of the earth: Thou hast made summer and winter.

**74:18**
Zolai: Topa aw, galte in nang hong thusim lohna le, dawibia mite in nangma min a hong simmawhna hong phawk ta in.
English: Remember this, that the enemy hath reproached, O LORD , And that the foolish people have blasphemed thy name.

**74:19**
Zolai: A cimawh mite a gal gilote uh khut sungah nusia kei inla, bawlsiatna a thuak mite mangngilh kei in.
English: O deliver not the soul of thy turtledove unto the multitude of the wicked: Forget not the congregation of thy poor for ever.

**74:20**
Zolai: Nangma thuciamna hong pi ngaihsut in; bang hang hiam cih leh leitung mun mialna khempeuh mi ngongtatte tawh kidim hi.
English: Have respect unto the covenant: For the dark places of the earth are full of the habitations of cruelty.

**74:21**
Zolai: A kisikcip mite zahhuaisak kei inla, mizawng le mi cimawhte nangma min kiphatsak in.
English: O let not the oppressed return ashamed: Let the poor and needy praise thy name.

**74:22**
Zolai: Pasian aw, tho inla, nangma thu-ah hong pang in. Dawibia mite in sun tawntungin nang a hong thusim lohna hong phawk ta in!
English: Arise, O God, plead thine own cause: Remember how the foolish man reproacheth thee daily.

**74:23**
Zolai: Nangma galte’ kikona aw, nang a hong langpangte a gamlum semsemna mangngilh kei ta in.
English: Forget not the voice of thine enemies: The tumult of those that rise up against thee increaseth continually.

## Chapter 75

**75:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, nangma tungah ka lungdam mahmah uh a, nangma tungah ka nuam mahmah uh hi. Nangma liatna thu ka gen uh a, a lamdang na bawlnate ka sut kikkik uh hi.
English: Unto thee, O God, do we give thanks, Unto thee do we give thanks: For that thy name is near Thy wondrous works declare.

**75:2**
Zolai: A hun ka sehsa ni ciangin thu a manin ka khen ding hi.
English: When I shall receive the congregation I will judge uprightly.

**75:3**
Zolai: Leitung le a tunga tengte khempeuh a kilin’ ciangin a khuampite a kipsak pa keimah ka hi hi.
English: The earth and all the inhabitants thereof are dissolved: I bear up the pillars of it. Selah.

**75:4**
Zolai: A kiphasakte tungah, “Kiphasak kei un,” a gilote tungah, “Kihisak kei un.
English: I said unto the fools, Deal not foolishly: And to the wicked, Lift not up the horn:

**75:5**
Zolai: Kihisak kei unla, kiphatsakna tawh kampau kei un,” ka ci hi.
English: Lift not up your horn on high: Speak not with a stiff neck.

**75:6**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh vangliatna pen nisuahna lam ahi a, nitumna lam ahi a, gamlak pan ahi zongin a hong pai hi lo hi.
English: For promotion cometh neither from the east, nor from the west, Nor from the south.

**75:7**
Zolai: Mihing khat a sangsak, mihing khat a niamsak thukhen pa pen Pasian ahi hi.
English: But God is the judge: He putteth down one, and setteth up another.

**75:8**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa’ khut sungah leenggahzu a phuan, a kihelkim ngingei hai khat om a, amah in tua sung panin hong bungkhia ding a, leitung migilo khempeuh in a tawdat dong takin a liaktum ding uh hi.
English: For in the hand of the LORD there is a cup, and the wine is red; It is full of mixture; and he poureth out of the same: But the dregs thereof, All the wicked of the earth shall wring them out, and drink them .

**75:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei ahihleh ka lungdam ngitnget ding a, Jakob Pasian’ tungah phatna late ka sa ding hi.
English: But I will declare for ever; I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.

**75:10**
Zolai: Migilote’ vangliatna khempeuh amah in susia ding a, ahih hangin thuman mite’ vangliatna khang semsem ding hi.
English: All the horns of the wicked also will I cut off; But the horns of the righteous shall be exalted.

## Chapter 76

**76:1**
Zolai: Judah gam sungah Pasian kithei a, Israel gam sungah ama min lian hi.
English: In Judah is God known: His name is great in Israel.

**76:2**
Zolai: Zion khua sungah ama tenna mun kibawl hi.
English: In Salem also is his tabernacle, And his dwelling place in Zion.

**76:3**
Zolai: Amah in tua lai-ah thaltangte, lum, namsau, le galhiamte a kuaitan hi.
English: There brake he the arrows of the bow, The shield, and the sword, and the battle. Selah.

**76:4**
Zolai: A om ngitnget mual liante sangin na min thangzaw a, na lianzaw hi.
English: Thou art more glorious and excellent Than the mountains of prey.

**76:5**
Zolai: A thahatte’ neihsa nate kisutkhia a, amaute ihmucip suak uh hi.
English: The stouthearted are spoiled, they have slept their sleep: And none of the men of might have found their hands.

**76:6**
Zolai: Jakob’ Pasian aw, nangma thuhilhna hangin sakol le a tung tuang pa khawlcip uh hi.
English: At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, Both the chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep.

**76:7**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nang na kihtakhuai mahmah hi. Na heh khit phot ciangin nangma mai-ah kua ding ngam nawn ding ahi hiam?
English: Thou, even thou, art to be feared: And who may stand in thy sight when once thou art angry?

**76:8**
Zolai: Vantung panin thukhenna na genkhia hi. Gimna a thuak leitung mi khempeuh a hon dingin thukhen dingin Pasian a kipat ciangin leitung lau mahmahin tang hetloin a om khikhe hi.
English: Thou didst cause judgment to be heard from heaven; The earth feared, and was still,

**76:10**
Zolai: Mihingte’ hehna in nang hong kiphatna ding piangsak ding a, na hehna panin a suakta mite in nangmah pahtawina pawi a bawl ding uh hi.
English: Surely the wrath of man shall praise thee: The remainder of wrath shalt thou restrain.

**76:11**
Zolai: Topa na Pasian’ tungah na thuciamnate uh pia unla, tuate khempeuh zui un. Leitung kumpite sangin a kihtakhuai zaw, uliante’ lungsim a niamkhiat, zahtak ding ahipa’ tungah, ama kiimah a om mi khempeuhte in letsong puak ta uh hen!
English: Vow, and pay unto the LORD your God: Let all that be round about him Bring presents unto him that ought to be feared.

## Chapter 77

**77:1**
Zolai: Pasian’ tungah a gingin ka kiko khia a, a hong zaktheih nadingin a gingin ka kiko hi.
English: I Cried unto God with my voice, Even unto God with my voice; and he gave ear unto me.

**77:2**
Zolai: Ka lungkham hunin keimah in Topa ka zong hi. Zanin thu ngenin gim hetloin ka khut ka zan a, ahi zongin hehnepna ka ngah kei hi.
English: In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord: My sore ran in the night, and ceased not: My soul refused to be comforted.

**77:3**
Zolai: Keimah in Pasian ka ngaihsun a, ka tautau hi. Lung ka geelgeel a, ka gim mahmah hi.
English: I remembered God, and was troubled: I complained, and my spirit was overwhelmed. Selah.

**77:4**
Zolai: A ihmu lo dingin kei na hong bawl a, lungkham lua-in ka pau thei kei hi.
English: Thou holdest mine eyes waking: I am so troubled that I cannot speak.

**77:5**
Zolai: Hun luite ka ngaihsun a, sawtpek lai-a kumte ka phawk hi.
English: I have considered the days of old, The years of ancient times.

**77:6**
Zolai: Zanthapai-in ka lungsimah ka kihoho a, lung geelgeelin thu ka kan ciangin:
English: I call to remembrance my song in the night: I commune with mine own heart: And my spirit made diligent search.

**77:7**
Zolai: “Topa in hong nial paisuakin, kei tungah maipha hong piakik lo ding hiam?
English: Will the Lord cast off for ever? And will he be favourable no more?

**77:8**
Zolai: Ama itna kip bei paisuakin, ama thuciamte maimang suak ding hiam?
English: Is his mercy clean gone for ever? Doth his promise fail for evermore?

**77:9**
Zolai: Pasian in hehpihna a neih ding mangngilh khinta ahi hiam? Ama hehna in hehpihnate vukcip khin ahi hiam?” ka ci hi.
English: Hath God forgotten to be gracious? Hath he in anger shut up his tender mercies? Selah.

**77:10**
Zolai: Tua bang ahihleh, “Sangpenpa’ hat nawn lohna pen ka khakham veina ahi hi,” ka ci hi.
English: And I said, This is my infirmity: But I will remember the years of the right hand of the Most High.

**77:11**
Zolai: Topa’ sepnate ka lungsimah ka phawk ding a, hun lui lai-a nangma na lamdangte ka ciamteh ding hi.
English: I will remember the works of the LORD : Surely I will remember thy wonders of old.

**77:12**
Zolai: Nangma nasepna khempeuh ka lungngaingai ding a, nangma sep na liante ka ngaihsunsun ding hi.
English: I will meditate also of all thy work, And talk of thy doings.

**77:13**
Zolai: Pasian aw, nangma lampi siangtho hi. Eima Pasian tawh kibangin bang pasian lian ahi hiam?
English: Thy way, O God, is in the sanctuary: Who is so great a God as our God?

**77:14**
Zolai: Nang pen na lamdangte a bawl, minam dangte’ lakah na vangliatna a langkhiasak khin Pasian na hi hi.
English: Thou art the God that doest wonders: Thou hast declared thy strength among the people.

**77:15**
Zolai: Nangmah in na vangliatna tawh Jakob le Josef’ suante, na mite na honkhia hi.
English: Thou hast with thine arm redeemed thy people, The sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah.

**77:16**
Zolai: Tui in nang hong muh ciangin Pasian aw, tuite in nang hong muh ciangin a lau uh hi. Tui thukpi zong a ling hi.
English: The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee; they were afraid: The depths also were troubled.

**77:17**
Zolai: Meiipite in tui sungkhia-in, vante ging damdam a, nangma thaltangte mun citengah a leeng uh hi.
English: The clouds poured out water: The skies sent out a sound: Thine arrows also went abroad.

**77:18**
Zolai: Na vanging lianpi pingpei sungah omin, khuaphialepte in leitung taan a, leitang linggawpin a kising damdam hi.
English: The voice of thy thunder was in the heaven: The lightnings lightened the world: The earth trembled and shook.

**77:19**
Zolai: Nangma lamlianpi tuipi tung hi a, nangma lamneute zong luiliante’ tung mah ahi hi. Ahi zongin na khekhapte kimu lo hi.
English: Thy way is in the sea, and thy path in the great waters, And thy footsteps are not known.

**77:20**
Zolai: Nangmah in Moses le Aaron’ khut tawh nangma mite tuuhon bangin na makaih hi.
English: Thou leddest thy people like a flock By the hand of Moses and Aaron.

## Chapter 78

**78:1**
Zolai: Ka mite aw, keima hilhna ngai unla, ka kam tawh ka thugente na bil uh hong ngat un.
English: Give ear, O my people, to my law: Incline your ears to the words of my mouth.

**78:2**
Zolai: Note tungah thugentehna zangin ka kam ka-in thu ka hong gen ding hi. I pu i pate in hong gensa, eite in i zaksa le i theihsa, tanglai-a thuthukte ka hong genkhia ding hi.
English: I will open my mouth in a parable: I will utter dark sayings of old:

**78:4**
Zolai: Hih thute, i tate tungah eite in im loin, a hong piang lai ding khang thakte tungah, Topa’ minthang nasepna, ama vangliatna, ama sepsa na lamdangte i gen ding hi.
English: We will not hide them from their children, shewing to the generation to come, The praises of the LORD , and his strength, and his wonderful works that he hath done.

**78:5**
Zolai: Amaute pen Pasian tungah a lungsim thuman lo, lungsim kip a nei lo khangmi, lungsim khauhin a lehdo khangmi, amau’ pulepate tawh kibang loin, amaute in Pasian sungah amau’ lametna koihin, Pasian’ nasepnate mangngilh loin, ama thupiakte zui-in, a suak nai lo naupangte, a hong piangkik khang thakte in a thu thei-in, amaute ding khia-in amau’ tuletate tungah a thu a gentheih nadingin, amah in, i pate in a tate a hilhsawn dinga a sawl ahi, Israel sungah thukham khat koihin, Jakob sungah tecipanna khat a koih hi.
English: For he established a testimony in Jacob, and appointed a law in Israel, Which he commanded our fathers, that they should make them known to their children:

**78:9**
Zolai: Thal a tawi Efraim mite, galkido ni-in nungkik uh hi.
English: The children of Ephraim, being armed, and carrying bows, Turned back in the day of battle.

**78:10**
Zolai: Amaute in Pasian’ thuciamna zui lo uh a, ama thukham bangin gamta nuam lo uh hi.
English: They kept not the covenant of God, And refused to walk in his law;

**78:11**
Zolai: Ama bawlsa le amaute tungah nalamdang a lahsate amaute in mangngilh uh hi.
English: And forgat his works, And his wonders that he had shewed them.

**78:12**
Zolai: Egypt gam sung Zoan munah, a pu a pate uh’ muhna-ah amah in nalamdang a bawl hi.
English: Marvellous things did he in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, In the field of Zoan.

**78:13**
Zolai: Amah in tuipi kikhensakin amaute kantansak a, tuite a lompi-in a omsak hi.
English: He divided the sea, and caused them to pass through; And he made the waters to stand as an heap.

**78:14**
Zolai: Sun hunin amah in amaute meiipi khat tawh kha a, zan tawntung, meikuang taang khat tawh amaute a kha hi.
English: In the daytime also he led them with a cloud, And all the night with a light of fire.

**78:15**
Zolai: Amah in gam sungah suangpite kitamsak a, tuithukpi sung panin a piangkhia bangin amaute’ tungah tui dawn ding tampi a pia hi.
English: He clave the rocks in the wilderness, And gave them drink as out of the great depths.

**78:16**
Zolai: Amah in suangpi sung panin luitui luangkhiasak a, guntui luang bangin tuite a luangsak hi.
English: He brought streams also out of the rock, And caused waters to run down like rivers.

**78:17**
Zolai: Ahi zongin ama tungah amaute khial lailai uh a, Sehnel gam sungah Sangpen pa a lehpan uh hi.
English: And they sinned yet more against him By provoking the most High in the wilderness.

**78:18**
Zolai: Amaute in amau’ duh mahmah an a kalhna uh tawh amaute in a lungsim sung uhah Pasian a ze-et uh hi.
English: And they tempted God in their heart By asking meat for their lust.

**78:19**
Zolai: Amaute in Pasian gensia uh a, “Pasian in gamlakah an pia thei ding ahi hiam?
English: Yea, they spake against God; They said, Can God furnish a table in the wilderness?

**78:20**
Zolai: Amah in suangpi sat a, tui lengkhia-in tuite dimlet takpi ahi hiam? Amah in ama mite, an ahi a, sameh ahi zongin a pia thei takpi ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
English: Behold, he smote the rock, that the waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed; Can he give bread also? Can he provide flesh for his people?

**78:21**
Zolai: Topa in tua thu a zak ciangin hehna tawh kidimin, meikuang tawh Jakob sugawp a, Israel tungah a heh semsem hi.
English: Therefore the LORD heard this , and was wroth: So a fire was kindled against Jacob, and anger also came up against Israel;

**78:22**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in Pasian um lo uh a, a honkhiazo dingin muang lo uh hi.
English: Because they believed not in God, And trusted not in his salvation:

**78:23**
Zolai: Ahi zongin amah in, tunga om vantungte thu pia-in, vantung kongte hong a,
English: Though he had commanded the clouds from above, And opened the doors of heaven,

**78:24**
Zolai: nek dingin amau tungah manna an zusakin, amaute tungah vantung an a pia hi.
English: And had rained down manna upon them to eat, And had given them of the corn of heaven.

**78:25**
Zolai: Mihingte in vantung mite’ an ne uh a, amah in amaute tungah an tampi a puak hi.
English: Man did eat angels' food: He sent them meat to the full.

**78:26**
Zolai: Amah in vantungah nisuahna huih nungsakin, ama vangliatna tawh leitaw lam huih paikhiatpih a,
English: He caused an east wind to blow in the heaven: And by his power he brought in the south wind.

**78:27**
Zolai: amah in amaute tungah leivui zah-a tam sa zusak a, tuipi sehnel zah-a tam vasate a khiatsuk hi.
English: He rained flesh also upon them as dust, And feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea:

**78:28**
Zolai: Amau’ giahphual laizang, amau’ omna kiim khempeuhah tuate a kiasak hi.
English: And he let it fall in the midst of their camp, Round about their habitations.

**78:29**
Zolai: Amau’ duh pen pia ahih manin, amaute in ne-in gilvah uh hi.
English: So they did eat, and were well filled: For he gave them their own desire;

**78:30**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in a duh pen uh a kham ma, amau’ kam sungah an a omlaipi mahin,
English: They were not estranged from their lust. But while their meat was yet in their mouths,

**78:31**
Zolai: amaute’ tungah Pasian’ hehna tungkikin amah in amaute lakah a hatpen teng thatin, Israel-te’ muanlesuan teng a vatlum hi.
English: The wrath of God came upon them, and slew the fattest of them, And smote down the chosen men of Israel.

**78:32**
Zolai: Hih na lamdangte khempeuh a omkhin hinapi-in amaute khial lai veve uh a, ama na lamdangte’ hangin amaute in um tuan lo uh hi.
English: For all this they sinned still, And believed not for his wondrous works.

**78:33**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in amau’ hunte husan’ khat bangin maimangsak a, amau’ nuntakna, launa lianpi tawh a beisak hi.
English: Therefore their days did he consume in vanity, And their years in trouble.

**78:34**
Zolai: Amaute pawlkhat a thah khit ciangin a omlai mite in amah zong pan uh hi. Amaute kisikin, lungsim taktak tawh Pasian a zong uh hi.
English: When he slew them, then they sought him: And they returned and enquired early after God.

**78:35**
Zolai: Amaute in Pasian pen, amaute a honkhia, Sangpen Pasian, amaute a hupa ahihna a phawk uh hi.
English: And they remembered that God was their rock, And the high God their redeemer.

**78:36**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in a kampi bek uh tawh amah phatkhem uh a, a leii uh tawh ama tungah zuaugen uh hi.
English: Nevertheless they did flatter him with their mouth, And they lied unto him with their tongues.

**78:37**
Zolai: Amaute’ lungsim ama lamah kip lo uh a, ama thuciamna-ah amaute thuman lo uh hi.
English: For their heart was not right with him, Neither were they stedfast in his covenant.

**78:38**
Zolai: Ahi zongin amah in hehpihna lungsim nei ahih manin amau’ khialhnate maisakin, amaute susia lo hi. Amah in a hehna ip zelzel a, a hehna khempeuh phongkhia lo hi.
English: But he, being full of compassion, Forgave their iniquity, and destroyed them not: Yea, many a time turned he his anger away, And did not stir up all his wrath.

**78:39**
Zolai: Amah in, amaute pen mihing hi lel a, a hong paikik nawn lo huihnung bang ahihna uh a phawk hi.
English: For he remembered that they were but flesh; A wind that passeth away, and cometh not again.

**78:40**
Zolai: Amaute in gamlakah amah lehdo zelzel uh a, sehnel gam sungah amah dahsak uh hi.
English: How oft did they provoke him in the wilderness, And grieve him in the desert!

**78:41**
Zolai: Amaute in amah ze-et kikkik uh a, Israel-te’ Siangtho Pasian a phin uh hi.
English: Yea, they turned back and tempted God, And limited the Holy One of Israel.

**78:42**
Zolai: Galte’ kiang panin amah in amaute a hotkhiat ni hitaleh, Egypt gamah ama limte a bawl hun lai hitaleh, Zoan gamah a bawl a na lamdangte hitaleh, ama vangliatna hitaleh, amaute in ngaihsutin nei lo uh hi.
English: They remembered not his hand, Nor the day when he delivered them from the enemy.

**78:44**
Zolai: Amaute in a luituite uh a dawn theih loh nadingin amau’ guntuite amah in sisan a suaksak hi.
English: And had turned their rivers into blood; And their floods, that they could not drink.

**78:45**
Zolai: Amaute a petthei cippi honte, amaute’ lote a susia uiphukte amau’ lakah a sawl hi.
English: He sent divers sorts of flies among them, which devoured them; And frogs, which destroyed them.

**78:46**
Zolai: Amau’ lo ante tangngol pia a, amau’ sepna gahte kauphe a pia hi.
English: He gave also their increase unto the caterpiller, And their labour unto the locust.

**78:47**
Zolai: A leengguite uh gial tawh denggawp a, a theithekte uh vukkhal tawh susia hi.
English: He destroyed their vines with hail, And their sycomore trees with frost.

**78:48**
Zolai: A ganhingte uh gial tawh denglum a, a gan khawite uh keek tawh a denglum hi.
English: He gave up their cattle also to the hail, And their flocks to hot thunderbolts.

**78:49**
Zolai: Amaute’ tungah a lauhuai ama sinsona, hehna, thangpaihna, gimna, le a susiathei van mi honkhat a khah hi.
English: He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, and indignation, and trouble, By sending evil angels among them .

**78:50**
Zolai: Amah in a sinsona ip loin, kuamah hinkhawi lo a, pulnatna tawh amaute a sisak hi.
English: He made a way to his anger; He spared not their soul from death, But gave their life over to the pestilence;

**78:51**
Zolai: Ham’ suante’ inn sungah a ta upa pen teng, Egypt gam sung tacil khempeuh amah in a vatmai hi.
English: And smote all the firstborn in Egypt; The chief of their strength in the tabernacles of Ham:

**78:52**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in tua bangin ama mite gamlakah paikhiatpihin, ganhing honpi bangin amaute a paipih hi.
English: But made his own people to go forth like sheep, And guided them in the wilderness like a flock.

**78:53**
Zolai: Amah in a muanhuaina munah amaute paipih ahih manin amaute lau lo uh hi. Ahih hangin tuipi in amau’ galte tuumcip hi.
English: And he led them on safely, so that they feared not: But the sea overwhelmed their enemies.

**78:54**
Zolai: A khut taklam tawh ama ngahsa mual ahi, a gam siangtho-ah amaute a paipih hi.
English: And he brought them to the border of his sanctuary, Even to this mountain, which his right hand had purchased.

**78:55**
Zolai: Amau’ mai panin midangte hawlkhia-in, amaute’ luah ding neihsa hawmsak a, Israel minamte amau’ buk sungah a tengsak hi.
English: He cast out the heathen also before them, And divided them an inheritance by line, and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents.

**78:56**
Zolai: Ahi zongin amaute in Sangpen Pasian ze-etin lehdo uh a, ama thupiakna zui loin,
English: Yet they tempted and provoked the most high God, And kept not his testimonies:

**78:57**
Zolai: a pu a pate uh mah bangin kiheikhia-in a zuau gamtat uh hi. Thal ginalo bangin amaute a kihuiheek uh hi.
English: But turned back, and dealt unfaithfully like their fathers: They were turned aside like a deceitful bow.

**78:58**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in a munsangte uh tawh amah a sinso nadingin phinphin uh a, amau’ milim bawlte tawh ama hazatna ding a piangsak uh hi.
English: For they provoked him to anger with their high places, And moved him to jealousy with their graven images.

**78:59**
Zolai: Pasian in a zak ciangin heh pha mahmah a, amah in Israel-te a nial siangtho hi.
English: When God heard this , he was wroth, And greatly abhorred Israel:

**78:60**
Zolai: Mihingte’ lakah ama omna puanbuk ahi, Shiloh khua-a ama omna biakinn nusia a,
English: So that he forsook the tabernacle of Shiloh, The tent which he placed among men;

**78:61**
Zolai: ama vangliatna, galte’ tungah ap a, ama minthanna, galte’ khutah a pia hi.
English: And delivered his strength into captivity, And his glory into the enemy's hand.

**78:62**
Zolai: Amah in ama mite namsau tawh sisak a, ama luahte tungah a hehna a nga hi.
English: He gave his people over also unto the sword; And was wroth with his inheritance.

**78:63**
Zolai: Mei in a tangvalte kanglum a, a nungakte’ pasal ding kuamah om nawn lo hi.
English: The fire consumed their young men; And their maidens were not given to marriage.

**78:64**
Zolai: Amau’ siampite, namsau in puksak a, amau’ zite in a pasalte kah zo lo uh hi.
English: Their priests fell by the sword; And their widows made no lamentation.

**78:65**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa pen zukhamin a awng mi thahatpa, a ihmu tho bangin a khanglo hi.
English: Then the Lord awaked as one out of sleep, And like a mighty man that shouteth by reason of wine.

**78:66**
Zolai: Amah in a langpangte zo a, a maizum tawntung dingin amaute a koih hi.
English: And he smote his enemies in the hinder parts: He put them to a perpetual reproach.

**78:67**
Zolai: Amah in Josef’ suante nial a, Efraim minamte teello hi.
English: Moreover he refused the tabernacle of Joseph, And chose not the tribe of Ephraim:

**78:68**
Zolai: Ahih hangin ama it Zion Mual, Judah minam a teel hi.
English: But chose the tribe of Judah, The mount Zion which he loved.

**78:69**
Zolai: A kip den dingin a phuhsa leitang bang leh, a vantung inn bangin ama biakinn a lam hi.
English: And he built his sanctuary like high palaces , Like the earth which he hath established for ever.

**78:70**
Zolai: Amah in ama mi Jakob, ama luah Israel a cing dingin, no a nei tuupite a cinna, tuubukte panin la-in, ama nasem David a teel hi.
English: He chose David also his servant, And took him from the sheepfolds:

**78:72**
Zolai: Amah in lungsim thutang tawh amaute hoihtakin cingin, a siam mahmah a khut tawh amaute lam a lak hi.
English: So he fed them according to the integrity of his heart; And guided them by the skilfulness of his hands.

## Chapter 79

**79:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, na luah gam sungah dawibiate hong pai uh hi. Amaute in na biakinn siangtho ninsak gawp uh a, Jerusalem khuapi siasak gawp khin uh hi.
English: O God, the heathen are come into thine inheritance; Thy holy temple have they defiled; They have laid Jerusalem on heaps.

**79:2**
Zolai: Amaute in, na nasemte’ luanghawmte huihlak vasate pia uh a, na mi siangthote’ sate leilak ganhingte a pia uh hi.
English: The dead bodies of thy servants have they given to be meat unto the fowls of the heaven, The flesh of thy saints unto the beasts of the earth.

**79:3**
Zolai: Amaute in Jerusalem kimkotah tui buakkhiat bangin amaute’ sisan buakhia uh a, amaute a vui ding kuamah om lo hi.
English: Their blood have they shed like water round about Jerusalem; And there was none to bury them .

**79:4**
Zolai: Kote pen ka vengte uh’ zahko, ka kiim uha omte in a hong ko a hong nuihsat ka suak khinta uh hi.
English: We are become a reproach to our neighbours, A scorn and derision to them that are round about us.

**79:5**
Zolai: Topa aw, bang tanvei hi ding ahi hiam? Heh paisuak ding na hi hiam? Nangma hazat hehna meikuang bangin kuang paisuak ding ahi hiam?
English: How long, LORD ? Wilt thou be angry for ever? Shall thy jealousy burn like fire?

**79:6**
Zolai: Nangmah a hong thei lo minamte tung le, nangma tungah thu a hong ngen lo kumpi gamte tungah hehgawp in.
English: Pour out thy wrath upon the heathen that have not known thee, And upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy name.

**79:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in ka mite uh thatmang khin uh a, ka gam sung khempeuh uh susiagawp khin uh hi.
English: For they have devoured Jacob, And laid waste his dwelling place.

**79:8**
Zolai: Ka pu ka pate uh mawhna hangin ko a suanlekhakte hong lang ngaihsut kei inla, hong kiniamkoih ahih manin kote a huh dingin na hehpihna hong paisak mengmeng in.
English: O remember not against us former iniquities: Let thy tender mercies speedily prevent us: For we are brought very low.

**79:9**
Zolai: Kote a hong honkhia Pasian aw, nangma min a than nadingin kote hong huhin, nangma min hangin kote hong khahkhia-in, ka mawhnate uh hong maisak ta in.
English: Help us, O God of our salvation, for the glory of thy name: And deliver us, and purge away our sins, for thy name's sake.

**79:10**
Zolai: “Amaute’ Pasian koi-ah om ahi hiam?” minam dangte in a cih ding kilawm ding ahi hiam? Na nasemte’ sisan luangkhia a phulakna pen, minam dangte’ lak, komau’ muhna-ah kitheisak in.
English: Wherefore should the heathen say, Where is their God? Let him be known among the heathen in our sight By the revenging of the blood of thy servants which is shed.

**79:11**
Zolai: Thongkiate’ tauna ngai inla, thah dingin a kisehte na vangliatna tawh kizui-in suaktasak in.
English: Let the sighing of the prisoner come before thee; According to the greatness of thy power preserve thou those that are appointed to die;

**79:12**
Zolai: Amaute in nang hong zahkona mah tawh ka vengte uh’ ang sungah a zah sagihin thuk in, Topa !
English: And render unto our neighbours sevenfold into their bosom Their reproach, wherewith they have reproached thee, O Lord.

**79:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin nangma mi, nangma gam sung tuu kote in nangma tungah lungdamna kong lak ngitnget ding uh a, a khang khangin nangmah phatnate ka gengen ding uh hi.
English: So we thy people and sheep of thy pasture will give thee thanks for ever: We will shew forth thy praise to all generations.

## Chapter 80

**80:1**
Zolai: Tuuhon bangin Josef a paipih, Israel Tuucingpa aw, ngai in! Kherub tungah a tupa aw,
English: Give ear, O Shepherd of Israel, thou that leadest Joseph like a flock; Thou that dwellest between the cherubims, shine forth.

**80:2**
Zolai: Efraim, Benjamin le Manasseh’ mai-ah taangkhia in! Na tha saan inla, kote a honkhia dingin hong pai ta in.
English: Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh stir up thy strength, And come and save us.

**80:3**
Zolai: Ka ngei uh hong bangsakkik in, Pasian aw. Kote khempeuh hong kihotkhiat theih nadingin na maitang hong taangsak in.
English: Turn us again, O God, And cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.

**80:4**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa Pasian aw, na mite’ thungetna-ah bang tanvei sinso niloh ding na hi hiam?
English: O LORD God of hosts, How long wilt thou be angry against the prayer of thy people?

**80:5**
Zolai: Nangmah in a an dingun amaute tungah khitui na pia a, amaute’ dawn dingin khitui tampi na pia hi.
English: Thou feedest them with the bread of tears; And givest them tears to drink in great measure.

**80:6**
Zolai: Nangmah in, ka vengte uh’ thusim lohin kote na hong bawl a, ka galte un hong thusim loin hong nuihsan uh hi.
English: Thou makest us a strife unto our neighbours: And our enemies laugh among themselves.

**80:7**
Zolai: Ka ngei uh hong bangsakkik in, Vanglian Pasian aw. Kote khempeuh hong kihotkhiat theih nadingin na maitang hong taangsak in.
English: Turn us again, O God of hosts, And cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.

**80:8**
Zolai: Nangmah in Egypt panin leenggui khat na la a, minam dangte hawlkhia-in, tua leenggui na suan hi.
English: Thou hast brought a vine out of Egypt: Thou hast cast out the heathen, and planted it.

**80:9**
Zolai: Nangmah in tua leenggui a dingin leitang na hahsiang a, amah in zungthuk kha-in gam sung a dim hi.
English: Thou preparedst room before it, And didst cause it to take deep root, and it filled the land.

**80:10**
Zolai: Ama liim in mual liante hoihtakin liimsun a, a hiang in taamtak sing liante hoihtakin khuh a,
English: The hills were covered with the shadow of it, And the boughs thereof were like the goodly cedars.

**80:11**
Zolai: tuipi lamah a hiangte zamin, a dawnngekte in Gunpi lam a zuan hi.
English: She sent out her boughs unto the sea, And her branches unto the river.

**80:12**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin, lampi-ah a pai mi khempeuh in a gah a lawhtheih nadingin, bang hangin nangmah in a daigawl suvang na hi hiam?
English: Why hast thou then broken down her hedges, So that all they which pass by the way do pluck her?

**80:13**
Zolai: Gamlak a om ngal in susiagawp a, zangsung sa khempeuh in kivakna-in nei uh hi.
English: The boar out of the wood doth waste it, And the wild beast of the field doth devour it.

**80:14**
Zolai: Hong kiheikik in, Vanglian Pasian aw. Vantung panin hong ensukin hong mu in. Na khut taklam in a suansa, hih leenggui hong don in.
English: Return, we beseech thee, O God of hosts: Look down from heaven, And behold, and visit this vine;

**80:16**
Zolai: Amaute in mei tawh halin sattan gawp uh hi. Amaute heh et inla, susiagawp in.
English: It is burned with fire, it is cut down: They perish at the rebuke of thy countenance.

**80:17**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nangma a dingin na hatsak mi’ tapa, na taklama om mipa tungah na thahatna guan in.
English: Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand, Upon the son of man whom thou madest strong for thyself.

**80:18**
Zolai: Tua ciangin nang kiang panin ka kiheikik nawn kei ding uh hi. Kote hong nungtasak in, nang kong phat ding uh hi.
English: So will not we go back from thee: Quicken us, and we will call upon thy name.

**80:19**
Zolai: Ka ngei uh hong bangsakkik in, Vanglian Topa Pasian aw. Kote khempeuh hong kihotkhiat theih nadingin na maitang hong taangsak in.
English: Turn us again, O LORD God of hosts, Cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.

## Chapter 81

**81:1**
Zolai: Eite’ thahatna Pasian’ tungah nakpitakin la sa unla, Jakob Pasian’ tungah lungdamin awng un.
English: Sing aloud unto God our strength: Make a joyful noise unto the God of Jacob.

**81:2**
Zolai: La khat phuangin, khuangno tumin, a ngaih laiza khausai lasakna le harp khausai lasakna limtakin tum un.
English: Take a psalm, and bring hither the timbrel, The pleasant harp with the psaltery.

**81:3**
Zolai: Khadet, khalik, i pawi ni-in peengkul tum un.
English: Blow up the trumpet in the new moon, In the time appointed, on our solemn feast day.

**81:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh, tua bang hih ding pen Israel-te a dingin thukham hi a, Jakob Pasian’ biakna ngeina a kip khat ahi hi.
English: For this was a statute for Israel, And a law of the God of Jacob.

**81:5**
Zolai: Egypt gamah a pai lai-un Israel mite’ tungah thupiakna-in amah in a neih ahi hi. Ka theih ngei loh kampau khat hih bangin ka za hi:
English: This he ordained in Joseph for a testimony, When he went out through the land of Egypt: Where I heard a language that I understood not.

**81:6**
Zolai: “Na liangko uha om na vangikte uh ka hong lakkhiatsak a, na khut uha vangikte ka hong khiasak hi.
English: I removed his shoulder from the burden: His hands were delivered from the pots.

**81:7**
Zolai: Na cihmawh uh ciangin kei na hong sam uh a, keimah in note ka hong honkhia hi. A kilang lo vanging sung panin note ka hong dawng a, Meribah tui phualte-ah note ka hong ze-et hi.
English: Thou calledst in trouble, and I delivered thee; I answered thee in the secret place of thunder: I proved thee At the waters of Meribah. Selah.

**81:8**
Zolai: Ka mite aw, note kong thuhilh laitakin limtakin hong ngai un. Israel-te aw, keima thu a hong ngai hi hoh le-uh cin!
English: Hear, O my people, and I will testify unto thee: O Israel, if thou wilt hearken unto me;

**81:9**
Zolai: Note’ lakah pasian dang om lo ding a, pasian dang khat’ mai-ah na kun kei ding uh hi.
English: There shall no strange god be in thee; Neither shalt thou worship any strange god.

**81:10**
Zolai: Egypt gam panin note a hong lakhia, Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi. Na kam uh a golin ka un, keimah in kong dimsak ding hi.
English: I am the LORD thy God, which brought thee out of the land of Egypt: Open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it.

**81:11**
Zolai: “Ahih hangin ka mite in keima thu hong ngai lo uh a, Israel-te in keima thu themkha zong zui lo uh hi.
English: But my people would not hearken to my voice; And Israel would none of me.

**81:12**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin a ut bangun a gamta dingin amau’ lungsim khauhna bangin ka gamtasak hi.
English: So I gave them up unto their own hearts' lust: And they walked in their own counsels.

**81:13**
Zolai: Ka mite in ka thu hong ngai-in, keima deih bangin Israel a gamta hileh!
English: Oh that my people had hearkened unto me, And Israel had walked in my ways!

**81:14**
Zolai: Amau’ galte khempeuh ka zawhsak pak ding a, amau’ galte langpangin ka khut ka liik ding hi.
English: I should soon have subdued their enemies, And turned my hand against their adversaries.

**81:15**
Zolai: Kei a hong mudahte ka mai-ah hong kun ding uh a, amaute’ gimthuakna kip paisuak ding hi.
English: The haters of the LORD should have submitted themselves unto him: But their time should have endured for ever.

**81:16**
Zolai: Mangbuh hoihpen tawh note ka hong vak ding a, suangpi pana khuaizu tawh note kong gilvahsak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: He should have fed them also with the finest of the wheat: And with honey out of the rock should I have satisfied thee.

## Chapter 82

**82:1**
Zolai: Thu vaihawm kikhopna sungah Pasian in ama panmun hong len a, amah in pasian-te’ lakah thu a khen hi.
English: God standeth in the congregation of the mighty; He judgeth among the gods.

**82:2**
Zolai: “Note in bang tanvei a man loin thu khenin, migilote tungah angvanna zang ding na hi uh hiam?
English: How long will ye judge unjustly, And accept the persons of the wicked? Selah.

**82:3**
Zolai: A ginalo mite le pa a nei lo mite tungah thuman unla, a thuakte le a cimawhte’ thu a manin khen un.
English: Defend the poor and fatherless: Do justice to the afflicted and needy.

**82:4**
Zolai: A ginalo mite le a cimawh mite hon unla, migilote’ khutsung panin amaute honkhia un,” a ci hi.
English: Deliver the poor and needy: Rid them out of the hand of the wicked.

**82:5**
Zolai: Amaute in thutheihna ahi a, thutelna ahi zongin bangmah nei lo uh a, khuamial sungah gamta uh ahih manin leitung bulpite khempeuh a kilinggawp hi.
English: They know not, neither will they understand; They walk on in darkness: All the foundations of the earth are out of course.

**82:6**
Zolai: Ke’n kong cihin-ah, “Note khempeuh, Sangpenpa’ tate, pasian-te na hi uh hi.
English: I have said, Ye are gods; And all of you are children of the most High.

**82:7**
Zolai: Ahi zongin mite bangin si-in, kumpi khat peuhpeuh bangin na kia ding uh hi,” kong ci hi.
English: But ye shall die like men, And fall like one of the princes.

**82:8**
Zolai: Pasian aw, tho in; leitung mite thu khen in. Bang hang hiam cih leh minam khempeuh nangma a’ ahi hi.
English: Arise, O God, judge the earth: For thou shalt inherit all nations.

## Chapter 83

**83:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, dai dide-in om kei in. Lungnuamin, tang loin ommawk kei in, Pasian aw.
English: Keep not thou silence, O God: Hold not thy peace, and be not still, O God.

**83:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh na galte in gamlumna piangsak uh a, nang hong mudahte kiphasak mahmah uh hi.
English: For, lo, thine enemies make a tumult: And they that hate thee have lifted up the head.

**83:3**
Zolai: Amaute in khem siamna tawh na mite thangsiah uh a, amaute in na it mite langpangin thu kikum uh hi.
English: They have taken crafty counsel against thy people, And consulted against thy hidden ones.

**83:4**
Zolai: Amaute in, “Hong pai un, minam khat hihna panin amaute beisak ni. Israel min peuhmah kiphawksak nawn kei ni!” ci uh hi.
English: They have said, Come, and let us cut them off from being a nation; That the name of Israel may be no more in remembrance.

**83:5**
Zolai: Amaute in siatna ding geelin kithukhat uh a, nangmah hong langpangin thuciamna a bawl uh hi.
English: For they have consulted together with one consent: They are confederate against thee:

**83:6**
Zolai: Edom mite le Ishmael mite, Moab le Hagri mite,
English: The tabernacles of Edom, and the Ishmaelites; Of Moab, and the Hagarenes;

**83:7**
Zolai: Gebal, Ammon, le Amalek mite, Filistia le Taia khua mite tawh thuciam a bawl uh hi.
English: Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek; The Philistines with the inhabitants of Tyre;

**83:8**
Zolai: Assiria mite in zong amaute pawlpih uh a, amaute pen Lot’ suanlekhakte a dingin pawl muanhuaite ahi uh hi.
English: Assur also is joined with them: They have holpen the children of Lot. Selah.

**83:9**
Zolai: Endor munah a kizogawp, leilakah a luang uh a muatgawp, Midian mite’ tungah na bawl bang leh, Kishon gun-a Sisera le Jabin-te’ tungah na bawl bangin amaute tungah bawl in.
English: Do unto them as unto the Midianites; As to Sisera, as to Jabin, at the brook of Kison:

**83:11**
Zolai: “Pasian’ gam hoihte eima tan’ dingin la ni,” a ci Oreb le Zeeb-te bangin amau’ miliante bawl inla, Zeba le Zalmunna-te bangin amau a ukte khempeuh bawl in.
English: Make their nobles like Oreb, and like Zeeb: Yea, all their princes as Zebah, and as Zalmunna:

**83:13**
Zolai: Ka Pasian aw, amaute pen pingpei sunga ninnen, huih mai-a ansi leeng bangsak ta in.
English: O my God, make them like a wheel; As the stubble before the wind.

**83:14**
Zolai: Mei in gamlak a haltum bang, mualliante a kuansak bangin
English: As the fire burneth a wood, And as the flame setteth the mountains on fire;

**83:15**
Zolai: na khuapi huihpi tawh amaute delh inla, na huihpi tawh amaute lausak gawp in.
English: So persecute them with thy tempest, And make them afraid with thy storm.

**83:16**
Zolai: Topa aw, amaute in na min hong zontheih nadingin amaute khempeuh maizumna tawh kidimsak in.
English: Fill their faces with shame; That they may seek thy name, O LORD .

**83:17**
Zolai: Amaute maizumin lungkia densak inla, a mindai-in siasak in.
English: Let them be confounded and troubled for ever; Yea, let them be put to shame, and perish:

**83:18**
Zolai: Topa a kici min nei nangmah bek leitung khempeuhah a Sangpenpa na hihna amaute theisak in.
English: That men may know that thou, whose name alone is JEHOVAH, Art the Most High over all the earth.

## Chapter 84

**84:1**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa aw, nangma tenna mun bangzah takin etlawm ahi hiam?
English: How amiable are thy tabernacles, O LORD of hosts!

**84:2**
Zolai: Ke’n ka lunggulh mahmah hi. Topa’ huangsung ka lunggulh mahmah a, ka lungsim le ka pumpi a nungta Pasian’ tungah lungdam mahmahin la a sa hi.
English: My soul longeth, yea, even fainteth for the courts of the LORD : My heart and my flesh crieth out for the living God.

**84:3**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa, ka kumpi le ka Pasian aw, na biakna tau-ah, kawlgit nangawn in a inn ding mu a, phialphiah in a omna ding, a note a koihna ding bu a mu hi.
English: Yea, the sparrow hath found an house, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may lay her young, Even thine altars, O LORD of hosts, my King, and my God.

**84:4**
Zolai: Nangma inn sungah tengin, nangmah phatna a sa ngitnget mite thupha ngah mi ahi uh hi.
English: Blessed are they that dwell in thy house: They will be still praising thee. Selah.

**84:5**
Zolai: Nangma tung panin thahatna ngahin Zion zuatna lampi a tawn nuam mite thupha ngah mi ahi uh hi.
English: Blessed is the man whose strength is in thee; In whose heart are the ways of them .

**84:6**
Zolai: Amaute in Kuamkeu mun kantanin a pai laitakun tua kuam pen ciktui tampi tawh kidim a, guahzu masate in zong tua mun pen bualtuite tawh a kidimsak hi.
English: Who passing through the valley of Baca make it a well; The rain also filleth the pools.

**84:7**
Zolai: Amaute a paikawmun a tha uh hat semsem a, pasian-te’ Pasian Zion-ah mu ding uh hi.
English: They go from strength to strength, Every one of them in Zion appeareth before God.

**84:8**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa Pasian aw, ka thungetna hong za inla, ka thungetna hong ngai in, Jakob Pasian!
English: O LORD God of hosts, hear my prayer: Give ear, O God of Jacob. Selah.

**84:9**
Zolai: Pasian aw, kote a hong hu ding pa hong etsak inla, na sathau nilh pa hong kem in.
English: Behold, O God our shield, And look upon the face of thine anointed.

**84:10**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh mun dangah ni tulkhat om sangin nangma huang sungah ni khat om hoihzaw hi. Gitlohna inn sungah ka ten sangin ka Pasian’ inn kongcing pa ka hi nuamzaw hi.
English: For a day in thy courts Is better than a thousand. I had rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God, Than to dwell in the tents of wickedness.

**84:11**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa Pasian pen eite a hong hupa a minthang i kumpi hi a, maipha le pahtawina a hong piapa ahi hi. Thumanin a gamta mite tungah Topa in na hoih bangmah siit lo hi.
English: For the LORD God is a sun and shield: The LORD will give grace and glory: No good thing will he withhold from them that walk uprightly.

**84:12**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa aw, nangmah a hong muang mite, thupha ngah mi ahi uh hi.
English: O LORD of hosts, Blessed is the man that trusteth in thee.

## Chapter 85

**85:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma leitang na hehpih a, Jakob’ nopsaknate a ngeina na bangsakkik hi.
English: LORD , thou hast been favourable unto thy land: Thou hast brought back the captivity of Jacob.

**85:2**
Zolai: Na mite’ mawhna na maisak a, amau’ khialhna khempeuh na maisak hi.
English: Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people, Thou hast covered all their sin. Selah.

**85:3**
Zolai: Na hehna khempeuh na damsak a, na sinsona na daisak hi.
English: Thou hast taken away all thy wrath: Thou hast turned thyself from the fierceness of thine anger.

**85:4**
Zolai: Kote hong honkhia Pasian aw, kote ka ngei uh hong bangsakkik inla, kote tunga na lungkim lohna hong beisak ta in.
English: Turn us, O God of our salvation, And cause thine anger toward us to cease.

**85:5**
Zolai: Kote’ tungah heh paisuak ding na hi hiam? Khang tawntungin heh paisuak ding na hi hiam?
English: Wilt thou be angry with us for ever? Wilt thou draw out thine anger to all generations?

**85:6**
Zolai: Kote in nangmah kong phat theih nadingun ko na mite hong nungtasakkik lo ding na hi hiam?
English: Wilt thou not revive us again: That thy people may rejoice in thee?

**85:7**
Zolai: Topa aw, kote tungah na itna kip hong lak inla, hong huhin hong hon in.
English: Shew us thy mercy, O LORD , And grant us thy salvation.

**85:8**
Zolai: Topa Pasian’ thugen ding hong zasak dih un. Bang hang hiam cih leh ama lamah lungsim takpi tawh a kihei ama mi siangtho, ama mite’ tungah kilemna thu a gen ding hi.
English: I will hear what God the LORD will speak: For he will speak peace unto his people, and to his saints: But let them not turn again to folly.

**85:9**
Zolai: I gam sungah minthanna a om theih nadingin amah a zahtakte a dingin ama hong hotkhiatna hong om takpi hi.
English: Surely his salvation is nigh them that fear him; That glory may dwell in our land.

**85:10**
Zolai: Itna kip le thutak kigawm ding a, thuman le kilemna kihual ding uh hi.
English: Mercy and truth are met together; Righteousness and peace have kissed each other .

**85:11**
Zolai: Leilak panin thutak hong pokhia ding a, vantung panin thuman in hong ensuk ding hi.
English: Truth shall spring out of the earth; And righteousness shall look down from heaven.

**85:12**
Zolai: Topa in a hoih nate eite tungah hong pia ding a, i leitang in hauhna piangsak ding hi.
English: Yea, the LORD shall give that which is good; And our land shall yield her increase.

**85:13**
Zolai: Topa’ mai-ah thuman na ma pai ding a, ama lampi a bawlkhol ding hi.
English: Righteousness shall go before him; And shall set us in the way of his steps.

## Chapter 86

**86:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, kei hehpihhuai-in cimawh ka hih manin na bil hong ngat inla, hong dawng in.
English: Bow down thine ear, O LORD , hear me: For I am poor and needy.

**86:2**
Zolai: Mihoih ka hih manin kei hong kem in. Nangmah a hong muang na nasempa hong hon in.
English: Preserve my soul; for I am holy: O thou my God, save thy servant that trusteth in thee.

**86:3**
Zolai: Nang pen ka Pasian na hi hi. Topa aw, sun tawntung hong kiko ka hih manin kei hong hehpih in.
English: Be merciful unto me, O Lord: For I cry unto thee daily.

**86:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma tungah thu hong ngen ka hih manin na nasempa hong kipaaksak in.
English: Rejoice the soul of thy servant: For unto thee, O Lord, do I lift up my soul.

**86:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa aw, nangmah hoihin mawhna na maisak a, hong ngente khempeuh tungah itna kip tampi na nei hi.
English: For thou, Lord, art good, and ready to forgive; And plenteous in mercy unto all them that call upon thee.

**86:6**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka thungetna hong za inla, nang tungah thumin kong kikona hong ngai in.
English: Give ear, O LORD , unto my prayer; And attend to the voice of my supplications.

**86:7**
Zolai: Kei hong dawng na hih manin ka haksat hun ciangin nangma tungah kong ngen hi.
English: In the day of my trouble I will call upon thee: For thou wilt answer me.

**86:8**
Zolai: Topa aw, pasian-te lakah nang tawh a kibang kuamah om lo a, nangma sep bang, kuamah in sem thei lo hi.
English: Among the gods there is none like unto thee, O Lord; Neither are there any works like unto thy works.

**86:9**
Zolai: Topa aw, na bawlsa minam khempeuh hong pai-in na mai-ah hong kun ding uh a, nangma min hong phat ding uh hi.
English: All nations whom thou hast made shall come and worship before thee, O Lord; And shall glorify thy name.

**86:10**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nangmah lianin na lamdangte na bawl a, nang bek Pasian na hi hi.
English: For thou art great, and doest wondrous things: Thou art God alone.

**86:11**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang tungah hong thumanin nangma lampi ka zuih theih nadingin kei hong hilh inla, nangma min a zahtakte tawh keima lungsim pumkhat hong bangsak in.
English: Teach me thy way, O LORD ; I will walk in thy truth: Unite my heart to fear thy name.

**86:12**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, ka lungsim khempeuh tawh na tungah ka lungdam a, nangma min ka thangsak ngitnget ding hi.
English: I will praise thee, O Lord my God, with all my heart: And I will glorify thy name for evermore.

**86:13**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh keimah na hong itna kip lian mahmah a, Leinuai thuk sung panin kei nong honkhia khin hi.
English: For great is thy mercy toward me: And thou hast delivered my soul from the lowest hell.

**86:14**
Zolai: Pasian aw, mi kihisakte, kei langpangin hong kipan hi. Thu-helhawt mi pawlkhat in kei, thah hong sawm uh a, amaute in nang hong thudon lo uh hi.
English: O God, the proud are risen against me, And the assemblies of violent men have sought after my soul; And have not set thee before them.

**86:15**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa aw, nang pen a hehpih thei, a dik Pasian na hi a, heh hak mahmahin, itna kip le thumanna tawh a kidim na hi hi.
English: But thou, O Lord, art a God full of compassion, and gracious, Longsuffering, and plenteous in mercy and truth.

**86:16**
Zolai: Kei lamah hong kihei inla, kei hong hehpih in. Na nasempa thahatsak inla, na nasem numei’ tapa hong hon in.
English: O turn unto me, and have mercy upon me; Give thy strength unto thy servant, and save the son of thine handmaid.

**86:17**
Zolai: Topa nangmah in kei hong huhin, nong thahatsakna hangin, kei hong mudahte in mu-in a zahhuai nadingun keima tungah na maipha hong lak in.
English: Shew me a token for good; That they which hate me may see it , and be ashamed: Because thou, LORD , hast holpen me, and comforted me.

## Chapter 87

**87:1**
Zolai: Mual Siangtho tungah ama phuhsa khuapi om hi.
English: His foundation is in the holy mountains.

**87:2**
Zolai: Topa in Israel gam mundang khempeuhte sangin Zion kulhkongpi itzaw hi.
English: The LORD loveth the gates of Zion more than all the dwellings of Jacob.

**87:3**
Zolai: Pasian’ khuapi aw, na minthanna teng hong kigengen hi.
English: Glorious things are spoken of thee, O city of God. Selah.

**87:4**
Zolai: Kei hong theite lakah Egypt le Babylon ka hel hi. Filistia, Taia le Ethiopia te zong kihel a, “Hihte pen hua lai mah panin a piang ahi hi,” kici ding hi.
English: I will make mention of Rahab and Babylon to them that know me: Behold Philistia, and Tyre, with Ethiopia; This man was born there.

**87:5**
Zolai: Zion tawh kisai-in ahihleh, “Minam khempeuh ama sung pana suak ahi hi,” kici ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Sangpenpa mahmah in amah kipsak ding hi.
English: And of Zion it shall be said, This and that man was born in her: And the highest himself shall establish her.

**87:6**
Zolai: Topa in, “Hihte pen hua lai-a suak,” ci-in minam khempeuh ciamtehin a gelh ding hi.
English: The LORD shall count, when he writeth up the people, That this man was born there. Selah.

**87:7**
Zolai: Tua sunga teng mite in, “Kote’ lungdamna khempeuh nangma sungah om hi,” ci ciat ding uh hi.
English: As well the singers as the players on instruments shall be there: All my springs are in thee.

## Chapter 88

**88:1**
Zolai: Topa, ka Pasian aw, sunin huhna kong ngen a, zan hun sungin nangma mai-ah kong kiko hi.
English: O LORD God of my salvation, I have cried day and night before thee:

**88:2**
Zolai: Ka thungetna hong za inla, nong huh ding ka hong ngetna hong ngai in.
English: Let my prayer come before thee: Incline thine ear unto my cry;

**88:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh lungkhamna tampi thuakin, ka si dektak hi.
English: For my soul is full of troubles: And my life draweth nigh unto the grave.

**88:4**
Zolai: Kei pen a sidek mi tawh ka kibang ta a, ka thahatna khempeuh beimang khinta hi.
English: I am counted with them that go down into the pit: I am as a man that hath no strength:

**88:5**
Zolai: Misite lakah a kinusia, a kithatlum, han sunga lum, na huh zawh ahi nawn lo, na phawk nawn lohte ka bang ta hi.
English: Free among the dead, like the slain that lie in the grave, Whom thou rememberest no more: And they are cut off from thy hand.

**88:6**
Zolai: Kei pen, mialin a thukna mun, Leihawm thuk sungah nong koih khinta hi.
English: Thou hast laid me in the lowest pit, In darkness, in the deeps.

**88:7**
Zolai: Nangma hehna keima tungah gik mahmah a, na tuihualte khempeuh tawh kei na hong vukcip hi.
English: Thy wrath lieth hard upon me, And thou hast afflicted me with all thy waves. Selah.

**88:8**
Zolai: Ka kikholhpih mite in kei a hong pelh dingin na hong bawl a, amaute tungah a cikzethuai khatin kei na hong bawl hi. Ka suahtak theih loh nadingin kei hong kikhumcip a,
English: Thou hast put away mine acquaintance far from me; Thou hast made me an abomination unto them: I am shut up, And I cannot come forth.

**88:9**
Zolai: ka gim thuakna hangin ka mit a mial ta hi. Topa aw, nisimin nangma tungah kong ngen a, thu ngenin ka khutte nangma lamah kong zan hi.
English: Mine eye mourneth by reason of affliction: LORD , I have called daily upon thee, I have stretched out my hands unto thee.

**88:10**
Zolai: A sisate a dingin nalamdang a bawl na hi hiam? Nangmah a phat dingin mi a si khinsate hong tho ding ahi hiam?
English: Wilt thou shew wonders to the dead? Shall the dead arise and praise thee? Selah.

**88:11**
Zolai: Han sungah na itna kip kigen ding a, siatna munah nangma thumannate kigen ding ahi hiam?
English: Shall thy lovingkindness be declared in the grave? Or thy faithfulness in destruction?

**88:12**
Zolai: Khuamialna sungah na na lamdangte kithei a, mangngilhna gam sungah na hotkhiat huhna kithei ahi hiam?
English: Shall thy wonders be known in the dark? And thy righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?

**88:13**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa aw, na tungah huhna kong ngen a, zingsang simin na mai-ah thu ka hong ngen hi.
English: But unto thee have I cried, O LORD ; And in the morning shall my prayer prevent thee.

**88:14**
Zolai: Topa aw, bang hangin kei hong paaikhia na hi hiam? Bang hangin kei kiang panin na maitang seel na hi hiam?
English: LORD , why castest thou off my soul? Why hidest thou thy face from me?

**88:15**
Zolai: Ka neu tung a kipan gim thuakin ka si dektak hi. Nong gimpiakte ka thuak a, ka cih nading mel ka thei nawn kei hi.
English: I am afflicted and ready to die From my youth up: While I suffer thy terrors I am distracted.

**88:16**
Zolai: Nangma hehna in keimah hong nawkgawp khin a, a lauhuai mahmah nangma hong sukgawpna in kei hong susia ta hi.
English: Thy fierce wrath goeth over me; Thy terrors have cut me off.

**88:17**
Zolai: Amaute in tuikhang bangin sun tawntungin kei hong umcih uh a, kei hong tuamcip uh hi.
English: They came round about me daily like water; They compassed me about together.

**88:18**
Zolai: Kei hong itte le ka lawmte keimah nong pelhsak khin a, khuamial bekbek, keima kikholhpih ahi hi.
English: Lover and friend hast thou put far from me, And mine acquaintance into darkness.

## Chapter 89

**89:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, na itna kip la-in ka sa tawntung ding a, nangma thutakna ka gen tawntung ding hi.
English: I will sing of the mercies of the LORD for ever: With my mouth will I make known thy faithfulness to all generations.

**89:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma itna kip tawntung a, na thutakna zong vantung bangin kip tawntung hi.
English: For I have said, Mercy shall be built up for ever: Thy faithfulness shalt thou establish in the very heavens.

**89:3**
Zolai: Nangmah in, “Ka teelpa tawh thuciamna ka bawlzo a, ka nasem David tungah thu ka ciamzo hi:
English: I have made a covenant with my chosen, I have sworn unto David my servant,

**89:4**
Zolai: ‘Na suan na khakte kumpi-in ka kipsak ding a, na kumpi gam khang tawntungin ka kipsak ding hi,’” na ci khin hi.
English: Thy seed will I establish for ever, And build up thy throne to all generations. Selah.

**89:5**
Zolai: Topa aw, na nasepna a lamdangte, vantungte phatsak inla, mi siangthote’ kikhopna sungah na thumanna phatsak in.
English: And the heavens shall praise thy wonders, O LORD : Thy faithfulness also in the congregation of the saints.

**89:6**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa pen vantung a kua tawh kitehthei ding ahi hiam? Mi siangthote’ kikhopna sungah a kizahtak Pasian, a kiima omte khempeuh tungah lianin a zahtakhuai Topa pen van mite’ lakah kua pen tawh kibang ahi hiam?
English: For who in the heaven Can be compared unto the LORD ? Who among the sons of the mighty Can be likened unto the LORD ?

**89:8**
Zolai: Vanglian Topa Pasian aw, na khempeuhah na thutak a, nangmah bangin a vanglian kua om ahi hiam, Topa aw.
English: O LORD God of hosts, who is a strong LORD like unto thee? Or to thy faithfulness round about thee?

**89:9**
Zolai: Nang in tuipi khang na uk a, a tuihualte a san ciangin na daisak hi.
English: Thou rulest the raging of the sea: When the waves thereof arise, thou stillest them.

**89:10**
Zolai: Nangmah in a kithat lumsa luanghawm khat bangin ganhing golpi Rahab na sugawp a, na thahatna tawh na galte na zogawp hi.
English: Thou hast broken Rahab in pieces, as one that is slain; Thou hast scattered thine enemies with thy strong arm.

**89:11**
Zolai: Vantungte nangma a’ hi a, leitung zong nangma a’ mah ahi hi. Leitung le a sunga om khempeuh nangma phuhsa ahi hi.
English: The heavens are thine, the earth also is thine: As for the world and the fulness thereof, thou hast founded them.

**89:12**
Zolai: Saklam le khanglamte nangma bawlsa hi a, Tabor mual le Hermon mual in lungdamna tawh na min hong phat uh hi.
English: The north and the south thou hast created them: Tabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name.

**89:13**
Zolai: Nangma vang lian mahmah a, na thahatna kigen thei lo hi.
English: Thou hast a mighty arm: Strong is thy hand, and high is thy right hand.

**89:14**
Zolai: Thuman le thutang tawh na ukna za na phut a, itna kip le thuman tawh na khempeuh na sem hi.
English: Justice and judgment are the habitation of thy throne: Mercy and truth shall go before thy face.

**89:15**
Zolai: Topa aw, lungdamin lasakna tawh nang hong bia a, na migitna khuavak sungah nuamtakin a nungta, nangma hangin sunthapai-in lungdam a, nangma hoihna hong phat mite mi nuamsa ahi uh hi.
English: Blessed is the people that know the joyful sound: They shall walk, O LORD , in the light of thy countenance.

**89:17**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nangmah in nakpitakin kote na hong gualzosak a, kote hong angvanin na hong gualzosak hi.
English: For thou art the glory of their strength: And in thy favour our horn shall be exalted.

**89:18**
Zolai: Kote a hong hu Topa hi a, Israel-te’ Siangtho Pasian nangmah in ka kumpipa uh nong pia hi.
English: For the LORD is our defence; And the Holy One of Israel is our King.

**89:19**
Zolai: Hun lui lai-in na thuman mipa tungah mang sungah thu na gen a, “A vanglian khat pa tungah lukhu ka koih khinzo a, mite lak panin a kitengkhia mi khat ka liansakzo hi.
English: Then thou spakest in vision to thy holy one, and saidst, I have laid help upon one that is mighty; I have exalted one chosen out of the people.

**89:20**
Zolai: Ka nasempa David ka muzo hi. Ka thahatna ama tungah a om ngitnget theih nading, ka vangliatna in zong, amah a thakhauhsak theih nadingin ka sathau siangtho amah ka nilh khin hi.
English: I have found David my servant; With my holy oil have I anointed him:

**89:22**
Zolai: Galte in amah khemzo ngei lo ding a, migilote in zong amah zo ngei lo ding uh hi.
English: The enemy shall not exact upon him; Nor the son of wickedness afflict him.

**89:23**
Zolai: Ama mai-ah a galte ka sugawp ding a, amah a mudahte ka satpuk ding hi.
English: And I will beat down his foes before his face, And plague them that hate him.

**89:24**
Zolai: Amah it tawntungin ama tungah ka thutak ding a, amah a gualzo-in ka bawl tawntung ding hi.
English: But my faithfulness and my mercy shall be with him: And in my name shall his horn be exalted.

**89:25**
Zolai: Mediterranean Tuipi a kipan Eufratis Gunpi dong amah ka uksak ding hi.
English: I will set his hand also in the sea, And his right hand in the rivers.

**89:26**
Zolai: Amah in kei kiangah, ‘Nang pen keima Pa le ka Pasian na hi a, kei a hong honkhia pa le a hong hupa na hi hi,’ hong ci ding hi.
English: He shall cry unto me, Thou art my father, My God, and the rock of my salvation.

**89:27**
Zolai: Keimah in amah ta upa penin ka bawl ding a, leitung kumpite lakah a lianpenin ka bawl ding hi.
English: Also I will make him my firstborn, Higher than the kings of the earth.

**89:28**
Zolai: Amah ka itna ka kipsak tawntung ding a, ama tungah ka thuciamna ka kipsak tawntung ding hi.
English: My mercy will I keep for him for evermore, And my covenant shall stand fast with him.

**89:29**
Zolai: Ama suanlekhakte kumpi ka hisak ngitnget ding a, a ukna za, vantung bangin ka kipsak ding hi.
English: His seed also will I make to endure for ever, And his throne as the days of heaven.

**89:30**
Zolai: “Ama tate in ka thukhamte nusia-in, ka biakna ngeina kip om bangin a gamtat kei uh a, amaute in ka ngeina siasakin ka thupiak a zuih kei uhleh, amaute’ thupalsatna hangin ciang tawh gim ka pia ding a, amau’ mawhnate hangin satna tawh gim ka pia ding hi.
English: If his children forsake my law, And walk not in my judgments;

**89:33**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah ka itna ka khiam kei ding a, ka thuciamna ka kipelhsak kei ding hi.
English: Nevertheless my lovingkindness will I not utterly take from him, Nor suffer my faithfulness to fail.

**89:34**
Zolai: Ka thuciamna siasak loin, ka kam pana paikhia thute ka kheel kei ding hi.
English: My covenant will I not break, nor alter the thing that is gone out of my lips.

**89:35**
Zolai: “A tawntung a kimang dingin ka sianthona tawh khatvei ka kiciam khin a, David’ tungah ka zuau kei ding hi.
English: Once have I sworn by my holiness that I will not lie unto David.

**89:36**
Zolai: Ama suanlekhakte kizom paisuak ding a, vana ni a taan laiteng a kumpi gam ka kipsak ding hi.
English: His seed shall endure for ever, And his throne as the sun before me.

**89:37**
Zolai: Khapi bangin tua pen kipsuak ding a, vantung a om laiteng kip ding hi,” na ci hi.
English: It shall be established for ever as the moon, And as a faithful witness in heaven. Selah.

**89:38**
Zolai: Ahih hangin tu-in amah nialin na lawnkhia a, na sathau nilh pa’ tungah na heh mahmah hi.
English: But thou hast cast off and abhorred, Thou hast been wroth with thine anointed.

**89:39**
Zolai: Na nasempa tawh na thuciamna na pelh khin a, ama kumpi lukhu leivui lakah na paihsak hi.
English: Thou hast made void the covenant of thy servant: Thou hast profaned his crown by casting it to the ground.

**89:40**
Zolai: Ama kulhte khempeuh na sukham khin a, ama galpanmun kipte a sia na suah khin hi.
English: Thou hast broken down all his hedges; Thou hast brought his strong holds to ruin.

**89:41**
Zolai: A pai khempeuh in ama nate sutgawp uh a, amah pen a vengte’ nuihsat a suak hi.
English: All that pass by the way spoil him: He is a reproach to his neighbours.

**89:42**
Zolai: Ama galte na gualzosak a, ama galte na lungdamsak khin hi.
English: Thou hast set up the right hand of his adversaries; Thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice.

**89:43**
Zolai: Ama galhiamte a mawkna na suaksak a, gal kidona-ah amah na guallelsak hi.
English: Thou hast also turned the edge of his sword, And hast not made him to stand in the battle.

**89:44**
Zolai: Nangmah in ama khut panin a kumpi ciangkhut na lakhia a, a kumpi tokhom leilak na denna hi.
English: Thou hast made his glory to cease, And cast his throne down to the ground.

**89:45**
Zolai: Nangmah in a teek hun nai lopi-in amah na teeksak a, maizumna tawh na kidimsak hi.
English: The days of his youth hast thou shortened: Thou hast covered him with shame. Selah.

**89:46**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang bang tanvei bucip den ding na hi hiam? Na hehna bang tanvei meikuang bangin kuangkuang ding ahi hiam?
English: How long, LORD ? wilt thou hide thyself for ever? Shall thy wrath burn like fire?

**89:47**
Zolai: Topa aw, nuntak hun a tom mahmahlam hong phawk in. Mihingte a mawk nadingin bawl na hi hiam?
English: Remember how short my time is: Wherefore hast thou made all men in vain?

**89:48**
Zolai: A si thei lo kua om ahi hiam? Sihna hankhuk panin kua suaktazo ahi hiam?
English: What man is he that liveth, and shall not see death? Shall he deliver his soul from the hand of the grave? Selah.

**89:49**
Zolai: Topa aw, na thumanna tawh David tunga na thuciamna, hun lui lai-a na itna kip koi-ah omta ahi hiam?
English: Lord, where are thy former lovingkindnesses, Which thou swarest unto David in thy truth?

**89:50**
Zolai: Topa aw, na nasempa bangzah takin hong kithusim lohna, galte in phinna-in a hong neihna, Topa aw, amaute in na sathau nilh pa a paina khempeuhah a hong nuihsatna uh hong phawk ta in.
English: Remember, Lord, the reproach of thy servants; How I do bear in my bosom the reproach of all the mighty people;

**89:52**
Zolai: Topa in thupha ngah tawntung tahen. Amen! Amen!
English: Blessed be the LORD for evermore. Amen, and Amen.

## Chapter 90

**90:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, khang tawntungin kote’ omna mun na hi hi.
English: LORD , thou hast been our dwelling place In all generations.

**90:2**
Zolai: Mual liante a kipiansak ma, leitang le leitung na bawl ma pek, a tawntung a kipan a tawntung dongin Pasian na hi hi.
English: Before the mountains were brought forth, or ever thou hadst formed the earth and the world, Even from everlasting to everlasting, thou art God.

**90:3**
Zolai: Mi, leivui na suaksakkik a, “Mihingte aw, ciahkik un,” na ci hi.
English: Thou turnest man to destruction; And sayest, Return, ye children of men.

**90:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma muhna-ah kum tulkhat a bei ciangin zanni ahi a, zan ihmut laitakin khanlawh khat sung tawh ahi zongin a kibang bek hi.
English: For a thousand years in thy sight are but as yesterday When it is past, and as a watch in the night.

**90:5**
Zolai: Nangmah in mite na phiatkhia hi. Amaute pen a ihmu tawh kibang uh a, zingsangin a nokik lopa tawh kibang uh hi.
English: Thou carriest them away as with a flood; they are as a sleep: In the morning they are like grass which groweth up.

**90:6**
Zolai: Zingsangin palhin thaksuak kik a, nitak ciangin vulin a keu uh hi.
English: In the morning it flourisheth, and groweth up; In the evening it is cut down, and withereth.

**90:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma sinsona in kote hong susia a, na hehluatna in kote hong lausak gawp hi.
English: For we are consumed by thine anger, And by thy wrath are we troubled.

**90:8**
Zolai: Nangmah in ka mawhnate uh na mai-ah na koih a, ka khialh simnate uh na maitangah na koih hi.
English: Thou hast set our iniquities before thee, Our secret sins in the light of thy countenance.

**90:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka hun khempeuh uh na hehna-in bei a, ka nuntak hun uh husan’ khat bangin a bei hi.
English: For all our days are passed away in thy wrath: We spend our years as a tale that is told .

**90:10**
Zolai: Kote’ nuntak sung kum sawmsagih bang hi a, cidam le-ung kum sawmgiat bang hithei hi. Ahih hangin tua hunsung nangawn gimna le haksatna hi a, tua hunte bei pakin kote ka maimang uh hi.
English: The days of our years are threescore years and ten; And if by reason of strength they be fourscore years, Yet is their strength labour and sorrow; For it is soon cut off, and we fly away.

**90:11**
Zolai: Nang hong kizahtak nadingin na sinsona’ vangliatna kua in thei a, na hehna’ husiatna kua in thei ahi hiam?
English: Who knoweth the power of thine anger? Even according to thy fear, so is thy wrath.

**90:12**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin pilna lungsim ka ngah theih nadingun ka nuntak hun uh a tomlam ka theih nadingun hong hilh in.
English: So teach us to number our days, That we may apply our hearts unto wisdom.

**90:13**
