Zolai: Topa aw, hong kihei kik in. Bang tan sauvei ding hiam? Na nasemte hong hehpih in.
English: Return, O LORD , how long? And let it repent thee concerning thy servants.

**90:14**
Zolai: Ka nuntak tawntung uh lungdamin ka kipak theih nadingun zingsangin na itna kip tawh kote hong lungkimsak in.
English: O satisfy us early with thy mercy; That we may rejoice and be glad all our days.

**90:15**
Zolai: Kote nong gimsak ni zah, siatna ka thuak uh kum phazah mah, kote hong kipaaksak in.
English: Make us glad according to the days wherein thou hast afflicted us, And the years wherein we have seen evil.

**90:16**
Zolai: Na nasemte tungah na nasepna, a tate uh tungah na minthanna, na vang hong kilangsak in.
English: Let thy work appear unto thy servants, And thy glory unto their children.

**90:17**
Zolai: Kote’ Topa Pasian aw, kote tungah na thupha hong tungsak inla, kote’ nasepna khempeuh hong tangtungsak in.
English: And let the beauty of the LORD our God be upon us: And establish thou the work of our hands upon us; Yea, the work of our hands establish thou it.

## Chapter 91

**91:1**
Zolai: Sangpenpa’ liahna sung, Vanglianpa’ liim sungah a om mi khempeuh in
English: He that dwelleth in the secret place of the Most High Shall abide under the shadow of the Almighty.

**91:2**
Zolai: Topa’ tungah, “Ka bukna le ka munkip muanhuai, ka muan ka Pasian na hi hi,” ci ding uh hi.
English: I will say of the LORD , He is my refuge and my fortress: My God; in him will I trust.

**91:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in thangsiah pa’ thangzak le a lauhuai pulnatna panin nang hong honkhia ding hi.
English: Surely he shall deliver thee from the snare of the fowler, And from the noisome pestilence.

**91:4**
Zolai: Amah in a khate tawh nang hong tuam ding a, ama khate’ nuai-ah bukna ding na mu ding hi. Ama thumanna in nang hong dalin hong hu ding hi.
English: He shall cover thee with his feathers, and under his wings shalt thou trust: His truth shall be thy shield and buckler.

**91:5**
Zolai: Nangmah in zan a lauhuaina, sun-a thaltang leengte, khuamial lakah a vak khiankhian pulnatna, sun nitaang a suksiatnate na kihta kei ding hi.
English: Thou shalt not be afraid for the terror by night; Nor for the arrow that flieth by day;

**91:7**
Zolai: Na kiangah mi tulkhat, na kimkotah mi tul sawm, hong tukin a sih hangin bangmah na ci kei ding hi.
English: A thousand shall fall at thy side, and ten thousand at thy right hand; But it shall not come nigh thee.

**91:8**
Zolai: Na mit tawh na en bek ding a, migilote a kithukkikna na mu ding hi.
English: Only with thine eyes shalt thou behold And see the reward of the wicked.

**91:9**
Zolai: Nangmah in Topa pen na buk nadingin bawlin, Sangpenpa, nang a hong hu dingin bawl khin na hih manin
English: Because thou hast made the LORD , which is my refuge, Even the most High, thy habitation;

**91:10**
Zolai: nangma tungah siatna hong tung lo ding a, na inn sungah gimna hong tung lo ding hi.
English: There shall no evil befall thee, Neither shall any plague come nigh thy dwelling.

**91:11**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh nangmah a hong cing dingin amah in ama vantungmi nang hong kemsak ding hi.
English: For he shall give his angels charge over thee, To keep thee in all thy ways.

**91:12**
Zolai: Na khete le suang a kitahkhak loh nadingin amaute in a khut uh tawh nang hong dom ding uh hi.
English: They shall bear thee up in their hands, Lest thou dash thy foot against a stone.

**91:13**
Zolai: Nangmah in humpinelkai le gul gunei tung na tawn ding a, na khenuai-ah humpinelkai khanglai le gulpi na tuancil ding hi.
English: Thou shalt tread upon the lion and adder: The young lion and the dragon shalt thou trample under feet.

**91:14**
Zolai: Itna tawh hong bel ahih manin amah ka honkhia ding a, ka min hong thei ahih manin mun sangna-ah amah ka koih ding hi.
English: Because he hath set his love upon me, therefore will I deliver him: I will set him on high, because he hath known my name.

**91:15**
Zolai: Amah in hong sap ciangin amah ka dawng ding hi. Haksatna sungah amah ka ompih ding a, amah honkhia-in ka pahtawi ding hi.
English: He shall call upon me, and I will answer him: I will be with him in trouble; I will deliver him, and honour him.

**91:16**
Zolai: Nuntak sau tawh amah ka lungkimsak ding a, amah ka honkhia ding hi.
English: With long life will I satisfy him, And shew him my salvation.

## Chapter 92

**92:1**
Zolai: Sangpenpa aw, Topa tungah lungdamna lah ding, nangma min phatna la sak dingin kilawm a, zangsawm khausai lasakna le harp lasakna, laiza lasaknate tumin, zingsangin nangma itna kip, zanin na thumanna genkhiat dingin a kilawm ahi hi.
English: It is a good thing to give thanks unto the LORD , And to sing praises unto thy name, O most High:

**92:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa aw, nangma sepna tawh kei nong lungdamsak a, nangma sepnate hangin lungdamin la ka sa hi.
English: For thou, LORD , hast made me glad through thy work: I will triumph in the works of thy hands.

**92:5**
Zolai: Topa aw, na nasepnate lian mahmah a, na ngaihsutnate thuk mahmah hi.
English: O LORD , how great are thy works! And thy thoughts are very deep.

**92:6**
Zolai: Migilote, lopa bangin selkhia-in, siatna bawl khempeuh a pun’ mahmah hangun, a tawntungin siatna a thuak ding uh ahi hi. Ahih hangin Topa aw, nang pen a sangna-ah a omden na hihna thu, lungsimmawl mi in theithei lo a, lungsim tei lo mi in tel thei lo hi.
English: A brutish man knoweth not; Neither doth a fool understand this.

**92:9**
Zolai: Topa aw, na galte si ta ding! Bang hang hiam cih leh na galte beimang ding a, siatna a bawl khempeuhte kithehthang ding uh hi.
English: For, lo, thine enemies, O LORD , for, lo, thine enemies shall perish; All the workers of iniquity shall be scattered.

**92:10**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nangmah in zangsial bangin kei na hong hatsak a, kei thupha hong pia-in nong lungdamsak hi.
English: But my horn shalt thou exalt like the horn of an unicorn: I shall be anointed with fresh oil.

**92:11**
Zolai: Ka galte’ pukna ka mit in mu khinta a, keimah a hong do a gilote’ siatna ka bil in za khinta hi.
English: Mine eye also shall see my desire on mine enemies, And mine ears shall hear my desire of the wicked that rise up against me.

**92:12**
Zolai: Nisuh kung bangin thuman mi palh a, Lebanon mualtung a om taamtak kung bangin a khang hi.
English: The righteous shall flourish like the palm tree: He shall grow like a cedar in Lebanon.

**92:13**
Zolai: Topa’ inn sungah amaute kisuan a, i Pasian’ huang sungah amaute palh uh hi.
English: Those that be planted in the house of the LORD Shall flourish in the courts of our God.

**92:14**
Zolai: Topa thutang hi, ci-in a lah nadingun amaute teek napi-in gah lailai uh a, amaute tui kiuhkeuhin hing sitset uh hi. Amah pen kei hong hupa hi a, ama sungah thuman lohna om lo hi.
English: They shall still bring forth fruit in old age; They shall be fat and flourishing;

## Chapter 93

**93:1**
Zolai: Topa in uk a, vangliatna kumpi puan kisilhsak hi. Topa, kumpi puan kisilhsak a, thahatna tawh amah kidim hi. Leitung kikipsak a, kiling ngei lo ding hi.
English: The LORD reigneth, he is clothed with majesty; The LORD is clothed with strength, wherewith he hath girded himself: The world also is stablished, That it cannot be moved.

**93:2**
Zolai: Tanglai pek panin na tokhom a kipsa hi a, nang pen a tawntung a om na hi hi.
English: Thy throne is established of old: Thou art from everlasting.

**93:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, gunte hong khangin, a aw uh hong sangsak a, nakpitakin hong ging hi.
English: The floods have lifted up, O LORD , the floods have lifted up their voice; The floods lift up their waves.

**93:4**
Zolai: A sangna munah a om Topa vanglian hi. Tui tampi gingte sangin vanglian zaw a, tuipi hualte sangin vanglian zaw hi.
English: The LORD on high is mightier than the noise of many waters, Yea, than the mighty waves of the sea.

**93:5**
Zolai: Na thupiaknate kip mahmah hi. Topa aw, sianthona pen a tawntungin na inn tawh a kilawm ahi hi.
English: Thy testimonies are very sure: Holiness becometh thine house, O LORD , for ever.

## Chapter 94

**94:1**
Zolai: A thukkik Pasian, a thukkik Pasian, Topa aw, na hehna hong lakkhia in.
English: O LORD God, to whom vengeance belongeth; O God, to whom vengeance belongeth, shew thyself.

**94:2**
Zolai: Tho in, leitung thukhen pa aw, a kiphasak mite tungah amau’ ngah ding a kilawm gimna pia ta in.
English: Lift up thyself, thou judge of the earth: Render a reward to the proud.

**94:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, migilote bang tanvei lungdam ding uh a, migilote bang tanvei lungnuamin omom lai ding ahi uh hiam?
English: LORD , how long shall the wicked, How long shall the wicked triumph?

**94:4**
Zolai: Gamtatsiate bang tanvei kihisak lai ding uh a, a siat gamtatna uh bang tanvei kisialhpih lai ding ahi uh hiam?
English: How long shall they utter and speak hard things? And all the workers of iniquity boast themselves?

**94:5**
Zolai: Topa aw, amaute in nangma mite sugawp uh a, nangma luahte gimsak uh hi.
English: They break in pieces thy people, O LORD , And afflict thine heritage.

**94:6**
Zolai: Amaute in meigong numeite le khualmite thatlumin pa nei lote suamlum uh hi.
English: They slay the widow and the stranger, And murder the fatherless.

**94:7**
Zolai: Amaute in, “ Topa in mu lo hi; Jakob Pasian in thei lo hi,” hong ci uh hi.
English: Yet they say, The LORD shall not see, Neither shall the God of Jacob regard it .

**94:8**
Zolai: Theitel un, mi lungsimmawl pente aw! Lung pillote aw, cik ciangin pil ding na hi uh hiam?
English: Understand, ye brutish among the people: And ye fools, when will ye be wise?

**94:9**
Zolai: I bil a bawlpa in khua za lo ding ahi hiam? I mit a piangsak pa in khua mu lo ding ahi hiam?
English: He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? He that formed the eye, shall he not see?

**94:10**
Zolai: Minamte a thuhilhpa in mi thuhilh lo ding ahi hiam? Mihingte tungah theihtheihna a hilh Topa in mihingte’ ngaihsutna thei a, amaute pen husan’ bang bek ahihna teltakin a thei hi.
English: He that chastiseth the heathen, shall not he correct? He that teacheth man knowledge, shall not he know?

**94:12**
Zolai: Topa aw, migilote a dingin gum khat a kitawh hun mateng, haksat hun sungteng a tawlngak theih nadingin na thukham na hilh mi, na thuhilh mi, mi nuamsa ahi hi.
English: Blessed is the man whom thou chastenest, O LORD , And teachest him out of thy law;

**94:14**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in ama mite nusia lo ding a, ama luahte paidak lo ding hi.
English: For the LORD will not cast off his people, Neither will he forsake his inheritance.

**94:15**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh thutang pen thuman mite tungah hong tungkik ding a, lungsim thutang khempeuh in amah zui ding uh hi.
English: But judgment shall return unto righteousness: And all the upright in heart shall follow it.

**94:16**
Zolai: Kei a dingin migilote a do dingin kua kipan ahi hiam? Kei a dingin siatna a bawlte’ langkhatah kua ding ahi hiam?
English: Who will rise up for me against the evildoers? Or who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity?

**94:17**
Zolai: Topa in kei hong huh lo hileh, gamkhing sungah ka tung khinta ding hi.
English: Unless the LORD had been my help, My soul had almost dwelt in silence.

**94:18**
Zolai: Topa aw, “Ka khe taal,” ci-in ka ngaihsut ciangin na itna kip in kei hong kaito hi.
English: When I said, My foot slippeth; Thy mercy, O LORD , held me up.

**94:19**
Zolai: Ka lungsim ngaihsutna a tam mahmah ciangin kei na hong hehnem a, na hong lungdamsak hi.
English: In the multitude of my thoughts within me Thy comforts delight my soul.

**94:20**
Zolai: Sihna ding ngeina a bawl, a gilo gam ukte, nang tawh kipawl ding ahi hiam?
English: Shall the throne of iniquity have fellowship with thee, Which frameth mischief by a law?

**94:21**
Zolai: Amaute in thuman mihoihte thah sawm uh a, a mawhbaang lo mite sihna thuaksak uh hi.
English: They gather themselves together against the soul of the righteous, And condemn the innocent blood.

**94:22**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa pen keima munkip, keima Pasian, ka belh suangpi a suak khinta hi.
English: But the LORD is my defence; And my God is the rock of my refuge.

**94:23**
Zolai: Amah in amau’ mawhnate amau’ tung mahah tungsakkikin, a gitlohna hangun amaute a maimangsak ding hi. Topa, i Pasian in amaute maimangsak ding hi.
English: And he shall bring upon them their own iniquity, and shall cut them off in their own wickedness; Yea , the LORD our God shall cut them off.

## Chapter 95

**95:1**
Zolai: Hong pai un, Topa phat ni. Eite a hong hu, a hong honkhia pa tungah lungdamna la sa ni.
English: O come, let us sing unto the LORD : Let us make a joyful noise to the rock of our salvation.

**95:2**
Zolai: Ama omna-ah lungdamna ko-in pai ni. Phatna late, ama tungah lungdam takin sa ni.
English: Let us come before his presence with thanksgiving, And make a joyful noise unto him with psalms.

**95:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa, a lian Pasian hi a, pasian khempeuh tungah Kumpi lianpa ahi hi.
English: For the LORD is a great God, And a great King above all gods.

**95:4**
Zolai: Amah in leitung khempeuh uk a, guam thuk pen panin mual sang pen dawn dongin amah in a uk hi.
English: In his hand are the deep places of the earth: The strength of the hills is his also.

**95:5**
Zolai: Ama bawlsa tuipite uk a, ama bawlsa leitung zong amah in a uk hi.
English: The sea is his, and he made it: And his hands formed the dry land .

**95:6**
Zolai: Hong pai un, amah bia-in kun ni. Eite hong Bawl Topa’ mai-ah khukdin ni.
English: O come, let us worship and bow down: Let us kneel before the LORD our maker.

**95:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah pen eite’ Pasian hi a, eite pen ama hong kep mite le ama khutsunga om a tuute ihi hi. Tuni-in hih bangin ama hong thugen za un:
English: For he is our God; And we are the people of his pasture, and the sheep of his hand. To day if ye will hear his voice,

**95:8**
Zolai: Amaute in ka nasepna mu khin uh hinapi, Meribah le Massah munah na pate un kei hong ze-etin, gamtatna tawh ka lah ding hong kalh hun lai uh bangin, note in na lungsim uh khauhsak kei un.
English: Harden not your heart, As in the provocation, and as in the day of temptation in the wilderness:

**95:10**
Zolai: Kum sawmli sung tua minam ka kih a, “Amaute pen a lungsim uhah a khial mi hi a, amaute in ka thupiakte mang lo uh hi,” ka ci hi.
English: Forty years long was I grieved with this generation, And said, It is a people that do err in their heart, and they have not known my ways:

**95:11**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin keima nopsakna munah amaute a lut lo dingin sinso kawmin ka kiciam hi.
English: Unto whom I sware in my wrath That they should not enter into my rest.

## Chapter 96

**96:1**
Zolai: Leitung mi khempeuh aw, Topa tungah la thak khat sa un. Topa tungah la sa un.
English: O Sing unto the LORD a new song: Sing unto the LORD , all the earth.

**96:2**
Zolai: Topa tungah la sa unla, ama min phat un. Ni khat khit ni khat ama hong hotkhiatna thu gen tawntung un.
English: Sing unto the LORD , bless his name; Shew forth his salvation from day to day.

**96:3**
Zolai: Ama minthanna minamte lakah gen unla, ama nalamdang septe mi khempeuh lakah pulak un.
English: Declare his glory among the heathen, His wonders among all people.

**96:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa lian a, nakpitakin phat ding ahi hi; pasian dangte khempeuh sangin amah zahtak zawk ding ahi hi.
English: For the LORD is great, and greatly to be praised: He is to be feared above all gods.

**96:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh minam dangte’ pasian khempeuh milim hi lel a, ahih hangin Topa ahihleh vantungte a bawlpa ahi hi.
English: For all the gods of the nations are idols: But the LORD made the heavens.

**96:6**
Zolai: Pahtawina le liatnate ama mai-ah om a, hatna le hoihnate ama omna mun siangtho-ah om hi.
English: Honour and majesty are before him: Strength and beauty are in his sanctuary.

**96:7**
Zolai: Mi namkimte aw, Topa in minthanna le hatna nei hi, ci-in mang un. Topa in nei hi, ci-in mang un.
English: Give unto the LORD , O ye kindreds of the people, Give unto the LORD glory and strength.

**96:8**
Zolai: Ama min in a ngah dingin a kilawm minthanna Topa’ tungah pia unla, biakpiakna hong kengin ama huang sungah hong pai un.
English: Give unto the LORD the glory due unto his name: Bring an offering, and come into his courts.

**96:9**
Zolai: Puan siangtho silhin Topa bia un. Leitung mi khempeuh aw, ama mai-ah ling un.
English: O worship the LORD in the beauty of holiness: Fear before him, all the earth.

**96:10**
Zolai: Minam khempeuh lakah thu gen kawikawi unla, “ Topa in uk hi. Leitung kikipsak a, kiling ngei lo ding hi. Amah in mihingte’ thu a manin khen ding hi,” ci un.
English: Say among the heathen that the LORD reigneth: The world also shall be established that it shall not be moved: He shall judge the people righteously.

**96:11**
Zolai: Vantung mite kipak hen la, leitung mite lungdam hen. Tuipi le a sunga om khempeuh awng ta uh hen.
English: Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad; Let the sea roar, and the fulness thereof.

**96:12**
Zolai: Lo le a sunga om khempeuh nuamin diang uh hen. Gamlak a sing om khempeuh in Topa’ mai-ah lungdamin la sa hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah hong pai ta hi. Leitung mite’ thu a khen dingin hong pai ta hi. Amah in thumanna tawh leitung ukin mite’ thu ahi bangin khen ding hi.
English: Let the field be joyful, and all that is therein: Then shall all the trees of the wood rejoice

## Chapter 97

**97:1**
Zolai: Topa in uk hi. Leitung lungdam hen la, tuikulh neu tampite zong lungdam ta uh hen.
English: The LORD reigneth; let the earth rejoice; Let the multitude of isles be glad thereof .

**97:2**
Zolai: Meiipite le khuamial sahpite ama kiimah om a, thumanna le thutannate ama tokhom bulpi ahi hi.
English: Clouds and darkness are round about him: Righteousness and judgment are the habitation of his throne.

**97:3**
Zolai: Ama mai-ah mei pai a, ama kiima om a galte a kangtum hi.
English: A fire goeth before him, And burneth up his enemies round about.

**97:4**
Zolai: Ama khuaphialepte in leitung taangsak a, leitung in mu-in a ling hi.
English: His lightnings enlightened the world: The earth saw, and trembled.

**97:5**
Zolai: Topa’ mai, leitung mi khempeuh’ Topa’ mai-ah mual liante khuainun bangin a tuisuak uh hi.
English: The hills melted like wax at the presence of the LORD , At the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.

**97:6**
Zolai: Vantungte in ama thumanna genkhia uh a, mi khempeuh in ama minthanna mu uh hi.
English: The heavens declare his righteousness, And all the people see his glory.

**97:7**
Zolai: Bangmah a man lo milimte a kisaktheihpih, milim a bia mi khempeuhte maizumin kikoih a, ama mai-ah pasian khempeuh kun uh hi.
English: Confounded be all they that serve graven images, That boast themselves of idols: Worship him, all ye gods.

**97:8**
Zolai: Pasian aw, Zion in za-in nuam a, na thukhennate hangin Judah khuapite lungdam uh hi.
English: Zion heard, and was glad; And the daughters of Judah rejoiced because of thy judgments, O LORD .

**97:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa aw, leitung khempeuh a ukpa na hi a, pasian dang khempeuh sangin nakpitakin na lianzaw hi.
English: For thou, LORD , art high above all the earth: Thou art exalted far above all gods.

**97:10**
Zolai: Topa in gitlohna a mudahte it a, amah in a mi siangthote’ nuntakna siatna ding pan a kem hi. Amah in migilote’ khutsung panin amaute a honkhia hi.
English: Ye that love the LORD , hate evil: He preserveth the souls of his saints; He delivereth them out of the hand of the wicked.

**97:11**
Zolai: Thuman mite’ tungah khuavak hong taang a, lungsim thutang mite tungah lungdamna hong tung hi.
English: Light is sown for the righteous, And gladness for the upright in heart.

**97:12**
Zolai: Thuman mite aw, Topa’ nasepnate hangin lungdam unla, ama min siangtho phat un.
English: Rejoice in the LORD , ye righteous; And give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.

## Chapter 98

**98:1**
Zolai: Amah in na lamdangte bawl ahih manin Topa’ tungah la thak sa un. Ama khut taklam le ama khut siangthote in amah gualzosak hi.
English: O sing unto the LORD a new song; For he hath done marvellous things: His right hand, and his holy arm, Hath gotten him the victory.

**98:2**
Zolai: Topa in ama gualzawhna kitheisak khinzo a, amah in minamte’ muhna-ah ama thumanna langsak khin hi.
English: The LORD hath made known his salvation: His righteousness hath he openly shewed in the sight of the heathen.

**98:3**
Zolai: Amah thutakin, it tawntungna nei ahih manin Israel-te tungah a thuciamna a tungsak hi. Leitung mi khempeuh in eite’ Pasian’ gualzawhna mu khinta uh hi.
English: He hath remembered his mercy and his truth toward the house of Israel: All the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God.

**98:4**
Zolai: Leitung mi khempeuh aw, Topa’ tungah lungdamin la sa-in lungdamin awngkhia unla, phatna la sa un.
English: Make a joyful noise unto the LORD , all the earth: Make a loud noise, and rejoice, and sing praise.

**98:5**
Zolai: Laia lasakna tawh Topa’ tungah phatna late sa unla, laiza lasakna le la ngaih tawh phat un.
English: Sing unto the LORD with the harp; With the harp, and the voice of a psalm.

**98:6**
Zolai: Peengkulte le saki aw tawh Topa, Kumpipa’ mai-ah lungdamna gingsak un.
English: With trumpets and sound of cornet Make a joyful noise before the LORD , the King.

**98:7**
Zolai: Tuipi le a sunga omte khempeuh aw, awng unla, leitung le a tunga teng khempeuhte aw, la sa un.
English: Let the sea roar, and the fulness thereof; The world, and they that dwell therein.

**98:8**
Zolai: Gunte aw, na khut uh beeng un. Mualte aw, Topa’ mai-ah lungdamin la sa un. Bang hang hiam cih leh leitung a uk dingin amah hong pai ta a, thumanna tawh leitung mite’ thu ahi ding bangin hong khen ding hi.
English: Let the floods clap their hands: Let the hills be joyful together

## Chapter 99

**99:1**
Zolai: Topa in uk hi. Mihonte ling hen. Kherub-te tungah amah tu hi. Leitung ling tahen.
English: The LORD reigneth; let the people tremble: He sitteth between the cherubims; let the earth be moved.

**99:2**
Zolai: Zion khuapi-ah Topa lian a, amah in leitung mi khempeuh uk hi.
English: The LORD is great in Zion; And he is high above all the people.

**99:3**
Zolai: A lian a kihtakhuai ama min mi khempeuh in phat ta uh hen. Amah siangtho hi.
English: Let them praise thy great and terrible name; For it is holy.

**99:4**
Zolai: Thutang a deih, Vanglian Kumpipa aw, nangmah in thuman na phut khin a, Israel-te sungah thutang le thuman na semkhia hi.
English: The king's strength also loveth judgment; Thou dost establish equity, Thou executest judgment and righteousness in Jacob.

**99:5**
Zolai: I Topa Pasian phat unla, ama khengakna munah bia un. Amah siangtho hi.
English: Exalt ye the LORD our God, And worship at his footstool; For he is holy.

**99:6**
Zolai: Moses le Aaron-te ama siampi hi uh a, amah a biate lakah Samuel zong a kihel hi. Topa’ tungah amaute kiko uh a, amah in amaute a dawng hi.
English: Moses and Aaron among his priests, and Samuel among them that call upon his name; They called upon the LORD , and he answered them.

**99:7**
Zolai: Amah in meii khuampi sung pan amaute tungah thu gen a, ama teci pannate le amah in amaute tungah a thukham piakte amaute in a zui uh hi.
English: He spake unto them in the cloudy pillar: They kept his testimonies, and the ordinance that he gave them.

**99:8**
Zolai: Kote’ Topa Pasian aw, nang in amaute na dawng hi. Amau’ mawhna hangin gim na piak tei hangin amau’ mawhnate a maisak nuam Pasian na hihna amaute’ tungah na kilangsak hi.
English: Thou answeredst them, O LORD our God: Thou wast a God that forgavest them, though thou tookest vengeance of their inventions.

**99:9**
Zolai: I Topa Pasian phat unla, ama mual siangtho-ah bia un; bang hang hiam cih leh i Topa Pasian a siangtho hi.
English: Exalt the LORD our God, and worship at his holy hill; For the LORD our God is holy.

## Chapter 100

**100:1**
Zolai: Gam khempeuh aw, Topa’ tungah lungdamna aw gingsak un.
English: Make a joyful noise unto the LORD , all ye lands.

**100:2**
Zolai: Lungdamna tawh Topa’ na sem un. Ama omna-ah la sa kawmin hong pai un.
English: Serve the LORD with gladness: Come before his presence with singing.

**100:3**
Zolai: Topa, Pasian ahihna thei un. Eite hong bawlpa amah hi a, eite ama a’ ihi hi. Eite ama mi ihi a, ama gankhahna sunga om a tuute ihi hi.
English: Know ye that the LORD he is God: It is he that hath made us, and not we ourselves; We are his people, and the sheep of his pasture.

**100:4**
Zolai: Lungdam kohna tawh ama kongpi-ah lut unla, amah phatna tawh ama huang sungah tum un. Ama tungah lungdam ko unla, ama min phat un.
English: Enter into his gates with thanksgiving, And into his courts with praise: Be thankful unto him, and bless his name.

**100:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa hoih hi. Ama itna kipin kho tawntung a, ama thumanna a khang khangin kip hi.
English: For the LORD is good; his mercy is everlasting; And his truth endureth to all generations.

## Chapter 101

**101:1**
Zolai: Keima la pen thumanna le thutanna la ahi hi. Nang ka hong sak ding hi; Topa aw, kong sak ding hi.
English: I will sing of mercy and judgment: Unto thee, O LORD , will I sing.

**101:2**
Zolai: Paubaanna a om lo thu bek ka kin ding hi. Cik ciangin kei kiangah hong pai ding na hi hiam? Lungsim hoihna tawh ka inn sungah ka gamta ding hi.
English: I will behave myself wisely In a perfect way. O when wilt thou come unto me? I will walk within my house with a perfect heart.

**101:3**
Zolai: A sia na peuhmah ka deih kei ding hi. Lamkhial mite’ nasepna ka mudah a, tuate tawh ka kisukha kei ding hi.
English: I will set no wicked thing before mine eyes: I hate the work of them that turn aside; It shall not cleave to me.

**101:4**
Zolai: Lungsim kawina ka deih hetkei a, siatna, ngaihsutin zong ka neikha kei ding hi.
English: A froward heart shall depart from me: I will not know a wicked person .

**101:5**
Zolai: A vengte a gensia sim mite ka susia ding a, kiphatsakna, kihihsakna lungsim a nei mi ka thuak kei ding hi.
English: Whoso privily slandereth his neighbour, Him will I cut off: Him that hath an high look And a proud heart will not I suffer.

**101:6**
Zolai: Leitungah a thuman mite kei tawh a om theih nadingin maipha ka pia ding a, paubaanna om loin a gamta mi in keima na hong sem ding hi.
English: Mine eyes shall be upon the faithful Of the land, that they may dwell with me: He that walketh in a perfect way, He shall serve me.

**101:7**
Zolai: Khemna a zang mi peuhmah keima inn-ah teng lo ding a, zuauthu a gen mi peuhmah keima omna-ah om thei nawn lo ding hi.
English: He that worketh deceit shall not dwell within my house: He that telleth lies shall not tarry in my sight.

**101:8**
Zolai: Zingsang simin leitung a migilote khempeuh ka susia ding a, Topa’ khuapi panin siatna bawlte khempeuh ka khenkhia ding hi.
English: I will early destroy all the wicked of the land; That I may cut off All wicked doers from the city of the LORD .

## Chapter 102

**102:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka thungetna hong za inla, ka thumna hong ngai in.
English: Hear my prayer, O LORD , And let my cry come unto thee.

**102:2**
Zolai: Ka cihmawh hunin kei kiang panin bu kei in. Keima lam hong nga inla, kong sap ciangin hong dawng pah in.
English: Hide not thy face from me in the day when I am in trouble; Incline thine ear unto me: In the day when I call answer me speedily.

**102:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka nuntakna, meikhu bangin beimang a, ka pumpi meikuang bangin a sa hi.
English: For my days are consumed like smoke, And my bones are burned as an hearth.

**102:4**
Zolai: Lungkham luatna hangin lopa bangin ka keutum a, an nangawn ka nezo kei hi.
English: My heart is smitten, and withered like grass; So that I forget to eat my bread.

**102:5**
Zolai: A gingin ka tautauna hangin ka guh guakin ka om hi.
English: By reason of the voice of my groaning My bones cleave to my skin.

**102:6**
Zolai: Gamlak a om musane le mun kolhna-ah a om simbu tawh ka kibang hi.
English: I am like a pelican of the wilderness: I am like an owl of the desert.

**102:7**
Zolai: Ihmu thei loin ka om a, innkhum dawna vasa khat guak a om tawh ka kibang hi.
English: I watch, and am as a sparrow Alone upon the house top.

**102:8**
Zolai: Sun nilohin ka galte in kei hong zahko uh a, kei hong simmawhte in samsiatna-in ka min a zang uh hi.
English: Mine enemies reproach me all the day; And they that are mad against me are sworn against me.

**102:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh vut bek ka annek hita a, na thangpaihna le na hehna hangin ka tuidawnte khitui tawh kihel hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang in kei hong domto napi-in lei nong denna hi.
English: For I have eaten ashes like bread, And mingled my drink with weeping,

**102:11**
Zolai: Keima nuntakna pen nitak lama a om niliim tawh kibang lel a, lopa bangin ka vulgawp hi.
English: My days are like a shadow that declineth; And I am withered like grass.

**102:12**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa aw, nang na kip ngitnget a, khang tawntungin nang hong kiphawkna kip hi.
English: But thou, O LORD , shalt endure for ever; And thy remembrance unto all generations.

**102:13**
Zolai: Nangmah tho-in Zion khua na hehpih ding hi. Amah na angvan hun ding hita a, a kiciangtansa hun hong tung khin hi.
English: Thou shalt arise, and have mercy upon Zion: For the time to favour her, yea, the set time, is come.

**102:14**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh na nasemte in tua khua suangtumte it uh a, a leivuite nangawn pammaih sa uh hi.
English: For thy servants take pleasure in her stones, And favour the dust thereof.

**102:15**
Zolai: Minamte in Topa hong zahtakin, leitung kumpi khempeuh in na minthanna hong zahtak ding uh hi.
English: So the heathen shall fear the name of the LORD , And all the kings of the earth thy glory.

**102:16**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in Zion khua lam ding a, ama minthanna hong kilang ding hi.
English: When the LORD shall build up Zion, He shall appear in his glory.

**102:17**
Zolai: Amah in mi cimawhte’ thungetna kinin, amau’ thumna simmawh lo ding hi.
English: He will regard the prayer of the destitute, And not despise their prayer.

**102:18**
Zolai: A suak nai lo mite in Topa a phat theih nadingin a hong tung lai ding khang mite a dingin hih thu kiciamteh hen:
English: This shall be written for the generation to come: And the people which shall be created shall praise the LORD .

**102:19**
Zolai: Mihingte, kumpi gamte, Topa a bia dingin a kikaihkhop uh ciangin, mite in Zion khua sungah Topa’ min, Jerusalem khua sungah amah phatna a pulak theih nadingun, thongkiate’ taunate a za ding le a si dingin a kisehte a khahkhia dingin a sangna ama siangtho mun panin amah in hong ensukin, vantung panin Topa in leitung hong en hi.
English: For he hath looked down from the height of his sanctuary; From heaven did the LORD behold the earth;

**102:23**
Zolai: Amah in kei a khangtung kimlai ka thahatna hong suktat sakin, ka hunte hong khiapsak hi.
English: He weakened my strength in the way; He shortened my days.

**102:24**
Zolai: Keimah in, “Khang tawntungin a kip ka Pasian aw, hong khansihsak kei in,” ka ci hi.
English: I said, O my God, take me not away in the midst of my days: Thy years are throughout all generations.

**102:25**
Zolai: Tanglai hunin nangmah in leitung bulpi na koih a, vantungte zong nangma khut tawh na bawlsa ahi hi.
English: Of old hast thou laid the foundation of the earth: And the heavens are the work of thy hands.

**102:26**
Zolai: Amaute sia ding uh a, ahih hangin nang na kip ding hi. Puan bangin amaute paatkhia ding uh hi. Nangmah in amaute puan bangin na khek a, amaute a maimang uh hi.
English: They shall perish, but thou shalt endure: Yea, all of them shall wax old like a garment; As a vesture shalt thou change them, and they shall be changed:

**102:27**
Zolai: Ahi zongin nang na kibang ngitnget a, na nuntak hun in mong nei lo hi.
English: But thou art the same, and thy years shall have no end.

**102:28**
Zolai: Na nasemte’ tate lungmuangin om ding uh a, amau’ suanlekhakte na mai-ah kip ding uh hi.
English: The children of thy servants shall continue, And their seed shall be established before thee.

## Chapter 103

**103:1**
Zolai: Topa ka phat ding a, ka lungsim khempeuh tawh ama min siangtho ka phat ding hi.
English: Bless the LORD , O my soul: And all that is within me, bless his holy name.

**103:2**
Zolai: Topa ka phat ding a, ama migitna ka mangngilh kei ding hi.
English: Bless the LORD , O my soul, And forget not all his benefits:

**103:3**
Zolai: Amah in ka mawhna khempeuh hong maisak a, ka natna khempeuh hong damsak hi.
English: Who forgiveth all thine iniquities; Who healeth all thy diseases;

**103:4**
Zolai: Hankhuk tung ding kimlai hong suaktasak a, itna le hehpihna tampi hong pia hi.
English: Who redeemeth thy life from destruction; Who crowneth thee with lovingkindness and tender mercies;

**103:5**
Zolai: Muvanlai bangin ka tha a hat theih nadingin thupha namkim hong pia hi.
English: Who satisfieth thy mouth with good things ; So that thy youth is renewed like the eagle's.

**103:6**
Zolai: Topa in a kinengniamte a dingin thuman thutangin thu a khen hi.
English: The LORD executeth righteousness and judgment For all that are oppressed.

**103:7**
Zolai: Amah in ama geelna Moses tungah gen a, ama nasepnate Israel mite a musak hi.
English: He made known his ways unto Moses, His acts unto the children of Israel.

**103:8**
Zolai: Topa dikin hehpihna tawh kidim a, heh hakin, a lian mahmah itna kip tawh a kidim hi.
English: The LORD is merciful and gracious, Slow to anger, and plenteous in mercy.

**103:9**
Zolai: Amah in a tawntungin hong taii ngitnget lo ding a, amah heh paisuak lo ding hi.
English: He will not always chide: Neither will he keep his anger for ever.

**103:10**
Zolai: Amah in eite’ khialhna tawh a kituakin eite tungah hong bawl lo a, eite’ mawhna tawh a kituakin hong thukkik lo hi.
English: He hath not dealt with us after our sins; Nor rewarded us according to our iniquities.

**103:11**
Zolai: Vantung pen leitung panin a san mah bangin amah a zahtakte’ tungah ama itna kip lianin sang mahmah hi.
English: For as the heaven is high above the earth, So great is his mercy toward them that fear him.

**103:12**
Zolai: Nisuahna pen nitumna panin a gamlat mah bangin i mawhna hangin gimnate eite’ kiang panin gamlapi-ah a nilkhia hi.
English: As far as the east is from the west, So far hath he removed our transgressions from us.

**103:13**
Zolai: Pa in tate a hehpih bangin Topa in amah a zahtakte hong hehpih hi.
English: Like as a father pitieth his children, So the LORD pitieth them that fear him.

**103:14**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in eite’ pianna hong thei a, eite pen leivui ihihna a phawk hi.
English: For he knoweth our frame; He remembereth that we are dust.

**103:15**
Zolai: Eite ihih leh i nuntakna pen lopa tawh kibang a, lolai-ah a po paakte bangin a palh hi.
English: As for man, his days are as grass: As a flower of the field, so he flourisheth.

**103:16**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh huih in amah semin beimang a, tua mun in amah thei nawn lo hi.
English: For the wind passeth over it, and it is gone; And the place thereof shall know it no more.

**103:17**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa’ itna kip pen amah a zahtak mite tungah a tawntung pan a tawntung dongin kip ngitnget a, ama thumanna pen ama thuciamna zui-in a thupiak bangin sep ding a phawk mite tungah a khang khangin a kip tawntung hi.
English: But the mercy of the LORD is from everlasting to everlasting upon them that fear him, And his righteousness unto children's children;

**103:19**
Zolai: Topa in vantungah ama tokhom phutkhin a, amah in mun khempeuh a uk hi.
English: The LORD hath prepared his throne in the heavens; And his kingdom ruleth over all.

**103:20**
Zolai: Ama thugen a ngai, ama thu bangin a sem no a thahat, no ama vantung mite aw, Topa phat un.
English: Bless the LORD , ye his angels, that excel in strength, That do his commandments, hearkening unto the voice of his word.

**103:21**
Zolai: Ama deih bangin a gamta ama nasem, ama mihon khempeuhte aw, Topa phat un.
English: Bless ye the LORD , all ye his hosts; Ye ministers of his, that do his pleasure.

**103:22**
Zolai: Ama ukna sunga a om ama bawlsate aw, Topa phat un. Ke’n, Topa ka phat ding hi.
English: Bless the LORD , all his works in all places of his dominion: Bless the LORD , O my soul.

## Chapter 104

**104:1**
Zolai: Topa ka phat ding hi. Topa ka Pasian aw, nang na lian mahmah hi. Minthanna le liatna nang na silh hi.
English: Bless the LORD , O my soul. O LORD my God, thou art very great; Thou art clothed with honour and majesty:

**104:2**
Zolai: Puanza tawh tuam bangin khuavak tawh na kituam a, vantungte pen puanbuk bangin na zal hi.
English: Who coverest thyself with light as with a garment: Who stretchest out the heavens like a curtain:

**104:3**
Zolai: Vana om tui tungah na inn na lam a, na leeng dingin meiipite na bawl a, huih khate tungah nang na tuang hi.
English: Who layeth the beams of his chambers in the waters: Who maketh the clouds his chariot: Who walketh upon the wings of the wind:

**104:4**
Zolai: Na kamtai dingin huihte na bawl a, mei le meikuangte na nasemte na hisak hi.
English: Who maketh his angels spirits; His ministers a flaming fire:

**104:5**
Zolai: Leitung a ling ngei lo dingin ama bulpi tungah na phut hi.
English: Who laid the foundations of the earth, That it should not be removed for ever.

**104:6**
Zolai: Nangmah in puan tawh tuam bangin leitung pen tui thukpi tawh na tuam a, tuate in mualte tuumcip hi.
English: Thou coveredst it with the deep as with a garment: The waters stood above the mountains.

**104:7**
Zolai: Na thuhilhna hangin tua tuite taikhia uh a, na thupiakna awging a zak uh ciangin kikhawhkhia uh hi.
English: At thy rebuke they fled; At the voice of thy thunder they hasted away.

**104:8**
Zolai: Mualtung le guam sungah tua tuite luang uh a, amau a dingin na sehsa munah a tung uh hi.
English: They go up by the mountains; they go down by the valleys Unto the place which thou hast founded for them.

**104:9**
Zolai: Tua tuite in leitung a tuamkik loh nadingin amaute’ kantan loh ding gamgi khat na phut hi.
English: Thou hast set a bound that they may not pass over; That they turn not again to cover the earth.

**104:10**
Zolai: Kuamte sung panin ciktui na phulkhiasak a, mualte kikalah a luang uh hi.
English: He sendeth the springs into the valleys, Which run among the hills.

**104:11**
Zolai: Gamlak ganhingte’ dawn ding tui na pia a, gamlak sakolte in a dangtakna uh tua tui-ah a phasak uh hi.
English: They give drink to every beast of the field: The wild asses quench their thirst.

**104:12**
Zolai: Tua tui kiangah huihlak vasate om uh a, singhiangte lakah amaute ham zaizai uh hi.
English: By them shall the fowls of the heaven have their habitation, Which sing among the branches.

**104:13**
Zolai: A sangna mun na omna panin mite tungah guah na zusak a, nangma thupha tawh leitung a kidim hi.
English: He watereth the hills from his chambers: The earth is satisfied with the fruit of thy works.

**104:14**
Zolai: Nangmah in ganhingte a dingin lopa, mihing in leilak panin an a ngah theih nadingin a khawh ding ankungte,
English: He causeth the grass to grow for the cattle, And herb for the service of man: That he may bring forth food out of the earth;

**104:15**
Zolai: mihing lungsim a nuamsak ding leenggahzu, mihing maitang a zolsak ding sathau, mihing lungsim a hatsak ding an na piangsak hi.
English: And wine that maketh glad the heart of man, And oil to make his face to shine, and bread which strengtheneth man's heart.

**104:16**
Zolai: Topa in a suan, Lebanon muala om taamtak singte, tua ama singkungte in guahtui tampi a ngah hi.
English: The trees of the LORD are full of sap ; The cedars of Lebanon, which he hath planted;

**104:17**
Zolai: Tua singte tungah vasate in bu bawl uh a, taksing kungte lakah gun vapite in bu a tom uh hi.
English: Where the birds make their nests: As for the stork, the fir trees are her house.

**104:18**
Zolai: Mual sangte pen sathakte a’ ding hi a, suangtumte pen sakhite’ belh ding ahi hi.
English: The high hills are a refuge for the wild goats; And the rocks for the conies.

**104:19**
Zolai: Hun ciamteh nadingin khapi na bawl a, ni in zong a tum ding hun a thei hi.
English: He appointed the moon for seasons: The sun knoweth his going down.

**104:20**
Zolai: Nangmah in khuamial na bawl a, gamlak ganhing khempeuh a vakkhiat hun pen zan hunsung ahi hi.
English: Thou makest darkness, and it is night: Wherein all the beasts of the forest do creep forth .

**104:21**
Zolai: Humpinelkai khanglaite in amau’ nek ding sa a ngah nadingun nakpitakin hawk uh a, amau’ an ding Pasian’ tung pan a ngah uh hi.
English: The young lions roar after their prey, And seek their meat from God.

**104:22**
Zolai: Ni a suah ciangin amaute kihemkhia uh a, a kua sung uhah a lum hithiat uh hi.
English: The sun ariseth, they gather themselves together, And lay them down in their dens.

**104:23**
Zolai: Mite pen nasem dingin kuankhia uh a, nitak mateng na sem uh hi.
English: Man goeth forth unto his work And to his labour until the evening.

**104:24**
Zolai: Topa aw, na sepsa nate tam mahmah hi. Nangmah in ciimna tawh tuate khempeuh na bawl a, na piansak ganhingte tawh leitung a kidim hi.
English: O LORD , how manifold are thy works! In wisdom hast thou made them all: The earth is full of thy riches.

**104:25**
Zolai: Hua lai-ah, ganhing a lian a neu, simzawh lohin a tam, a vak muamua-na, lianin a zai mahmah tuipi om hi.
English: So is this great and wide sea, Wherein are things creeping innumerable, both small and great beasts.

**104:26**
Zolai: Hua tuipi tungah teembawte le gualnop nadingin na bawl Awle a pai hi.
English: There go the ships: There is that leviathan, Whom thou hast made to play therein.

**104:27**
Zolai: A hun ciangin an na piak ding ngakin hihte khempeuh in nangmah hong en uh hi.
English: These wait all upon thee; That thou mayest give them their meat in due season.

**104:28**
Zolai: Na piak ciangin amaute in ne uh a, an na pia a, amaute lungkim uh hi.
English: That thou givest them they gather: Thou openest thine hand, they are filled with good.

**104:29**
Zolai: Na maitang na seel ciangin amaute khasia uh hi. Amau’ husanna na lakkhiat ciangin amaute si-in amau’ pianna leivui-ah a ciahkik uh hi.
English: Thou hidest thy face, they are troubled: Thou takest away their breath, they die, and return to their dust.

**104:30**
Zolai: Na hu na sankhiat ciangin amaute a kipiangsak hi a, nangmah in leitung na bawlthak hi.
English: Thou sendest forth thy spirit, they are created: And thou renewest the face of the earth.

**104:31**
Zolai: Leitung a et ciangin tua leitung kilingin, mualte a lawn’ ciangin tua mualte meikhu a suak, ama nasepna-ah Topa lungdam hen la, Topa’ minthanna kip tawntung tahen.
English: The glory of the LORD shall endure for ever: The LORD shall rejoice in his works.

**104:33**
Zolai: Ka nuntak laiteng Topa tungah la ka sa ding a, ka hin laiteng ka Pasian phatna la ka sasa ding hi.
English: I will sing unto the LORD as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.

**104:34**
Zolai: Topa in hong lungdamsak ahih manin ka lasaknate in zong amah lungdamsak tahen.
English: My meditation of him shall be sweet: I will be glad in the LORD .

**104:35**
Zolai: Leitung panin mawhnei mite beimang hen la, migilote om nawn kei hen. Ke’n, Topa ka phat ding hi. Topa ka phat ding hi.
English: Let the sinners be consumed out of the earth, and let the wicked be no more. Bless thou the LORD , O my soul. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 105

**105:1**
Zolai: Topa tungah lungdamna ko-in, ama min phat unla, ama sepnate khempeuh mite lakah kitheisak un.
English: O give thanks unto the LORD ; call upon his name: Make known his deeds among the people.

**105:2**
Zolai: Ama tungah la sa un. Ama tungah phatna la sa unla, a lamdang a septe khempeuh gen ciat ta un.
English: Sing unto him, sing psalms unto him: Talk ye of all his wondrous works.

**105:3**
Zolai: Ama min siangtho hangin lungdam unla, Topa a zong mite lungdam tahen.
English: Glory ye in his holy name: Let the heart of them rejoice that seek the LORD .

**105:4**
Zolai: Topa le ama huh ding zon belin nei unla, a tawntungin ama maipha zong niloh un.
English: Seek the LORD , and his strength: Seek his face evermore.

**105:5**
Zolai: No ama nasem, Abraham’ suanlekhak, Jakob’ tate, ama teel mite aw, ama sepsa a lamdang nate, ama nalamdang lahte, a genkhiat a thukhennate phawk ciat ta un!
English: Remember his marvellous works that he hath done; His wonders, and the judgments of his mouth;

**105:7**
Zolai: Amah pen Topa, eite’ Pasian hi a, ama thupiaknate leitung khempeuh in a zuih ding ahi hi.
English: He is the LORD our God: His judgments are in all the earth.

**105:8**
Zolai: “Na luah dingin Kanaan gam ka hong pia ding hi,” ci-in Abraham tawh thuciam a bawlsa, Isaac tungah a thuciamsa, Jakob tungah thupiakna a kipsak, Israel tungah tawntung thuciamna, ama thupiaksa kammal, ama thuciamna pen khang tulkhat dongin amah in phawk ngitnget hi.
English: He hath remembered his covenant for ever, The word which he commanded to a thousand generations.

**105:12**
Zolai: Amaute tawm mahmahin, bangmah gentham lo uh a, khualmi hi-in,
English: When they were but a few men in number; Yea, very few, and strangers in it.

**105:13**
Zolai: minam khat panin minam dang khatah, gam khat pan gam khatah a vak kawikawi laitakun,
English: When they went from one nation to another, From one kingdom to another people;

**105:14**
Zolai: amah in amaute kuamah nengniamsak lo hi. Amaute’ hangin amah in kumpite thuhilhin,
English: He suffered no man to do them wrong: Yea, he reproved kings for their sakes;

**105:15**
Zolai: “Ka sathau nilhte sukha kei un; ka kamsangte tungah siatna bawl kei un,” ci hi.
English: Saying , Touch not mine anointed, And do my prophets no harm.

**105:16**
Zolai: Amah in leitungah kialpi tungsakin, nektheih an khempeuh a siatsak ciangin,
English: Moreover he called for a famine upon the land: He brake the whole staff of bread.

**105:17**
Zolai: amah in, Josef a kici, sila-a a kizuak mi khat, amaute’ mai-ah a sawl hi.
English: He sent a man before them, Even Joseph, who was sold for a servant:

**105:18**
Zolai: Ama khete pen kolte in nasak a, ama ngawng pen sikkol sungah kikoih hi.
English: Whose feet they hurt with fetters: He was laid in iron:

**105:19**
Zolai: Ama thugente a tun matengin Topa in amah ze-et hi.
English: Until the time that his word came: The word of the LORD tried him.

**105:20**
Zolai: Amah a khahkhia dingin kumpipa in mi paisak a, mihingte a ukpa in amah a khahkhia hi.
English: The king sent and loosed him; Even the ruler of the people, and let him go free.

**105:21**
Zolai: Josef in kumpipa’ uliante ama ut bangin lamlakin, a upate pen pilna hilhsak a, ama innsung topa ama neihsa khempeuh a ukpa-in a koih hi.
English: He made him lord of his house, And ruler of all his substance:

**105:23**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Egypt gamah Israel va pai a, Ham’ gam sungah peemta-in Jakob va om hi.
English: Israel also came into Egypt; And Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.

**105:24**
Zolai: Topa in ama mite pungsak mahmah a, a galte sangin amaute hatzaw sak hi.
English: And he increased his people greatly; And made them stronger than their enemies.

**105:25**
Zolai: Ama mite mudahin, ama nasemte siamna tawh a khem dingin amaute’ lungsim amah in kiheisak hi.
English: He turned their heart to hate his people, To deal subtilly with his servants.

**105:26**
Zolai: Amah in, ama nasem Moses le ama teelsa Aaron a sawl hi.
English: He sent Moses his servant; And Aaron whom he had chosen.

**105:27**
Zolai: Amaute in ama limte amaute’ lakah na lamdangte Ham’ gam sungah a bawl uh hi.
English: They shewed his signs among them, And wonders in the land of Ham.

**105:28**
Zolai: Amah in khuamial sawl a, leitung khim a zingsak hi. Ahih hangin Egypt mite in ama thu a langpang uh hi.
English: He sent darkness, and made it dark; And they rebelled not against his word.

**105:29**
Zolai: Amah in amau’ tuite sisan suaksak a, a ngasate uh a sisak hi.
English: He turned their waters into blood, And slew their fish.

**105:30**
Zolai: Amau’ leitang tung le a kumpipa’ innsung nangawn uiphukte tawh a kidim hi.
English: Their land brought forth frogs in abundance, In the chambers of their kings.

**105:31**
Zolai: Amah kampau a, thohonpi le thokangte gam sung dimin hong om hi.
English: He spake, and there came divers sorts of flies, And lice in all their coasts.

**105:32**
Zolai: Amah in a guah dingun gialpi, amau’ gam sung khempeuh a taangsak khuaphialep, amaute a pia hi.
English: He gave them hail for rain, And flaming fire in their land.

**105:33**
Zolai: Amah in amau’ leengguite le a theikungte uh vattansak a, amau’ gam sung sing khempeuh a kuaihtansak hi.
English: He smote their vines also and their fig trees; And brake the trees of their coasts.

**105:34**
Zolai: Amah kampau a, kauphete le tangngolte, simzawh lohin hong pai uh a,
English: He spake, and the locusts came, and caterpillers, and that without number,

**105:35**
Zolai: gam sunga kung khempeuh, amau’ leitang panin a gah khempeuh a nektumsak mang hi.
English: And did eat up all the herbs in their land, and devoured the fruit of their ground.

**105:36**
Zolai: Amau’ sung pan a piang masa Egypt tacil khempeuh a satlum hi.
English: He smote also all the firstborn in their land, The chief of all their strength.

**105:37**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in ngun le kham tawh Israel-te paikhiatpih a, amaute a vekpi-in cidamin thahat kim uh hi.
English: He brought them forth also with silver and gold: And there was not one feeble person among their tribes.

**105:38**
Zolai: Amaute a paikhiat ciangun Egypt mite lungdam mahmah uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute kihta uh hi.
English: Egypt was glad when they departed: For the fear of them fell upon them.

**105:39**
Zolai: Amaute a liah dingin amah in meiipi kaisak a, zanin khua muh nadingin mei a omsak hi.
English: He spread a cloud for a covering; And fire to give light in the night.

**105:40**
Zolai: Amaute in ngen a, vantung panin anlum tampi a pia hi.
English: The people asked, and he brought quails, And satisfied them with the bread of heaven.

**105:41**
Zolai: Amah in suangpi hong a, tui a phulkhia hi. Guntui bangin sehnel gamah tui a luang hi.
English: He opened the rock, and the waters gushed out; They ran in the dry places like a river.

**105:42**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh a siangtho ama thuciamna le ama nasem Abraham a phawk hi.
English: For he remembered his holy promise, And Abraham his servant.

**105:43**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin ama mite lungdamna tawh, ama teel mite lasakna tawh a paikhiatpih hi.
English: And he brought forth his people with joy, And his chosen with gladness:

**105:44**
Zolai: Amaute in ama ngeina kipte zui-in, ama thukhamte a neih theih nadingun, amah in amaute tungah minam dangte’ leitang pia a, midangte’ nasepna gahte zong amaute a ngahsak hi. Topa phat un.
English: And gave them the lands of the heathen: And they inherited the labour of the people;

## Chapter 106

**106:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Topa’ tungah lungdam ko un; bang hang hiam cih leh amah hoih a, ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: Praise ye the LORD . O give thanks unto the LORD ; for he is good: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**106:2**
Zolai: Topa’ nasepna lianpite kua in genkhia thei ding a, kua in a kicingin amah phat thei ding ahi hiam?
English: Who can utter the mighty acts of the LORD ? Who can shew forth all his praise?

**106:3**
Zolai: Thutang a zui, a tawntungin thumanin a gamta mite, mi nuamsa ahi hi.
English: Blessed are they that keep judgment, And he that doeth righteousness at all times.

**106:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma teel mite’ daupaina ka muh theih nading, nangma minamte’ kipakna sungah ka lungkim theih nading, nangma luahte tawh ka minthan’ khawm theih nadingin na mite tungah maipha na lah ciangin kei hong phawk inla, amaute na hotkhiat ciangin kei zong hong huh in.
English: Remember me, O LORD , with the favour that thou bearest unto thy people: O visit me with thy salvation;

**106:6**
Zolai: Ka pu ka pate uh a kipan kote ka khial khin uh hi. Mawhna ka bawl khin uh a, ka gilo gamtat khin uh hi.
English: We have sinned with our fathers, We have committed iniquity, we have done wickedly.

**106:7**
Zolai: Ka pu ka pate un Egypt gamah a om lai-un nangma nasepna a lamdangte ngaihsun lo uh hi. Na itna kip a tampite phawk lo uh a, San Tuipi-ah Sangpenpa hong lehdo uh hi.
English: Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt; They remembered not the multitude of thy mercies; But provoked him at the sea, even at the Red sea.

**106:8**
Zolai: Ahi zongin amah in a lian mahmah a vangliatna a kitheihsak nadingin ama min a ngaihsutna-in amaute a honkhia hi.
English: Nevertheless he saved them for his name's sake, That he might make his mighty power to be known.

**106:9**
Zolai: Amah in San Tuipi thuhilh a, tua tuipi a kang hi. Amah in gamlak kantan bangin tuithuk kantanin amaute a paipih hi.
English: He rebuked the Red sea also, and it was dried up: So he led them through the depths, as through the wilderness.

**106:10**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in galte’ khutsung panin amaute honkhia a, langpangte’ vangliatna panin amaute a khahkhia hi.
English: And he saved them from the hand of him that hated them , And redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.

**106:11**
Zolai: Tui in amau’ langte tuummang khin a, amaute a suakta khat zong om lo uh hi.
English: And the waters covered their enemies: There was not one of them left.

**106:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in ama thu um uh a, amah phatna la a sa uh hi.
English: Then believed they his words; They sang his praise.

**106:13**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in ama nasepte mangngilh pah uh a, ama thugen ding ngak loin a gamta pah uh hi.
English: They soon forgat his works; They waited not for his counsel:

**106:14**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in gamlakah duhluat mahmahna nei uh a, sehnel gam sungah Pasian a ze-et uh hi.
English: But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, And tempted God in the desert.

**106:15**
Zolai: Amah in amaute’ nget pen pia a, ahih hangin amaute lakah natsia a tungsak hi.
English: And he gave them their request; But sent leanness into their soul.

**106:16**
Zolai: Gamlakah Moses le Topa’ mi siangtho Aaron a hazat uh ciangin,
English: They envied Moses also in the camp, And Aaron the saint of the LORD .

**106:17**
Zolai: lei kihongin Dathan valhtum a, Abiram’ pawlte a vukcip hi.
English: The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan, And covered the company of Abiram.

**106:18**
Zolai: Amaute’ sungah mei hong piangkhia a, meikuang in migilote a kangtum hi.
English: And a fire was kindled in their company; The flame burned up the wicked.

**106:19**
Zolai: Amaute in Horeb gam sungah bawngno khat bawl uh a, a kisung tua milim a bia uh hi.
English: They made a calf in Horeb, And worshipped the molten image.

**106:20**
Zolai: Amaute in Pasian’ minthanna pen lopa a ne bawngtal lim tawh a khek uh hi.
English: Thus they changed their glory Into the similitude of an ox that eateth grass.

**106:21**
Zolai: Amaute in Egypt gam sungah na lianpite a bawl, Ham’ gam sungah na lamdangte le San Tuipi-ah a kihtakhuai nate a bawl, amau’ Honpa, Pasian mangngilh uh hi.
English: They forgat God their saviour, Which had done great things in Egypt;

**106:23**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute a suksiatna ding a hehna panin a heikhia dingin Pasian’ mai-ah ama teelpa Moses ding hikeileh amaute ka susia ding hi, amah in ci hi.
English: Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach, To turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy them .

**106:24**
Zolai: Amaute in gam nuam simmawh uh a, ama thuciamna um lo uh hi.
English: Yea, they despised the pleasant land, They believed not his word:

**106:25**
Zolai: Amaute a puanbuk sung uhah phun niloh uh a, Topa’ thu ngai lo uh hi.
English: But murmured in their tents, And hearkened not unto the voice of the LORD .

**106:26**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in a khut laamto-in gam sungah amaute puksak a, leitung gam khempeuh minamte’ lakah amau’ suanlekhakte a thehthang ding a kiciam hi.
English: Therefore he lifted up his hand against them, To overthrow them in the wilderness:

**106:28**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in Peor-a Baal pasian bel uh a, nuntakna a nei lote tungah biakna-in a kipia sate a ne uh hi.
English: They joined themselves also unto Baalpeor, And ate the sacrifices of the dead.

**106:29**
Zolai: Amau’ gamtatna tawh Topa’ hehna ding piangsak uh a, amaute’ lakah pulnatna hong tung hi.
English: Thus they provoked him to anger with their inventions: And the plague brake in upon them.

**106:30**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Finehas dingin hong palai a, pulnatna a hong dai hi.
English: Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: And so the plague was stayed.

**106:31**
Zolai: Tua thu pen a khang a khangin ama thumanna-in kiciamteh tawntung hi.
English: And that was counted unto him for righteousness Unto all generations for evermore.

**106:32**
Zolai: Amaute in Meribah tuiphualah amah sinso sakin, amah a langpang uh hi. Thakhatin kamguh a paukha Moses in amaute’ huhau-in siatna a ngahlawh hi.
English: They angered him also at the waters of strife, So that it went ill with Moses for their sakes:

**106:34**
Zolai: Topa in amaute a thupiak bangin amaute in tua mite that lo uh hi.
English: They did not destroy the nations, Concerning whom the LORD commanded them:

**106:35**
Zolai: Minam dangte tawh kihelin amau’ gamtat bangbang a gamta dingin a kisin uh hi.
English: But were mingled among the heathen, and learned their works.

**106:36**
Zolai: Amau a dingin thangzak ahi amau’ milimte a biakpih uh hi.
English: And they served their idols: Which were a snare unto them.

**106:37**
Zolai: Amaute in a tapate uh le a tanute uh dawi biakna-in a nei uh hi.
English: Yea, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters unto devils,

**106:38**
Zolai: Amaute in Kanaan gam milimte a biakna-un mawhna nei lo a tanute uh le a tapate uh that uh a, hih mi thahna hangin gam sung a nin a suak hi.
English: And shed innocent blood, Even the blood of their sons and of their daughters, Whom they sacrificed unto the idols of Canaan: And the land was polluted with blood.

**106:39**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amau’ sepna tawh amaute a nin suak uh a, amau’ gamtatnate tawh palhngulhna a bawl uh hi.
English: Thus were they defiled with their own works, And went a whoring with their own inventions.

**106:40**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ama mite tungah Topa’ hehna hong kitawhkuang a, amah in ama luah minamte a kih hi.
English: Therefore was the wrath of the LORD kindled against his people, Insomuch that he abhorred his own inheritance.

**106:41**
Zolai: Amau a mudah minamte in amaute a uk theih nadingin tua minamte’ khut sungah amaute a pia hi.
English: And he gave them into the hand of the heathen; And they that hated them ruled over them.

**106:42**
Zolai: A galte un amaute nengniam uh a, amau’ khutnuai-ah amaute a koih uh hi.
English: Their enemies also oppressed them, And they were brought into subjection under their hand.

**106:43**
Zolai: Amah in amaute tam veipi honkhia hi. Ahih hangin amaute in lehdona lungsim vom uh a, amau’ mawhna hangin amaute a kiniamkoih hi.
English: Many times did he deliver them; But they provoked him with their counsel, and were brought low for their iniquity.

**106:44**
Zolai: Tua bang ahi ta zongin amaute’ kikona a zak ciangin amaute’ cihmawhna a don hi.
English: Nevertheless he regarded their affliction, When he heard their cry:

**106:45**
Zolai: Amaute a’ ding a ngaihsutna-in ama thuciamna phawk a, ama itna kip tawh kizui-in a kolsak hi.
English: And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented according to the multitude of his mercies.

**106:46**
Zolai: Amaute a man mi khempeuhte in a khasiatpih zah dong dingin amah in amau’ tungah a piangsak hi.
English: He made them also to be pitied of all those that carried them captives.

**106:47**
Zolai: Topa, kote’ Pasian aw, kote hong hon inla, nangma min siangtho kong phat theih nading uh le nangma tungah lungdamna kong koh theih nadingun minam dangte’ lak panin kote hong kaikhawmkik in.
English: Save us, O LORD our God, and gather us from among the heathen, To give thanks unto thy holy name, and to triumph in thy praise.

**106:48**
Zolai: Topa, Israel Pasian in a tawntung a kipan a tawntung dongin thupha ngah tahen. Mi khempeuh in, “Amen,” ci ta uh hen. Topa phat un.
English: Blessed be the LORD God of Israel from everlasting to everlasting: And let all the people say, Amen. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 107

**107:1**
Zolai: “ Topa tungah lungdam ko un; bang hang hiam cih leh amah hoih a, ama itna kip tawntung!”
English: O give thanks unto the LORD , for he is good: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**107:2**
Zolai: Tu-a teng mah, nisuahna le nitumna, leilu lam le leitaw lam, leitung pana ama kaihkhop, galte’ khutsung panin a hong hotkhiat mite in ci kikkik ta uh hen.
English: Let the redeemed of the LORD say so , Whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy;

**107:4**
Zolai: Pawlkhatte gamlakah gammang uh a, a tenna ding uh khuapi tunna lampi mu zo lo uh hi.
English: They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way; They found no city to dwell in.

**107:5**
Zolai: Gilkial dangtakin amaute sibup uh hi.
English: Hungry and thirsty, Their soul fainted in them.

**107:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in a lungkhamna uhah Topa ko uh a, amau’ cihmawhna panin amah in a honkhia hi.
English: Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, And he delivered them out of their distresses.

**107:7**
Zolai: Amau’ tenna ding khuapi a tun matengun amah in lampi manah amaute a paipih hi.
English: And he led them forth by the right way, That they might go to a city of habitation.

**107:8**
Zolai: Ama itna kip le mihing tate tungah a lamdang ama sepnate hangin amaute in Topa’ tungah lungdamna ko ta uh hen.
English: Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, And for his wonderful works to the children of men!

**107:9**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in a gilkial a dangtakte phasak a, bangmah a nei lote tungah na hoih tampi a pia hi.
English: For he satisfieth the longing soul, And filleth the hungry soul with goodness.

**107:10**
Zolai: Pawlkhatte, khuamial sung, a zing sungah tu uh a, sikkol kibulhin gimna thuakin thong kia uh hi.
English: Such as sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, Being bound in affliction and iron;

**107:11**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in Pasian’ thu sel uh a, Sangpenpa’ thugente a nial uh hi.
English: Because they rebelled against the words of God, And contemned the counsel of the Most High:

**107:12**
Zolai: Nasep haksa tawh amaute’ lungsim niamsak hi. Amaute puk uh a, a huh ding kuamah om lo hi.
English: Therefore he brought down their heart with labour; They fell down, and there was none to help.

**107:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in a lungkhamna uhah Topa ko uh a, amau’ cihmawhna panin amah in a honkhia hi.
English: Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, And he saved them out of their distresses.

**107:14**
Zolai: Amah in khuamial sung le a zing sung panin amaute lakhia a, amau a kihennate a botsat hi.
English: He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, And brake their bands in sunder.

**107:15**
Zolai: Ama itna kip le mihing tate tungah a lamdang a nasepnate hangin amaute in Topa tungah lungdamna ko ta uh hen.
English: Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, And for his wonderful works to the children of men!

**107:16**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in sumngo kongkhakte sukhamin sikzawlte tum nih a suah hi.
English: For he hath broken the gates of brass, And cut the bars of iron in sunder.

**107:17**
Zolai: Pawlkhatte amau’ khialhna hangin a ci uh na a, a mawhna hangun gimna a thuak uh hi.
English: Fools because of their transgression, And because of their iniquities, are afflicted.

**107:18**
Zolai: Amaute in an peuhmah kih uh a, sihna kongpi tawh amaute kinai ta uh hi.
English: Their soul abhorreth all manner of meat; And they draw near unto the gates of death.

**107:19**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in a lungkhamna uhah Topa ko uh a, amau’ cihmawhna panin amah in a honkhia hi.
English: Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, And he saveth them out of their distresses.

**107:20**
Zolai: Amah in thu vaikhakin amaute damsak a, siatna ding panin amaute a honkhia hi.
English: He sent his word, and healed them, And delivered them from their destructions.

**107:21**
Zolai: Ama itna kip le mihing tate tungah a lamdang a nasepnate hangin amaute in Topa tungah lungdamna ko ta uh hen.
English: Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, And for his wonderful works to the children of men!

**107:22**
Zolai: Lungdam koh piaknate pia-in ama nasepnate lungdam la tawh amaute gensak un.
English: And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving, And declare his works with rejoicing.

**107:23**
Zolai: Pawlkhatte, teembaw tawh tuipi-ah pai uh a, tui liante tungah sumbawl na a sem uh hi.
English: They that go down to the sea in ships, That do business in great waters;

**107:24**
Zolai: Amaute in tuithuk tungah Topa’ gamtatna a lamdang a septe a mu uh hi.
English: These see the works of the LORD , And his wonders in the deep.

**107:25**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in thu pia a, tuipi hualte a piangsak huihpi a nungsak hi.
English: For he commandeth, and raiseth the stormy wind, Which lifteth up the waves thereof.

**107:26**
Zolai: Amaute, vanah kilawnto-in, a thukna-ah kiasuk uh hi. A lauhuai siatna sungah amau’ lungsim hanna a bei hi.
English: They mount up to the heaven, they go down again to the depths: Their soul is melted because of trouble.

**107:27**
Zolai: Amaute zukham bangin hoisuk hoito uh a, a cih nading mel uh thei nawn lo uh hi.
English: They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, And are at their wits' end.

**107:28**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in a lungkhamna uhah Topa ko uh a, amau’ cihmawhna panin amah in a honkhia hi.
English: Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, And he bringeth them out of their distresses.

**107:29**
Zolai: Amah in huihpi daisak a, tuipi hualte a bei hi.
English: He maketh the storm a calm, So that the waves thereof are still.

**107:30**
Zolai: Tua ciangin, tua tuihualte a khawl manin amaute a lungdam uh hi. Amah in amaute’ utna khua-ah a paipih hi.
English: Then are they glad because they be quiet; So he bringeth them unto their desired haven.

**107:31**
Zolai: Ama itna kip le mihing tate tungah a lamdang a sepnate hangin amaute in Topa tungah lungdamna ko ta uh hen.
English: Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, And for his wonderful works to the children of men!

**107:32**
Zolai: Amaute in mihon kikhopna sungah amah pahtawi-in, upate’ kikhopna sungah amah phat ta uh hen.
English: Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people, And praise him in the assembly of the elders.

**107:33**
Zolai: Amah in, a tunga a teng mihingte’ gitlohna hangin gunte sehnel gam suaksakin ciktuite leikeu suaksak a, an tampi a pianna leitang pen ci-lei a suaksak hi.
English: He turneth rivers into a wilderness, And the watersprings into dry ground;

**107:35**
Zolai: Amah in sehnel gam pen bualtuite suaksak a, leitang keu pen ciktui a suaksak hi.
English: He turneth the wilderness into a standing water, And dry ground into watersprings.

**107:36**
Zolai: Amah in tua munah gilkialte tengsak a, a tenna ding uh khuapi amaute in a sat uh hi.
English: And there he maketh the hungry To dwell, that they may prepare a city for habitation;

**107:37**
Zolai: Amaute in lo-ah an tuhin leenggui suan uh a, a gah tampi tak a ngah uh hi.
English: And sow the fields, and plant vineyards, Which may yield fruits of increase.

**107:38**
Zolai: Ama thupha piakna hangin ante nakpitakin pung a, amau’ bawngte zong kiamsak lo hi.
English: He blesseth them also, so that they are multiplied greatly; And suffereth not their cattle to decrease.

**107:39**
Zolai: Amaute pen nenniamna, haksatna le dahna tawh khiamsuk gawpin a kiniamkoih suk ciangin
English: Again, they are minished and brought low Through oppression, affliction, and sorrow.

**107:40**
Zolai: amah in, amau a bawlsiate tungah simmawhna buak sukin lampi om lohna gam sungah amaute a vakvaisak hi.
English: He poureth contempt upon princes, And causeth them to wander in the wilderness, where there is no way.

**107:41**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in amau’ thuakna sung panin a cimawhte laamto a, tuu honpite bangin amau’ innkuante a pungsak hi.
English: Yet setteth he the poor on high from affliction, And maketh him families like a flock.

**107:42**
Zolai: Lungsim thutangte in hih thu mu-in kipak uh a, a gilote in ahihleh amau’ kam a cih ciat uh hi.
English: The righteous shall see it , and rejoice: And all iniquity shall stop her mouth.

**107:43**
Zolai: A pil peuhmah in hih thute don hen la, Topa’ itna kip lungngaingai tahen.
English: Whoso is wise, and will observe these things , Even they shall understand the lovingkindness of the LORD .

## Chapter 108

**108:1**
Zolai: Pasian aw, ka lungsim a kigingsa-in om hi. Ka sa ding hi; nangmah phatna late ka sa ding hi. Kei ka khanglo ding hi.
English: O God, my heart is fixed; I will sing and give praise, even with my glory.

**108:2**
Zolai: Harp lasakna le laiza lasakna aw, khanglo un. Zingsang khuavak hong phong ning.
English: Awake, psaltery and harp: I myself will awake early.

**108:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, mite lakah nangma tungah lungdamna kong ko ding a, minam dangte lakah nangma tungah phatna ka sa ding hi.
English: I will praise thee, O LORD , among the people: And I will sing praises unto thee among the nations.

**108:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh na itna kip in vantung ban a, na thumanna in meiipite banto hi.
English: For thy mercy is great above the heavens: And thy truth reacheth unto the clouds.

**108:5**
Zolai: Pasian aw, vantungte’ tungah sangto lai in. Leitung khempeuhah na minthanna omsak in.
English: Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: And thy glory above all the earth;

**108:6**
Zolai: Nangma it mite, na hatna tawh hon inla, kong ngetna bangun hong pia in.
English: That thy beloved may be delivered: Save with thy right hand, and answer me.

**108:7**
Zolai: Ama biakinn sungah Pasian in thu ciam khin a, “Gualzo a lungdamna tawh Shekhem gam khenkhia-in, Sukkoth gam kuam ka sehkhia ding hi.
English: God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.

**108:8**
Zolai: Gilead gam keima a’ hi a, Manasseh gam zong keima-a’ mah ahi hi. Efraim gam ka siklukhu hi a, Judah gam ka ciangkhut ahi hi.
English: Gilead is mine; Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is the strength of mine head; Judah is my lawgiver;

**108:9**
Zolai: Moab gam ka kisilna kuang hi a, keima neihsa hi, cih lahna limin Edom gam tungah ka khedap ka lawn hi. Filistia gam tungah gualzawhna tawh ka awng hi,” a ci hi.
English: Moab is my washpot; Over Edom will I cast out my shoe; Over Philistia will I triumph.

**108:10**
Zolai: Kua in khuapi muanhuai-ah kei hong paipih ding hiam? Kua in Edom gamah kei hong paipih ding hiam?
English: Who will bring me into the strong city? Who will lead me into Edom?

**108:11**
Zolai: Pasian aw, nangmah in kote hong don lo khinta hi lo na hi hiam? Pasian aw, komau galkapte tawh na kuankhia kei hi.
English: Wilt not thou , O God, who hast cast us off? And wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our hosts?

**108:12**
Zolai: Ka galdona uhah kote hong huh in. Bang hang hiam cih leh mihing’ huhna a mawkna hi.
English: Give us help from trouble: For vain is the help of man.

**108:13**
Zolai: Pasian tawh khauhtakin i hih ding hi. Amah pen i galte hong sikcipsak ding pa ahi hi.
English: Through God we shall do valiantly: For he it is that shall tread down our enemies.

## Chapter 109

**109:1**
Zolai: Keima hong phat Pasian aw, dai dide-in ommawk kei in.
English: Hold not thy peace, O God of my praise;

**109:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh migilote le zuauthu gente keima langah hong pang uh a, keimah hong gensia-in, zuauthu bekbek genin nei uh hi.
English: For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful are opened against me: They have spoken against me with a lying tongue.

**109:3**
Zolai: Amaute in muhdah kamte pau-in kei hong gensia uh a, thu om lopi-in kei hong langpang uh hi.
English: They compassed me about also with words of hatred; And fought against me without a cause.

**109:4**
Zolai: Amaute ka itna, amaute a dingin thu ka ngetsakna nangawn amaute in hong thukna-in kei hong mawhsak uh hi.
English: For my love they are my adversaries: But I give myself unto prayer.

**109:5**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in hoihna a dingin siatna itna a dingin muhdahna tawh kei hong thuk uh hi.
English: And they have rewarded me evil for good, And hatred for my love.

**109:6**
Zolai: Ka gal pa’ langah migilo khat pangsak inla, thusitna a thuak dingin mawhna a zong mi khat paipih sak in.
English: Set thou a wicked man over him: And let Satan stand at his right hand.

**109:7**
Zolai: Amah thu a kisit ciangin thu lelin pusuaksak inla, ama hong thumnate zong mawhna suaksak in.
English: When he shall be judged, let him be condemned: And let his prayer become sin.

**109:8**
Zolai: Amah khantom hen la, midang khat in ama nasep za ngah tahen.
English: Let his days be few; And let another take his office.

**109:9**
Zolai: Ama tate pa nei lo hi ta hen la, a zi zong meigong numei hi tahen.
English: Let his children be fatherless, And his wife a widow.

**109:10**
Zolai: Ama tate vak kawikawi-in khut dawhin ngen hen la, a kisiasa a tenna mun panun kihawlkhia ta uh hen.
English: Let his children be continually vagabonds, and beg: Let them seek their bread also out of their desolate places.

**109:11**
Zolai: Ama leibatna pa in a neih khempeuh man hen la, khualmite in a omlai sunsunte sut tahen.
English: Let the extortioner catch all that he hath; And let the strangers spoil his labour.

**109:12**
Zolai: Ama tungah kuamah migi kei hen la, pa nei lo ama tate kuamah in hehpih kei tahen.
English: Let there be none to extend mercy unto him: Neither let there be any to favour his fatherless children.

**109:13**
Zolai: Ama suanlekhakte bei hen la, khang khat sungin a vangliatna maimang tahen.
English: Let his posterity be cut off; And in the generation following let their name be blotted out.

**109:14**
Zolai: Topa’ mai-ah a pu a pate’ mawhna kiciamteh hen la, a nu’ mawhna kimaisak kei tahen.
English: Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the LORD ; And let not the sin of his mother be blotted out.

**109:15**
Zolai: Topa’ mai-ah tua mawhnate omsak inla, leitung panin amah a kiphawkna bei tahen.
English: Let them be before the LORD continually, That he may cut off the memory of them from the earth.

**109:16**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh migitna lah ding ngaihsun lo a, a zawng a cimawhte le lungsim kitamzan mite a sih dongun a bawlsia hi.
English: Because that he remembered not to shew mercy, But persecuted the poor and needy man, That he might even slay the broken in heart.

**109:17**
Zolai: Amah in mi samsiat nuam a sa hi. Ama tungah samsiatnate tungsak in. Amah in thupha pia nuam lo hi. Kuamah in amah thupha pia kei tahen.
English: As he loved cursing, so let it come unto him: As he delighted not in blessing, so let it be far from him.

**109:18**
Zolai: Amah pen puansilh bangin samsiatna kingeina seh hi. Tua a samsiatnate ama pumpi sungah tui bangin a guhte sungah sathau bangin lutin kizel tahen.
English: As he clothed himself with cursing like as with his garment, So let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his bones.

**109:19**
Zolai: Tua samsiatnate pen ama kituamna puan tawh kibang hen la, nisimin amah a kigakna a kawnggak tawh kibang tahen.
English: Let it be unto him as the garment which covereth him, And for a girdle wherewith he is girded continually.

**109:20**
Zolai: Hih bang teng pen keimah hong mawhsakte’ tung, kei hong gensiate’ tungah Topa’ kiang pan a thaman hi tahen.
English: Let this be the reward of mine adversaries from the LORD , And of them that speak evil against my soul.

**109:21**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa ka Pasian aw, na min na ngaihsutna tawh keima tangin hong pang inla, na itna kip hoih ahih manin kei hong honkhia in.
English: But do thou for me, O GOD the Lord, for thy name's sake: Because thy mercy is good, deliver thou me.

**109:22**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh kei genthei-in ka cimawh a, ka lungsim tawng dongin na hong nasak hi.
English: For I am poor and needy, And my heart is wounded within me.

**109:23**
Zolai: Nitak a niliim bangin kei ka bei a, kauphe bangin kei hong kisingkhia hi.
English: I am gone like the shadow when it declineth: I am tossed up and down as the locust.

**109:24**
Zolai: An ngolhna hangin ka khukte zaw a, ka pumpi silesa zong kiamgawp khinta hi.
English: My knees are weak through fasting; And my flesh faileth of fatness.

**109:25**
Zolai: Amaute’ nuihsatin kei ka om a, amaute in kei hong muh ciangun lusu ngeungeu uh hi.
English: I became also a reproach unto them: When they looked upon me they shaked their heads.

**109:26**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian aw, kei hong huh in. Nangma itna kip tawh kituakin kei hong hon in.
English: Help me, O LORD my God: O save me according to thy mercy:

**109:27**
Zolai: Topa aw, hih pen nangma bawl, nangma khut in a sep ahihna amaute theisak in.
English: That they may know that this is thy hand; That thou, LORD , hast done it.

**109:28**
Zolai: Amaute in kei hong samsiat hangin nangmah in kei thupha nong pia ding hi. Ka langte zahhuaisak inla, na nasempa keimah hong kipsak ta in.
English: Let them curse, but bless thou: When they arise, let them be ashamed; but let thy servant rejoice.

**109:29**
Zolai: Kei hong mawhsakte in mindaina silh uh hen la, puanza silh bangin amau’ maizumna tawh kituamcip ta uh hen.
English: Let mine adversaries be clothed with shame, And let them cover themselves with their own confusion, as with a mantle.

**109:30**
Zolai: Topa tungah ka lungdamna a gingpha-in ka ko ding a, mihonte lakah amah ka phat ding hi.
English: I will greatly praise the LORD with my mouth; Yea, I will praise him among the multitude.

**109:31**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh sih nading gimna a piapa’ khutsung pan a honkhia dingin mi cimawh pa’ taklamah amah hong ding hi.
English: For he shall stand at the right hand of the poor, To save him from those that condemn his soul.

## Chapter 110

**110:1**
Zolai: Topa in ka to kumpipa tungah, “Na galte nangma khengakna-in ka bawl matengin ka taklamah tu in,” a ci hi.
English: The LORD said unto my Lord, Sit thou at my right hand, until I make thine enemies thy footstool.

**110:2**
Zolai: Topa in Zion panin na kumpi ciangkhut hong puak hi. Na galte’ tungah uk in.
English: The LORD shall send the rod of thy strength out of Zion: Rule thou in the midst of thine enemies.

**110:3**
Zolai: Nangma mihonte mual siangtho tungah na makaih ciangin, utna lungsim tawh na mite hong kipia ding uh hi. Daitui bangin zingsangin na khangnona nangma tungah hong tung ding hi.
English: Thy people shall be willing in the day of thy power, In the beauties of holiness from the womb of the morning: Thou hast the dew of thy youth.

**110:4**
