Zolai: Topa in thu ciamzo a, ama ngaihsutna kheel lo ding hi. “Melkhizedek bangin a tawntungin siampi na hi hi,” a ci hi.
English: The LORD hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou art a priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek.

**110:5**
Zolai: Nangma taklamah Topa hong om a, ama heh ni-in kumpite a zogawp ding hi.
English: The Lord at thy right hand Shall strike through kings in the day of his wrath.

**110:6**
Zolai: Kumpipa in minamte lakah thu khen ding a, tua munte si luanghawm tawh a dimsak ding hi. Amah in a zai mahmah leitungah ukpite a susia ding hi.
English: He shall judge among the heathen, he shall fill the places with the dead bodies; He shall wound the heads over many countries.

**110:7**
Zolai: Amah in lampi gei-a om luitui dawn ding a, amah a tha hatin a gualzo pa hi ding hi.
English: He shall drink of the brook in the way: Therefore shall he lift up the head.

## Chapter 111

**111:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Lungsim thutangte a omna, mihon kikhopna sungah ka lungsim khempeuh tawh Topa’ tungah lungdamna ka ko ding hi.
English: Praise ye the LORD . I will praise the LORD with my whole heart, In the assembly of the upright, and in the congregation.

**111:2**
Zolai: Topa’ nasepna lian a, hoih a sa mi khempeuh in tuate kankan uh hi.
English: The works of the LORD are great, Sought out of all them that have pleasure therein.

**111:3**
Zolai: Ama nasepnate, pahtawina le minliatna tawh kidim a, ama thumanna kip tawntung hi.
English: His work is honourable and glorious: And his righteousness endureth for ever.

**111:4**
Zolai: Amah in phawk tawntung dingin a lamdang nasepnate hong bawl a, Topa dikin hehpihna nei hi.
English: He hath made his wonderful works to be remembered: The LORD is gracious and full of compassion.

**111:5**
Zolai: Amah in amah a zahtakte an pia a, a thuciamna a phawk tawntung hi.
English: He hath given meat unto them that fear him: He will ever be mindful of his covenant.

**111:6**
Zolai: Amah in ama mite tungah minamte’ gamh a piakna tawh ama vangliatna hong lak khin hi.
English: He hath shewed his people the power of his works, That he may give them the heritage of the heathen.

**111:7**
Zolai: Ama nasepnate khempeuhah amah thumanin citak a, a thupiaknate muantaak mahmah hi.
English: The works of his hands are verity and judgment; All his commandments are sure.

**111:8**
Zolai: A tawntungin tuate kip ngitnget a, thuman le thutang tawh zuih ding ahi hi.
English: They stand fast for ever and ever, And are done in truth and uprightness.

**111:9**
Zolai: Amah in ama mite honkhia a, a tawntung a kimang dingin thupiakna a bawl khin hi. Ama min siangtho-in vanglian mahmah hi.
English: He sent redemption unto his people: He hath commanded his covenant for ever: Holy and reverend is his name.

**111:10**
Zolai: Topa zahtakna pen pilna kipatna ahi hi. Ama thupiak a zuite khempeuh tungah thukhen siamna a pia hi. Amah phat tawntung ding ahi hi.
English: The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom: A good understanding have all they that do his commandments: His praise endureth for ever.

## Chapter 112

**112:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Topa zahtakin a thupiaknate nuam a sa mahmah mi, thupha ngah mi ahi hi.
English: Praise ye the LORD . Blessed is the man that feareth the LORD , That delighteth greatly in his commandments.

**112:2**
Zolai: Ama suanlekhakte leitungah vanglian ding a, a lungsim thutang mite’ suanlekhakte thupha kipia ding hi.
English: His seed shall be mighty upon earth: The generation of the upright shall be blessed.

**112:3**
Zolai: Hauhna le nopsaknate a innkuan sungah dim ding a, ama thumanna kip tawntung ding hi.
English: Wealth and riches shall be in his house: And his righteousness endureth for ever.

**112:4**
Zolai: Lungsim thutangte a dingin khuamial sung panin khuavak hong taangkhia hi. Topa dik a, hehpihna nei-in, amah thuman hi.
English: Unto the upright there ariseth light in the darkness: He is gracious, and full of compassion, and righteous.

**112:5**
Zolai: Cingh gamtatin mite tungah leitawi pia a, thutangin a gamta mite tungah thu a hoih hi.
English: A good man sheweth favour, and lendeth: He will guide his affairs with discretion.

**112:6**
Zolai: Amah kiling lo taktak ding a, kiphawk tawntung ding hi.
English: Surely he shall not be moved for ever: The righteous shall be in everlasting remembrance.

**112:7**
Zolai: Amah in thusia zak ding lau lo hi. Topa muang a, ama lungsim a kip hi.
English: He shall not be afraid of evil tidings: His heart is fixed, trusting in the LORD .

**112:8**
Zolai: Amah lau loin, lunghimawh loin om hithiat a, amah a langpangte a guallelh ding a theitel hi.
English: His heart is established, he shall not be afraid, Until he see his desire upon his enemies.

**112:9**
Zolai: Amah in hawmkhia zuahzuah a, mizawngte tungah a piakhia hi. Ama migitna kip tawntung a, amah vanglianin kipahtawi ding hi.
English: He hath dispersed, he hath given to the poor; His righteousness endureth for ever; His horn shall be exalted with honour.

**112:10**
Zolai: Migilo in hih thu mu-in a heh suak mahmah a, a ha gawigawi-in a tuimang hi. Migilote’ lametna a mawkna a suakta hi.
English: The wicked shall see it , and be grieved; He shall gnash with his teeth, and melt away: The desire of the wicked shall perish.

## Chapter 113

**113:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Topa’ nasemte aw, phat un. Topa’ min phat un.
English: Praise ye the LORD . Praise, O ye servants of the LORD , Praise the name of the LORD .

**113:2**
Zolai: Topa’ min in tu a kipanin thupha ngah tawntung tahen.
English: Blessed be the name of the LORD From this time forth and for evermore.

**113:3**
Zolai: Nisuahna pan nitumna dongin Topa’ min phat ding ahi hi.
English: From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the same The LORD 's name is to be praised.

**113:4**
Zolai: Topa in minam khempeuh tungah uk a, ama minthanna vantung sangin sangzaw hi.
English: The LORD is high above all nations, And his glory above the heavens.

**113:5**
Zolai: A sangna munah a tu, vantung le leitung a hong ensuk Topa, eite’ Pasian pen kua tawh kibang ahi hiam?
English: Who is like unto the LORD our God, who dwelleth on high,

**113:7**
Zolai: Amah in leivui panin mizawngte laamto-in, ninphual panin mi cimawhte le a lungkhamte domto a,
English: He raiseth up the poor out of the dust, And lifteth the needy out of the dunghill;

**113:8**
Zolai: uliante tawh kikhawl sakin ama mite’ ulianin a bawl hi.
English: That he may set him with princes, Even with the princes of his people.

**113:9**
Zolai: Amah in tasel numei tungah ta guan a, ta a nei nu a lungdamin a bawl hi. Topa phat un.
English: He maketh the barren woman to keep house, And to be a joyful mother of children. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 114

**114:1**
Zolai: Israel-te, Egypt gam panin pusuakin, Jakob innkuanpihte paudang a zang mite kiang pan a paikhiat uh ciangin
English: When Israel went out of Egypt, The house of Jacob from a people of strange language;

**114:2**
Zolai: Judah-te, Topa’ mi siangtho suak a, Israel-te, ama uk mi a suak hi.
English: Judah was his sanctuary, And Israel his dominion.

**114:3**
Zolai: Tuipi in amaute mu-in taikhia a, Jordan gun a nungkik hi.
English: The sea saw it , and fled: Jordan was driven back.

**114:4**
Zolai: Mual liante tuutal bangin diang uh a, mual neute tuuno bangin a diang uh hi.
English: The mountains skipped like rams, And the little hills like lambs.

**114:5**
Zolai: Tuipi aw, na taikhiatna ding, Jordan gun aw, na nungkikna ding,
English: What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou fleddest? Thou Jordan, that thou wast driven back?

**114:6**
Zolai: mual liante aw, tuu bangin mual neute aw, tuuno bangin na dianna ding uh bang in hong nasak ahi hiam?
English: Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams; And ye little hills, like lambs?

**114:7**
Zolai: Leitung aw, suangpi, bualtui suaksak a, meisuang, ciktui a suaksak, Jakob’ Pasian’ omna, Topa’ omna-ah ling in.
English: Tremble, thou earth, at the presence of the Lord, At the presence of the God of Jacob;

## Chapter 115

**115:1**
Zolai: Kote tungah hi loin, Topa aw, kote tungah hi loin, na itna kip le na thumanna hangin nangma tungah minthanna om tahen.
English: Not unto us, O LORD , not unto us, but unto thy name give glory, For thy mercy, and for thy truth's sake.

**115:2**
Zolai: Bang hangin minam dangte in, “Amaute’ Pasian koi-ah om ahi hiam?” ci laizang ding ahi uh hiam?
English: Wherefore should the heathen say, Where is now their God?

**115:3**
Zolai: Vantungah eite’ Pasian om a, ama ut peuhpeuh a hih hi.
English: But our God is in the heavens: He hath done whatsoever he hath pleased.

**115:4**
Zolai: Amau’ milimte pen ngun le kham hi lel a, mihingte’ khut tawh a kibawl ahi hi.
English: Their idols are silver and gold, The work of men's hands.

**115:5**
Zolai: Amaute in kam nei napi-in pau thei lo uh a, mit nei napi-in khua mu thei lo uh hi.
English: They have mouths, but they speak not: Eyes have they, but they see not:

**115:6**
Zolai: Amaute in bil nei napi-in khua za lo uh a, nak nei napi-in a nam thei lo uh hi.
English: They have ears, but they hear not: Noses have they, but they smell not:

**115:7**
Zolai: Amaute in khut nei napi-in lawng thei lo uh a, khe nei napi-in pai thei lo uh hi. Amaute in aw gingsak thei lo uh hi.
English: They have hands, but they handle not: Feet have they, but they walk not: Neither speak they through their throat.

**115:8**
Zolai: Tuate a bawlte le tuate a muangte khempeuh pen tuate mah tawh kibang uh hi.
English: They that make them are like unto them; So is every one that trusteth in them.

**115:9**
Zolai: Israel-te aw, Topa muang un. Amah pen note hong huhpa le hong hupa ahi hi.
English: O Israel, trust thou in the LORD : He is their help and their shield.

**115:10**
Zolai: Aaron innkuante aw, Topa muang un. Amah pen note hong huhpa le hong hupa ahi hi.
English: O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD : He is their help and their shield.

**115:11**
Zolai: Topa a zahtakte aw, Topa muang un. Amah pen note hong huhpa le hong hupa ahi hi.
English: Ye that fear the LORD , trust in the LORD : He is their help and their shield.

**115:12**
Zolai: Topa in eite hong phawk a, thupha hong pia ding hi. Amah in Israel mite, thupha hong pia ding a, amah in Aaron innkuante thupha hong pia ding hi.
English: The LORD hath been mindful of us: he will bless us ; He will bless the house of Israel; He will bless the house of Aaron.

**115:13**
Zolai: Amah in Topa a zahtakte a lian a neu-in thupha hong pia ding hi.
English: He will bless them that fear the LORD , both small and great.

**115:14**
Zolai: Topa in note le na tate uh hong pungsak tahen.
English: The LORD shall increase you more and more, You and your children.

**115:15**
Zolai: Van le lei a bawl Topa in note thupha hong pia tahen.
English: Ye are blessed of the LORD Which made heaven and earth.

**115:16**
Zolai: Vantung pen Topa a’ hi a, ahih hangin leitung pen mihingte tungah hong pia khin hi.
English: The heaven, even the heavens, are the LORD 's: But the earth hath he given to the children of men.

**115:17**
Zolai: Misite ahi a, gamdaihna sungah a pai peuhpeuhte in ahi zongin Topa phat lo uh hi.
English: The dead praise not the LORD , Neither any that go down into silence.

**115:18**
Zolai: Ahih hangin eite in tu a kipanin a tawntungin Topa i phat ngitnget ding hi. Topa phat un.
English: But we will bless the LORD From this time forth and for evermore. Praise the LORD .

## Chapter 116

**116:1**
Zolai: Topa ka it hi; bang hang hiam cih leh amah in ka aw hong za-in ka thumnate hong ngai hi.
English: I love the LORD , Because he hath heard my voice and my supplications.

**116:2**
Zolai: Amah ka sap sialin ka sapna aw hong ngai hi.
English: Because he hath inclined his ear unto me, Therefore will I call upon him as long as I live.

**116:3**
Zolai: Sihna khau in kei hong gakcip hi. Leinuai sihna in kei hong mancip a, natna le lungkhamna ka thuak hi.
English: The sorrows of death compassed me, And the pains of hell gat hold upon me: I found trouble and sorrow.

**116:4**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa’ tungah thu ngenin, “ Topa aw, nang tungah kong thum hi; kei hong hon in,” ka ci hi.
English: Then called I upon the name of the LORD ; O LORD , I beseech thee, deliver my soul.

**116:5**
Zolai: Topa dikin thuman a, i Pasian in hehpihna nei hi.
English: Gracious is the LORD , and righteous; Yea, our God is merciful.

**116:6**
Zolai: Topa in thu thei lo mi hong kem a, kei hong kiniamkoih ciangin amah in hong huh hi.
English: The LORD preserveth the simple: I was brought low, and he helped me.

**116:7**
Zolai: Lungmuang takin ka om ding hi; bang hang hiam cih leh keima tungah Topa hong thunuam hi.
English: Return unto thy rest, O my soul; For the LORD hath dealt bountifully with thee.

**116:8**
Zolai: Topa in sihna panin kei hong honkhia hi. Ka khituite hong kangsak a, kei hong guallelsak lo hi.
English: For thou hast delivered my soul from death, Mine eyes from tears, and my feet from falling.

**116:9**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin mihingte’ omna leitung, Topa’ mai-ah nungta-in ka vak kawikawi hi.
English: I will walk before The LORD in the land of the living.

**116:10**
Zolai: “Nakpi takin gimna ka thuak hi,” ka cih hun ciang nangawnin ka upna mah ka len cinten hi.
English: I believed, therefore have I spoken: I was greatly afflicted:

**116:11**
Zolai: Lunghihmawhna tawh, “Mi khempeuh zuau gen vive hi,” ka cih hun nangawnin ka um lailai hi.
English: I said in my haste, all men are liars.

**116:12**
Zolai: Kei tunga ama thupha tampite Topa’ tungah bangci thuk ding ka hi hiam?
English: What shall I render unto the LORD For all his benefits toward me?

**116:13**
Zolai: Topa in kei hong hotkhiat ka lungdamna hangin, ama kiangah tuiphih biakna ka paipih ding hi.
English: I will take the cup of salvation, And call upon the name of the LORD .

**116:14**
Zolai: Topa’ tungah ka thuciamnasa pen ama mite khempeuh a kikhopna munah ka pia ding hi.
English: I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his people.

**116:15**
Zolai: Ama mi siangthote a sih ciangin Topa in na sa mahmah hi.
English: Precious in the sight of the LORD is the death of his saints.

**116:16**
Zolai: Topa aw, kei pen nangma nasem ka hi hi. Nangma nasem ka hi a, na nasemnu’ ta ka hi hi. Keimah hong kikhihnate nong sutkhiatsak zo hi.
English: O LORD , truly I am thy servant; I am thy servant, and the son of thine handmaid: Thou hast loosed my bonds.

**116:17**
Zolai: Lungdam koh biakpiakna nang tungah kong pia ding a, Topa’ tungah thu kong ngen ding hi.
English: I will offer to thee the sacrifice of thanksgiving, And will call upon the name of the LORD .

**116:18**
Zolai: Jerusalem khuapi aw, ama mi khempeuh a omna sung, Topa’ inn huangsung, nangma laizangah, Topa’ tungah ka thuciamnasa ka pia ding hi. Topa phat un.
English: I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his people,

## Chapter 117

**117:1**
Zolai: Minam khempeuhte aw, Topa phat un. Minam khempeuhte aw, amah phat un.
English: O praise the LORD , All ye nations: Praise him, all ye people.

**117:2**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh eite a hong itna lian mahmah a, Topa’ thutakna a tawntungin kip ngitnget hi. Topa phat un.
English: For his merciful kindness is great toward us: And the truth of the LORD endureth for ever. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 118

**118:1**
Zolai: Topa’ tungah lungdamna ko un. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah hoih a, ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: O give thanks unto the LORD ; for he is good: Because his mercy endureth for ever.

**118:2**
Zolai: “Ama itna kip tawntung hi,” Israel-te in ci ta uh hen.
English: Let Israel now say, That his mercy endureth for ever.

**118:3**
Zolai: “Ama itna kip tawntung hi,” Aaron innkuante in ci ta uh hen.
English: Let the house of Aaron now say, That his mercy endureth for ever.

**118:4**
Zolai: “Ama itna kip tawntung hi,” amah a zahtakte in ci ta uh hen.
English: Let them now that fear the LORD say, That his mercy endureth for ever.

**118:5**
Zolai: Ka cihmawhna-ah Topa ka sam a, Topa in hong dawngin mun tanzau-ah hong koih hi.
English: I called upon the LORD in distress: The LORD answered me, and set me in a large place.

**118:6**
Zolai: Topa in kei hong ompih hi. Bangmah ka kihta kei ding hi. Mihingte in kei, bang hong cihzo ding ahi uh hiam?
English: The LORD is on my side; I will not fear: What can man do unto me?

**118:7**
Zolai: Kei hong huh dingin kei lamah Topa om hi. Kei hong mudahte pen gualzawhna tawh ka en ding hi.
English: The LORD taketh my part with them that help me: Therefore shall I see my desire upon them that hate me.

**118:8**
Zolai: Mi i muan sangin Topa belh ding hoihzaw hi.
English: It is better to trust in the LORD Than to put confidence in man.

**118:9**
Zolai: Uliante i muan sangin Topa belh ding hoihzaw hi.
English: It is better to trust in the LORD Than to put confidence in princes.

**118:10**
Zolai: Minam khempeuh in kei hong umcih uh hi. Ahih hangin Topa’ vang tawh amaute ka sugawp hi.
English: All nations compassed me about: But in the name of the LORD will I destroy them.

**118:11**
Zolai: Amaute in ka kimkotah kei hong umcih uh hi. Ahih hangin Topa’ vang tawh amaute ka sugawp hi.
English: They compassed me about; yea, they compassed me about: But in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.

**118:12**
Zolai: Amaute in khuaipi bangin kei hong umcih uh a, ahi zongin selkeu kuang bangin amaute daikik pak uh hi. Topa’ vang tawh amaute ka sugawp hi.
English: They compassed me about like bees; they are quenched as the fire of thorns: For in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.

**118:13**
Zolai: Kei ka puk nadingin nakpitakin hong kisawn a, ahih hangin Topa in kei hong huh hi.
English: Thou hast thrust sore at me that I might fall: But the LORD helped me.

**118:14**
Zolai: Topa in a vanglian, a thahatin kei hong bawl a, amah pen kei a hong honpa ahi hi.
English: The LORD is my strength and song, And is become my salvation.

**118:15**
Zolai: Ngai un! Thuman mite’ puanbuk sungah gualzawh lungdamna la kisa a, “ Topa’ taklam khut in a lian nate hih khin hi.
English: The voice of rejoicing and salvation is in the tabernacles of the righteous: The right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly.

**118:16**
Zolai: Topa’ taklam khut kipahtawi a, Topa’ taklam khut in a lian nate hih khin hi,” kici hi.
English: The right hand of the LORD is exalted: The right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly.

**118:17**
Zolai: Kei ka si kei ding a, ka hing ding hi. Topa’ sepnate ka gengen ding hi.
English: I shall not die, but live, And declare the works of the LORD .

**118:18**
Zolai: Topa in nasia takin kei hong thuhilh a, ahih hangin kei hong sisak lo hi.
English: The LORD hath chastened me sore: But he hath not given me over unto death.

**118:19**
Zolai: Topa’ tungah lungdamna ko-in ka lut theih nadingin biakinn kongpite kei hong hon in.
English: Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will go into them, and I will praise the LORD :

**118:20**
Zolai: Hih pen Topa’ kongpi ahi hi. Thuman mi bek hih kongpi-ah lut ding hi.
English: This gate of the LORD , Into which the righteous shall enter.

**118:21**
Zolai: Nangmah in kei hong dawngin, hong honkhia na hih manin nangma tungah ka lungdam hi.
English: I will praise thee: for thou hast heard me, And art become my salvation.

**118:22**
Zolai: Innlamte in a nilkhiat suang pen innkiu suang bulpi suak khinta hi.
English: The stone which the builders refused Is become the head stone of the corner.

**118:23**
Zolai: Hih pen Topa’ nasepna hi a, eite’ mitah lamdang hi.
English: This is the LORD 's doing; It is marvellous in our eyes.

**118:24**
Zolai: Hih ni pen Topa’ hong piak ni hi a, eite lungdamin i kipak ding hi.
English: This is the day which the LORD hath made; We will rejoice and be glad in it.

**118:25**
Zolai: Topa aw, kote hong hon in; hong thum ung. Topa aw, kong thum uh hi; kote hong daupaisak in.
English: Save now, I beseech thee, O LORD : O LORD , I beseech thee, send now prosperity.

**118:26**
Zolai: Topa’ min tawh hong pai pa in thupha ngah tahen. Topa’ inn panin nang kong phat uh hi.
English: Blessed be he that cometh in the name of the LORD : We have blessed you out of the house of the LORD .

**118:27**
Zolai: Topa pen Pasian ahi hi. Amah in eite tungah nopsakna hong piazo hi. Na khut uhah singhiang tawi-in, biakna tau kimkotin pai un.
English: God is the LORD , which hath shewed us light: Bind the sacrifice with cords, even unto the horns of the altar.

**118:28**
Zolai: Nang pen keima Pasian na hi a, nangma tungah lungdamna kong ko ding hi. Nang pen keima Pasian na hi a, nangmah kong phat ding hi.
English: Thou art my God, and I will praise thee: Thou art my God, I will exalt thee.

**118:29**
Zolai: Topa tungah lungdamna ko un; bang hang hiam cih leh amah hoih a, ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: O give thanks unto the LORD ; for he is good: For his mercy endureth for ever.

## Chapter 119

**119:1**
Zolai: Amau’ gamtatna-ah paubaan om loin Topa’ ngeina sungah a gamtate thupha ngah ahi hi.
English: Blessed are the undefiled in the way, Who walk in the law of the LORD .

**119:2**
Zolai: Ama thuhilhnate zui-in, a lungsim khempeuh uh tawh amah zongin, khialhna zong bawl loin, ama lampi a zuite, thupha ngah ahi hi.
English: Blessed are they that keep his testimonies, And that seek him with the whole heart.

**119:4**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhte limtakin zuih dingin thu nong pia hi.
English: Thou hast commanded us To keep thy precepts diligently.

**119:5**
Zolai: Nangma ngeina kipte zuihna-ah ka gamtatna kip tahen.
English: O that my ways were directed To keep thy statutes!

**119:6**
Zolai: Na thupiakte khempeuh mitsuanin nei ka hih manin, kei ka maizum kei ding hi.
English: Then shall I not be ashamed, When I have respect unto all thy commandments.

**119:7**
Zolai: Nangmah biakna ngeina kipte ka sin khit ciangin lungsim thutang tawh nangmah kong phat ding hi.
English: I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, When I shall have learned thy righteous judgments.

**119:8**
Zolai: Nangma ngeina kipte ka zui ding hi; kei hong nusia suak kei in.
English: I will keep thy statutes: O forsake me not utterly.

**119:9**
Zolai: Tangval khat in ama gamtatna a siangtho mahmah dingin bangci kep ding ahi hiam? Nangma thu zuihna tawh ama gamtatna siangthosak thei ding hi.
English: Wherewithal shall a young man cleanse his way? By taking heed thereto according to thy word.

**119:10**
Zolai: Ka lungsim khempeuh tawh nang ka hong zong hi. Na thupiaknate panin kei hong pialsak kei in.
English: With my whole heart have I sought thee: O let me not wander from thy commandments.

**119:11**
Zolai: Nangma tungah kong khialh loh nadingin ka lungsim sungah nangma thu ka khol hi.
English: Thy word have I hid in mine heart, That I might not sin against thee.

**119:12**
Zolai: Topa aw, thupha ngah ta in; na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh in.
English: Blessed art thou, O LORD : Teach me thy statutes.

**119:13**
Zolai: Nangma hong piak nangmah biakna ngeina kipte khempeuh ka gengen ding hi.
English: With my lips have I declared All the judgments of thy mouth.

**119:14**
Zolai: Hauhnate khempeuh sangin nangma thuhilhnate nuam ka sa zaw hi.
English: I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, As much as in all riches.

**119:15**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhnate lungngaingai-in, nangma lampite ka mitsuan ding hi.
English: I will meditate in thy precepts, And have respect unto thy ways.

**119:16**
Zolai: Nangma ngeina kipte-ah nuam ka sa ding a, nangma thu ka mangngilh ngei kei ding hi.
English: I will delight myself in thy statutes: I will not forget thy word.

**119:17**
Zolai: Nungta-in nangma thu ka zuih theih nadingin na nasempa tungah hong cingh in.
English: Deal bountifully with thy servant, That I may live, and keep thy word.

**119:18**
Zolai: Nangma thukham sung panin a lamdang nate ka muh theih nadingin keima mitte hong honsak in.
English: Open thou mine eyes, That I may behold wondrous things out of thy law.

**119:19**
Zolai: Kei pen hih leitungah peemta ka hi hi; kei’ kiang panin na thuphate seel kei in.
English: I am a stranger in the earth: Hide not thy commandments from me.

**119:20**
Zolai: Nangmah biakna ngeina kipte a tawntungin ka lunggulh venvan hi.
English: My soul breaketh for the longing That it hath unto thy judgments at all times.

**119:21**
Zolai: Nangmah in na thupiaknate panin a pialkhia, a kisamsiat, a kiphasakte na thuhilh hi.
English: Thou hast rebuked the proud That are cursed, which do err from thy commandments.

**119:22**
Zolai: Na thuhilhnate zui ka hih manin amau’ hong nuihsatna le hong simmawhnate panin kei hong suaktasak in.
English: Remove from me reproach and contempt: For I have kept thy testimonies.

**119:23**
Zolai: Uliante in kei hong langpangin thu a vaihawm uh hangin na nasempa in na ngeina kipte ngaihsunsun ding hi.
English: Princes also did sit and speak against me: But thy servant did meditate in thy statutes.

**119:24**
Zolai: Na thuhilhnate ka deih hi. Tuate pen keimah thu hong lakte ahi hi.
English: Thy testimonies also are My delight and my counsellors.

**119:25**
Zolai: Guallelin leivui lakah ka lum hi. Na thu omsa bangin kei hong hingsak in.
English: My soul cleaveth unto the dust: Quicken thou me according to thy word.

**119:26**
Zolai: Ka gamtatnate kong gen ciangin nangmah in kei nong dawng hi. Na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh in.
English: I have declared my ways, and thou heardest me: Teach me thy statutes.

**119:27**
Zolai: Nangma ngeina kipte kei hong theitel sak in. Nangma nasep lamdangte ka ngaihsunsun ding hi.
English: Make me to understand the way of thy precepts: So shall I talk of thy wondrous works.

**119:28**
Zolai: Dahna in kei hong vukcip hi. Nangma thu omsa bangin kei hong thakhauhsak in.
English: My soul melteth for heaviness: Strengthen thou me according unto thy word.

**119:29**
Zolai: A man lo lampite ka zuih khak loh nadingin kei hong kem in. Hong hehpih inla, na ngeinate hong hilh in.
English: Remove from me the way of lying: And grant me thy law graciously.

**119:30**
Zolai: Thuman lampi ka teel khin a, na biakna ngeina kipte ka deih hi.
English: I have chosen the way of truth: Thy judgments have I laid before me .

**119:31**
Zolai: Topa aw, na thuhilhnate ka pom hi. Kei hong zahhuaisak kei in.
English: I have stuck unto thy testimonies: O LORD , put me not to shame.

**119:32**
Zolai: Keima theihna nong zaisak ciangin nangma thupiaknate lawpna tawh ka zui ding hi.
English: I will run the way of thy commandments, When thou shalt enlarge my heart.

**119:33**
Zolai: Topa aw, na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh in. A mong dongin ka zui ding hi.
English: Teach me, O LORD , the way of thy statutes; And I shall keep it unto the end.

**119:34**
Zolai: Nangma thute kemin ka lungsim khempeuh tawh ka zuih theih nadingin thu theihtelna hong pia in.
English: Give me understanding, and I shall keep thy law; Yea, I shall observe it with my whole heart.

**119:35**
Zolai: Nangma thupiakna lampi-ah kei hong paipih in. Bang hang hiam cih leh tua-ah nuam ka sa hi.
English: Make me to go in the path of thy commandments; For therein do I delight.

**119:36**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhnate’ lamah ka lungsim awnsak inla, ngahna ding bekah awnsak kei in.
English: Incline my heart unto thy testimonies, And not to covetousness.

**119:37**
Zolai: Bangmahin a kimang lo nate, kei hong kinsak kei inla, nangma thu omsa bangin hong nungtasak in.
English: Turn away mine eyes from beholding vanity; And quicken thou me in thy way.

**119:38**
Zolai: Na thu hong mangte tungah na thuciamnate, na nasempa tungah hong kipsak in.
English: Stablish thy word Unto thy servant, who is devoted to thy fear.

**119:39**
Zolai: Ka kihtak hong kikonate kei’ kiang pan heikhia in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nangmah biakna ngeina kipte hoih mahmah hi.
English: Turn away my reproach which I fear: For thy judgments are good.

**119:40**
Zolai: En in, na thuhilhnate ka lunggulh hi. Na thumanna tawh kei hong hingsak in.
English: Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: Quicken me in thy righteousness.

**119:41**
Zolai: Topa aw, na ciamna bangin na itna kip, na hotkhiatna kei tungah hong tungsak in.
English: Let thy mercies come also unto me, O LORD , Even thy salvation, according to thy word.

**119:42**
Zolai: Tua hileh na thu ka muanna hangin kei hong zahkote ka dawnna ding hong om ding hi.
English: So shall I have wherewith to answer him that reproacheth me: For I trust in thy word.

**119:43**
Zolai: Nangmah biakna ngeina kipte lamenin om ka hih manin a man thu hong gen theisak tawntung in.
English: And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth; For I have hoped in thy judgments.

**119:44**
Zolai: Nangma thu tatsat loin ka zui ngitnget ding hi.
English: So shall I keep thy law continually for ever and ever.

**119:45**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhnate zuih ding hanciam ka hih manin nuamtakin ka nungta ding hi.
English: And I will walk at liberty: For I seek thy precepts.

**119:46**
Zolai: Kumpite’ mai-ah nangma thute ka gen ding a, maizumna ka thuak kei ding hi.
English: I will speak of thy testimonies also before kings, And will not be ashamed.

**119:47**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka deih nangma thupiakna zuih ding nuam ka sa hi.
English: And I will delight myself In thy commandments, which I have loved.

**119:48**
Zolai: Keima deih ahi na thupiakte ka zahtak a, na ngeina kipte ka lungngaingai ding hi.
English: My hands also will I lift up unto thy commandments, which I have loved; And I will meditate in thy statutes.

**119:49**
Zolai: Keimah nong lametsakna ahi na nasempa’ tungah na thuciamna hong phawk in.
English: Remember the word unto thy servant, Upon which thou hast caused me to hope.

**119:50**
Zolai: Hih pen ka thuakna-ah keima kihehnepna hi a, na thuciamna in kei tungah nuntakna hong pia hi.
English: This is my comfort in my affliction: For thy word hath quickened me.

**119:51**
Zolai: Mi kiphasakte in kei hong zahko gawp uh a, ahih hangin nangma thupiakna panin kei ka pial kei hi.
English: The proud have had me greatly in derision: Yet have I not declined from thy law.

**119:52**
Zolai: Topa aw, hun lui lai-a nangmah biakna ngeina kipte ka ngaihsut ciangin ka lung hong nuam hi.
English: I remembered thy judgments of old, O LORD ; And have comforted myself.

**119:53**
Zolai: Nangma thu a nusia migilote’ hangin ka heh a suak hi.
English: Horror hath taken hold upon me Because of the wicked that forsake thy law.

**119:54**
Zolai: Hih leitung ka omna peuhah nangma ngeina kipte la phuahin ka sa hi.
English: Thy statutes have been my songs In the house of my pilgrimage.

**119:55**
Zolai: Topa aw, zanin na min ka phawk a, nangma thu ka zui hi.
English: I have remembered thy name, O LORD , in the night, and have kept thy law.

**119:56**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhte zui ka hih manin keima tungah hih thupha hong tung hi.
English: This I had, because I kept thy precepts.

**119:57**
Zolai: Topa pen keima tanh ahi hi. Na thute zuih ding ka kiciam hi.
English: Thou art my portion, O LORD : I have said that I would keep thy words.

**119:58**
Zolai: Ka lungsim khempeuh tawh na maipha kong ngen hi. Na thuciamna omsa bangin kei hong hehpih in.
English: I intreated thy favour with my whole heart: Be merciful unto me according to thy word.

**119:59**
Zolai: Ka gamtatnate ka ngaihsun a, na ngeinate zuih ding ka kiciam hi.
English: I thought on my ways, And turned my feet unto thy testimonies.

**119:60**
Zolai: Kei kinawhin, na thupiakte zuih ding ka zekai kei hi.
English: I made haste, and delayed not To keep thy commandments.

**119:61**
Zolai: Migilote’ khau in kei hong vialh hangin nangma thu ka mangngilh tuan kei hi.
English: The bands of the wicked have robbed me: But I have not forgotten thy law.

**119:62**
Zolai: A thuman na ngeina kipte hangin nangmah a phat dingin zankim laitakin ka tho hi.
English: At midnight I will rise to give thanks unto thee Because of thy righteous judgments.

**119:63**
Zolai: Kei pen, na thuhilhte a zui, nangmah a hong zahtakte tawh a kikhawlpa ka hi hi.
English: I am a companion of all them That fear thee, and of them that keep thy precepts.

**119:64**
Zolai: Topa aw, leitung pen nangma itna kip tawh kidim hi. Na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh in.
English: The earth, O LORD , is full of Thy mercy: Teach me thy statutes.

**119:65**
Zolai: Topa aw, na thuciamna bangin na nasempa na limbawl hi.
English: Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O LORD , according unto thy word.

**119:66**
Zolai: Na thupiakte um ka hih manin thu khentel theihna le theihsiamna hong hilh in.
English: Teach me good judgment and knowledge: For I have believed thy commandments.

**119:67**
Zolai: Gim nong piak ma-in lam ka pial thei zel a, ahih hangin tu-in na thu ka zui hi.
English: Before I was afflicted I went astray: But now have I kept thy word.

**119:68**
Zolai: Nangmah na hoih a, a hoih nate na sem hi. Na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh in.
English: Thou art good, and doest good; Teach me thy statutes.

**119:69**
Zolai: Mi kiphasakte in kei’ thu, zuau vive gengen uh a, ahih hangin keimah in ka lungsim khempeuh tawh na thuhilhte ka zui hi.
English: The proud have forged a lie against me: But I will keep thy precepts with my whole heart.

**119:70**
Zolai: Amaute’ lungsim in thu theithei loin khikcip a, ahih hangin keimah in nangma thu sung nuam ka sa hi.
English: Their heart is as fat as grease; But I delight in thy law.

**119:71**
Zolai: Nangma ngeina kipte ka sin theih nadingin gimna ka thuak pen kei a dingin hoih mahmah hi.
English: It is good for me that I have been afflicted; That I might learn thy statutes.

**119:72**
Zolai: Nangma kam sung pana thu pen kham le ngun tul tampite sangin kei a dingin hoihzaw hi.
English: The law of thy mouth is better unto me Than thousands of gold and silver.

**119:73**
Zolai: Nangmah in kei hong piangsakin na hong bawl hi. Na thupiaknate ka sin theih nadingin thu theihtelna hong pia in.
English: Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: Give me understanding, that I may learn thy commandments.

**119:74**
Zolai: Nangma thuciamna muang ka hih manin nang hong zahtakte in kei hong mu-in lungdam ding uh hi.
English: They that fear thee will be glad when they see me; Because I have hoped in thy word.

**119:75**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangmah biakna ngeina kipte man hi, ci-in ka thei a, na thumanna hangin kei gim na hong pia hi.
English: I know, O LORD , that thy judgments are right, And that thou in faithfulness hast afflicted me.

**119:76**
Zolai: Na nasempa tungah na thuciamna bangin keimah hong hehnem dingin na itna kip a baihsa-in hong omsak in.
English: Let, I pray thee, thy merciful kindness be for my comfort, According to thy word unto thy servant.

**119:77**
Zolai: Ka nuntak theih nadingin kei hong hehpih in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma thu nuam ka sa hi.
English: Let thy tender mercies come unto me, that I may live: For thy law is my delight.

**119:78**
Zolai: Mi kiphasakte zahhuaisak in. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in khemna tawh kei hong lumlet uh hi. Ke’n ahihleh na thuhilhte ka lungngaingai ding hi.
English: Let the proud be ashamed; for they dealt perversely with me without a cause: But I will meditate in thy precepts.

**119:79**
Zolai: Na teci pannate a theih nadingun nang hong zahtakte kei’ lamah hong kiheisak in.
English: Let those that fear thee turn unto me, And those that have known thy testimonies.

**119:80**
Zolai: Guallelh maizumna ka thuak loh nadingin nangma ngeina kipte a kicing takin a zuizo mi hong hisak ta in.
English: Let my heart be sound in thy statutes; That I be not ashamed.

**119:81**
Zolai: Na hong hotkhiat ding ka ngakngakna-in ka tha bei ta a, nangma thu muangin ka lamen hi.
English: My soul fainteth for thy salvation: But I hope in thy word.

**119:82**
Zolai: Na thuciamnate ka etetna-in ka mitte thazaw ta hi. “Cik ciangin hong hehnem ding na hiam?” kong ci hi.
English: Mine eyes fail for thy word, Saying, When wilt thou comfort me?

**119:83**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh kei pen meikhu lak a a kikoihdak savun-um tawh ka kibang a, ahi zongin nangma ngeina kipte ka mangngilh tuan kei hi.
English: For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; Yet do I not forget thy statutes.

**119:84**
Zolai: Na nasempa in bang tanvei ngaklai ding ka hi hiam? Kei hong bawlsiate cik ciangin thu khen ding na hi hiam?
English: How many are the days of thy servant? When wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me?

**119:85**
Zolai: Nangma thu a zui lo, mi kiphasakte in keimah hong siahna-in gum a to uh hi.
English: The proud have digged pits for me, Which are not after thy law.

**119:86**
Zolai: Nangma thupiakte khempeuh man taktak hi. Amaute in thuman lopi-in kei hong bawlsia uh hi. Kei hong huh in.
English: All thy commandments are faithful: They persecute me wrongfully; help thou me.

**119:87**
Zolai: Amaute in kei hong thatzo dektak uh hi. Ahih hangin na thuhilhnate ka mangngilh tuan kei hi.
English: They had almost consumed me upon earth; But I forsook not thy precepts.

**119:88**
Zolai: Na kam pana na teci pannate ka zuih theih nadingin na itna kip tawh kei hong hingsak in.
English: Quicken me after thy lovingkindness; So shall I keep the testimony of thy mouth.

**119:89**
Zolai: Topa aw, vantungah nangma thu kip tawntung hi.
English: For ever, O LORD , Thy word Is settled in heaven.

**119:90**
Zolai: Nangma thumanna khang tawntungin kip hi. Nangmah in leitung na kipsak a, om tawntung hi.
English: Thy faithfulness is unto all generations: Thou hast established the earth, and it abideth.

**119:91**
Zolai: Nangma sehna tawh tu dongin amaute kip uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh na khempeuh nangma nasem ahi hi.
English: They continue this day according to thine ordinances: For all are thy servants.

**119:92**
Zolai: Nangma thu, nuam a sa lo hileng, ka gimthuakna-ah ka kisia khinzo ta ding hi.
English: Unless thy law had been my delights, I should then have perished in mine affliction.

**119:93**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhte ka mangngilh ngei kei ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh tuate tawh nong nungtasak hi.
English: I will never forget thy precepts: For with them thou hast quickened me.

**119:94**
Zolai: Kei pen nangma a’ ka hi hi. Kei hong hon in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma thuhilhte zuih ding ka hanciam hi.
English: I am thine, save me; For I have sought thy precepts.

**119:95**
Zolai: Migilote in keimah a hong that dingin hong buk uh hi. Ahih hangin na teci pannate ke’n ka lungngaingai ding hi.
English: The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: But I will consider thy testimonies.

**119:96**
Zolai: A kicinga a kingaihsun nate khempeuh in mong a neihna ka mu khin a, ahih hangin na thupiakna in mong nei loin zai mahmah hi.
English: I have seen an end of all perfection: But thy commandment is exceeding broad.

**119:97**
Zolai: Na thu deih mahmah ing. Sun tawntungin ka lungngaihngaih ahi hi.
English: O how love I thy law! It is my meditation all the day.

**119:98**
Zolai: Na thupiakna in ka langte khempeuh sangin a pilzaw-in hong bawl hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh tua pen kei tawh omkhawm den hi.
English: Thou through thy commandments hast made me wiser than mine enemies: For they are ever with me.

**119:99**
Zolai: Ka siate khempeuh sangin thu ka telzaw hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh na teci pannate ka ngaihsunsun hi.
English: I have more understanding than all my teachers: For thy testimonies are my meditation.

**119:100**
Zolai: Khanghamte sangin thu ka telzaw hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh na thuhilhnate ka zui hi.
English: I understand more than the ancients, Because I keep thy precepts.

**119:101**
Zolai: Na thu ka zuih theih nadingin gamtatsia khempeuh ka pelh hi.
English: I have refrained my feet from every evil way, That I might keep thy word.

**119:102**
Zolai: Nangmah in hong hilh khin na hih manin na biakna ngeina kipte panin kei ka pial kei hi.
English: I have not departed From thy judgments: For thou hast taught me.

**119:103**
Zolai: Nangma thute khum mahmah a, khuaizu sangin khumzaw hi.
English: How sweet are thy words unto my taste! Yea, sweeter than honey to my mouth!

**119:104**
Zolai: Na thuhilhnate hangin thu theihtelna ka ngah hi. Tua ahih ciangin a man lo lampi khempeuh ka mudah hi.
English: Through thy precepts I get understanding: Therefore I hate every false way.

**119:105**
Zolai: Nangma thu pen lam hong lak ding meivak hi a, ka paina lampi-ah khuavak ahi hi.
English: Thy word is a lamp unto my feet, And a light unto my path.

**119:106**
Zolai: A thuman ahi nangmah biakna ngeina kipte a zui dingin ka kiciam khin a, ka kipsak khin hi.
English: I have sworn, and I will perform it , That I will keep thy righteous judgments.

**119:107**
Zolai: Nakpi takin gimna ka thuak hi. Topa aw, nong ciamsa bangin kei hong nungtasak in.
English: I am afflicted very much: Quicken me, O LORD , according unto thy word.

**119:108**
Zolai: Topa aw, phatin kong biaknate hong sang inla, nangmah biakna ngeina kipte kei hong hilh in.
English: Accept, I beseech thee, the freewill offerings of my mouth, O LORD , And teach me thy judgments.

**119:109**
Zolai: Nisimin ka nuntakna a lauhuai sungah om ngitnget a, ahih hangin nangma thu ka mangngilh tuan kei hi.
English: My soul is continually in my hand: Yet do I not forget thy law.

**119:110**
Zolai: Migilote in kei thang hong siah uh a, ahih hangin na thuhilhnate panin kei ka pial kei hi.
English: The wicked have laid a snare for me: Yet I erred not from thy precepts.

**119:111**
Zolai: Nangmah biakna ngeina kipte tawntung keima luah ahi hi. Tuate pen keima lungdamna ahi hi.
English: Thy testimonies have I taken as an heritage for ever: For they are the rejoicing of my heart.

**119:112**
Zolai: Nangma ngeina kipte ka sih mateng a zui tawntung dingin ka lungsim ka khensat hi.
English: I have inclined mine heart to perform thy statutes Alway, even unto the end.

**119:113**
Zolai: Nangma tungah a thuman lote ka mudah a, ahih hangin keimah in nangma thu ka deih hi.
English: I hate vain thoughts: But thy law do I love.

**119:114**
Zolai: Nang pen keima bukna mun le kei hong hupa na hi hi. Na thuciamna ka muang hi.
English: Thou art my hiding place and my shield: I hope in thy word.

**119:115**
Zolai: No, siatna a bawlte aw, Pasian’ thupiakte ka zuih theih nadingin kei kiang panin paikhia un.
English: Depart from me, ye evildoers: For I will keep the commandments of my God.

**119:116**
Zolai: Kei ka nuntak theih nadingin na thuciamna tawh kizui-in kei hong huh inla, ka lametna-ah kei hong zahhuaisak kei in.
English: Uphold me according unto thy word, that I may live: And let me not be ashamed of my hope.

**119:117**
Zolai: Ka suahtak theih nading le na ngeina kipte sungah nuamsa-in ka om ngitnget theih nadingin kei hong huh in.
English: Hold thou me up, and I shall be safe: And I will have respect unto thy statutes continually.

**119:118**
Zolai: Nangma ngeina kipte panin a pialkhiate khempeuh na nilkhia hi. Amau’ khem siamna a mawkna ahi hi.
English: Thou hast trodden down all them that err from thy statutes: For their deceit is falsehood.

**119:119**
Zolai: Leitung a migilote khempeuh sik-ek bangin na ngaihsun hi. Tua ahih ciangin na teci pannate ka deih hi.
English: Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth like dross: Therefore I love thy testimonies.

**119:120**
Zolai: Nang kong zahtakna hangin ka khuasikmul suak a, na thukhennate ka zahtak hi.
English: My flesh trembleth for fear of thee; And I am afraid of thy judgments.

**119:121**
Zolai: Thutang thumanin ka gamta hi. Hong nengniamte’ khut sungah kei hong nusia kei in.
English: I have done judgment and justice: Leave me not to mine oppressors.

**119:122**
Zolai: Na nasempa a dingin nangmah hong kikham inla, mi kiphasakte hong nengniamsak kei in.
English: Be surety for thy servant for good: Let not the proud oppress me.

**119:123**
Zolai: Nangma hotkhiatna le a man na thuciamna hong tun ding ka etna-in ka mitte a gim ta hi.
English: Mine eyes fail for thy salvation, And for the word of thy righteousness.

**119:124**
Zolai: Na itna kip tawh kituakin na nasempa tungah hong bawl inla, na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh in.
English: Deal with thy servant according unto thy mercy, And teach me thy statutes.

**119:125**
Zolai: Kei pen na nasempa ka hi hi. Na thuhilhnate ka theih nadingin thu theihtelna hong guan in.
English: I am thy servant; give me understanding, That I may know thy testimonies.

**119:126**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma thu kipalsat khin ahih ciangin thu na khen ding hun hita hi.
English: It is time for thee, LORD , to work: For they have made void thy law.

**119:127**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin khamte, le kham hoihpente sangin nangma thupiakna ka deihzaw hi.
English: Therefore I love thy commandments Above gold; yea, above fine gold.

**119:128**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin na thuhilhnate khempeuh tawh a kituakin kei ka gamta a, a man lo lampi khempeuh ka mudah hi.
English: Therefore I esteem all thy precepts concerning all things to be right; And I hate every false way.

**119:129**
Zolai: Na thuhilhnate lamdang pha mahmah a, ka lungsim khempeuh tawh tuate ka zui hi.
English: Thy testimonies are wonderful: Therefore doth my soul keep them.

**119:130**
Zolai: Na thute gentelna in khua vaksak a, thu thei lote tungah thu theihtelna a guan hi.
English: The entrance of thy words giveth light; It giveth understanding unto the simple.

**119:131**
Zolai: Na thupiakte ka lunggulhna-in ka kam ka-in ka leii ka kha hi.
English: I opened my mouth, and panted: For I longed for thy commandments.

**119:132**
Zolai: Nangmah hong itte tungah na hih ngei bangin kei lamah hong kihei-in kei hong hehpih in.
English: Look thou upon me, and be merciful unto me, As thou usest to do unto those that love thy name.

**119:133**
Zolai: Na hong ciamsa bangin ka pukna ding panin hong kem inla, keima tungah siatna gualzosak kei in.
English: Order my steps in thy word: And let not any iniquity have dominion over me.

**119:134**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhte ka zuih theih nadingin hong nengniamte’ kiang pan kei hong honkhia in.
English: Deliver me from the oppression of man: So will I keep thy precepts.

**119:135**
Zolai: Na nasempa tungah na mai hong taangsak inla, na ngeina kipte hong hilh in.
English: Make thy face to shine upon thy servant; And teach me thy statutes.

**119:136**
Zolai: Mite in nangma thu zui lo uh ahih manin ka khitui hawk luanin a luang hi.
English: Rivers of waters run down mine eyes, Because they keep not thy law.

**119:137**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang na thuman a, na thukhennate zong thuman mahmah hi.
English: Righteous art thou, O LORD , And upright are thy judgments.

**119:138**
Zolai: Nangma koihsa ngeina kipte thumanin thutak hi.
English: Thy testimonies that thou hast commanded are righteous and very faithful.

**119:139**
Zolai: Ka galte in nangma thu kin het lo uh ahih manin keima hehna mei bangin a kuang hi.
English: My zeal hath consumed me, Because mine enemies have forgotten thy words.

**119:140**
Zolai: Na thuciamnate kician mahmah a, na nasempa in tuate deih mahmah hi.
English: Thy word is very pure: Therefore thy servant loveth it.

**119:141**
Zolai: Kei ka neu a, hong kisimmawh hi. Ahih hangin na thuhilhnate ka mangngilh tuan kei hi.
English: I am small and despised: Yet do not I forget thy precepts.

**119:142**
Zolai: Nangma thumanna kip tawntung a, na thukham zong man tawntung hi.
English: Thy righteousness is an everlasting righteousness, And thy law is the truth.

**119:143**
Zolai: Dahna le lungkhamna ka tungah hong tung a, ahih hangin na thupiaknate nuam ka sakna ahi hi.
English: Trouble and anguish have taken hold on me: Yet thy commandments are my delights.

**119:144**
Zolai: Na teci pannate a tawntungin thuman hi. Thu theihtelna hong guan in; tua hileh ka nungta ding hi.
English: The righteousness of thy testimonies is everlasting: Give me understanding, and I shall live.

**119:145**
Zolai: Ka lungsim khempeuh tawh nang tungah kong kiko hi. Hong dawng in, Topa ! Na ngeina kipte ka zui ding hi.
English: I cried with my whole heart; hear me, O LORD : I will keep thy statutes.

**119:146**
Zolai: Nang tungah kong kiko hi. Na thuhilhnate ka zuih theih nadingin kei hong hon in.
English: I cried unto thee; save me, and I shall keep thy testimonies.

**119:147**
Zolai: Khuavak ma-in tho-in huhna ngenin kong kiko a, nangma thuciamna hong tun ding lamenin ka om niloh hi.
English: I prevented the dawning of the morning, and cried: I hoped in thy word.

**119:148**
Zolai: Nangma thuciamna a lungngaingai dingin zan khuavakin ka zanhak hi.
English: Mine eyes prevent the night watches, That I might meditate in thy word.

**119:149**
Zolai: Topa aw, na itna kip tawh a kizui-in ka aw hong za inla, nangma thutang tawh kizui-in ka nuntakna hong kem in.
English: Hear my voice according unto thy lovingkindness: O LORD , quicken me according to thy judgment.

**119:150**
Zolai: Gitloh ngimna tawh kei hong bawlsia mite in kei hong nehta uh a, amaute in nangma thu ngaihsutin nei lo uh hi.
English: They draw nigh that follow after mischief: They are far from thy law.

**119:151**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa aw, kei kiangah nang nong nai a, na thupiaknate khempeuh ahi taktak vive ahi hi.
English: Thou art near, O LORD ; And all thy commandments are truth.

**119:152**
Zolai: Tuate a tawntungin a kip dingin na bawl ahihna thu, nangma thuhilhnate panin sawtpi-in ka thei hi.
English: Concerning thy testimonies, I have known of old That thou hast founded them for ever.

**119:153**
Zolai: Ka thuakna hong en inla, kei hong honkhia in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma thu ka mangngilh kei hi.
English: Consider mine affliction, and deliver me: For I do not forget thy law.

**119:154**
Zolai: Ka thu-ah hong pang inla, kei hong suaktasak in. Na ciamsa bangin kei hong honkhia in.
English: Plead my cause, and deliver me: Quicken me according to thy word.

**119:155**
Zolai: Migilote, kihonkhia lo ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in na thukhamte zui lo uh hi.
English: Salvation is far from the wicked: For they seek not thy statutes.

**119:156**
Zolai: Topa aw, na hehpihna lian hi. Na biakna ngeina kip tawh a kituakin kei hong honkhia in.
English: Great are thy tender mercies, O LORD : Quicken me according to thy judgments.

**119:157**
Zolai: Kei hong bawlsiate, ka langte tam mahmah a, ahih hangin nangma thu panin kei ka pial tuan kei hi.
English: Many are my persecutors and mine enemies; Yet do I not decline from thy testimonies.

**119:158**
Zolai: Thuman lo mite ka muh ciangin ka kih mahmah hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in nangma thupiakte zui lo uh hi.
English: I beheld the transgressors, and was grieved; Because they kept not thy word.

**119:159**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhnate bangzah takin ka deihna hong ngaihsun in. Topa aw, na itna kip tawh a kizui-in kei hong hon in.
English: Consider how I love thy precepts: Quicken me, O LORD , according to thy lovingkindness.

**119:160**
Zolai: Na thubulpi thumanna hi a, a man mahmah, nangmah biakna ngeina kipte khempeuh a tawntungin kip paisuak hi.
English: Thy word is true from the beginning: And every one of thy righteous judgments endureth for ever.

**119:161**
Zolai: Uliante in thu om lopi-in kei hong bawlsia uh a, ahih hangin na thute lamdang sa mahmahin ka thupi ngaihsut hi.
English: Princes have persecuted me without a cause: But my heart standeth in awe of thy word.

**119:162**
Zolai: Vankinusia tampi tak a ngah pa bangin na thuciamna-ah ka lung a dam mahmah hi.
English: I rejoice at thy word, As one that findeth great spoil.

**119:163**
Zolai: Zuaunate zadahin ka kih a, ahih hangin nangma thu ka deih mahmah hi.
English: I hate and abhor lying: But thy law do I love.

**119:164**
Zolai: Nangmah biakna ngeina kipte hangin nisimin sagihvei nang kong phat hi.
English: Seven times a day do I praise thee Because of thy righteous judgments.

**119:165**
Zolai: Nangma thu a deihte in lungnopna lianpi ngah uh a, amaute a tuksakzo ding bangmah om lo hi.
English: Great peace have they which love thy law: And nothing shall offend them.

**119:166**
Zolai: Topa aw, nong hotkhiat ding ka ngak a, na thupiakte ka sem hi.
English: LORD , I have hoped for thy salvation, And done thy commandments.

**119:167**
Zolai: Na thuhilhnate ka zui a, tuate ka nak deih mahmah hi.
English: My soul hath kept thy testimonies; And I love them exceedingly.

**119:168**
Zolai: Na thuhilhnate le na ngeina kip omte khempeuh hoihtakin ka zui a, ka gamtatna khempeuh nangmah in na hong mu hi.
English: I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies: For all my ways are before thee.

**119:169**
Zolai: Topa aw, kong kikona aw, na kiang hong tung hen la, nangma thu omsa tawh kizui-in thu theihtelna kei hong guan in.
English: Let my cry come near before thee, O LORD : Give me understanding according to thy word.

**119:170**
Zolai: Keima thumna in na kiang hong ban hen la, nangma thu omsa tawh kizui-in kei hong honkhia in.
English: Let my supplication come before thee: Deliver me according to thy word.

**119:171**
Zolai: Na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh na hih manin kong phat tawntung ding hi.
English: My lips shall utter praise, When thou hast taught me thy statutes.

**119:172**
Zolai: Na thupiak khempeuh man mahmah ahih manin nangma thu phatna la ka sa ding hi.
English: My tongue shall speak of thy word: For all thy commandments are righteousness.

**119:173**
Zolai: Nangma thuhilhte hong zui ka hih manin keimah hong huh dingin a kigingsa-in om tawntung in.
English: Let thine hand help me; For I have chosen thy precepts.

**119:174**
Zolai: Topa aw, nong hotkhiat ding ka lamen a, nangma khut sungah nuam ka sa mahmah hi.
English: I have longed for thy salvation, O LORD ; And thy law is my delight.

**119:175**
Zolai: Nang kong phat theih nadingin kei hong nungtasak inla, nangmah biakna ngeina kipte kei hong huhsak in.
English: Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; And let thy judgments help me.

**119:176**
Zolai: A gammang tuu bangin lam ka pial khin hi. Tua ahih manin na nasempa hong zong in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma thupiaknate ka pelh kei hi.
English: I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek thy servant; For I do not forget thy commandments.

## Chapter 120

**120:1**
Zolai: Ka cihmawh ciangin Topa’ tungah ka kiko a, amah in hong dawng hi.
English: In my distress I cried unto the LORD , and he heard me.

**120:2**
Zolai: Topa aw, mizuaute le mikhemte’ kiang panin kei hong honkhia in.
English: Deliver my soul, O LORD , from lying lips, And from a deceitful tongue.

**120:3**
Zolai: Mikhem theite aw, note’ tungah bang hong kipia ding a, note’ tungah bang hong kihih ding ahi hiam?
English: What shall be given unto thee? or what shall be done unto thee, thou false tongue?

**120:4**
Zolai: Galhang pa’ thal hiamte le sesing hol-am hi ding hi.
English: Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper.

**120:5**
Zolai: Note lakah ka omkhak pen Meshek gam sungah tenkhak sangin haksazaw a, Kedar mite lakah tenkhak sangin siahuaizaw hi.
English: Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, That I dwell in the tents of Kedar!

**120:6**
Zolai: Gal kilemna a deih lo mite lakah sauvei ka teng luakha hi.
English: My soul hath long dwelt With him that hateth peace.

**120:7**
Zolai: Kei pen gal kilemna a ngaihsun mi ka hi hi. Ahih hangin kilemna ding thu ka gen ciangin amaute in galkido ding utna tengin nei uh hi.
English: I am for peace: But when I speak, they are for war.

## Chapter 121

**121:1**
Zolai: Keimah in mualtung lam ka ento hi. Keimah huhna koi lai pan hong pai ding ahi hiam?
English: I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, From whence cometh my help.

**121:2**
Zolai: Van le lei a bawl Topa’ kiang panin keimah huhna hong pai hi.
English: My help cometh from the LORD , Which made heaven and earth.

**121:3**
Zolai: Amah in ka khe taalsak lo ding a, kei hong kem pa lusu lo ding hi.
English: He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: He that keepeth thee will not slumber.

**121:4**
Zolai: En un, Israel a kem pa lusu lo a, zong ihmu lo hi.
English: Behold, he that keepeth Israel Shall neither slumber nor sleep.

**121:5**
Zolai: Topa in nang hong cing ding a, nangmah a hong hu dingin na kiangah hong om hi.
English: The LORD is thy keeper: The LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.

**121:6**
Zolai: Sunin ni in nang hong gimsak lo ding a, zanin kha in zong nang hong sukha lo ding hi.
English: The sun shall not smite thee by day, Nor the moon by night.

**121:7**
Zolai: Topa in siatna khempeuh panin nang hong hu ding a, amah in a muanhuai-in nang hong kem ding hi.
English: The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil: He shall preserve thy soul.

**121:8**
Zolai: Topa in tua kipan a tawntungin na vaksuk na vaktohna-ah nang hong kem ding hi.
English: The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in From this time forth, and even for evermore.

## Chapter 122

**122:1**
Zolai: Amaute in kei tungah, “ Topa’ inn-ah pai ni,” hong cih uh ciangin kei ka kipak hi.
English: I was glad when they said unto me, Let us go into the house of the LORD .

**122:2**
Zolai: Jerusalem aw, na kulhkongpi sungah kote hong tungin ka ding khinta uh hi.
English: Our feet shall stand Within thy gates, O Jerusalem.

**122:3**
Zolai: Jerusalem khuapi pen Israel-te tungah thu a kipiaksa bangin Topa’ tungah lungdamna a ko dingin Topa’ minamte, Israel minamte, a hong paitohna, khuapi lian tawh a kibangin a kibawl, kiptakin a kilam bikbek khuapi ahi hi.
English: Jerusalem is builded As a city that is compact together:

**122:5**
Zolai: David’ innkuante’ kumpi tokhom, thukhenna ding kumpi tokhomte, tua lai-ah kikoih hi.
English: For there are set thrones of judgment, The thrones of the house of David.

**122:6**
Zolai: Jerusalem khuapi, a nopsakna ding thu ngen unla, “Nang hong itte a dau pai tahen.
English: Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: They shall prosper that love thee.

**122:7**
Zolai: Na khua sungah lungnopna om hen la, na galvilna tausangte’ huam sungah lungmuanna om ta hen,” ci-in ngen un.
English: Peace be within thy walls, And prosperity within thy palaces.

**122:8**
Zolai: Sanggamte le kikholhpihte ka khualna-in, “Jerusalem in nopna om ta hen,” ka ci ding hi.
English: For my brethren and companions' sakes, I will now say, Peace be within thee.

**122:9**
Zolai: Topa eite’ Pasian’ inn ka khualna-in nangma hoihna ding thu ka ngen ding hi.
English: Because of the house of the LORD our God I will seek thy good.

## Chapter 123

**123:1**
Zolai: Vantungah a om pa aw, nangmah kong ento hi.
English: Unto thee lift I up mine eyes, O thou that dwellest in the heavens.

**123:2**
Zolai: Nasem pasalte in a topa uh muang a, nasem numeite in a tonu uh a muan mah bangin ko tungah hehpihna nong neih matengin Topa kote’ Pasian kong mitsuan uh hi.
English: Behold, as the eyes of servants Look unto the hand of their masters, and as the eyes of a maiden unto the hand of her mistress; So our eyes wait upon the LORD our God, Until that he have mercy upon us.

**123:3**
Zolai: Kote hong hehpih in. Topa aw, kote hong hehpih in. Bang hang hiam cih leh kote in ka thuak zawh loh uh simmawhna ka thuak uh hi.
English: Have mercy upon us, O LORD , have mercy upon us: For we are exceedingly filled with contempt.

**123:4**
Zolai: A ututin a gamta mite in kote a hong zahkona, a kiphasak mite in hong simmawh bawlna hangin ka gimthuakna uh sauvei lua khinta hi.
English: Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those that are at ease, And with the contempt of the proud.

## Chapter 124

**124:1**
Zolai: Israel mite aw, Topa in hong panpih lo hileh i tuah ding thu thei un.
English: If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, now may Israel say;

**124:2**
Zolai: Eite langpangin mite hong kipat ciangin eite’ lamah Topa hong pang lo hileh,
English: If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, when men rose up against us:

**124:3**
Zolai: eite’ tungah a hehna uh a kisosuah ciangin amaute in eite a hingin hong nawmvalh khin ding uh hi.
English: Then they had swallowed us up quick, When their wrath was kindled against us:

**124:4**
Zolai: Tuikhang in eite hong tai-in, tuihual in hong tum khin ding a,
English: Then the waters had overwhelmed us, The stream had gone over our soul:

**124:5**
Zolai: tuipi husiate in hong tuummang khin ding hi.
English: Then the proud waters, Had gone over our soul.

**124:6**
Zolai: Amaute’ suksiat dingin eite a hong piakhia lo Topa in thupha ngah tahen.
English: Blessed be the LORD , Who hath not given us as a prey to their teeth.

**124:7**
Zolai: Thangsiahte’ thangzak panin vasa a suahtak bangin eite i suakta hi. Thangkhau kibottat a, eite i suakta khinta hi.
English: Our soul is escaped as a bird out of the snare of the fowlers: The snare is broken, and we are escaped.

**124:8**
Zolai: Van le lei a bawl Topa’ tung panin eite huhna hong pai hi.
English: Our help is in the name of the LORD , Who made heaven and earth.

## Chapter 125

**125:1**
Zolai: Topa a muang mite pen ling hetloin a om tawntung Zion Mual tawh kibang hi.
English: They that trust in the LORD Shall be as mount Zion, Which cannot be removed, But abideth for ever.

**125:2**
Zolai: Jerusalem kimkotah mualte a om mah bangin ama mite’ kimkotah tua kipan a tawntungin Topa om ding hi.
English: As the mountains are round about Jerusalem, So the LORD is round about his people from henceforth even for ever.

**125:3**
Zolai: Thuman mite a khialhkhak loh nadingun amau a kipia leitang tungah migilote in amaute uk paisuak lo ding hi.
English: For the rod of the wicked shall not rest upon the lot of the righteous; Lest the righteous put forth their hands unto iniquity.

**125:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, a hoih mite tung le na thupiakna a zui mite tungah hehpihna hong nei in.
English: Do good, O LORD , Unto those that be good, and to them that are upright in their hearts.

**125:5**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amau’ gitlohna a zuite pen siatna a bawlte gim na piak ciangin amaute tawh piakhawm in. Israel tungah nopna om ta hen!
English: As for such as turn aside unto their crooked ways, the LORD shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity: But peace shall be upon Israel.

## Chapter 126

**126:1**
Zolai: Topa in Zion-ah eite hong ciahpih kik ciangin i mang tawh kibang liang hi.
English: When the LORD turned again the captivity of Zion, We were like them that dream.

**126:2**
Zolai: Lungdamin i nui a, lungdam lua-in la i sa hi. Tua ciangin minam dangte kiho-in, “ Topa in amau a dingin na lianpite bawl khinta hi,” kici uh hi.
English: Then was our mouth filled with laughter, And our tongue with singing: Then said they among the heathen, The LORD hath done great things for them.

**126:3**
Zolai: Topa in eite a dingin na lianpite bawl khinta a, eite i kipak hi.
English: The LORD hath done great things for us; Whereof we are glad.

**126:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, lei keuna munah guah in tui a puak bangin kote’ nopsaknate a ngei hong bangsakkik ta in.
English: Turn again our captivity, O LORD , As the streams in the south.

**126:5**
Zolai: Khitui tawh khai a tuhte lungdamin kikona tawh an la sak ta in.
English: They that sow in tears Shall reap in joy.

**126:6**
Zolai: Kap kawmin kuankhia-in a tuh ding khaici a pua mi lungdamin kikona tawh buhlomte pua-in hong ciah ding hi.
English: He that goeth forth and weepeth, bearing precious seed, Shall doubtless come again with rejoicing, bringing his sheaves with him .

## Chapter 127

**127:1**
Zolai: Topa in inn lampih kei leh innlamte’ sepna a mawkna ahi hi. Topa in khuapi hutpih kei leh khuapi cingte’ cinna a mawkna ahi hi.
English: Except the LORD build the house, They labour in vain that build it: Except the LORD keep the city, The watchman waketh but in vain.

**127:2**
Zolai: Zingsangin tho baihin, gimpi a nangma sepsa an na nek hakna zong a mawkna mah ahi hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in ama itte tungah a ihmut sung nangawnun a pia hi.
English: It is vain for you to rise up early, to sit up late, to eat the bread of sorrows: For so he giveth his beloved sleep.

**127:3**
Zolai: En un, tate pen Topa’ tung pana letsong hi a, tapate pen ama hong piak thupha ahi hi.
English: Lo, children are an heritage of the LORD : And the fruit of the womb is his reward.

**127:4**
Zolai: Mi khat in a khangno lai-in a neih tate pen galhang pa’ khutsunga a om a thaltangte tawh kibang hi.
English: As arrows are in the hand of a mighty man; So are children of the youth.

**127:5**
Zolai: A thallawng dimin tua bang thaltang a nei pa mi lungdam ahi hi. Amah guallel ngei lo ding a, zahhuai ngei lo ding hi.
English: Happy is the man that hath his quiver full of them: They shall not be ashamed, but they shall speak with the enemies in the gate.

## Chapter 128

**128:1**
Zolai: Topa zahtakin ama thu a zui mi khempeuh thupha ngah mi ahi hi.
English: Blessed is every one that feareth the LORD ; That walketh in his ways.

**128:2**
Zolai: Na khut tawh na sep thaman na ne ding a, na lungdamin na maavang ding hi.
English: For thou shalt eat the labour of thine hands: Happy shalt thou be , and it shall be well with thee.

**128:3**
Zolai: Nangma inn sungah na zi, a gah pha mahmah leenggui tawh kibang ding a, na sabuai kiimah a tu na tate, oliv no dawng hilhhelh tawh kibang ding uh hi.
English: Thy wife shall be as a fruitful vine by the sides of thine house: Thy children like olive plants round about thy table.

**128:4**
Zolai: En un, Topa a zahtak mi tua bangin thupha kipia ding hi.
English: Behold, that thus shall the man be blessed that feareth the LORD .

**128:5**
Zolai: Topa in Zion panin nang thupha hong pia hen la, na nuntak sung tawntung Jerusalem’ nopsakna mu ta in.
English: The LORD shall bless thee out of Zion: And thou shalt see the good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life.

**128:6**
Zolai: Na tute a mu dingin hong siam tahen. Israel tungah nopna om ta hen!
English: Yea, thou shalt see thy children's children, And peace upon Israel.

## Chapter 129

**129:1**
Zolai: “Ka neu lai a kipanin nakpitakin amaute in kei hong gimsak uh hi,” Israel in tu-in ci tahen.
English: Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth, May Israel now say:

**129:2**
Zolai: “Ka neu lai a kipanin nakpitakin amaute in kei hong gimsak uh a, ahih hangin amaute in kei hong zo nai lo uh hi.
English: Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth: Yet they have not prevailed against me.

**129:3**
Zolai: Lo khote in lei a kuih bangin ka nungzang hong kuikek uh a, tu-ma-kuakte tawh kibangsak uh hi.
English: The plowers plowed upon my back: They made long their furrows.

**129:4**
Zolai: Topa thuman a, amah in migilote’ henna khaute sutat khinta hi,” amaute in ci ta uh hen.
English: The LORD is righteous: He hath cut asunder the cords of the wicked.

**129:5**
Zolai: Zion a mudahte khempeuh maizumin kinungkiksak tahen.
English: Let them all be confounded and turned back That hate Zion.

**129:6**
Zolai: Amaute pen a khan khit ma-a a vul, innkhumzanga lopa, an at pa in a khut sungah a kaihkhop loh, buhlom hen pa in a ang-ah a pom loh, amau a mukhate in, “ Topa’ thupha na tungah om tahen. Topa’ min tawh thupha kong pia uh hi,” a cih loh mite tawh kibangsak in.
English: Let them be as the grass upon the housetops, Which withereth afore it groweth up:

## Chapter 130

**130:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka lungkham mahmahna panin nang tungah kong kiko hi.
English: Out of the depths have I cried unto thee, O LORD .

**130:2**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka aw hong za in. Ka thumna awgingte hong ngai in.
English: Lord, hear my voice: Let thine ears be attentive To the voice of my supplications.

**130:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangmah in mawhneite ciamteh lecin, Topa aw, kua in thuakzo ding ahi hiam?
English: If thou, LORD , shouldest mark iniquities, O Lord, who shall stand?

**130:4**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nangmah hong kizahtak theih nadingin nangmah in mawhna na maisak hi.
English: But there is forgiveness with thee, That thou mayest be feared.

**130:5**
Zolai: Topa’ hong huh ding lawpna tawh ka ngak a, ama thugen ka muang hi.
English: I wait for the LORD , my soul doth wait, And in his word do I hope.

**130:6**
Zolai: Galvilte in zingsang hun ding a ngaklah sangin galvilte in phalvak hun ding a ngaklah sangin, Topa ka ngaklah zaw hi.
English: My soul waiteth for the Lord More than they that watch for the morning: I say, more than they that watch for the morning.

**130:7**
Zolai: Israel aw, Topa muang in. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa’ itna kip tawntungin, hong honkhia nuam tawntung hi.
English: Let Israel hope in the LORD : For with the LORD there is mercy, And with him is plenteous redemption.

**130:8**
Zolai: Mawhna a om khempeuh panin amah in Israel-te a honkhia ding hi.
English: And he shall redeem Israel from all his iniquities.

## Chapter 131

**131:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka lungsim kiliansak nawn lo a, kei ka kihisak nawnkei hi. Kei a dingin a lianlua le a lamdang luate ngaihsutin ka nei kei hi.
English: LORD , my heart is not haughty, Nor mine eyes lofty: Neither do I exercise myself in Great matters, or in things too high for me.

**131:2**
Zolai: A nu’ nawi tawh a kikhenta naupang bangin daitakin ka om dide zota hi. A dai hithiat-a om naupang tawh ka kibangta hi.
English: Surely I have behaved and quieted myself, As a child that is weaned of his mother: My soul is even as a weaned child.

**131:3**
Zolai: Israel aw, tu a kipanin a tawntungin Topa muang in.
English: Let Israel hope in the LORD From henceforth and for ever.

## Chapter 132

**132:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, David na ngaihsutna-in a gim thuaknate khempeuh le amah in, “Jakob’ Vanglianpa’ tenna ding, Topa a’ ding mun ka muh matengin ka inn sungah ka lum kei ding a, ka lupna ka zuan kei ding hi. Ka ihmu kei ding a, ka mitkhute ka kikhupsak kei ding hi,” ci-in Jakob’ Vanglianpa’ tungah hong thuciamna le Topa’ tungah hong kiciamnate phawk in.
English: LORD , remember David, And all his afflictions:

**132:6**
Zolai: Jaar gam sungah Thuciamna Singkuang ka mu uh hi, cihna thuthak Bethlehem-ah kiza hi.
English: Lo, we heard of it at Ephratah: We found it in the fields of the wood.

**132:7**
Zolai: “Ama omna munah va pai ni; ama khengakna-ah va bia ni,” ka ci uh hi.
English: We will go into his tabernacles: We will worship at his footstool.

**132:8**
Zolai: Topa aw, tho inla na vangliatna lim Thuciamna Singkuang tawh na omna munah pai in.
English: Arise, O LORD , into thy rest; Thou, and the ark of thy strength.

**132:9**
Zolai: Na mite na hotkhiatna thu, na siampite in taangko hen la, na mi siangthote lungdamin awng ta uh hen.
English: Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness; And let thy saints shout for joy.

**132:10**
Zolai: Na nasempa David tungah thu na ciamzo hi; na sathau nilh pa nial kei in.
English: For thy servant David's sake Turn not away the face of thine anointed.

**132:11**
Zolai: Topa in a pelh loh ding kiciamna taktak khat David tungah kiciam a, “Nang’ sung pana na tate khat na kumpi tokhom tungah ka koih ding hi.
English: The LORD hath sworn in truth unto David; He will not turn from it; Of the fruit of thy body Will I set upon thy throne.

**132:12**
Zolai: Na tate in, amau’ tungah ka hilh ding ka thuciamna le ka teci pannate a zuih nak-uhleh, amau’ tate zong na kumpi tokhom tungah tu paisuak ding uh hi,” na ci hi.
English: If thy children will keep my covenant and my testimony that I shall teach them, Their children shall also sit upon thy throne for evermore.

**132:13**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in Zion teel khinzo a, amah in tua mun pen ama ten nadingin a deih hi.
English: For the LORD hath chosen Zion; He hath desired it for his habitation.

**132:14**
Zolai: “Hih mun pen ka om tawntungna ding ahi hi; hih mun deih ka hih manin hih lai-ah ka teng ding hi.
English: This is my rest for ever: Here will I dwell; for I have desired it.

**132:15**
Zolai: Ama beemlepang thupha tampi ka pia ding a, a mizawngte an ka vak kham ding hi.
English: I will abundantly bless her provision: I will satisfy her poor with bread.

**132:16**
Zolai: Ka hotkhiatna thu, a siampite ka taangkosak ding a, a mi siangthote lungdamin la sa-in awng ding uh hi.
English: I will also clothe her priests with salvation: And her saints shall shout aloud for joy.

**132:17**
Zolai: Keimah in tua lai-ah David’ suanlekhakte kumpi lianin ka koih ding a, ka sathau nilh pa’ ukna ka kipsak ding hi.
English: There will I make the horn of David to bud: I have ordained a lamp for mine anointed.

**132:18**
Zolai: Ama galte maizumna tawh ka dimsak ding a, ahih hangin ama kumpi gam khangin zai semsem ding hi,” na ci hi.
English: His enemies will I clothe with shame: But upon himself shall his crown flourish.

## Chapter 133

**133:1**
Zolai: En un, sanggamte pumkhat suakin a tut khawm uh ciangin bangzahin hoihin nuam ahi hiam?
English: Behold, how good and how pleasant it is For brethren to dwell together in unity!

**133:2**
Zolai: Tua pen a puan ngawng tungah Aaron’ khamul kaisuk zui-in a lu tung panin a taaksuk, sathau manpha tawh kibang hi.
English: It is like the precious ointment upon the head, that ran down upon the beard, Even Aaron's beard: That went down to the skirts of his garments;

**133:3**
Zolai: Tua pen Zion mualte tungah a kia, Hermon mual pana hong piang daitui tawh kibang hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in nuntak tawntungna thupha tua munah a pia hi.
English: As the dew of Hermon, And as the dew that descended upon the mountains of Zion: For there the LORD commanded the blessing, Even life for evermore.

## Chapter 134

**134:1**
Zolai: Zan khuavakin Topa’ inn sungah a ding, Topa’ nasemte khempeuh aw, hong pai-in Topa phat un.
English: Behold, bless ye the LORD , All ye servants of the LORD , Which by night stand in the house of the LORD .

**134:2**
Zolai: Siangtho mun lamah na khutte uh laamto-in Topa phat un.
English: Lift up your hands in the sanctuary, And bless the LORD .

**134:3**
Zolai: Van le lei a bawl Topa in Zion panin note tungah thupha hong pia tahen.
English: The LORD that made heaven and earth Bless thee out of Zion.

## Chapter 135

**135:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. I Pasian’ inn huangsung, Topa’ innsunga a ding, Topa’ nasemte aw, Topa phat un; ama min phat un.
English: Praise ye the LORD . Praise ye the name of the LORD ; Praise him , O ye servants of the LORD .

**135:3**
Zolai: Topa phat un; bang hang hiam cih leh Topa hoih hi. Ama min phatna la sak un; bang hang hiam cih leh amah phatnophuai hi.
English: Praise the LORD ; for the LORD is good: Sing praises unto his name; for it is pleasant.

**135:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in ama a dingin Jakob teel a, ama neihsa dingin Israel teel khinta hi.
English: For the LORD hath chosen Jacob unto himself, And Israel for his peculiar treasure.

**135:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa lian hi, ci-in ka thei a, eite’ Topa pen pasian dang khempeuh sangin a lianzaw hi.
English: For I know that the LORD is great, And that our Lord is above all gods.

**135:6**
Zolai: Vantung le leitung, tuipi le a thukna sung khempeuhah Topa in ama ut peuhpeuh a bawl hi.
English: Whatsoever the LORD pleased, that did he in heaven, and in earth, In the seas, and all deep places.

**135:7**
Zolai: Amah in leimong panin meiipi kaisakin, guahzuk nadingin khuaphialepte bawl a, a huihkua panin huih a pusuaksak hi.
English: He causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the earth; He maketh lightnings for the rain; He bringeth the wind out of his treasuries.

**135:8**
Zolai: Amah in Egypt gam sungah mihing ganhing tacil khempeuh a vatmai hi.
English: Who smote the firstborn of Egypt, Both of man and beast.

**135:9**
Zolai: Egypt aw, nangma sungah lim le na lamdangte, Faro le a nasem khempeuhte gimpiakna-in a lak hi.
English: Who sent tokens and wonders into the midst of thee, O Egypt, Upon Pharaoh, and upon all his servants.

**135:10**
Zolai: Minam tampite vatmai-in kumpi vangliante that a,
English: Who smote great nations, And slew mighty kings;

**135:11**
Zolai: Amor kumpipa Sihon, Bashan kumpipa Og le Kanaan kumpite a that hi.
English: Sihon king of the Amorites, and Og king of Bashan, And all the kingdoms of Canaan:

**135:12**
Zolai: Amau’ leitang khempeuh, ama mi Israel-te’ luah dingin a piakhia hi.
English: And gave their land for an heritage, An heritage unto Israel his people.

**135:13**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma min kip tawntung hi. Topa aw, na minthanna khang tawntungin a kip hi.
English: Thy name, O LORD , endureth for ever; And thy memorial, O LORD , throughout all generations.

**135:14**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in ama mite’ thu khenin, ama nasemte tungah hehpihna a nei ding hi.
English: For the LORD will judge his people, And he will repent himself concerning his servants.

**135:15**
Zolai: Minam dangte’ pasian-te pen mihingte’ khut tawh a kibawl, ngun le kham ahi hi.
English: The idols of the heathen are silver and gold, the work of men's hands.

**135:16**
Zolai: Amaute in kam nei napi, pau thei lo uh hi. Amaute in mit nei napi, khua mu thei lo uh hi.
English: They have mouths, but they speak not; Eyes have they, but they see not;

**135:17**
Zolai: Amaute in bil nei napi, khua za thei lo uh hi. Amaute’ kam sungah naksuk naktoh theihna nei lo uh hi.
English: They have ears, but they hear not; Neither is there any breath in their mouths.

**135:18**
Zolai: Milim a bawl mite pen milim mah bangsak in. Milim a muang khempeuhte zong tua milimte mah bangsak in.
English: They that make them are like unto them: So is every one that trusteth in them.

**135:19**
Zolai: Israel mite aw, Topa phat un. Aaron’ innkuante aw, Topa phat un.
English: Bless the LORD , O house of Israel: Bless the LORD , O house of Aaron:

**135:20**
Zolai: Levi mite aw, Topa phat un. Topa a zahtakte aw, Topa phat un.
English: Bless the LORD , O house of Levi: Ye that fear the LORD , bless the LORD .

**135:21**
Zolai: Jerusalem inn-a a nei, Zion-a om Topa in thupha ngah tahen. Topa phat un.
English: Blessed be the LORD out of Zion, Which dwelleth at Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 136

**136:1**
Zolai: Amah hoih ahih manin Topa tungah lungdamna ko un; bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: O give thanks unto the LORD ; for he is good: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:2**
Zolai: Lungdamna pen pasian-te’ Pasian’ tungah ko un; bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: O give thanks unto the God of gods: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:3**
Zolai: Lungdamna pen topate’ Topa’ tungah ko un; bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: O give thanks to the Lord of lords: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:4**
Zolai: Na lamdang lian a bawl amah bek Pasian ahipa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him who alone doeth great wonders: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:5**
Zolai: Theihna tawh vantungte a bawlpa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him that by wisdom made the heavens: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:6**
Zolai: Tuite tungah leitung a zal pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him that stretched out the earth above the waters: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:7**
Zolai: Khuavak lianpite a bawlpa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him that made great lights: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:8**
Zolai: Sun pen ni a uksak pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: The sun to rule by day: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:9**
Zolai: Zan pen kha le aksite a uksak pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: The moon and stars to rule by night: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:10**
Zolai: Egypt gam tacil khempeuh a vatmaipa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him that smote Egypt in their firstborn: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:11**
Zolai: Amau’ gam sung pan Israel-te a paikhiatpih pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
