English: And brought out Israel from among them: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:12**
Zolai: A baan zanin a khut thahat tawh a paikhiatpih pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: With a strong hand, and with a stretched out arm: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:13**
Zolai: San Tuipi a phelkham pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him which divided the Red sea into parts: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:14**
Zolai: Israel-te tui laizang a kantan sakpa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: And made Israel to pass through the midst of it: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:15**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Faro le a mihonte San Tuipi sungah a thalpaih pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: But overthrew Pharaoh and his host in the Red sea: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:16**
Zolai: Sehnel gam nawkin ama mite a paipihpa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him which led his people through the wilderness: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:17**
Zolai: Kumpi liante a vatmaipa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: To him which smote great kings: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:18**
Zolai: Kumpi minthangte a that pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: And slew famous kings: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:19**
Zolai: Amor mite’ kumpipa Sihon’ hang le, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi;
English: Sihon king of the Amorites: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:20**
Zolai: Bashan kumpipa Og’ hangin, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: And Og the king of Bashan: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:21**
Zolai: Amaute’ leitang pen gamhluah dingin a piakhia pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: And gave their land for an heritage: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:22**
Zolai: Ama nasem Israel tungah gamh a a piapa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: Even an heritage unto Israel his servant: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:23**
Zolai: Miniam ihih laitakin a hong phawk pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: Who remembered us in our low estate: For his mercy endureth for ever:

**136:24**
Zolai: I galte’ kiang pan eite hong honkhia pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: And hath redeemed us from our enemies: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:25**
Zolai: Nuntakna a nei khempeuh an a vak pa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: Who giveth food to all flesh: For his mercy endureth for ever.

**136:26**
Zolai: Vantung Pasian’ tungah lungdamna ko un; bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
English: O give thanks unto the God of heaven: For his mercy endureth for ever.

## Chapter 137

**137:1**
Zolai: Zion khuapi i ngaihsut khak ciangin Babylon luite gei-ah eite tusukin i kapkap hi.
English: By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down, yea, we wept, When we remembered Zion.

**137:2**
Zolai: Tua lai-a gialhek kungte tungah i laiza lasaknate i khai hi;
English: We hanged our harps Upon the willows in the midst thereof.

**137:3**
Zolai: bang hang hiam cih leh ei hong man mite in la i sak ding hong deih a, ei hong bawlsiate in i gualnop ding hong deihin, “Zion late khat hong sak un,” hong ci uh hi.
English: For there they that carried us away captive required of us a song; And they that wasted us required of us mirth, saying , Sing us one of the songs of Zion.

**137:4**
Zolai: Topa’ la, gam dangah bangci sak theih ding ihi hiam?
English: How shall we sing The LORD 's song in a strange land?

**137:5**
Zolai: Jerusalem khuapi aw, nang kong mangngilh taak leh ka taklam khut buisum ta hen!
English: If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, Let my right hand forget her cunning .

**137:6**
Zolai: Nang kong phawk kei a, kei’ lungdamna a lian pen sangin Jerusalem a sangzaw-in kong koih kei taak leh ka dang tawngah ka leii toncip ta hen!
English: If I do not remember thee, let my tongue cleave to the roof of my mouth; If I prefer not Jerusalem above my chief joy.

**137:7**
Zolai: Topa aw, Jerusalem a siat hun lai-in Edom mite in, “Sumai un, sumai un! A bulpi dongin sumai un!” a cih vialna uh phawk in.
English: Remember, O LORD , the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem; Who said, Rase it , rase it , even to the foundation thereof.

**137:8**
Zolai: Misusia Babylon aw, kote’ tungah nong bawl bangin nang tungah hong thukpa in lungdamna ngah ta hen!
English: O daughter of Babylon, who art to be destroyed; Happy shall he be , that rewardeth thee as thou hast served us.

**137:9**
Zolai: Na taneute hong laksakin suangtumpi denna-in a hong neihsak pa in lungdamna ngah ta hen!
English: Happy shall he be , that taketh and dasheth thy little ones Against the stones.

## Chapter 138

**138:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka lungsim khempeuh tawh nangma tungah lungdamna kong ko a, pasian-te’ mai-ah nangmah phatna ka sa hi.
English: I will praise thee with my whole heart: Before the gods will I sing praise unto thee.

**138:2**
Zolai: Na biakinn siangtho lamah kei ka kun a, na itna kip le na thumanna hangin na min kong phat hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh na dang khempeuh sangin na min le na thu a liatzawkna na lak hi.
English: I will worship toward thy holy temple, and praise thy name for thy lovingkindness and for thy truth: For thou hast magnified thy word above all thy name.

**138:3**
Zolai: Nang kong sap ciangin kei nong dawng a, na thahatna tawh kei nong thakhauhsak hi.
English: In the day when I cried thou answeredst me, And strengthenedst me with strength in my soul.

**138:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, leitung khempeuh in na thuciamnate za khin uh ahih manin nang hong phat ding uh hi.
English: All the kings of the earth shall praise thee, O LORD , When they hear the words of thy mouth.

**138:5**
Zolai: Topa’ minthanna lian mahmah ahih manin amaute in Topa’ nasepna ziate la-in sa ding uh hi.
English: Yea, they shall sing in the ways of the LORD : For great is the glory of the LORD .

**138:6**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa lian mahmah napi-in amah in a neute don a, a kiphasakte ahihleh amah in gamlapi panin mu thei veve hi.
English: Though the LORD be high, yet hath he respect unto the lowly: But the proud he knoweth afar off.

**138:7**
Zolai: Haksatna tuamtuamte ka thuak ciangin kei nong kem hi. A heh ka galte, kei’ tangin nong dosak a, na thahatna tawh kei na hong honkhia hi.
English: Though I walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive me: Thou shalt stretch forth thine hand against the wrath of mine enemies, and thy right hand shall save me.

**138:8**
Zolai: Topa in kei a dingin a ngaihsutte hong tungsak ding hi. Topa aw, na itna kip tawntung hi. Na sepsa na maban hong tun ta in.
English: The LORD will perfect that which concerneth me: Thy mercy, O LORD , endureth for ever: Forsake not the works of thine own hands.

## Chapter 139

**139:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangmah in kei na hong entel a, nong thei khin hi.
English: O LORD , thou hast searched me, and known me .

**139:2**
Zolai: Nangmah in ka heksukna, ka hektohnate na thei hi. Nangmah in ka ngaihsutnate gamlapi pek panin na thei hi.
English: Thou knowest my downsitting and mine uprising, thou understandest my thought afar off.

**139:3**
Zolai: Nangmah in ka sep laitak ahi a, ka khawl laitak ahi zongin na hong mu a, ka gamtatna khempeuh a vekpi-in na thei hi.
English: Thou compassest my path and my lying down, And art acquainted with all my ways.

**139:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, kam khat bek nangawn ka paukhiat ma-in, nangmah in ka gen dingteng a vekpi-in na thei khin hi.
English: For there is not a word in my tongue, But , lo, O LORD , thou knowest it altogether.

**139:5**
Zolai: Nangmah in ka nung le ka mai-ah nong dal a, na thahatna tawh kei na hong hu hi.
English: Thou hast beset me behind and before, And laid thine hand upon me.

**139:6**
Zolai: Tua bangin kei nong theihna pen kei a dingin lamdang lua mahmah a, thuthuk lua ahih manin kei’ theihtel zawh ding hi lo hi.
English: Such knowledge is too wonderful for me; It is high, I cannot attain unto it.

**139:7**
Zolai: Nangmah a pelh dingin koi-ah pai ding a, nangma omna panin koi lai-ah taikhia ding ka hi hiam?
English: Whither shall I go from thy spirit? Or whither shall I flee from thy presence?

**139:8**
Zolai: Vantungah kahto leng tua lai-ah nang na om ding a, Leinuai misite’ gamah lupna bawlta leng zong tua lai-ah zong nang na om veve ding hi.
English: If I ascend up into heaven, thou art there: If I make my bed in hell, behold, thou art there .

**139:9**
Zolai: Leimong pekah leengin, tuipi mong pekah omta leng zong,
English: If I take the wings of the morning, And dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea;

**139:10**
Zolai: tua lai nangawnah nangma khut in kei hong paipihin, na khut taklam in kei hong len ding hi.
English: Even there shall thy hand lead me, And thy right hand shall hold me.

**139:11**
Zolai: “Khuamial in kei hong tuamcip hen la, ka kiima khuavak omte zan khuamial suak hen,” ci taleng zong,
English: If I say, Surely the darkness shall cover me; Even the night shall be light about me.

**139:12**
Zolai: tua nangawnah, nangma a dingin khuamial pen mial lo a, zan khuamial pen sun nitaang tawh kibang hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang a dingin khuamial pen khuavak mah bang lel hi.
English: Yea, the darkness hideth not from thee; But the night shineth as the day: The darkness and the light are both alike to thee .

**139:13**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ka pumpi na khempeuh na hong piangsak a, ka nu’ gil sungah keimah nong khuituah hi.
English: For thou hast possessed my reins: Thou hast covered me in my mother's womb.

**139:14**
Zolai: Kihtak dingin a kilawm na hih manin nang ka hong phat hi. Na nasepnate lamdang mahmah! Nangmah in kei nong lim theih mahmah hi.
English: I will praise thee; for I am fearfully and wonderfully made: Marvellous are thy works; And that my soul knoweth right well.

**139:15**
Zolai: A thukna sung mun simthamah kei hong kikhuituahin hong kibawl laitakin, ka guh ka taang, na mai-ah kiliah lo hi.
English: My substance was not hid from thee, When I was made in secret, and curiously wrought in the lowest parts of the earth.

**139:16**
Zolai: A kipiangsak nai lo keima pumpi nate na mit in a mu hi. Ka pumpi nate khat beek a om ma, ka ni zah ding a kiciangtan laitakin, tuate khempeuh na laibu sungah kigelh khin hi.
English: Thine eyes did see my substance, yet being unperfect; And in thy book all my members were written, Which in continuance were fashioned, When as yet there was none of them.

**139:17**
Zolai: Pasian aw, na ngaihsutnate kei a dingin manpha mahmah a, tuate khempeuh a vekpi-in zai mahmah hi.
English: How precious also are thy thoughts unto me, O God! How great is the sum of them!

**139:18**
Zolai: Tuate a mal sim leng sehnel sangin tamzaw hi. Ka khanlawh ciangin nang tawh ka omkhawm lai hi.
English: If I should count them, they are more in number than the sand: When I awake, I am still with thee.

**139:19**
Zolai: Pasian aw, migilote that inla, kei kiang panin mi that theite paikhia sak in.
English: Surely thou wilt slay the wicked, O God: Depart from me therefore, ye bloody men.

**139:20**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in nang hong dem uh a, ngimna hoih lo tawh nang hong pang uh hi.
English: For they speak against thee wickedly, And thine enemies take thy name in vain.

**139:21**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang hong mudah mite ke’n mudah hi lo ka hi hiam? Nang’ langah hong pangte ke’n kih hi lo ka hi hiam?
English: Do not I hate them, O LORD , that hate thee? And am not I grieved with those that rise up against thee?

**139:22**
Zolai: Amaute ka mudah mahmah a, amaute ka galin ka seh hi.
English: I hate them with perfect hatred: I count them mine enemies.

**139:23**
Zolai: Pasian aw, kei hong entel inla, ka lungsim hong thei in. Kei hong sit inla, ka ngaihsutnate hong thei in.
English: Search me, O God, and know my heart: Try me, and know my thoughts:

**139:24**
Zolai: Kei sungah siattheihna a omkha hiam hong en inla, tawntung lampi-ah kei hong kha in.
English: And see if there be any wicked way in me, And lead me in the way everlasting.

## Chapter 140

**140:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, migilote kiang panin kei hong honkhia inla, mi ngongtatte kiang panin kei hong kem in.
English: Deliver me, O LORD , from the evil man: Preserve me from the violent man;

**140:2**
Zolai: Amaute in a lung sung uhah thusia geelgeel uh a, gal phuang ngitnget uh hi.
English: Which imagine mischiefs in their heart; Continually are they gathered together for war.

**140:3**
Zolai: A leii uh gulpi leii bang a, a thugente uh gulgu bang hi.
English: They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent; Adders' poison is under their lips. Selah.

**140:4**
Zolai: Topa aw, migilote’ khutsung panin kei hong cing inla, kei, sukpaih ding a hong sawm mi ngongtatte kiang panin kei hong kem in.
English: Keep me, O LORD , from the hands of the wicked; Preserve me from the violent man; Who have purposed to overthrow my goings.

**140:5**
Zolai: Mi kiphasakte in keimah hong siahna-in tehlop tung sim uh a, amaute in ngenthang zakin lam gei-ah thangzak tawh kei hong siah uh hi.
English: The proud have hid a snare for me, and cords; They have spread a net by the wayside; They have set gins for me. Selah.

**140:6**
Zolai: Topa’ tungah hih bangin ka ci hi: Nang pen keima Pasian na hi hi; ka thumna awte hong ngai in, Topa !
English: I said unto the LORD , Thou art my God: Hear the voice of my supplications, O LORD .

**140:7**
Zolai: Topa, keima Topa, a thahat hong honkhia pa aw, galkidona sungah keimah nong hu hi.
English: O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, Thou hast covered my head in the day of battle.

**140:8**
Zolai: Topa aw, migilo pa’ deihnate tangtungsak kei inla, ama thusia sawmna a maban sotsak kei in!
English: Grant not, O LORD , the desires of the wicked: Further not his wicked device; lest they exalt themselves. Selah.

**140:9**
Zolai: Kei hong umcih mite gualzosak kei inla, kei hong sawmnate uh amau’ lu tung mah tusak in!
English: As for the head of those that compass me about, Let the mischief of their own lips cover them.

**140:10**
Zolai: Amaute tungah mei-am kuang zusak in. A thokikzo nawn lo dingin dum sungah amaute kiasak in!
English: Let burning coals fall upon them: Let them be cast into the fire; Into deep pits, that they rise not up again.

**140:11**
Zolai: Mi gensia pa leitungah mavangsak kei inla, mi ngongtat pa pen thusia in sulzuih ta hen!
English: Let not an evil speaker be established in the earth: Evil shall hunt the violent man to overthrow him .

**140:12**
Zolai: Topa in gimna a thuak mite’ thu a panpihna, mi cimawhte a dingin thu a manin a khenna ka thei hi.
English: I know that the LORD will maintain the cause of the afflicted, And the right of the poor.

**140:13**
Zolai: Thuman mite in nangma min hong phat pelmawh ding uh a, lungsim thutangte pen nangma omna-ah teng ding uh hi.
English: Surely the righteous shall give thanks unto thy name: The upright shall dwell in thy presence.

## Chapter 141

**141:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang kong sam hi; hong kinawh in. Nang kong sap ciangin ka aw hong ngai in.
English: LORD , I cry unto thee: make haste unto me; Give ear unto my voice, when I cry unto thee.

**141:2**
Zolai: Ka thungetna pen na mai-ah paknamtui bangsak inla, ka khutte ka laptohna pen nitak biakpiakna bangsak in.
English: Let my prayer be set forth before thee as incense; And the lifting up of my hands as the evening sacrifice.

**141:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, keima kam a cing ding khat koih inla, ka mukte’ kongkhak a vil ding khat koih in.
English: Set a watch, O LORD , before my mouth; Keep the door of my lips.

**141:4**
Zolai: Mawh bawlnopna lungsim hong neisak kei inla, a gilo mite tawh hong kikhawlsak kei in. Amau’ anlimte hong duhgawh sak kei ta in.
English: Incline not my heart to any evil thing, To practise wicked works with men that work iniquity: And let me not eat of their dainties.

**141:5**
Zolai: Mipha pa kei hong vuasak inla, ahih hangin migilote ka lu sathau nilhsak kei in; bang hang hiam cih leh amau’ gitloh gamtatnate nakpitakin langpangin thu ka ngenngen hi.
English: Let the righteous smite me; It shall be a kindness: And let him reprove me; It shall be an excellent oil, which shall not break my head: For yet my prayer also shall be in their calamities.

**141:6**
Zolai: Amaute, thu kisitin mawhsakna a thuak uh ciangin, Topa’ thute man hi, ci-in a thei ding uh hi.
English: When their judges are overthrown in stony places, They shall hear my words; for they are sweet.

**141:7**
Zolai: Mi khat in suangpi khat sukhamin leitungah a thehthang gawp bangin Leinuai’ kongvangah amau’ guhte kithehthang hi.
English: Our bones are scattered at the grave's mouth, As when one cutteth and cleaveth wood upon the earth.

**141:8**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa Pasian aw, nang ka hong muang tawntung a, nangmah ka hong bel hi. Tua ahih manin kei hong nusia kei in.
English: But mine eyes are unto thee, O GOD the Lord: In thee is my trust; leave not my soul destitute.

**141:9**
Zolai: Amaute in kei hong siahna uh tehlop le siatna bawlte’ thangzak panin kei hong kem in.
English: Keep me from the snares which they have laid for me, and the gins of the workers of iniquity.

**141:10**
Zolai: Kei ka suahtak khit ciangin amau’ ngenthang sung mahah migilote awksak in.
English: Let the wicked fall into their own nets, whilst that I withal escape.

## Chapter 142

**142:1**
Zolai: Topa’ hong huh ding ngenin ka kiko a, Topa’ tungah ka thum hi.
English: I cried unto the LORD with my voice; With my voice unto the LORD did I make my supplication.

**142:2**
Zolai: Ama mai-ah ka lungkim lohna ka sung a, ama mai-ah ka haksatna teng ka gen hi.
English: I poured out my complaint before him; I shewed before him my trouble.

**142:3**
Zolai: Ka cih nading ka theih nawn loh ciangin, amah in ka mailam ding hong theihsak hi. Ka paina lampi-ah ka galte in tehlop khat tawh kei hong siah uh hi.
English: When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, then thou knewest my path. In the way wherein I walked have they privily laid a snare for me.

**142:4**
Zolai: Ka kiim ka pam khuadakin ka en kawikawi a, ahih hangin kei hong huh ding kuamah om lo hi. Ka belh ding kuamah om lo a, kuamah in kei hong don lo hi.
English: I looked on my right hand, And beheld, but there was no man that would know me: Refuge failed me; No man cared for my soul.

**142:5**
Zolai: Topa aw, nang tungah kong kiko hi. Nang pen keima belh na hi a, a hingte’ leitangah keima tanh na hi hi, ka hong ci hi.
English: I cried unto thee, O LORD : I said, Thou art my refuge and my portion in the land of the living.

**142:6**
Zolai: Ka kikona hong ngai in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nakpitakin kei hong kiniamkoih suk hi. Kei hong bawlsiate’ kiang pan hong honkhia in. Bang hang hiam cih leh kei a dingin amaute hatlua uh hi.
English: Attend unto my cry; For I am brought very low: Deliver me from my persecutors; For they are stronger than I.

**142:7**
Zolai: Thong sung panin kei hong lakhia in. Tua ciangin nangma mite tawh kong phatkhawm ding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh itna lianpi tawh kei tungah nong gamta hi.
English: Bring my soul out of prison, That I may praise thy name: The righteous shall compass me about; For thou shalt deal bountifully with me.

## Chapter 143

**143:1**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka thungetna hong za inla, kong thumnate hong ngai in. Na thumanna le na thutakna tawh kizui-in kei hong dawng in.
English: Hear my prayer, O LORD , give ear to my supplications: In thy faithfulness answer me, and in thy righteousness.

**143:2**
Zolai: Na nasempa, thu hong sit kei in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma mai-ah mihing a dikzo kuamah om lo hi.
English: And enter not into judgment with thy servant: For in thy sight shall no man living be justified.

**143:3**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh gal in kei hong bawlsia-in hong zogawp hi. Sauveipi lai-a a site bangin a mial sungah hong tusak hi.
English: For the enemy hath persecuted my soul; He hath smitten my life down to the ground; He hath made me to dwell in darkness, as those that have been long dead.

**143:4**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin cih nading ka thei nawn kei a, ka lungtangah si teng nawn lo hi.
English: Therefore is my spirit overwhelmed within me; My heart within me is desolate.

**143:5**
Zolai: Hun luite ka phawk a, na sepsa khempeuh ka ngaihsunsun hi. Na khut in a sepsa nate ka lungngaingai hi.
English: I remember the days of old; I meditate on all thy works; I muse on the work of thy hands.

**143:6**
Zolai: Thu ngenin nang lamah ka khutte ka hong zan a, lei keu in tui a duh bangin nang ka hong duh hi.
English: I stretch forth my hands unto thee: My soul thirsteth after thee, as a thirsty land. Selah.

**143:7**
Zolai: Topa aw, kei hong dawng mengmeng in. Kei ka cimawh ta hi. Leihawm sung misite kiangah a paisukte tawh ka kibat loh nadingin kei kiang panin na maitang seel kei in.
English: Hear me speedily, O LORD : my spirit faileth: Hide not thy face from me, lest I be like unto them that go down into the pit.

**143:8**
Zolai: Nang hong muang ka hih manin zingsang simin na itna kip kei hong phawksak in. Nangma tungah thu hong ngen ka hih manin ka pai nading lampi hong hilh ta in.
English: Cause me to hear thy lovingkindness in the morning; For in thee do I trust: Cause me to know the way wherein I should walk; For I lift up my soul unto thee.

**143:9**
Zolai: Topa aw, ka langte’ kiang panin kei hong honkhia in. Nangmah a bel dingin ka hong tai hi.
English: Deliver me, O LORD , from mine enemies: I flee unto thee to hide me.

**143:10**
Zolai: Keima Pasian na hih manin nangma deih bangin a gamta dingin kei hong hilh in. Kei hong hehpih inla, lam phei-ah hong kha in.
English: Teach me to do thy will; for thou art my God: Thy spirit is good; lead me into the land of uprightness.

**143:11**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma min na ngaihsutna-in keima nuntakna hong kem in. Nangma thumanna tawh kituakin haksatna panin hong paikhiatpih in.
English: Quicken me, O LORD , for thy name's sake: For thy righteousness' sake bring my soul out of trouble.

**143:12**
Zolai: Kei pen nangma nasem ka hih manin na itna kip tawh kituakin ka galte khenkhia inla, ka langte khempeuh susia in.
English: And of thy mercy cut off mine enemies, And destroy all them that afflict my soul: For I am thy servant.

## Chapter 144

**144:1**
Zolai: Ka khutte galdona ding ka khutmete galkap nadingin a hilh, keimah a hong hu, Topa in thupha ngah tahen.
English: Blessed be the LORD my strength, Which teacheth my hands to war, and my fingers to fight:

**144:2**
Zolai: Amah pen ka suangpi le ka munkip muanhuai, ka kulhpi le hong honkhia pa, ka lum le ka belh pa, ka nuai-ah mite a zopa ahi hi.
English: My goodness, and my fortress; My high tower, and my deliverer; My shield, and he in whom I trust; Who subdueth my people under me.

**144:3**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangmah in na hong phawk tham dingin mi pen bang hi a, nangmah in na hong ngaihsut tham dingin mihing’ tapa bang ahi hiam?
English: LORD , what is man, that thou takest knowledge of him! Or the son of man, that thou makest account of him!

**144:4**
Zolai: Mi pen husan’ khat tawh kibang a, ama hunte pen a tai dandan niliim tawh kibang hi.
English: Man is like to vanity: His days are as a shadow that passeth away.

**144:5**
Zolai: Topa aw, na vanpite niamsak inla, hong paisuk in. Mualte lawng inla, meikhu suaksak in.
English: Bow thy heavens, O LORD , and come down: Touch the mountains, and they shall smoke.

**144:6**
Zolai: Khuaphialep phiasak inla, amaute kithehthang sak in. Na thaltangte lawn inla, amaute susia in.
English: Cast forth lightning, and scatter them: Shoot out thine arrows, and destroy them.

**144:7**
Zolai: A sangna mun panin na khut hong zan inla, tui lian lauhuaite le gamdang mite’ vangliatna panin hong honkhia in.
English: Send thine hand from above; Rid me, and deliver me out of great waters, from the hand of strange children;

**144:8**
Zolai: A kam uh tawh zuauthu a gente le limtakin kiciamna a bawl khit ciang nangawnin zuauthu mah a gen lai vevete’ kiang pan kei hong phel inla, hong honkhia ta in.
English: Whose mouth speaketh vanity, And their right hand is a right hand of falsehood.

**144:9**
Zolai: Pasian aw, la thak khat kong sak ding a, harp zangsawm khausai lasakna nang kong tum ding hi.
English: I will sing a new song unto thee, O God: Upon a psaltery and an instrument of ten strings will I sing praises unto thee.

**144:10**
Zolai: Kumpite tungah gualzawhna a piapa, na nasem David a honkhia pa na hi hi.
English: It is he that giveth salvation unto kings: Who delivereth David his servant from the hurtful sword.

**144:11**
Zolai: A gilo galte kiang panin kei hong hon inla, a kam uh tawh zuauthu a gen limtakin kiciamna a bawl khit ciang nangawnin zuau a gen lai veve gamdang mite’ khutsung pan kei hong honkhia in.
English: Rid me, and deliver me from the hand of strange children, Whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood:

**144:12**
Zolai: Ka tapate uh a tangval lai-in khang cingin a khauh mahmah singkungte bang ta hen la, ka tanute uh a nungak lai-in kumpi inn lamna dinga a kisui innkiu khuampite bang tahen.
English: That our sons may be as plants grown up in their youth; That our daughters may be as corner stones, polished after the similitude of a palace:

**144:13**
Zolai: Ka saalte uh a dimin an nam khempeuh om ta hen la, ka tuute uh a tultul a thenthen-in gamlakah suak tahen.
English: That our garners may be full, affording all manner of store: That our sheep may bring forth thousands and ten thousands in our streets:

**144:14**
Zolai: Ka kongzingte uhah cimawhin kikona om kei tahen.
English: That our oxen may be strong to labour; That there be no breaking in, nor going out; That there be no complaining in our streets.

**144:15**
Zolai: Tua bang thupha a ngah mi mi lungdam ahi hi. Topa pen amau’ Pasian ahi mite pen mi lungdam ahi hi.
English: Happy is that people, that is in such a case: Yea , happy is that people, whose God is the LORD .

## Chapter 145

**145:1**
Zolai: Ka Pasian le ka Kumpipa aw, nangmah hong pahtawi-in a tawntungin nangma min kong phatphat ding hi.
English: I will extol thee, my God, O King; And I will bless thy name for ever and ever.

**145:2**
Zolai: Nisimin hong pahtawi-in a tawntungin nangma min kong phatphat ding hi.
English: Every day will I bless thee; And I will praise thy name for ever and ever.

**145:3**
Zolai: Topa lian hi; nakpitakin phat ding hi a, ama liatna ngaihsutzawh ding hi lo hi.
English: Great is the LORD , and greatly to be praised; And his greatness is unsearchable.

**145:4**
Zolai: A khang a khangin nangma nasepnate kiphatphat ding a, a vanglian na bawlnate kigengen ding hi.
English: One generation shall praise thy works to another, And shall declare thy mighty acts.

**145:5**
Zolai: Na liatna le na minthanna a lamdang nangma sepnate ka lungngaingai ding hi.
English: I will speak of the glorious honour of thy majesty, And of thy wondrous works.

**145:6**
Zolai: A vanglian nangma bawlnate mite in taangko ding uh a, nangma vangliatna mah kei zong ka pulak ding hi.
English: And men shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: And I will declare thy greatness.

**145:7**
Zolai: Amaute in nangma liatna, na minthanna genkhia-in nangma thumanna nakpitakin sa ding uh hi.
English: They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness, And shall sing of thy righteousness.

**145:8**
Zolai: Topa dikin hehpihna nei a, heh hak mahmahin itna kip lianpi a nei hi.
English: The LORD is gracious, and full of compassion; Slow to anger, and of great mercy.

**145:9**
Zolai: Topa pen mi khempeuh tungah hoih a, a bawlsa khempeuh tungah hehpihna a nei hi.
English: The LORD is good to all: And his tender mercies are over all his works.

**145:10**
Zolai: Topa aw, nangma bawlsa khempeuh in nangma tungah lungdamna hong ko ding uh a, na mi siangtho khempeuh in nang hong phat ding uh hi.
English: All thy works shall praise thee, O LORD ; And thy saints shall bless thee.

**145:11**
Zolai: Amaute in na kumpi gam a minthanna thu gengenin na vangliatna thu sutsut ding uh a,
English: They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, And talk of thy power;

**145:12**
Zolai: a vanglian nangma sepnate le na kumpi gam a hoihna, a minthannate mi khempeuh tungah kitheisak ding uh hi.
English: To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, And the glorious majesty of his kingdom.

**145:13**
Zolai: Nangma kumpi gam pen a kip tawntung kumpi gam hi a, nangma ukna khang tawntungin a kip hi. A thuciamna khempeuhah Topa thutak mahmah a, a gamtatna khempeuhah zong hehpihna a nei ahi hi.
English: Thy kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, And thy dominion endureth throughout all generations.

**145:14**
Zolai: Topa in a puk mite khempeuh huh a, niamsakna a thuakte khempeuh a sangtosak hi.
English: The LORD upholdeth all that fall, And raiseth up all those that be bowed down.

**145:15**
Zolai: Nuntak husanna a nei khempeuhte’ mit in nang hong en uh a, a hun a tun ciangin amaute an na vak hi.
English: The eyes of all wait upon thee; And thou givest them their meat in due season.

**145:16**
Zolai: Nangmah in na khut na hong a, nuntak husanna a nei khempeuhte’ deihna a kicingin na pia hi.
English: Thou openest thine hand, And satisfiest the desire of every living thing.

**145:17**
Zolai: Topa pen a sepna khempeuhah thutang a, a gamtatna khempeuhah hehpihna a nei hi.
English: The LORD is righteous in all his ways, And holy in all his works.

**145:18**
Zolai: Amah a sam mi khempeuh kiangah Topa nai om a, lungsim takpi tawh a sam mi khempeuh kiangah amah nai om hi.
English: The LORD is nigh unto all them that call upon him, To all that call upon him in truth.

**145:19**
Zolai: Amah a zahtakte’ deihna a kicingin tungsak a, amaute’ kikona zong za-in amaute a honkhia hi.
English: He will fulfil the desire of them that fear him: He also will hear their cry, and will save them.

**145:20**
Zolai: Topa in amah a itte khempeuh kem a, ahih hangin migilo khempeuh amah in susia ding hi.
English: The LORD preserveth all them that love him: But all the wicked will he destroy.

**145:21**
Zolai: Topa ka phat tawntung ding hi. Mi khempeuh in a tawntungin ama min siangtho phat ta uh hen.
English: My mouth shall speak the praise of the LORD : And let all flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever.

## Chapter 146

**146:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Ke’n, Topa ka phat ding hi.
English: Praise ye the LORD . Praise the LORD , O my soul.

**146:2**
Zolai: Ka hin laiteng Topa ka phat ding a, ka nuntak laiteng ka Pasian’ tungah phatnate ka sa ding hi.
English: While I live will I praise the LORD : I will sing praises unto my God while I have any being.

**146:3**
Zolai: Huhna a hong pia thei lo uliante ahi a, mi mawkmawkte ahi zongin muang kei un.
English: Put not your trust in princes, nor in the son of man, In whom there is no help.

**146:4**
Zolai: A husanna a bei ciangin lei-ah ciahkik uh a, tua ni mahmahin a ngaihsutnate uh beita hi.
English: His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; In that very day his thoughts perish.

**146:5**
Zolai: Jakob’ Pasian pen amah huhpa hi-in, ama Topa Pasian a muang mipa mi lungdam ahi hi.
English: Happy is he that hath the God of Jacob for his help, Whose hope is in the LORD his God:

**146:6**
Zolai: Amah in van le lei, tuipi le tuate sungah a om khempeuh bawl a, a tawntungin thuman hi.
English: Which made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that therein is: Which keepeth truth for ever:

**146:7**
Zolai: A kinengniam mite a dingin thumanna semkhia a, gilkialte an a vak hi. Topa in thongkiate a khahkhia hi.
English: Which executeth judgment for the oppressed: Which giveth food to the hungry. The LORD looseth the prisoners:

**146:8**
Zolai: Topa in mittawte khua a musak hi. Topa in niamsakna a thuak mite sangtosak a, Topa in thuman mite a it hi.
English: The LORD openeth the eyes of the blind: The LORD raiseth them that are bowed down: The LORD loveth the righteous:

**146:9**
Zolai: Topa in peemtate kem a, meigong numeite le pa nei lote a huh hi. Ahih hangin amah in migilote’ vaihawmna a suksiatsak hi.
English: The LORD preserveth the strangers; He relieveth the fatherless and widow: But the way of the wicked he turneth upside down.

**146:10**
Zolai: Zion aw, nangma Pasian Topa in khang tawntungin uk ding hi. Topa phat un.
English: The LORD shall reign for ever, even thy God, O Zion, Unto all generations. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 147

**147:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Bang hang hiam cih leh eite’ Pasian’ tungah phatnate i sak ding hoih hi. Phatna sak ding nuam a, zong a kilawm ahi hi.
English: Praise ye the LORD : For it is good to sing praises unto our God; For it is pleasant; and praise is comely.

**147:2**
Zolai: Topa in Jerusalem khuapi lam a, amah in a kinilkhia Israel-te a kaikhawm hi.
English: The LORD doth build up Jerusalem: He gathereth together the outcasts of Israel.

**147:3**
Zolai: Amah in lungsim kitamte damsak a, amau’ meimate a tuamsak hi.
English: He healeth the broken in heart, And bindeth up their wounds.

**147:4**
Zolai: Amah in aksite a phazah ding seh a, tua aksite amau min ciatin a sam hi.
English: He telleth the number of the stars; He calleth them all by their names.

**147:5**
Zolai: Eite’ Topa lian a, ama vang lian mahmah hi. Amah in thu a theihtelna pen ngaihsutzawh ding hi lo hi.
English: Great is our Lord, and of great power: His understanding is infinite.

**147:6**
Zolai: Topa in a kisikcip mite laamto-in, migilote leilak a denna hi.
English: The LORD lifteth up the meek: He casteth the wicked down to the ground.

**147:7**
Zolai: Topa tungah lungdamkohna la sa unla, laiza lasakna tawh eite’ Pasian’ tungah la ngaih sa un.
English: Sing unto the LORD with thanksgiving; Sing praise upon the harp unto our God:

**147:8**
Zolai: Amah in vanpite meiipi tawh tuamin, leitung a dingin gun bawl a, mualte tungah lopa a posak hi.
English: Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the earth, Who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains.

**147:9**
Zolai: Amah in ganhingte le a ham va-aknote an a vak hi.
English: He giveth to the beast his food, And to the young ravens which cry.

**147:10**
Zolai: Ama lungkimna le amah in nuam a saknate pen sakol thahatna le galhangte’ hang hi lo hi.
English: He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: He taketh not pleasure in the legs of a man.

**147:11**
Zolai: Amah a zahtak mite le ama itna kip a muangte tungah Topa a lungkim hi.
English: The LORD taketh pleasure in them that fear him, In those that hope in his mercy.

**147:12**
Zolai: Jerusalem khuapi aw, Topa phat in. Zion aw, nangma Pasian phat in.
English: Praise the LORD , O Jerusalem; Praise thy God, O Zion.

**147:13**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in na kulhkongpi zawlte tosak a, nangma mite thupha hong piaksak hi.
English: For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; He hath blessed thy children within thee.

**147:14**
Zolai: Amah in na gam sungah kilemna bawl a, mangbuh hoihpente tawh nang hong gilvahsak hi.
English: He maketh peace in thy borders, And filleth thee with the finest of the wheat.

**147:15**
Zolai: Amah in thu hong pia a, ama thu manlangin leitung hong tungsuk hi.
English: He sendeth forth his commandment upon earth: His word runneth very swiftly.

**147:16**
Zolai: Amah in tuumul bangin vukkhal hong pia a, vut bangin vukpak hong thehthang hi.
English: He giveth snow like wool: He scattereth the hoarfrost like ashes.

**147:17**
Zolai: Amah in suangtum bangin tuikhalte hong lawnkhia hi. Tua a votna kua in thuakzo ding ahi hiam?
English: He casteth forth his ice like morsels: Who can stand before his cold?

**147:18**
Zolai: Amah in thu pia-in tuate tuisuak hi. Amah in a huih nungsak a, tuite a luang hi.
English: He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: He causeth his wind to blow, and the waters flow.

**147:19**
Zolai: Amah in Jakob tungah ama thu gen a, Israel tungah ama ngeina kipte le ama biakna ngeina kipte a gen hi.
English: He sheweth his word unto Jacob, His statutes and his judgments unto Israel.

**147:20**
Zolai: Amah in tua bangin minam dang khat peuhpeuh tungah bawl ngei lo hi. Amaute in amah biakna ngeina kipte thei lo uh hi. Topa phat un.
English: He hath not dealt so with any nation: And as for his judgments, they have not known them. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 148

**148:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Vantung panin Topa phat unla, a sangna panin amah phat un.
English: Praise ye the LORD . Praise ye the LORD from the heavens: Praise him in the heights.

**148:2**
Zolai: Ama vantungmi khempeuh aw, amah phat un. Ama mihonte khempeuh aw, amah phat un.
English: Praise ye him, all his angels: Praise ye him, all his hosts.

**148:3**
Zolai: Ni le kha aw, amah phat un. A taang aksi khempeuh aw, amah phat un.
English: Praise ye him, sun and moon: Praise him, all ye stars of light.

**148:4**
Zolai: Van sangpente le vantung a om tuite aw, amah phat un.
English: Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, And ye waters that be above the heavens.

**148:5**
Zolai: Topa’ min amaute phatsak un. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in thu pia a, amaute a piang hi.
English: Let them praise the name of the LORD : For he commanded, and they were created.

**148:6**
Zolai: Amaute a tawntung a om dingin amah in kipsak a, a palsat loh ding uh thupiakna amah in a bawl hi.
English: He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: He hath made a decree which shall not pass.

**148:7**
Zolai: Leitung panin Topa phat un, no gulpi liante le tuipi thuk khempeuh,
English: Praise the LORD from the earth, Ye dragons, and all deeps:

**148:8**
Zolai: mei le gial, tuikhal le vuk, ama thupiakna a mang huihpi!
English: Fire, and hail; snow, and vapours; Stormy wind fulfilling his word:

**148:9**
Zolai: Amah phat un, no mual liante le mual neute khempeuh, gah a nei singkungte le taamtak singkung khempeuh!
English: Mountains, and all hills; Fruitful trees, and all cedars:

**148:10**
Zolai: Gamsate le innsate khempeuh, a bokvak ganhingte le a leeng vasate khempeuh!
English: Beasts, and all cattle; Creeping things, and flying fowl:

**148:11**
Zolai: No leitung kumpite le mihing khempeuh, leitung uliante le thukhente khempeuh!
English: Kings of the earth, and all people; Princes, and all judges of the earth:

**148:12**
Zolai: Nungakte le tangvalte, teeksiate le naupangte aw, amah phat un.
English: Both young men, and maidens; Old men, and children:

**148:13**
Zolai: Topa’ min phat un. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah bek a minlian hi a, ama minthanna pen leitung le vantung sangin sangzaw lai hi.
English: Let them praise the name of the LORD : For his name alone is excellent; His glory is above the earth and heaven.

**148:14**
Zolai: Amah in ama mite thahatsak a, ama mi siangthote khempeuh, ama mai-ah a om Israel-te khempeuh in amah phat uh hi. Topa phat un.
English: He also exalteth the horn of his people, The praise of all his saints; Even of the children of Israel, a people near unto him. Praise ye the LORD .

## Chapter 149

**149:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Topa’ tungah la thak sa un. A thuman mite’ kikhopna sungah amah phatna sa un.
English: Praise ye the LORD . Sing unto the LORD a new song, And his praise in the congregation of saints.

**149:2**
Zolai: Amah a Bawlpa tungah Israel lungdam hen la, amau’ Kumpipa’ tungah Zion mite kipak tahen.
English: Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: Let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.

**149:3**
Zolai: Lamna tawh amah phat unla, khuang le laiza lasakna tawh ama tungah la ngaih sa un.
English: Let them praise his name in the dance: Let them sing praises unto him with the timbrel and harp.

**149:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ama mite tungah Topa lungdam a, miniamte gualzo sakin a pahtawi hi.
English: For the LORD taketh pleasure in his people: He will beautify the meek with salvation.

**149:5**
Zolai: A gualzawhna uhah thuman mite lungdamin diang uh hen la, ama mai-ah khukdinin nuamna la sa uh hen.
English: Let the saints be joyful in glory: Let them sing aloud upon their beds.

**149:6**
Zolai: Minam dangte tungah phu la-in gim a pia ding, a kumpite uh sikkhau tawh henin a miliante uh sikkol a bulh ding, a kigelhsa thukhenna bangin amaute tungah a semkhia dingin langnih a hiam namsau a tawi kawmun Pasian phatin awng ta uh hen. Hih pen Pasian’ mite’ gualzawhna ahi hi. Topa phat un.
English: Let the high praises of God be in their mouth, And a twoedged sword in their hand;

## Chapter 150

**150:1**
Zolai: Topa phat un. Ama biakinn sungah Pasian phat unla, ama vangliatna mun vantungah amah phat un.
English: Praise ye the LORD . Praise God in his sanctuary: Praise him in the firmament of his power.

**150:2**
Zolai: A vanglian ama sepnate hangin amah phat unla, a liat mahmahna tawh kituakin amah phat un.
English: Praise him for his mighty acts: Praise him according to his excellent greatness.

**150:3**
Zolai: Peengkul aw tawh amah phat unla, githa lasakna le harp lasakna tawh amah phat un.
English: Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: Praise him with the psaltery and harp.

**150:4**
Zolai: Khuang le lamna tawh amah phat unla, khausai lasaknate le tamngai tawh amah phat un.
English: Praise him with the timbrel and dance: Praise him with stringed instruments and organs.

**150:5**
Zolai: Daltuahte tawh amah phat unla, nakpitakin a ging daltuahte tawh amah phat un.
English: Praise him upon the loud cymbals: Praise him upon the high sounding cymbals.

**150:6**
Zolai: Husang thei khempeuh in Topa phat un. Topa phat un.
English: Let every thing that hath breath Praise the LORD . Praise ye the LORD .
